# Completed phases — archive

Pre-Phase 38 work (chart editor data spine, structured chart authoring, segment progress, Discovery + fork, collaboration core, history / branch / diff) plus Phase 41.x (F1 Pro subscription + dynamic symbols, closed at 41.5 / 41.5.1). Each entry preserves the full design rationale, scope cuts, and code-review findings from the original CLAUDE.md `### Completed` section.

Beta wave entries (Phase 38.x + 39.x) live in [`.claude/CLAUDE.md`](../../../.claude/CLAUDE.md) under `## Development Roadmap > ### Completed`. When a wave fully closes — OR at a major-release commit (e.g. v1.0 / Phase 40), whichever comes first — its entries are promoted here per the **Archive policy** in CLAUDE.md.

Index of phases (jump targets via the headings below or by `<C-f>` for `**Phase N`):

- Phase 1 — 1.5 — 2a-c — 3a-b — 3b+ — 3b-pre — Row counter, Result pattern, Project edit, UX polish, Supabase foundation, Sharing data spine
- Phase 4a — 4b — 5a-d — iOS app shell, Sharing UX, Comments, Activity feed, User profiles
- Phase 6 — 7a — 7b — 7.5 — iOS SwiftUI, Compose UI tests, XCTest, dependency cleanup
- Phase 8 — 15.5 — Dispatcher injection, CI/CD foundation, chart image, test coverage 80%, AGP 9.x KMP plugin migration
- Phase 16 — 23.1 — Search/filter, Settings + App Store readiness, Store submission + UI polish, Maestro E2E setup, Pattern management, Progress photos
- Phase 25 — 28 — Onboarding, Discovery (initial), v1 store submission prep, iOS ViewModel lifecycle fix, bundle ID rename
- Phase 30.x / 31 — Symbol dictionary + JIS crochet catalog (parts 1-4), structured chart viewer (Phase 31)
- Phase 32.x — Chart Editor MVP + parametric input + craft picker + system-back
- Phase 33.x — i18n consumer wiring + 15-screen sweep + Maestro testTag de-brittling + per-app locale
- Phase 34 — 35.1d — Per-segment progress + polar coord support
- Phase 36.x — Discovery upgrade + chart-clone fork + parent attribution
- Phase 37.x — Collaboration core: history, branch, diff, restore (ADR-013)
- Phase 41.x — F1 Pro subscription + dynamic symbols (ADR-016)

---

## Phase entries

- **Phase 1**: Row Counter — Project CRUD, increment/decrement, status tracking (62 tests)

- **Phase 1.5**: Progress Notes — row-level memos via ProgressRepository (79 tests)

- **Phase 2a**: Technical Debt — `updated_at` column on ProjectEntity (ADR-003 prerequisite)

- **Phase 2b**: Result Pattern — Unify UseCase error handling with `UseCaseResult<T>` (92 tests)

- **Phase 2c**: Project Edit — Update title/totalRows from detail screen (103 tests)

- **Phase 3a**: UX Polish — ViewModel stateIn unification, error channel consolidation, date formatting, Progress.note non-null (103 tests)

- **Phase 3b**: Supabase Foundation MVP — supabase-kt 3.5.0 integration, Auth (Email/Social), Local/Remote DataSource refactor, ConnectivityMonitor, coordinator repositories, SQL migration, ADR-004 (130 tests)

- **Phase 3b+**: Supabase Sync — PendingSync queue with coalescing/backoff, offline write support (local-first + syncOrEnqueue), RealtimeSyncManager (auth-aware 3-table subscriptions), SyncExecutor, ConnectivityMonitor (Android/iOS), currentRow conflict guard (ADR-003)

- **Phase 4b**: Sharing — Share entity, ShareRepository (remote-only with inline Realtime), fork, deep links

- **Phase 5a**: Comments — CommentRepository with Realtime subscriptions, CommentSectionViewModel

- **Phase 5b**: Activity Feed — ActivityRepository with Realtime, ActivityFeedViewModel

- **Phase 5c**: User Profiles — UserRepository, OfflineUserRepository fallback, Profile screen, GetCurrentUser/UpdateProfile UseCases

- **Phase 6**: iOS SwiftUI — Native SwiftUI screens (7 screens + CommentSection), FlowWrapper StateFlow bridge, KoinHelper ViewModel accessors, NavigationStack routing, deep linking, default hierarchy template fix, ContentView.swift Compose bridge removed

- **Phase 7a**: Android Compose UI Tests — 19 instrumented tests (ProjectList, ProjectDetail, Navigation, Profile screens)

- **Phase 7b**: iOS XCTest — 19 tests (UI + unit), ApplicationScope singleton, Koin startup diagnostics, resetDatabase error handling, UITest reliability improvements

- **Phase 7.5**: Technical Debt Cleanup — Dependency updates (AGP 9.1.0, Koin 4.2.1, Navigation 2.9.7), ProGuard/R8 rules, network security config, iOS safe casting, code quality improvements, SQLDelight indices

- **Phase 15**: Tech Debt Cleanup — RemoteSyncOperations insert→upsert rename, DefaultSyncLogger expect/actual (Android Log.d, iOS NSLog), Progress.ownerId fix with AuthRepository injection, SQLDelight default alignment (471 shared tests)

- **Phase 15.5**: AGP 9.x KMP Plugin Migration — `com.android.library` → `com.android.kotlin.multiplatform.library`, BuildConfig → generated SupabaseCredentials, `androidUnitTest` → `androidHostTest`, dependency updates (ktlint 14.2.0, kotlinx-serialization 1.11.0, Coil 3.4.0, Kover 0.9.8) (471 shared tests)

- **Phase 16**: Search/Filter + builtInKotlin — ViewModel-level search (title substring), status filter (All/Not Started/In Progress/Completed), sort (Recent/Alphabetical/Progress), Material 3 SearchBar + FilterChip (Android), SwiftUI .searchable + Picker (iOS), androidApp builtInKotlin migration (removed org.jetbrains.kotlin.android plugin, android.builtInKotlin=true) (491 shared tests)

- **Phase 27.1**: iOS ViewModel Lifecycle Fix — ScopedViewModel/ProjectDetailHolder holders pin Koin-resolved ViewModels across SwiftUI View re-inits, fixing a real-device onboarding bug where Next/Skip button taps dispatched events to orphan ViewModels while observers stayed bound to the original state flow. Migrated all 12 iOS screens + AppRootView to the holder pattern; added 2 XCTest regression cases and a Maestro `nextButton` flow. Android E2E stabilized against Pixel Launcher ANR via emulator RAM bump (4096 MB), VM heap (1024 MB), CPU pinning, cold-boot settle and dialog-dismiss loops. ADR-007 records the pivot away from v1.0 store submission. (591 shared + 21 iOS UI tests)

- **Phase 28**: Bundle ID Rename — `com.skeinly.*` → `io.github.b150005.skeinly` across Kotlin packages (322 files, 9 source-root directories moved), SQLDelight package, iOS bundle ID + bundleIdPrefix + CFBundleURLName, Android applicationId + namespace, ProGuard rules, Kover exclusions, generated SupabaseCredentials package, Maestro E2E flow appIds (Android + iOS), store-listing + e2e docs. `skeinly://` URL scheme, `skeinly.db` filename, "Skeinly" display name, and `Skeinly*` class names preserved. (591 shared tests × 2 platforms + 19 iOS UI tests)

- **Phase 31**: Structured Chart Viewer — `SymbolRenderTransform` pure helper (commonMain) maps unit-square (y-down, 0..1) symbol coordinates to a screen-space cell rect with axis-aligned rotation around the cell center (consumed by both renderers). Compose `ChartViewerScreen` (Scaffold + Canvas + grid background + FilterChip layer toggles + `Modifier.transformable` pan/zoom + parsed-path memoization + parameter-slot text + `?` placeholder for unknown symbol ids). SwiftUI `StructuredChartViewerScreen` mirror via shared bridge (`ScopedViewModel` pattern, magnification + drag gestures, `PathCommandCache` `ObservableObject`). `ChartViewerViewModel` observes by patternId with error surfacing. Wired through Koin (`SymbolCatalog` single, ViewModel factory), NavGraph (`ChartViewer(patternId)`), and ProjectDetail "View structured chart" entry on both platforms. +15 commonTest (SymbolRenderTransform 12 + ChartViewerViewModel 3 then later 4 with error path).

- **Phase 30.1**: Knitter review + Symbol Dictionary — `SymbolGalleryScreen` on both platforms (Compose `LazyVerticalGrid` / SwiftUI `LazyVGrid` over `SymbolCatalog.all()`, each card shows the rendered glyph plus JA + EN labels and id always visible per design direction until Phase 33 i18n). `SymbolGalleryViewModel` (category filter-ready, search-ready state shape). ProjectList entry point added (Android top-bar `GridView` IconButton, iOS overflow menu entry). Knitter written review committed to `docs/en/symbol-review/phase-30.1.md` (+ `docs/ja/`); ADR-008 addendum records next-category decision (`jis.crochet.*`) and geometry follow-up plan. +4 commonTest.

- **Phase 30.1-fix**: `KnitSymbols.kt` geometry corrections per knitter advisory — purl bar narrowed, cable under-strokes broken, SSK/k2tog/p2tog/k3tog redrawn as stem+slash, `std.cyc.kfb` namespace addition.

- **Phase 30.2 (+ fix)**: `jis.crochet.*` catalog first pass — ~25 glyphs (ch / sc / hdc / dc / tr / sl-st / cluster variants) per JIS L 0201 Table 2 + CYC. Follow-up fix added `SymbolDefinition.fill` field for glyphs that JIS / publisher convention draws filled (sl-st, bobble); stroke-vs-fill is now per-symbol.

- **Phase 30.3**: crochet catalog extension — `jis.crochet.{reverse-sc, puff, hdc-cluster-3}`.

- **Phase 30.4**: Knitter-priority glyph bundle — 7 new `jis.crochet.*` glyphs (`hdc-cluster-5` widthUnits=2 mirror of `dc-cluster-5`; `dc-crossed-2` widthUnits=2 aran-style X with per-stem top-bar+slash; `bullion` two-coil spring silhouette, JIS-silent; `solomon-knot` two-arc open loop, JIS-silent; `picot-4`/`picot-5` w=1 with progressive loop size; `picot-6` w=2 arch per ADR-009 §8 clause). `picot-3` gains bare `"picot"` alias per ADR-009 §4 (shortest family member carries the stem). `hdc-cluster-3` outer stems widened 0.25/0.75 → 0.22/0.78 per Phase 30.3 deferred polish (no-slash hdc-cluster stems read as one thick line on 24dp low-DPI Android without the gap). Existing `all entries declare a JIS reference to Table 2` test amended to exempt `solomon-knot` + `bullion` (intentionally null `jisReference`; JIS L 0201 Table 2 does not enumerate either). Knitter advisory caught and fixed pre-impl: M1 (solomon-knot closed-pill → open-loop form), m1 (bullion 3 coils → 2 to clear Phase 30.2 §3.5 density threshold at 24dp), m2 (dc-crossed-2 stem-endpoint comment so future readers don't "correct" top-bars back to pre-cross column positions), m3 (picot-6 loop x∈[0.1, 0.9] → x∈[0.05, 0.95] so widthUnits=2 stretch truly spans ~2 cells). Catalog total 35 crochet glyphs (~95% JP commercial coverage). Code review: APPROVED after 1 LOW fix (bullion `"bullion"` alias added for cross-convention lookup symmetry with `reverse-sc`'s `"rsc"` alias). +8 commonTest (776 total).

- **Phase 33**: i18n skeleton — 21 seed keys synced across `values/strings.xml` + `values-ja/strings.xml` + `iosApp/.../Localizable.xcstrings`. `iosApp/project.yml` CFBundleDevelopmentRegion + CFBundleLocalizations. `scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` drift-check wired into CI `shared-checks`. `docs/{en,ja}/i18n-convention.md` documents role-prefixed key naming. Consumer wiring from shared Compose screens is a follow-up (see Tech Debt Backlog).

- **Phase 33.2**: Maestro testTag sweep — follow-up to the Phase 33.1 i18n sweep that closed the "non-dialog" half of the `text: "Back"` / `text: "Clear search"` brittleness Tech Debt entry. Adds locale-independent testTags across 12 shared Compose screens and pivots all 9 Android Maestro flows away from content-description text selectors. **Kotlin additions**: (1) `backButton` testTag on the TopAppBar navigationIcon IconButton of `PatternEditScreen`, `ProfileScreen`, `SharedContentScreen`, `ChartEditorScreen` (renamed from pre-existing `editorBackButton` for uniformity — also updated iOS `StructuredChartEditorScreen.swift` `.accessibilityIdentifier`), `ProjectDetailScreen`, `ActivityFeedScreen`, `PatternLibraryScreen`, `DiscoveryScreen`, `ChartViewerScreen`, `SymbolGalleryScreen`, `SharedWithMeScreen`, `SettingsScreen` (12 screens total); (2) `clearSearchButton` testTag on the trailing-icon Clear IconButton of `ProjectListScreen`, `DiscoveryScreen`, `PatternLibraryScreen`; (3) `editProjectButton` testTag on `ProjectDetailScreen` TopAppBar Edit IconButton; (4) `newProjectDialog` / `editProjectDialog` root landmark testTags on `CreateProjectDialog` AlertDialog / `EditProjectDialog` AlertDialog respectively, plus `saveButton` testTag on the EditProjectDialog confirm TextButton; (5) `filterAllChip` / `filterInProgressChip` / `filterNotStartedChip` / `filterCompletedChip` per-chip testTags on the ProjectList status FilterChip row — parallel to the 33.1.9 `difficulty{All,Beginner,Intermediate,Advanced}Chip` pattern. **Maestro flow pivots (9 flows)**: `P1_edit_project.yaml` (2: `text: "Edit project"` → `id: "editProjectButton"`, `text: "Back"` → `id: "backButton"`); `P1_search_filter.yaml` (5: `text: "Back"` → `id: "backButton"`, `text: "Clear search"` → `id: "clearSearchButton"`, `tapOn: "In Progress"` / `"Not Started"` / `"All"` → `id: "filter*Chip"`); `P1_symbol_gallery.yaml` (1: back); `P1_discovery_browse.yaml` (2: back + clear-search); `P2_navigation.yaml` (3: two Profile/Settings back navs + one ProjectDetail back nav). **Dialog-content selectors NOT pivoted** (documented constraint per Phase 20b): `tapOn: "Project Name"` / `tapOn: "Total Rows (optional)"` / `tapOn: "Create"` / `tapOn: "Save"` / `assertVisible: "New Project"` / `assertVisible: "Edit Project"` / `below: "Edit Project"` scoping still use text selectors because Compose `AlertDialog` renders in a separate Android `Window` and `testTagsAsResourceId = true` on the root Box does not propagate through the dialog window boundary — Maestro cannot resolve dialog-content testTags on Android currently. The 33.2 dialog testTags (`newProjectDialog`, `editProjectDialog`, `createProjectButton`, `saveButton`) are added on the Compose side for forward-compat and Compose UI instrumented-test use, but do not unblock Maestro today. `createProjectButton` already existed per Phase 20a; 33.2 added the three new ones. Closing the dialog-content half of the brittleness debt is deferred pending either upstream Maestro cross-window testTag support or an invasive `CompositionLocalProvider`-based workaround inside the dialog content. **Test-code side effect**: `ProjectDetailScreenTest.backButton_callsCallback` still uses `onNodeWithContentDescription("Back")` — Compose instrumented tests run in the app's default locale (en-US on CI), not the user-app locale, so this keeps working. Not migrated to `onNodeWithTag("backButton")` in this sweep to keep the 33.2 diff scoped, but the testTag addition unblocks that future migration. **Behavior changes**: none — pure additive instrumentation. No i18n key additions (232 keys unchanged). No new commonTest (780 shared). **Scope cut**: the ja-JP E2E verification run was planned but the prior session's `/tmp/ja-e2e/` discovery artifacts were wiped by a filesystem reset, and the wrapper script + clearState-stripped flow copies would need to be recreated from the Maestro log to re-attempt; verification deferred to the next ja-JP run session. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 780 tests, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 232 keys). en-US run via `scripts/run-android.sh` not executed in this session (no Android emulator available) — en-US regression potential is low because every pivot is a `text:` → `id:` swap on a testTag that maps to the same DOM element via `testTagsAsResourceId = true`, and all touched screens remain compile-clean.

- **Phase 33.4**: Dialog i18n + cross-window testTag spike (closes Phase 33.2 dialog-half debt) — migrates the last two shared Compose surfaces still rendering English under `stringResource` consumers: `CreateProjectDialog.kt` (under `ui/projectlist/`) and `EditProjectDialog` private composable at the bottom of `ProjectDetailScreen.kt` (its outer screen was i18n'd in 33.1.3 / 33.1.12 but the nested dialog had been deferred per the "dialog-cross-window testTag" caveat). 4 new keys across all 5 i18n sources (236 total, +4): `dialog_new_project_title`, `label_pattern_optional`, `label_none`, `action_create`. Reuses: `label_title` (now harmonized with EditProjectDialog — Kotlin previously rendered "Project Name" and iOS "Project Title"; both now resolve `label_title` = "Title" since the dialog's own nav title "New Project" / "Edit Project" provides sufficient context, same platform-parity class as Phase 33.1.10 iOS delete-confirmation harmonization), `label_total_rows_optional`, `action_cancel`, `action_save`, `action_create_project` (empty-state CTA, pre-existing full-phrase form — `action_create` is the new short dialog-confirm variant, same platform-idiom split as `action_fork` / `action_fork_pattern` from 33.1.9). **The cross-window spike — closes 33.2's "dialog-content selectors NOT pivoted" debt**: new `ui/platform/DialogTestTagsSemantics.{kt,android.kt,ios.kt}` `expect/actual` helper following the Phase 32.4 `SystemBackHandler` pattern. Android `actual fun Modifier.dialogTestTagsAsResourceId(): Modifier = this.semantics { testTagsAsResourceId = true }`; iOS `actual fun Modifier.dialogTestTagsAsResourceId(): Modifier = this` no-op (SwiftUI sheets don't have the cross-window gap — accessibilityIdentifier propagates natively). Applied on the `AlertDialog` `modifier` chain alongside the existing root-landmark testTag. **Empirically verified**: a fresh `adb shell uiautomator dump` on an open create dialog now exposes `<node resource-id="newProjectDialog" ...>` plus `resource-id="projectNameInput"`, `"totalRowsInput"`, `"createProjectButton"` on every descendant node — previously only the `<hierarchy>` root existed, with zero `resource-id` on any dialog-internal node. Kover exclusion for `ui.platform.*` was already in place from Phase 32.4 and covers the new file. **Maestro flow pivots — 9 flows**: 5 Android (`P0_create_project.yaml`, `P0_row_counter.yaml`, `P1_edit_project.yaml`, `P1_search_filter.yaml`, `P2_navigation.yaml`) and 5 iOS (same list, plus `P0_app_launch.yaml`). Every `tapOn: "Project Name"` / `tapOn: "Project Title"` / `tapOn: "Total Rows (optional)"` / `tapOn: "Create"` / `tapOn: "Save"` / `assertVisible: "New Project"` / `assertVisible: "Edit Project"` / `below: "Edit Project"` scoping that Phase 33.2 had to leave as English-text-brittle is now `id:`-based (`projectNameInput`, `totalRowsInput`, `createProjectButton`, `saveButton`, `newProjectDialog`, `editProjectDialog`). Two deliberate holdouts on iOS flows: `P0_create_project.yaml:25` `assertVisible: "New Project"` and `P1_edit_project.yaml` `assertVisible: "Edit Project"` remain as English literal because SwiftUI `NavigationStack` nav title is not an `accessibilityIdentifier`-addressable element — a landmark id on an `.accessibilityElement(children: .contain)` wrapper would be the correct pivot but would require a bigger ProjectListScreen.swift refactor; deferred with explanatory inline comments pointing at the iOS ProjectList i18n sweep. Store-asset screenshot flows (`e2e/store-assets/capture_{android,ios}.yaml`) also pivoted (code review MEDIUM catch — they were not in the main CI E2E but would break the next screenshot run). **iOS SwiftUI mirror**: `createProjectSheet` in `ProjectListScreen.swift` migrated to `LocalizedStringKey(...)` wrapping per the convention doc literal-promotion table — `.navigationTitle(LocalizedStringKey("dialog_new_project_title"))`, `TextField(LocalizedStringKey("label_title"), ...)`, `Picker(LocalizedStringKey("label_pattern_optional"), ...)`, `Text(LocalizedStringKey("label_none"))`, `Button(LocalizedStringKey("action_create"))` etc; user-authored `pattern.title` uses `Text(verbatim:)` to block LocalizedStringKey from resolving arbitrary user text. **iOS accessibilityIdentifier rename** (code review LOW in 33.4 review — identified pre-existing collision, fixed): iOS toolbar `+` button renamed from `createProjectButton` → `createProjectFab` to align with Kotlin's `createProjectFab` naming and resolve a name collision with the sheet-confirm button, which now owns `createProjectButton`. `iosAppUITests/Helpers/TestHelpers.swift` + `ProjectListUITests.swift` updated accordingly. One remaining `app.buttons["Cancel"]` in `ProjectListUITests.swift:57` is explicitly flagged with an in-code comment (ProjectListScreen.swift still English-hardcoded so "Cancel" is a valid literal in the current test env; pivots alongside the pending iOS ProjectList sweep). **iOS `editSheet`** (already i18n'd in 33.1.12) gained `projectNameInput` / `totalRowsInput` / `saveButton` accessibilityIdentifiers for Maestro id-pivot on `P1_edit_project.yaml`. **iOS `editProjectButton` ToolbarItem** accessibilityIdentifier pre-existed from 33.2 and now routes the edit nav tap. **EditProjectDialog Kotlin side** gained `projectNameInput` / `totalRowsInput` testTags on its `OutlinedTextField`s (previously only outer landmark + save button were tagged); AlertDialog now also composes `.dialogTestTagsAsResourceId()` so those testTags resolve as Android resource-ids at runtime. **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 0 HIGH / 1 MEDIUM / 2 LOW — MEDIUM (stale `capture_ios.yaml` selectors) + one LOW (iOS nav-title text assertion) fixed pre-commit; the second LOW was an acknowledgement of the `@file:Suppress("ktlint:standard:filename")` annotation on the `.android.kt`/`.ios.kt` `expect/actual` files mirroring Phase 32.4, no change needed. **Ktlint recurring gotcha**: `.android.kt` `actual fun ...(): Modifier = this.semantics { ... }` initially split the body onto a second line, failed `ktlintAndroidMainSourceSetCheck` with "First line of body expression fits on same line as function signature (standard:function-signature)"; `:shared:ktlintFormat` auto-fixed. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 780 tests unchanged — CMP resource resolution is infrastructure not behavior, and the expect/actual helper is pure Compose plumbing, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 236 keys). **E2E** both locales green: en-US `bash e2e/run-android.sh` 8/8 ✅ in 3m 29s; ja-JP `bash /tmp/ja-e2e/run-ja.sh` 8/8 ✅ in 3m 32s — the ja-JP run was the first live-emulator proof that the 33.4 id-based selectors resolve correctly on a non-English locale, validating both the i18n migration and the dialog-window semantics spike end-to-end in a single run. - **Phase 34**: Per-Segment Progress — ships stitch/section granularity for todo/wip/done on the chart viewer, per ADR-010 and the Phase 34 PRD. Landed across two commits: `b5cf9cd` (data spine, ADR-010 steps 1–7) + `58395e4` (UI layer, US-1..US-4 + Realtime + Reset). **Data spine (b5cf9cd, +29 → 809 tests)**: `ProjectSegment` + `SegmentState` enum with deterministic id `seg:<projectId>:<layerId>:<x>:<y>` (ADR-010 §3 — avoids UUID round-trip and makes coalescing by id trivial); SQLDelight `ProjectSegment.sq` + `3.sqm` migration using `INSERT OR REPLACE` upsert (SQLDelight does not compile `ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE`, documented inline); `LocalProjectSegmentDataSource` + `RemoteProjectSegmentDataSource` + `ProjectSegmentRepositoryImpl`; Supabase migration 013 with `TEXT id` column (matches deterministic id), owner-only RLS (no public-read escape), and Realtime publication entry. Sync wiring: `SyncEntityType.PROJECT_SEGMENT` + `SyncExecutor` branch mapping INSERT/UPDATE both to `remote.upsert` and DELETE to the reset path; `remoteProjectSegment` ctor param added as trailing nullable default to keep existing `SyncExecutor` test call-sites untouched. 4 UseCases: `ObserveProjectSegmentsUseCase` (Flow for viewer overlay), `ToggleSegmentStateUseCase` (todo → wip → done → todo cyclic, AC-2.1..AC-2.3), `MarkSegmentDoneUseCase` (long-press → done idempotent, AC-3.1), `ResetProjectProgressUseCase` (AC-4.x; reads segment ids BEFORE bulk-delete so DELETEs can be enqueued per row for offline sync coalescing). Repository convention: plain-throw suspend returns (matching `StructuredChartRepository` / `ProgressRepository`) — ADR-010 §8 was updated from the initial Result<T> draft + §1 id column reconciled to TEXT. **UI layer (58395e4, +6 → 815 tests)**: Compose + SwiftUI overlay paint (done = filled `onSurface` @ 20%, wip = 2dp `primary` outline, UNDER the symbol glyph per AC-1.1/AC-1.2). Overlay respects `ChartLayer.visible` + `ChartViewerState.hiddenLayerIds` (AC-1.3). Polar charts paint no overlay and show an inline "ships in Phase 35" notice (AC-1.4) — `message_segment_progress_polar_deferred`. Tap → `ToggleSegmentStateUseCase` cycles todo → wip → done → todo via row-delete on done-tap (AC-2.1..AC-2.3). Long-press (≥500ms) → `MarkSegmentDoneUseCase` with platform haptic tick — Android `HapticFeedbackType.LongPress`, iOS `UIImpactFeedbackGenerator` (AC-3.1, AC-3.3). Reuses Phase 32 `GridHitTest` for screen→grid resolution with y-flip (AC-2.4). Empty-cell and invisible-layer taps no-op via shared `topmostLayerAt` helper (AC-2.5, AC-2.6). Project detail "Reset progress" destructive button + confirmation dialog gated on `hasStructuredChart && hasSegmentProgress`, reuses `ResetProjectProgressUseCase` from the data spine; offline-tolerant via existing PendingSync coalescing. `RealtimeSyncManager` gains a 4th channel `project-segments-<ownerId>` alongside projects / progress / patterns, owner-scoped per ADR-010 §6 — second-device sync (AC-6.x) wired end-to-end. Nav: `ChartViewer(patternId, projectId?)` threads project context; when `projectId == null` the viewer stays pure-pattern and the overlay stays empty without engaging the UseCase pipeline. 6 new i18n keys across all 5 sources (242 total, +6): `action_reset_progress`, `dialog_reset_progress_{title,body}`, `label_segments_completed` (parametric, pre-shipped for US-7 follow-up), `message_reset_progress_done`, `message_segment_progress_polar_deferred`. testTags / accessibilityIdentifiers per PRD: `segmentOverlay`, `resetProgressButton`, `resetProgressConfirmButton`. **Code review — 4 HIGH fixed pre-commit** (highest per-commit HIGH count in the codebase, worth the latent context): (1) Koin parameter cursor bug where `params.getOrNull<String>()` re-read `patternId` instead of `projectId`, silently breaking every tap — projectId always resolved to null, overlay engaged UseCase pipeline as pattern-only and taps no-op'd; (2) iOS `.simultaneousGesture` with an `Optional<Gesture>` ternary failing to compile because SwiftUI gesture modifier overloads don't accept Optional — restructured with in-closure `isPolar` guard so the modifier is unconditional and the guard sits inside the tap handler; (3) iOS tap hit-test ignored `.scaleEffect` + `.offset`, so zoomed/panned taps landed on wrong cells — added `toCanvasSpace` inverse transform; (4) iOS long-press + `onTapGesture` double-fire where the tap handler immediately cycled the freshly-done cell back to todo — added `longPressActive` flag with 0.3s suppression window after long-press fires. **Maestro**: P1 flows (Android + iOS) tagged `requires-supabase` — same linked-pattern gating constraint as Phase 32 editor: chart creation in local-only CI would need a pre-seeded fixture, deferred. **Scope cuts per PRD**: US-5 (resume viewport auto-pan) + US-7 (project detail "X / Y stitches (Z%)" summary) — both P1/P2, `label_segments_completed` parametric key pre-shipped so US-7 follow-up is a pure additive render (compute done-count / visible-cell-count in `ProjectDetailViewModel.state`, render under the counter on both platforms, deep-link to ChartViewer on tap). **Known latent iOS risk**: the `longPressActive` 0.3s suppression window is a heuristic that may double-fire on very fast taps; not exercised on a real simulator in the UI-session (compile-check only via `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`). If iOS E2E surfaces the issue, the fix is to gate `handleTap` on a dispatched-to-main-actor `DispatchTime` delta rather than a timer. CI for 58395e4 not verified at session boundary per the Temporary CI-wait policy; b5cf9cd E2E ✅. Pre-push invariants all green on both commits (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 815, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 242).

- **Phase 33.3**: Android per-app locale enablement — unblocks both the end-user Android Settings > App Info > Language picker on Android 13+ and the ja-JP Maestro verification deferred in Phase 33.2-verify. Two-file change: (1) `androidApp/build.gradle.kts` gains `androidResources { generateLocaleConfig = true; localeFilters += listOf("en", "ja") }` inside `android { }` between `buildFeatures` and `packaging`; (2) new `androidApp/src/main/res/resources.properties` declares `unqualifiedResLocale=en-US` (AGP's `extractSupportedLocales` task requires this file adjacent to `values*/` directories — without it the build fails with "No resources.properties file found"). AGP then generates `xml/_generated_res_locale_config.xml` listing `en-US` (default) + `ja` and auto-injects `android:localeConfig="@xml/_generated_res_locale_config"` into the merged manifest. Verified post-build: `aapt2 dump xmltree androidApp-debug.apk AndroidManifest.xml` shows the attribute, and the generated config file content is correct. **Runtime verification**: installed APK, `adb shell cmd locale set-app-locales io.github.b150005.skeinly.android --locales ja-JP`, force-stop, relaunch — home screen renders `プロジェクトを検索…` / `すべて`-`進行中`-`未着手`-`完了` / `プロジェクトがまだありません` / `プロジェクトを作成` correctly (screenshot at `/tmp/ja-e2e/screens/after-fix.png`). "Skeinly" stays English per the `app_name` locale-identical convention. Previously `Activity.Configuration.getLocales()` silently fell back to en-US regardless of the per-app locale stored in `LocaleManagerService`; that resolution path now honors the per-app value. **E2E**: en-US `e2e/run-android.sh` 8/8 ✅ in 3m 31s (no regression). ja-JP `/tmp/ja-e2e/run-ja.sh` 8/8 ✅ in 3m 30s — **important interpretation caveat**: the dialog-content text selectors in `P0_create_project.yaml` / `P1_edit_project.yaml` (`tapOn: "Project Name"`, `tapOn: "Total Rows (optional)"`, `tapOn: "Create"`, `assertVisible: "New Project"`, etc.) still resolve under ja-JP because `CreateProjectDialog.kt` and `EditProjectDialog.kt` (under `shared/src/commonMain/.../ui/projectlist/` and `ui/projectdetail/`) have not been i18n'd yet — they still hardcode `Text("New Project")` / `label = { Text("Project Name") }` / etc. This is independent i18n debt, not a sign that the Phase 33.2 dialog-cross-window testTag issue is resolved. Tracked under the "Maestro `text: \"Back\"` / `text: \"Clear search\"` brittleness" Tech Debt entry's open-dialog half; the "ja-JP currently-passing" nature of those selectors is load-bearing on those two dialogs staying English-hardcoded until the dialog-half is closed. **`localeFilters` format gotcha** (worth documenting for next reader): code reviewer's LOW suggested BCP 47 tags `listOf("en-US", "ja-JP")` to match `resources.properties`'s `unqualifiedResLocale=en-US` spelling; applied it and the build failed with aapt2 `error: invalid config 'en-US' for -c option.` at `:androidApp:generateDebugLocaleConfig`. AGP's `localeFilters` uses aapt2 resource-qualifier format (`<lang>` bare, or `<lang>-r<REGION>` for region-qualified like `en-rGB`), NOT BCP 47 — these two config systems are distinct despite both sitting on the Android side. Reverted to `listOf("en", "ja")` with an inline Gradle comment documenting the format requirement and naming `"en-rGB"` as the hypothetical future region-variant spelling so the next reader doesn't repeat the experiment. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 780 tests, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 232 keys). Code review: APPROVED with 1 LOW that was subsequently proven incorrect by the aapt2 format constraint — captured as an inline comment in the Gradle file so the experiment doesn't get re-run. No test delta — AGP locale config is infrastructure, not behavior.

- **Phase 33.2-verify**: post-push verification of the 33.2 testTag sweep. CI for 943ac55 confirmed green across all three jobs (CI, Security, E2E) — neither of the prior flake classes (Security CodeQL Swift ENOTFOUND, E2E iOS Maestro startup timeout) reappeared. Android emulator (API 37, `emulator-5554`) run via `e2e/run-android.sh` under the default en-US locale: **8/8 Maestro flows passed** in 3m 31s (9th flow `P1_discovery_browse` excluded by `--exclude-tags requires-supabase` as designed), confirming the 33.2 `text:` → `id:` pivots do not regress the existing en-US path. **Critical finding — ja-JP verification blocked on a latent prod gap**: attempting `adb shell cmd locale set-app-locales io.github.b150005.skeinly.android --locales ja-JP` + force-stop + relaunch rendered the app in English (`get-app-locales` returns `[ja-JP]` but the Activity's `Configuration.getLocales()` still resolves en-US). Root cause: `androidApp/src/main/AndroidManifest.xml` declares no `android:localeConfig` attribute and `androidApp/build.gradle.kts` has no `androidResources { generateLocaleConfig = true }`. Without one of those, Android 13+ `LocaleManagerService` stores the per-app locale but the runtime `Configuration` does not honor it — CMP's `Res.string.*` resolution (which reads `LocalConfiguration.current.locales`) falls back to the system locale, which was en-US on this emulator. `setprop persist.sys.locale ja-JP` failed (non-rooted emulator blocks the setprop) and `settings put system system_locales ja-JP,en-US` had no effect without a reboot, so the system-locale fallback path remained unavailable. This also explains retroactively why the prior session's "6/9 ja-JP fail" baseline was misleading — with per-app locale silently failing, those 6 failures could not have been Japanese-text-selector mismatches; they were likely stale-emulator or misconstructed-flow-copy artifacts from the `/tmp/ja-e2e/` scratch work that got wiped. **Consequence for the 33.2 sweep's acceptance criterion**: the non-dialog Tech Debt caveat ("dialog half remains open pending Maestro cross-window testTag resolution") is technically unverified under ja-JP, but the non-dialog pivots are all `text:` → `id:` swaps on testTags routed through `testTagsAsResourceId = true` — locale cannot regress an id-based selector that maps to a stable DOM `resource-id` string. en-US green confirms the pivot mechanics; ja-JP would be a sanity-assert, not a new-information test. **Scope decision**: the one-line `generateLocaleConfig = true` fix (plus adding `en` / `ja` to `androidResources.localeFilters` to constrain generation) is a legitimate production change — without it, users cannot switch the app to Japanese via Android's per-app language picker even if the app's Android-side `values-ja/strings.xml` and CMP `values-ja/strings.xml` ship complete translations. Bundling the fix into a ja-JP verification task would conflate infrastructure with verification, so per the task brief's "If a workaround approach is justified, that's a separate Phase 33.3" directive, the Gradle change lives in Phase 33.3. Discovery artifacts persist at `/tmp/ja-e2e/` (wrapper script + first-run log + two verification screenshots showing English rendering despite per-app locale set to ja-JP). Pre-push invariants unchanged from 33.2 (no code touched). No test delta.

`Text(verbatim:)` for user-authored authorName / comment.body / formattedDate to prevent the LocalizedStringKey overload from key-resolving arbitrary user text; iOS `label_someone` resolved via `NSLocalizedString("label_someone", comment: "")` since SwiftUI `LocalizedStringKey` does not expose a raw-string bridge inside computed-property contexts. **Compose `label_selected_prefix` parametric**: consumed via `stringResource(Res.string.label_selected_prefix, user.displayName)` — `%1$s` substitution matches Android XML format specifier; - **Phase 33.1.13**: Shared content i18n — thirteenth shared Compose screen migrated after ChartEditor (33.1), SymbolGallery (33.1.1), ChartViewer (33.1.2), ProjectList (33.1.3), Onboarding (33.1.4), Login (33.1.5), Profile (33.1.6), ActivityFeed (33.1.7), Settings (33.1.8), Discovery (33.1.9), PatternLibrary (33.1.10), PatternEdit (33.1.11), and ProjectDetail (33.1.12). `SharedContentScreen.kt` + `SharedContentScreen.swift` resolve every user-visible literal. 6 new keys (207 total, +6): `title_shared_pattern` (distinct from `title_pattern_library` despite "pattern" overlap), `state_pattern_not_found` (Android-only centered-text fallback when `pattern == null` and no error), `state_could_not_load` (**iOS-only** — ContentUnavailableView title paired with the raw error as description; still ships in Android sources for 5-source parity per `verify-i18n-keys.sh`, documented inline in the EN strings comment block so future readers know the asymmetry is intentional), `state_view_only_share` (persistent permission label — `state_*` not `message_*` because parallel to `state_forking_pattern` not transient feedback), `action_fork_to_projects` ("Fork to My Projects" full-phrase primary CTA; distinct from the shorter `action_fork` / `action_fork_pattern` split from 33.1.9 which covers space-constrained swipe/toolbar idioms — this is a dedicated-screen button so the full phrase reads naturally), `label_projects` (DetailRow count label). - **Phase 33.1.6**: Profile i18n + `message_*` role prefix + SwiftUI literal-promotion convention addendum — seventh shared Compose screen migrated after ChartEditor (33.1), SymbolGallery (33.1.1), ChartViewer (33.1.2), ProjectList (33.1.3), Onboarding (33.1.4), and Login (33.1.5). `ProfileScreen.kt` (Kotlin Compose) and `ProfileScreen.swift` (SwiftUI mirror) now resolve every user-visible literal: `title_profile` (TopAppBar / navigationTitle), `label_avatar` (Icon contentDescription / accessibilityLabel), `label_display_name` (OutlinedTextField label + SwiftUI Section / TextField), `label_bio` (same pattern), `state_profile_load_failed` (post-load `user == null` branch — reused on both platforms since the ViewModel doesn't distinguish "no profile created" from a load failure per review MEDIUM1), `message_profile_updated` (post-save Snackbar; new prefix — see below), and reused `title_error` / `action_ok` (iOS alert), `action_back` / `action_edit` / `action_cancel` / `action_save`. 6 new keys across all 5 i18n sources (91 total, +6). Compose Snackbar still renders `state.error` raw per the Tech Debt Backlog "ViewModel error-message localization" deferral. **New role prefix `message_*`** introduced and documented in `docs/{en,ja}/i18n-convention.md` for transient action-completion feedback (Snackbar / Toast / Alert body) — distinct from `state_*` (load / empty / idle state labels, not action-completion feedback) and `error_*` (failure messages). **Convention doc SwiftUI literal-promotion table** added under "How to reference" on review LOW1 — the table distinguishes APIs where a bare `String` literal auto-localizes (`Text("key")`, `Button("key") { … }`, `Label("key", systemImage:)`, `Section("key")`) from APIs where overload resolution on a bare literal can silently select the `String`-typed overload and skip localization (`.alert("key", ...)`, conditional `.navigationTitle("key")` with a ternary expression). This codifies the 33.1.5 `Text("app_name")` / `LocalizedStringKey(…)` mix and the review HIGH2 hit on this PR. **testTags / accessibilityIdentifiers** added: `profileScreen` (root; SwiftUI uses `ZStack` + `.accessibilityElement(children: .contain) + .accessibilityIdentifier("profileScreen")` — wrapping the state-branch `Group` in a `ZStack` was the review HIGH1 fix because `Group` is a layout-transparent container and propagates modifiers to each child branch independently, which would either duplicate the landmark or break queries depending on which branch is active), `editButton`, `displayNameField`, `bioField`, `cancelButton`, `saveButton`. `ProjectListScreen` (Compose + iOS) also gained a `profileButton` testTag on the Profile IconButton / menu Label so Maestro and XCUITest can route locale-independently — same pattern as the 33.1.3 `searchField` de-brittling. **Maestro pivot**: `e2e/flows/{android,ios}/P2_navigation.yaml` replaced `tapOn: text: "Profile"` / `assertVisible: "Profile"` with `id: "profileButton"` / `id: "profileScreen"` routes. iOS menu `tapOn: "Profile"` left as English literal with an inline comment because iOS `ProjectListScreen.swift` isn't i18n'd yet — that pivot ships with the iOS ProjectList migration PR. **HIGH pivot — iOS XCUITests**: `ProfileUITests.swift` and `NavigationFlowUITests.swift` pivoted from `app.buttons["Profile"]` + `app.navigationBars["Profile"]` to `app.buttons["profileButton"]` + `app.otherElements["profileScreen"]` per the 33.1.4 HIGH rule. These queries would have passed on English CI today and silently failed on any ja-locale simulator run. **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 1 LOW first pass. All 5 findings fixed pre-commit — HIGH1 `Group` → `ZStack` wrap (bare `Group` accessibility modifier propagation footgun), HIGH2 explicit `LocalizedStringKey("title_error")` wrap on `.alert(...)` (matches LoginScreen precedent; bare-literal overload resolution can drop to `String` and skip localization), MEDIUM1 dropped premature `state_no_profile` key (92 → 91; the ViewModel only emits "user == null" after a load failure, so both iOS and Kotlin branches reuse `state_profile_load_failed`), MEDIUM2 repositioned the error-deferral comment onto the `LaunchedEffect(state.error)` block it qualifies rather than the unrelated `profileUpdatedMessage` line above it, LOW1 added the SwiftUI literal-promotion table to the convention doc. Second-pass review: APPROVED, 0 findings. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 776 tests, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 91 keys). CI + Security + E2E all ✅ on commit `f69a365`. No test delta — CMP resource resolution is infrastructure, not behavior. **Scope cut**: 10 shared Compose screens still hardcode English (down from 11) — see Tech Debt Backlog.

- **Phase 33.1.3**: Project list i18n + search-field testTag — fourth shared Compose screen migrated after ChartEditorScreen (33.1), SymbolGalleryScreen (33.1.1), and ChartViewerScreen (33.1.2). `ProjectListScreen.kt` now resolves every user-visible literal via `stringResource(Res.string.*)`: TopAppBar title (reuses `app_name`), 7 IconButton contentDescriptions (Discover, Pattern Library, Symbol Dictionary, Profile, Activity Feed, Shared With Me, Settings), FAB New Project, search placeholder + clear button, 4 status FilterChips (All / In Progress / Not Started / Completed), SortOrder chip/menu labels (6 variants: `label_sort_*` + `_detail` siblings — `RECENT` intentionally reuses the single-form key in both chip and menu per in-code comment since "Recent" reads naturally as a menu entry), two empty-state variants (no-projects + no-matches), StatusChip (3 status variants), `ProjectCard` row-count text (parametric `label_rows_of_total` / `label_rows_current`), swipe-delete contentDescription (reuses `action_delete`), and `DeleteConfirmDialog` (title + parametric body + reused `action_delete` / `action_cancel`). 5-source parity now **65 keys** (+29). New `hint_` prefix introduced for input-field placeholders (`hint_search_projects`) and documented in `i18n-convention.md` (EN + JA) alongside explicit `title_*` / `label_*` role definitions that were implicit before. `SortOrder.chipLabelKey` / `menuLabelKey` extension properties switched from `String` to `StringResource` (pure getters; resolution happens at the composable call site — no composable-rules violation). Parametric strings use Android-standard `%1$d`/`%2$d`/`%1$s` format specifiers, mirrored as `%1$@` in xcstrings for SwiftUI native resolution. **Maestro**: 5 Android flows (`P0_app_launch`, `P0_row_counter`, `P0_create_project`, `P1_edit_project`, `P0_onboarding`) de-brittled by replacing 5 `"No projects yet"` + 1 `"Create Project"` + 1 `assertNotVisible: "No projects yet"` with the pre-existing locale-independent `createProjectFab` testTag landmark. iOS flows untouched (SwiftUI screens, separate literal surface). Other literal asserts (dialog titles, `ProjectDetail` content, status chips on specific cards) left for their respective screen-migration PRs; chip-filter taps (`"In Progress"` / `"Not Started"` / `"All"`) in `P1_search_filter` also left — they pass on CI's English locale and per-chip testTags would be a separate de-brittling sweep. **Known gotcha (fixed post-CI on follow-up commit b0fb3d8)**: Phase 33.1.3 initial commit `15a5ee5` changed the search placeholder from `"Search projects..."` (three ASCII dots) to `"Search projects\u2026"` (U+2026) per the i18n convention's `state_loading` ellipsis style — but Maestro's `tapOn: "text"` uses **regex** semantics, so the existing flow assertion `tapOn: "Search projects..."` was matching "Search projects" + any 3 chars, which does not match the single-char `…`. Failure surfaced only on the first live CI Android emulator run (`P1 - Search & Filter Projects` flow). Fixed by adding `Modifier.testTag("searchField")` to the `OutlinedTextField` and routing the Maestro tap through `id: "searchField"` — locale-independent and immune to future placeholder wording changes. Generalizable lesson: any shared-screen migration that introduces/changes a user-visible literal hit by a Maestro regex selector needs a testTag preflight. Code review: APPROVED with 2 LOW findings, both addressed pre-commit — (1) added `action_symbol_dictionary` key so the GridView IconButton's contentDescription no longer reuses the screen-title key `title_symbol_dictionary` (decouples action semantics from screen title; 5-source key addition); (2) in-code comment on `SortOrder.menuLabelKey` documenting RECENT's deliberate single-key reuse across chip + menu forms. Pre-push invariants all green on both commits (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh`, `testAndroidHostTest` 776 tests). CI + Security + E2E all ✅ on commit `b0fb3d8`. No test delta — CMP resource resolution is infrastructure, not behavior. **Scope cut**: still 13 shared Compose screens hardcoding English — see Tech Debt Backlog `i18n sweep across remaining shared screens`.
