- **Phase 33.1.1**: Symbol gallery i18n + Android CMP resource packaging fix — second shared screen migrated after ChartEditorScreen. `SymbolGalleryScreen.kt` adds one new key (`title_symbol_dictionary` = "Symbol Dictionary" / "記号辞典") and reuses existing `action_back` for the nav IconButton contentDescription. SymbolCatalog domain labels (`SymbolCategory.jaLabel/enLabel`, `SymbolDefinition.*Label/*Description`) intentionally left unmigrated per Phase 33 non-goals in ADR-008. 5-source parity now 34 keys (33 → 34). Existing E2E flows `e2e/flows/{android,ios}/P1_symbol_gallery.yaml` updated to drop the locale-dependent `assertVisible: "Symbol Dictionary"` assertion and rely on the pre-existing locale-independent `symbolGalleryGrid` testTag — this is the only robust E2E pattern once UI text is i18n'd. **Key discovery**: Phase 33.1 shipped a latent Android runtime crash — `org.jetbrains.compose.resources.MissingResourceException: Missing resource with path: composeResources/<pkg>/values/strings.commonMain.cvr`. Root cause: the AGP 9.x `com.android.kotlin.multiplatform.library` plugin (adopted in Phase 15.5) does not wire the CMP resource generator into Android asset packaging, so the CVR files never reach the APK. ChartEditorScreen never exercised this path in CI (no E2E opens the editor), so the crash stayed dormant until SymbolGalleryScreen's Maestro flow opened the gallery and the app returned to the home launcher. Fixed in `androidApp/build.gradle.kts` via a `@CacheableTask`-annotated `CopyComposeResourcesForAndroid` task with `@PathSensitive(PathSensitivity.RELATIVE)` inputs, anchored to `rootProject.layout.projectDirectory` (not the module path, per code review), wired via `androidComponents.onVariants { variant.sources.assets?.addGeneratedSourceDirectory(...); variant.androidTest?.sources?.assets?.addGeneratedSourceDirectory(...) }` so both the main APK and instrumented-test APK get `assets/composeResources/<package>/values{,-ja}/*.cvr`. Documented in `CI Known Limitations` above. Code review: 2 HIGH + 2 MEDIUM + 2 LOW — HIGHs + MEDIUMs fixed pre-commit (androidTest wiring gap, raw `../shared/...` path anchored to rootProject, `@PathSensitive(RELATIVE)`, `@CacheableTask`), LOWs carried as written comments. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 776 tests, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 34 keys). CI + Security + E2E all ✅ on commit `4402bf2`. **Scope cut**: still 15 shared Compose screens hardcoding English — see Tech Debt Backlog `i18n sweep across remaining shared screens`.

- **Phase 33.1**: i18n consumer wiring (plumbing + chart editor reference) — adds the `compose.components.resources` plugin to `shared/build.gradle.kts` with explicit `packageOfResClass = "io.github.b150005.skeinly.generated.resources"` so downstream imports are stable across any future `shared` rename. New source-of-truth pair `shared/src/commonMain/composeResources/values{,-ja}/strings.xml` holds the 33-key superset (21 existing + 12 editor-specific: `title_edit_chart`, `action_more_options`, `state_empty_chart`, `dialog_parameter_edit_title`, `dialog_parameter_enter_title`, `label_craft`, `label_reading`, `label_craft_{knit,crochet}`, `label_reading_{knit_flat,crochet_flat,round}`). `ChartEditorScreen.kt` now resolves every user-visible literal via `stringResource(Res.string.*)` — including craft/reading dropdown labels via private `craftLabelKey` / `readingLabelKey` helpers returning `StringResource`. `slot.enLabel` in `ParameterInputDialog` intentionally NOT migrated (SymbolCatalog labels are deferred per Phase 33 non-goals — ADR-008). `verify-i18n-keys.sh` extended to enforce 5-source key parity (androidApp en/ja + shared en/ja + iOS xcstrings) pivoting on androidApp en as canonical anchor — transitive coverage confirmed via chained diffs. Kover exclusion added for `generated.resources.*` (plugin-generated) and `ChartEditorScreenKt*` (previously missing from the Compose-UI exclusion list — filled the gap while adjacent). `i18n-convention.md` (EN + JA) updated to describe the dual Android-side source split (`R.string.*` for native, `Res.string.*` for shared Compose) and document the 5-file add/remove protocol. No new shared tests — CMP-generated `Res` is infrastructure, not behavior. Code review: APPROVED (0 CRITICAL/HIGH, 2 MEDIUM fixed pre-commit — Kover exclusion + script label ambiguity). 776 shared tests (unchanged). **Scope cut**: only `ChartEditorScreen.kt` migrated as the reference surface — other shared screens (ChartViewerScreen, SymbolGalleryScreen, ProjectListScreen, PatternLibraryScreen, etc.) still hardcode English and need the same treatment as follow-up work.

- **Phase 32.1**: StructuredChart schema v2 — `CraftType { KNIT, CROCHET }` + `ReadingConvention { KNIT_FLAT, CROCHET_FLAT, ROUND }` enums added to the document envelope. Schema bump 1→2 is backward compatible (v1 rows read with defaults, promoted to v2 on next save). `computeContentHash` unchanged (metadata lives outside drawing identity). `UpdateStructuredChartUseCase` has a `metadataUnchanged` guard + auto-promote. No DDL change. ADR-008 Phase 32.1 addendum. +15 commonTest (720 total).

- **Phase 32**: Chart Editor MVP — tap-to-place authoring with undo/redo and save. Shared: `ChartEditorViewModel` (one-shot load via `GetStructuredChartByPatternId` — intentionally not observing so external Realtime does not stomp mid-edit; conflict resolution is Phase 37 scope), `EditHistory` (50-entry `ArrayDeque` snapshot ring buffer with overflow eviction + redo-clear on record), `GridHitTest` (screen→grid with y-flip), `ChartEditorScreen` (Scaffold + Canvas + palette), `SymbolPaletteStrip` (category chips + eraser + symbol cells), `cellScreenRect` extracted from viewer to shared `SymbolDrawing.kt`. iOS: `StructuredChartEditorScreen.swift` via `ScopedViewModel`, `PalettePathCache` ObservableObject, Closeable cancelled in `onDisappear`. Koin + NavGraph + ProjectDetail entries on both platforms. **Scope cuts (MVP)**: `CraftType.KNIT` / `ReadingConvention.KNIT_FLAT` hardcoded (picker = Phase 32.2), 8×8 default grid (picker = Phase 35), flat rect only (polar = Phase 35), Maestro E2E deferred (requires linked-pattern prerequisite — see Tech Debt Backlog), i18n hardcoded English. **Known gotcha that burnt CI**: Kotlin/Native rejects backticked test-fun names containing `(`, `)`, `,` — JVM tolerates. 3 tests renamed in fix commit (6b65df4). +30 commonTest (750 total). Code review: 2 HIGH + 4 MEDIUM + 3 LOW fixes landed before merge (iOS Closeable leak, `save()` stale snapshot, `!!` on errorMessage, vacuous test assertion, eraser icon semantics, pointerInput over-keying, iOS palette SVG parse cache, `availableCategories` memoization).

- **Phase 32.3**: Parametric symbol input per ADR-009 §7 — Phase 32 MVP wrote `symbolParameters = emptyMap()` for every placement, so `ch-space` (the only parametric glyph today) stuck rendering the literal `"n"` placeholder. 32.3 forks `placeCell`: eraser and non-parametric selections keep the immediate-commit path; parametric selections open an inline input dialog and defer commit to `ConfirmParameterInput`. Re-edit reopens the same dialog pre-populated when the user taps a parametric cell with the matching symbol selected. `PendingParameterInput` holds (`symbolId`, `x`, `y`, `slots`, `currentValues`, `isEditingExisting`) and every mutating path — `placeCell`, `undo`, `redo` — short-circuits while it is set, so nothing can rewrite `draftLayers` between dialog-open and confirm. `save()` is async but untouched by parametric state and gated by `hasUnsavedChanges`, so it cannot interleave either. Overwrite of a parametric cell with a non-parametric selection intentionally wipes `symbolParameters` — ADR-009 §5 round-trip preservation is scoped to storage, not editor mutation; called out in-code. Compose: `AlertDialog` + `OutlinedTextField` per slot, drafts keyed by `(x, y, symbolId)`. SwiftUI: `NavigationStack` + `Form` sheet driven by a local `@State var isParameterSheetPresented: Bool` (not a reactive binding — avoids a transient confirm-path race where reading back from the state flow in a `Binding.set` closure could spuriously fire `CancelParameterInput`); `.id("\(symbolId)@\(x),\(y)")` forces a fresh view per-pending so `.onAppear` reseeds cleanly. +8 commonTest (768 total). Code review: 2 HIGH + 4 MEDIUM + 3 LOW — fixed before commit (undo/redo pending-guards, sheet presented-flag decoupling, `.id()` robustness, test 33 catalog pre-condition, ktlint import hygiene, ADR §5 comment, concurrency-invariant comment block).

- **Phase 32.4**: System-back discard dialog — Phase 32 only intercepted the top-bar back button, so Android hardware / predictive-back and iOS NavigationStack back both silently popped the editor and dropped unsaved edits. New `expect/actual` helper `ui/platform/SystemBackHandler` wires `androidx.activity.compose.BackHandler` on Android and stays a no-op on iOS (shared Compose isn't rendered on iOS for the editor — SwiftUI is). `ChartEditorScreen.kt` gates the intercept on `state.hasUnsavedChanges`, so the normal clean-state pop behavior is preserved. iOS `StructuredChartEditorScreen.swift` now sets `.navigationBarBackButtonHidden(true)` + a custom `ToolbarItem(.topBarLeading)` back button that routes through a new local `attemptBack(state:)` helper (mirrors the Compose `attemptBack` closure). `androidx.activity.compose` dep added to shared `androidMain`. Kover exclusion for the new `ui.platform.*` package (Compose plumbing, JVM-untestable; logic is in `ChartEditorViewModel` tests). No new commonTest — the discard-dialog trigger is `state.hasUnsavedChanges` which is already covered. Known iOS limitation: edge-swipe-from-left still pops without the dialog (NavigationStack doesn't expose a swipe-disable API without dropping to UIKit); documented in CI Known Limitations. 768 shared tests (unchanged).

- **Phase 32.2**: Chart Editor craft/reading picker + iOS Closeable leak audit — surfaces `CraftType` + `ReadingConvention` in the editor so CROCHET authoring writes correct metadata instead of the Phase 32 KNIT default. `ChartEditorState` gains `draftCraftType` / `draftReadingConvention`; `SelectCraft` / `SelectReading` events update draft via atomic `_state.update { if (== val) return@update it; it.copy(...) }` guard. Metadata edits deliberately skip `EditHistory` (drawing-only) but still mark `hasUnsavedChanges` on existing charts. On a new chart, metadata alone does not mark dirty — cells are still required to save (21b/21c symmetric tests). `CreateStructuredChartUseCase` now accepts `craftType` + `readingConvention` params (defaults KNIT / KNIT_FLAT). Compose: TopBar overflow `MoreVert` → `DropdownMenu` with non-interactive `Text` section headers (no disabled-button a11y semantics), U+2713 check prefix. SwiftUI: `ellipsis.circle` `Menu` with nested `Picker`s. **Bundled iOS Closeable leak audit** (same anti-pattern fixed in Phase 32 `StructuredChartEditorScreen`): `PatternEditScreen`, `SharedContentScreen`, `DiscoveryScreen` now use `@State Closeable` + `close()` in `.onDisappear`; Discovery / SharedContent additionally guard against `.task { }` re-entry by closing prior subscription before reassigning. `iosApp/Info.plist` regenerated by xcodegen to align with Phase 33 i18n (`CFBundleDevelopmentRegion=en`, `CFBundleLocalizations=[en,ja]`). Code review: APPROVED after 2 HIGH + 2 MEDIUM fixes (TOCTOU guard moved inside `_state.update`, 21c test added, `.task { }` re-entry leak defense, DropdownMenu header a11y). +10 commonTest (760 total). **Gotcha**: `./gradlew ktlintCheck` must run locally before push — JVM toolchain tolerated prior multiline layout; CI ktlint required `computeUnsavedChanges(...)` to start on a new line (fix commit 739fc82).

- **Phase 37.4**: Branch picker + create / switch / restore (ADR-013 §6 §7) — fourth and final read/write slice of Phase 37 closes the entire collaboration-core MVP. Wires the data spine that 37.1 already shipped (`chart_branches` table + `LocalChartBranchDataSource` + `RemoteChartBranchDataSource` + `SyncEntityType.CHART_BRANCH` + `ensureDefaultBranch` auto-create on `create()` / `forkFor()`) into the user-facing branch model: branch picker on `ChartViewerScreen` overflow → "Switch branch" + "New branch" CTA, plus long-press → "Restore as new commit" on `ChartHistoryScreen` (closes the inert 37.2 reserved keys `action_restore_revision` / `dialog_restore_revision_{title,body}`). **Domain repo**: new `ChartBranchRepository` interface (`getByPatternIdAndName`, `getByPatternId`, `observeBranchesForPattern`, `createBranch`, `advanceTip`, `deleteBranch`) implemented by `ChartBranchRepositoryImpl` over the existing `LocalChartBranchDataSource` + `SyncManagerOperations`. `createBranch` is idempotent on `(patternId, branchName)` — reads first to suppress duplicate sync enqueue when the local INSERT-OR-IGNORE would no-op (same pattern as `ensureDefaultBranch`). `advanceTip` reads existing branch row first; if absent silently returns rather than upserting a new row from incomplete data (defensive against pre-37.4 charts that skipped the branch layer). `deleteBranch` enqueues a CHART_BRANCH DELETE — the existing `SyncExecutor.executeChartBranch` DELETE branch from 37.1 is now reachable. **Repository surface change**: `StructuredChartRepository.setTip(patternId: String, targetRevision: ChartRevision): StructuredChart?` is the new branch-switch primitive. `setTip` reads the current `chart_documents` row and rewrites it from the revision's payload INSIDE the same `writeMutex` that `update`/`create`/`forkFor` use — atomic read-then-write so a concurrent chart-editor save racing the switch cannot silently roll back the editor's commit (this was a HIGH from the first-pass code review on the original use-case-level read+write design; fixed by moving the read inside the mutex). Returns null when the pattern has no tip pointer row — caller treats as `NotFound`. `update()` also gains an `advanceCurrentBranchTip(patternId, previousRevisionId, newRevisionId)` private helper that finds every branch whose `tipRevisionId == previousRevisionId` and advances them in lock-step (defines "co-located branches all advance together" — after `createBranch` two branches share a tip; the next save advances both, matching the user's "I just branched from here" mental model). Defensive fallback: when no branch matches the prior tip, advance "main" via `advanceTip` so pre-37.4 charts that predate `ensureDefaultBranch` don't end up with a dangling `chart_documents.revision_id` not tracked by any branch row. Both `setTip` and `advanceCurrentBranchTip` are `null`-default-safe via the existing `chartRevisionRepository: ChartRevisionRepository?` + new `chartBranchRepository: ChartBranchRepository?` optional ctor params on `StructuredChartRepositoryImpl` — existing test call-sites that bypass the branch layer continue to compile unchanged. **Use cases**: 4 new factories registered in `UseCaseModule` — `GetChartBranchesUseCase` (live `observe(patternId)` Flow + paginated `invoke`), `CreateBranchUseCase` (validates name: empty after trim → Validation, "main" reserved case-insensitively → Validation, duplicate detected case-insensitively against `getByPatternId(...).any { equals(name, ignoreCase = true) }` → Validation; the DB itself stays case-sensitive so user-chosen casing renders verbatim), `SwitchBranchUseCase` (resolves branch + revision, delegates the atomic tip rewrite to `chartRepository.setTip`; surfaces `NotFound` if either lookup misses or the chart row is absent), `RestoreRevisionUseCase` (looks up the past revision + current chart, builds a new chart with the restored drawing payload + a new `revisionId` whose `parentRevisionId == current.revisionId` so restoration is a forward commit on top of tip — additive, NOT destructive; routes through the existing `update()` path which already handles append-history + tip-advance + branch-tip-advance). All 4 use cases use the project's standard `try { ... } catch (e: CancellationException) { throw e } catch (e: Exception) { e.toUseCaseError() }` envelope per the Phase 36.3 / 37.3 precedent — bare `catch (e: Exception)` would swallow `CancellationException` and silently convert a coroutine-cancelled timeout to a phantom `UseCaseError.Unknown`, which the first-pass code review flagged as HIGH. **`ChartBranchPickerViewModel`**: live branch list + `Channel<BranchSwitchedEvent>` for one-shot post-switch navigation. State derived via `combine(getBranches.observe(patternId), chartRepository.observeByPatternId(patternId))` so the "current branch" highlight tracks both branch tip moves AND chart updates landing through Realtime / sync — the picker stays correct across peer device pushes without a manual refresh. `BranchSwitchedEvent` carries `branchName: String` rather than being a `data object` — the ViewModel emits the user-supplied name from `handleSwitchBranch` so the consumer is independent of the timing race between `_branchSwitched.trySend` and the `combine` block writing the new `currentRevisionId` into `_state` (the two paths are concurrent on the same scope with no happens-before guarantee; first-pass code review flagged the original snapshot-from-state design as a MEDIUM where a fast switch would silently drop the Snackbar confirmation). **Compose UI**: new `ChartBranchPickerSheet` (`ModalBottomSheet` listing every branch alphabetically, current tip annotated with `AssistChip(label_current_branch)`, non-current rows expose a `Switch` `TextButton`, "+ New branch" CTA at the bottom opens an `AlertDialog` with `OutlinedTextField`). `ChartViewerScreen` adds `Icons.Default.AccountTree` "Switch branch" entry to the existing overflow menu next to the 37.2 "View history" item, threads `patternId` to the picker on selection, and bridges the `onBranchSwitched(branchName)` callback to a `Snackbar` via a `pendingSnackbar: String?` + `LaunchedEffect(pendingSnackbar)` pattern so the suspending `showSnackbar` doesn't block the picker callback. `ChartHistoryScreen` `RevisionRow` switches from `Modifier.clickable(role = Role.Button)` to `Modifier.combinedClickable(role = Role.Button, onClick, onLongClick)` (`@OptIn(ExperimentalFoundationApi::class)`); long-press dispatches `ChartHistoryEvent.LongPressRevision(revisionId)` which sets `state.pendingRestoreRevision`; that drives a Material 3 `AlertDialog` with `dialog_restore_revision_{title,body}` and confirm → `ChartHistoryEvent.ConfirmRestore` → `RestoreRevisionUseCase`. State extended with `pendingRestoreRevision: ChartRevision?` slot. `ChartHistoryViewModel` ctor gains an optional `restoreRevision: RestoreRevisionUseCase? = null` so 37.2 test call-sites stay compatible. **iOS mirror**: `iosApp/.../ChartBranchPickerSheet.swift` uses the established `ScopedViewModel` holder pattern. Sheet body is a `NavigationStack` + `List` with the `BranchRow` struct rendering each branch (current → `Label("Current", systemImage: "checkmark")`, non-current → `Button("Switch")` with `.buttonStyle(.bordered)`). "New branch" CTA in `.topBarTrailing` opens a nested `.sheet` with a `Form` containing a `TextField` for the branch name. `observeBranchSwitched()` collects the typed `wrapChartBranchSwitchedFlow` Closeable + reads `event.branchName` directly from the envelope (no state snapshot) before dispatching `onBranchSwitched(name)` on the main actor. `StructuredChartViewerScreen.swift` toolbar Menu gains a "Switch branch" `Button` with `arrow.triangle.branch` SF Symbol; switched-branch toast surfaces via a 2-second `.overlay(alignment: .bottom)` carrying the format-resolved `message_switched_to_branch` template (parity with Compose's Snackbar despite SwiftUI lacking a non-blocking equivalent in the codebase). `ChartHistoryScreen.swift` adds `.onLongPressGesture` to `RevisionRow` rendering + a `.confirmationDialog` driven by a `Binding<Bool>` derived from `state.pendingRestoreRevision != nil` — same parity contract as Compose. **DI**: `RepositoryModule` registers `ChartBranchRepositoryImpl` as `single<ChartBranchRepository>` and threads the new `chartBranchRepository = get()` into `StructuredChartRepositoryImpl`. `UseCaseModule` registers all 4 new factories. `ViewModelModule` registers `ChartBranchPickerViewModel` (parametric on `patternId`) and threads `restoreRevision = get()` into `ChartHistoryViewModel`. iOS bridge: `KoinHelper.kt` adds `getChartBranchPickerViewModel(patternId)` accessor + `wrapChartBranchPickerState` (StateFlow → FlowWrapper) + `wrapChartBranchSwitchedFlow` (Flow<BranchSwitchedEvent> → EventFlowWrapper). `ViewModelFactory.swift` adds the typed `chartBranchPickerViewModel(patternId:)` accessor. **i18n** — 8 new keys across all 5 sources (301 total, +8): `title_branch_picker`, `action_create_branch`, `dialog_create_branch_title`, `label_branch_name`, `label_current_branch`, `state_no_branches`, `action_switch`, `message_switched_to_branch` parametric (`Switched to %1$s` EN / `%1$sに切り替えました` JA where the JA puts the branch-name prefix per natural Japanese reading; iOS xcstrings uses `%1$@` per the SwiftUI native formatter convention). Reuses 37.2 `action_restore_revision` + `dialog_restore_revision_{title,body}` (no longer inert), plus existing `action_cancel` / `title_error` / `action_ok`. **Tests** — +14 commonTest landed (3 in `StructuredChartRepositoryImplTest`: update advances main branch tip, update advances co-located branches in lock-step, setTip rewrites tip pointer in place without history append; 1 in `GetChartBranchesUseCase`-coverage section: invoke returns Success with seeded branches; 5 in `CreateBranchUseCase`-coverage section: blank name rejected, "main" reserved case-insensitively, duplicate rejected, missing chart NotFound, happy path mints branch with tip at current chart revision; 4 in `SwitchBranchUseCase`-coverage section: unknown branch NotFound, missing tip revision NotFound, happy path materializes target revision preserving tip row id, missing chart row NotFound (covers the new `setTip` null return path); 2 in `RestoreRevisionUseCase`-coverage section: unknown revision NotFound, happy path appends new commit with restored payload + parent = old tip). Test fake `FakeChartBranchRepository` mirrors the production interface (idempotent `createBranch` semantics documented inline as unreachable from `CreateBranchUseCase` due to the validation pre-empt but kept for future repo-direct tests); `FakeStructuredChartRepository.setTip` updated to the new `(patternId, targetRevision)` signature with same atomic shape as production. `ChartViewerViewModelTest`'s inline `object : StructuredChartRepository` stub also updated. 1033 shared tests (+15 from 1018 baseline; ADR-013 §9's +10–15 target band, hit the upper bound). Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Kover exclusion**: `ChartBranchPickerSheetKt*` added to the Compose-UI exclusion list. `ChartBranchPickerViewModel` deliberately NOT excluded (testable mutation path; ViewModel-level coverage falls out of the use-case tests via `combine`). `ChartBranchRepositoryImpl` not excluded — pure delegate over the SQLDelight + sync layer, indirectly covered by `StructuredChartRepositoryImplTest`'s branch-tip-advance tests. **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 1 LOW first pass, all addressed pre-commit — HIGH1 (`CancellationException` swallowed in all 4 new use cases) fixed by adding the explicit `catch (e: CancellationException) { throw e }` ahead of the bare `Exception` catch per the Phase 36.3 / 37.3 precedent; HIGH2 (`SwitchBranchUseCase` TOCTOU between use-case-level chart read and repo-level write) fixed by changing the `setTip` contract from `setTip(chart): chart` to `setTip(patternId, targetRevision): chart?` and moving the read+write atomically inside `writeMutex.withLock`; MEDIUM1 (case-sensitive duplicate check vs case-insensitive "main" reservation creating UI inconsistency) fixed by switching `CreateBranchUseCase`'s duplicate check from `getByPatternIdAndName` to `getByPatternId(...).any { equals(trimmed, ignoreCase = true) }`; MEDIUM2 (`BranchSwitchedEvent` snapshot race between `_branchSwitched.trySend` and `combine` block writing `currentRevisionId`) fixed by promoting the event to `data class BranchSwitchedEvent(val branchName: String)` carrying the user-supplied name from the source-of-truth event handler; LOW1 (`FakeChartBranchRepository.createBranch` idempotent return path unreachable from use case) addressed via in-code comment documenting the use-case pre-empt. Second-pass review APPROVED with zero findings. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1033 tests), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (301 keys). iOS build via `xcodegen generate && xcodebuild -project iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅. **Closes Phase 37**: with this slice, the entire ADR-013 collaboration-core MVP — append-only history schema (37.1) → live history list (37.2) → side-by-side diff (37.3) → branch picker + restore (37.4) — is end-to-end functional. The "single-tip simplification" (only the checked-out branch's tip is materialized in `chart_documents` at any time) holds: switch branch reads the target's tip revision and rewrites the tip pointer atomically, the existing renderers are unchanged. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-013 §9**: no branch deletion UI yet (the `ChartBranchRepository.deleteBranch` method is wired but no caller surfaces it — defer until a real "I made too many branches" UX need shows up; the data layer is ready); no branch-from-arbitrary-revision affordance (ADR-013 §7 — branching from a past revision is the same shape as `RestoreRevisionUseCase` followed by branch-from-tip and adds picker complexity without a clear v1 use case); no Maestro E2E flow (linked-pattern + chart prerequisite same as Phase 32 / 37.3 deferral; reopen if real interaction-flow regressions surface). **Phase 38 forward-compat anchors hold**: `chart_revisions.author_id` is already provisioned for multi-author commits per 37.1; the owner-scoped `chart-revisions-<ownerId>` Realtime channel from 37.1 is the right shape for Phase 38's "watch upstream" subscription mechanism. Phase 38 (PR/merge) opens next.

- **Phase 37.3**: Chart diff view (ADR-013 §5 §6 §9) — third code slice of Phase 37, the read-side culmination that turns the 37.1 history spine + 37.2 history list into a side-by-side comparison surface. Closes the no-op `onRevisionClick` callback Phase 37.2 left in NavGraph at the `composable<ChartHistory>` block. **Domain**: `ChartDiff` envelope (`base: StructuredChart?`, `target: StructuredChart`, `cellChanges: List<CellChange>`, `layerChanges: List<LayerChange>`) under `domain/model/`. `base` is nullable so the initial-commit case (no parent → "Initial commit" view per ADR §6) loads cleanly without a special enum branch. Derived `isInitialCommit` / `addedCellCount` / `modifiedCellCount` / `removedCellCount` / `hasNoChanges` properties keep the UI free of recount loops. `CellChange` sealed interface (`Added` / `Removed` / `Modified`) with `layerId` + `x` / `y` resolved through a position-keyed contract — `Modified.before.x == Modified.after.x` by construction since the diff keys cells by `(x, y)` (a cell whose position moved is one Add + one Remove, NOT a "moved" category, per ADR-013 §5). `LayerChange` sealed interface (`Added` / `Removed` / `PropertyChanged`) — `PropertyChanged.before` and `.after` carry the full pre/post layer so the renderer can derive name / visible / locked deltas at the call site without a Kotlin enum union. **Diff algorithm**: `domain/chart/ChartDiffAlgorithm.kt` pure object with `diff(base: StructuredChart?, target: StructuredChart): ChartDiff`. Implements ADR §5 verbatim: layer-id union → categorize as Added / Removed / PropertyChanged; for shared layers, cell `(x, y)` union → categorize as CellAdded / CellRemoved / CellModified. **Cells in entirely-added or entirely-removed layers are NOT enumerated in `cellChanges`** — the layer-level event implies them; this prevents an N-cell blow-up when a 100-cell layer is added (one `LayerAdded` vs 100 `CellAdded`). Polar charts diff identically since `(cell.x, cell.y) = (stitch, ring)` is the canonical address regardless of `CoordinateSystem`. Parametric symbols diff via `ChartCell` data class equality — `symbolParameters` participates in `==` so a parameter-only edit surfaces as `CellModified`. O(N + M) over total cell counts; ~10K cells per side runs well under a millisecond, no memoization needed. **Use case**: `GetChartDiffUseCase(repository: ChartRevisionRepository)` with `suspend operator fun invoke(baseRevisionId: String?, targetRevisionId: String): UseCaseResult<ChartDiff>`. `baseRevisionId` nullable for initial-commit. `targetRevisionId` required — a missing target is hard `NotFound`. **`baseRevisionId` non-null + lookup miss is also `NotFound`** (semantically distinct from `baseRevisionId == null` initial-commit which succeeds with `isInitialCommit=true`) — silently degrading would hide a sync drift between `chart_documents.revision_id` and `chart_revisions` (ADR-013 Consequences→Negative §2 reverse-failure window). Both `getRevision` calls are `try { ... } catch (e: Exception) { e.toUseCaseError() }` — explicit `Exception` catch (not `runCatching`) so `CancellationException` propagates correctly. Wired through `UseCaseModule` Koin factory. **`ChartDiffViewModel`** — StateFlow holding `ChartDiffState(diff: ChartDiff?, isLoading: Boolean, error: String?)`. Single `init { load() }` resolves the diff once via `viewModelScope.launch` (no Flow observation — diff is a one-shot snapshot of two immutable revisions; Phase 37 has no scenario where revisions mutate after creation per the immutability invariant). `ClearError` event nulls the surfaced error. Snackbar consumer matches the `ChartHistoryScreen` pattern; raw error message per the project-wide "ViewModel error-message localization" Tech Debt deferral. **Channel pivot for tap routing**: 37.2 emitted `Channel<String>` carrying just the tapped `revisionId`. 37.3 pivots to `Channel<RevisionTapTarget>` carrying `(targetRevisionId, baseRevisionId?)`. The lookup happens in `ChartHistoryViewModel.onEvent(TapRevision)` because the ViewModel owns the revision graph — looks up the tapped row in `_state.value.revisions` and emits both ids. Unknown revisionId race emits `baseRevisionId = null` rather than crashing the navigation pipeline (test coverage included). Compose `ChartHistoryScreen` `onRevisionClick: (baseRevisionId: String?, targetRevisionId: String) -> Unit` callback signature changed accordingly; iOS bridge `wrapChartHistoryRevisionTaps` typed-rebound from `Flow<String>` to `Flow<RevisionTapTarget>`. **Compose `ChartDiffScreen`** — Scaffold + diff summary chip + layer-changes banner + dual-canvas panel. `DualCanvasPanel` uses a SHARED `transformableState` writing to common `scale` / `offsetX` / `offsetY` `mutableFloatStateOf` consumed by both panes via `graphicsLayer` — synchronized pan/zoom across the two canvases, the load-bearing UX engineering ADR-013 Negative §3 flagged as the hardest 37.3 risk surface. Highlight palette is traffic-light green (added) / yellow (modified) / red (removed) at 0.4 alpha — DELIBERATELY DISTINCT from the per-segment overlay's `onSurface` / `primary` palette per ADR-013 Considered alternatives row 8 (avoiding visual-language overload). `ChartDiffCanvas` paints under-glyph highlights then symbol paths via the shared `drawSymbolPath` / `polarLayoutFor` / `drawPolarGrid` / `drawPolarCells` helpers from `SymbolDrawing.kt` + `PolarDrawing.kt` (no duplication). New private helpers `drawRectDiff` (rect renderer with grid + per-cell highlight rect under glyph) + `drawPolarDiffOverlay` (polar wedge highlights painted via `polarWedgePath`). Initial commit (`diff.base == null`) renders `label_initial_commit` in the base pane instead of an empty canvas — clear semantic signal vs an empty rendering void. `state_no_changes` empty state when both revisions are byte-identical (common when comparing a `content_hash` collision). testTags per ADR §6: `chartDiffScreen` (root landmark), `diffSummaryChip`, `baseChartCanvas`, `targetChartCanvas`, `layerChangesBanner`, `backButton`. **NavGraph**: new `@Serializable data class ChartDiff(baseRevisionId: String?, targetRevisionId: String)` route. `composable<ChartDiff>` block consumes the route. The 37.2 `composable<ChartHistory>` `onRevisionClick = { _ -> }` no-op is pivoted to `{ baseRevisionId, targetRevisionId -> navController.navigate(ChartDiff(...)) }`. **iOS mirror**: `iosApp/.../ChartDiffScreen.swift` uses `ScopedViewModel<ChartDiffViewModel, ChartDiffState>` per the established holder pattern. SwiftUI `MagnificationGesture().simultaneously(with: DragGesture())` drives shared `@State scale: CGFloat` / `lastScale` / `offset: CGSize` / `lastOffset` — synchronized pan/zoom mirror of the Compose pattern. Highlight colors hand-tuned to the same 0.4-alpha traffic-light palette via `Color(red:green:blue:).opacity(0.4)`. `DiffCanvas` struct holds a private `PathCommandCache` final class that mirrors the Compose `parsedPathCache` map (avoids re-parsing SVG paths per render). `drawSymbolPath` / `polarLayout` / `polarWedgePath` / `cellRect` inlined in the diff screen file rather than refactored out of `StructuredChartViewerScreen`'s private `ChartCanvasView` struct — refactoring the gestural canvas is out of scope for 37.3, and same scope-cut precedent as 36.4's iOS Discovery thumbnail. The inline helpers carry an explicit "refactor to a shared helper if a third consumer surfaces" comment block. iOS classification mirror `classifyCells(diff:)` matches the Compose private function signature so reading both implementations side-by-side stays straightforward. `ChartHistoryScreen.swift` accepts a `Binding<NavigationPath>` and the `revisionTaps` collect closure now appends `Route.chartDiff(baseRevisionId:targetRevisionId:)` on each emission. `AppRouter.swift` gains the `Route.chartDiff` case + Hashable conformance + destinationView mapping. `ViewModelFactory.swift` + `KoinHelper.kt` bridge gain the `chartDiffViewModel(baseRevisionId:targetRevisionId:)` accessor + `wrapChartDiffState` / typed `wrapChartHistoryRevisionTaps` rebind. `xcodegen generate` regenerated `iosApp.xcodeproj` to register `ChartDiffScreen.swift`. **i18n** — 10 new keys across all 5 sources (293 total, +10): `title_chart_diff`, `label_diff_summary` parametric (`%1$d added · %2$d modified · %3$d removed` EN; JA `追加 %1$d ・ 変更 %2$d ・ 削除 %3$d` reorders with the 「追加」prefix per natural Japanese reading), `label_layer_renamed` parametric (`%1$s → %2$s` — same shape both languages, U+2192 arrow), 6 non-parametric `label_layer_{hidden,shown,locked,unlocked,added,removed}` (the layer's current name renders as a sibling Text in the banner so the verb is the change category; this avoids a parametric `%1$s hidden` / `%1$s shown` family that would balloon translation work without UX gain), `state_no_changes`. Reuses `label_initial_commit` from 37.2 + `action_back` / `title_error` / `action_ok`. iOS xcstrings parametric specifiers use `%1$@` for strings + `%1$d` for ints per the SwiftUI native formatter convention (same idiom as the `label_activity_*_by` family from Phase 33.1.7). **Tests** — +16 commonTest in `GetChartDiffUseCaseTest` covering: target lookup miss → NotFound; base lookup miss → NotFound (distinct from initial-commit success); base null → initial-commit diff with every layer Added; identical revisions → hasNoChanges; cell add/remove/modify-in-place; parametric symbol parameter edit (CellModified via `ChartCell.symbolParameters` equality); cell move surfaces as add+remove (no "moved" pairing); layer added → LayerAdded with no cell enumeration; layer removed → LayerRemoved with no cell enumeration; layer renamed → LayerPropertyChanged + cells diff in place; visibility/locked toggle → LayerPropertyChanged; polar revisions diff identically with stitch/ring keying; multi-layer mixed changes all surfaced in one diff; envelope carries base + target charts for renderer reuse. Test fake `FakeRepo` only implements `getRevision`; `getHistoryForPattern` + `append` are `error("Not used by GetChartDiffUseCase")` so a future refactor that accidentally reaches them through this fake fails loudly. +2 commonTest delta in `ChartHistoryViewModelTest` (replaced 1 old "channel emits target id" test with 3 new tests covering the RevisionTapTarget envelope: null parent on initial commit, parent resolution from tapped row, unknown revisionId emits null base instead of crashing). 1018 shared tests (+18 from 1000 baseline; ADR-013 §9's +12–18 target band, hit the upper bound). Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Kover exclusion**: `ChartDiffScreenKt*` added to the Compose-UI exclusion list alongside the other screen-level Composables. `ChartDiffViewModel` deliberately NOT excluded (testable load path). `ChartDiffAlgorithm` not excluded — pure logic, fully tested. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1018), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (293 keys). iOS build via `xcodegen generate && xcodebuild -project iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅ (one pre-existing `Color(red:green:blue:).opacity(0.4)` warning in non-37.3 code — `ld` warning about iOS 17.2 vs 17.0 simulator linker version is the existing CMP framework drift, unrelated). **Ktlint recurring gotcha**: my initial `Modifier.fillMaxSize().padding(4.dp)` chain in the `DualCanvasPanel`'s base + target `Box` modifiers triggered "Parameter should start on a newline" when later wrapped — `:shared:ktlintFormat` auto-fixed by splitting the chain across lines. Same recurring class as the Phase 32.2 / 33.4 / 35.1c / 36.3 / 37.1 multiline-formatting gotcha. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-013 §9**: branch picker + restore-revision flows reserved for 37.4 (the `action_restore_revision` / `dialog_restore_revision_*` keys shipped inert in 37.2 are still inert here). Maestro E2E flow deferred — flow needs a pre-seeded chart-with-multi-revision fixture which adds ~120 LOC Maestro setup (chart create → row count edit → save → repeat) with no clear value gain over the 16 use-case tests + 3 ViewModel tap-routing tests; reopen if Phase 37.4 surfaces a real interaction-flow regression. Fork-of-fork ancestry walk in attribution UI deferred per ADR-012 §8. Cached PNG revision thumbnails for the history-list path also still deferred per ADR-013 §11 (reuse Phase 36.4 live-render `ChartThumbnail` if the diff history surfaces a perf regression — diff screen renders two full canvases so a PNG cache would save more compute here than at the history list level if it ever became a bottleneck). **Closes Phase 37 read-side**: with this slice, the entire ADR-013 §1–§6 read path — append-only history schema (37.1) → live history list (37.2) → side-by-side diff (37.3) — is end-to-end functional. Phase 37.4 wraps the branch / restore write path on top.

- **Phase 37.2**: Chart history read surface (ADR-013 §6, §9) — second code slice of Phase 37 builds the read-side UX on top of 37.1's data spine. **Use cases**: `GetChartHistoryUseCase` wraps `ChartRevisionRepository.observeHistoryForPattern` for the live ViewModel flow + a paginated suspend `invoke(patternId, limit, offset)` returning `UseCaseResult<List<ChartRevision>>` for forward-compat with 37.4's pagination needs. `GetChartRevisionUseCase` wraps `getRevision(revisionId)` returning `UseCaseResult<ChartRevision?>` — both ship together so Phase 37.3's `ChartDiffScreen` load path can `get(revisionId)` against either side of a diff without further DI churn (the doc comment on `GetChartRevisionUseCase` is explicit about this 37.3 forward-compat justification, addressing the "reserved key ships unused" concern by routing through DI today even though no caller exists in 37.2). **Koin**: both use cases registered as `factory { ... }` in `UseCaseModule`; `ChartHistoryViewModel` registered as parameterized `viewModel { params -> ChartHistoryViewModel(patternId = params.get(), getChartHistory = get()) }` in `ViewModelModule`. **i18n** — 8 new keys across all 5 sources (283 total, +8): `title_chart_history`, `state_no_chart_history`, `state_no_chart_history_body`, `label_auto_save`, `label_initial_commit`, plus the three Phase 37.4 reserved keys `action_restore_revision` / `dialog_restore_revision_title` / `dialog_restore_revision_body` that ship inert today (the long-press → "Restore as new commit" affordance is reserved for 37.4 per ADR-013 §6 — UX shape is consistent end-to-end; only the wiring lands later). The strings.xml comment block in the EN source documents this convention so future readers understand why three keys appear with no `import` site. **`ChartHistoryViewModel`** — StateFlow + `Channel<String>` for one-shot tap-to-navigate events. Channel is `BUFFERED` so taps queued before the consumer attaches still deliver (e.g. SwiftUI `.task { }` may attach a frame after view binds). `revisionTaps: Flow<String>` exposed for both Compose `LaunchedEffect` and iOS `EventFlowWrapper.collect`. `init { }` collects `getChartHistory.observe(patternId).onEach { ... }.catch { ... }.launchIn(viewModelScope)` mirroring the `ActivityFeedViewModel` pattern — `Flow.catch` operator does NOT swallow `CancellationException` (kotlinx.coroutines library guarantee), so cancellation propagates through correctly. **Compose `ChartHistoryScreen`** — Scaffold + LazyColumn (newest-first per the repo's `created_at DESC` query). `RevisionRow` headline = `commitMessage` if non-blank, else `label_initial_commit` if `parentRevisionId == null`, else `label_auto_save`. Timestamp via existing `Instant.formatFull()` ext. testTags per ADR §6: `chartHistoryScreen` (root landmark), `revisionRow_<revisionId>` (per-row), `commitMessageLabel_<revisionId>`, `revisionTimestampLabel_<revisionId>`. Snackbar surfaces transient flow errors raw per the project-wide "ViewModel error-message localization" Tech Debt deferral (matches ActivityFeedScreen). **NavGraph** — `@Serializable data class ChartHistory(patternId: String)` route + `composable<ChartHistory>` block. The `onRevisionClick` callback is wired to a no-op for 37.2 (TODO comment naming Phase 37.3 `ChartDiff` as the future routing target); the ViewModel still emits the tapped revisionId on the channel for test coverage so 37.3 swaps the no-op for `navController.navigate(ChartDiff(...))` without touching the ViewModel layer. **Entry points**: (a) `ChartViewerScreen` Compose TopAppBar gains `actions = { IconButton(MoreVert) → DropdownMenu("View history") }` with `overflowMenuButton` + `viewHistoryMenuItem` testTags; new `onHistoryClick: () -> Unit` screen prop wired through NavGraph to `navController.navigate(ChartHistory(patternId))`. New `onChartHistoryClick: (String) -> Unit` screen-level prop threaded through `PatternInfoSection`. **iOS mirror** — `iosApp/.../ChartHistoryScreen.swift` uses `ScopedViewModel<ChartHistoryViewModel, ChartHistoryState>` per the established Phase 27.1 holder pattern. `ContentUnavailableView(LocalizedStringKey("state_no_chart_history"), …, description: Text(LocalizedStringKey("state_no_chart_history_body")))` for empty state. `List(state.revisions, id: \.revisionId)` rendering `RevisionRow` with `.contentShape(Rectangle()).onTapGesture { ... }` so the entire row catches the tap. `revisionTaps` channel collected via `.task { observeRevisionTaps() } / .onDisappear { closeable.close() }` lifecycle pattern from `DiscoveryScreen.swift` — `.task { }` re-fires on every view re-appearance so the helper closes any prior subscription before creating a new one (Phase 32.2 / 36.5 iOS Closeable leak audit pattern). `revisionTapCloseable` is reset on the Compose `DropdownMenu`. accessibilityIdentifiers `overflowMenuButton` + `viewHistoryMenuItem`. **`ProjectDetailScreen.swift`** `patternInfoSection` — new `onChartHistoryTap: @escaping () -> Void` param + a sibling `Button(action: onChartHistoryTap) { Label(LocalizedStringKey("title_chart_history"), systemImage: "clock.arrow.circlepath") }` with accessibilityIdentifier `openChartHistoryLink`, only when `hasStructuredChart`. Call site at the `Section(LocalizedStringKey("label_pattern_info_section"))` block plumbs `onChartHistoryTap: { path.append(Route.chartHistory(patternId: pattern.id)) }`. **Tests** — +7 commonTest in `ChartHistoryViewModelTest` (1000 total, +7 from 993 baseline; right inside ADR-013 §9's +6–10 target band): (a) loads revisions newest-first preserving repo `created_at DESC` order, (b) empty repo surfaces empty list + clears loading, (c) repo flow emission updates state live without re-init (simulates Realtime peer append landing through `LocalChartRevisionDataSource.upsert` → `observeHistoryForPattern` Flow), (d) flow error surfaces in state.error + clears loading (synchronous-throw flow exercises the `.catch { }` branch), (e) `TapRevision` event emits revision id on the navigation channel (covers the Channel→Flow bridge contract), (f) `ClearError` event nulls the surfaced error message, (g) ViewModel scopes observe to the supplied patternId only — second pattern's revisions do not leak. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 0 HIGH / 1 MEDIUM / 0 LOW first pass — MEDIUM was an accessibility-consistency catch on the two pre-existing `Modifier.clickable(onClick = ...)` calls in `PatternInfoSection` (`openChartViewerLink` line 1103, `openChartEditorLink` line 1132). The new "History" link uses `Modifier.clickable(role = Role.Button, ...)` for TalkBack-as-button announcement (parity with the iOS `Button(action:)` Label mirror), making the inconsistency on the two siblings visible — fixed pre-commit by adding `role = Role.Button` to both pre-existing `clickable` modifiers. Reviewer-acknowledged-out-of-scope: `Button("action_ok")` String literal in iOS error alert auto-promotes to LocalizedStringKey via SwiftUI overload resolution (matches Discovery/Settings/Profile/Login precedent); the three Phase 37.4 reserved i18n keys ship inert by design and are documented in the EN strings.xml comment block. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 1000 tests, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 283 keys). **Ktlint recurring gotcha** — `:shared:ktlintCheck` rejected an inline `/* TODO Phase 37.3: open ChartDiffScreen */` block comment on a lambda argument with "A block comment in between other elements on the same line is disallowed (cannot be auto-corrected)"; fixed by moving the TODO above the lambda as a standalone `// TODO ...` line comment. Same recurring class as the Phase 32.2 / 33.4 / 35.1c / 36.3 multiline-formatting gotchas. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-013 §9**: no diff view yet (`ChartDiffScreen` ships in 37.3); long-press → "Restore as new commit" reserved for 37.4 (the i18n keys ship today; the gesture wiring lands later); Maestro E2E flow deferred — flow needs a pre-seeded chart-with-revisions fixture which adds ~80 LOC Maestro setup with no clear value gain over the 7 ViewModel tests; reopen if Phase 37.3 surfaces a real interaction-flow regression.

- **Phase 37.1**: Collaboration core data spine (ADR-013 §1, §2, §3, §4, §7, §8) — first code slice of Phase 37, lands the append-only history schema + repository plumbing without any UI surface. Sets up `chart_revisions` as a sibling table to `chart_documents` (preserved as the tip pointer) and `chart_branches` for the upcoming 37.4 picker. **Migration 015** (`015_chart_revisions.sql`): `chart_revisions` table with `(pattern_id, revision_id)` UNIQUE + standalone `UNIQUE (revision_id)` so `chart_branches.tip_revision_id UUID REFERENCES chart_revisions(revision_id) ON DELETE RESTRICT` is a valid FK. `author_id UUID REFERENCES profiles(id) ON DELETE SET NULL` is **nullable** per ADR-013 §1 — `NOT NULL + ON DELETE SET NULL` would be a Postgres contradiction (the SET NULL action would fail the NOT NULL constraint and account-deletion would error rather than preserve the row); INSERT-time RLS still enforces `author_id = auth.uid()`. RLS exposes `SELECT` (own + public-pattern read parity with `chart_documents`) + `INSERT` (own only); no UPDATE/DELETE policies — revisions are immutable once written, mirroring Git's append-only invariant. `chart_branches` table with `(pattern_id, branch_name)` UNIQUE + the hard FK to `chart_revisions(revision_id)` with `ON DELETE RESTRICT` (stricter than the soft mirror between `chart_documents.revision_id` and `chart_revisions.revision_id` — branches are the entry point for SwitchBranchUseCase and a dangling tip would surface as a null chart with no recovery path; ADR-013 §7). Both tables added to `supabase_realtime` publication. **SQLDelight schemas**: `ChartRevision.sq` + `ChartBranch.sq` mirror the Postgres tables with `author_id TEXT` nullable + `commit_message TEXT` nullable. Both `.sq` files pair with `5.sqm` containing the same `CREATE TABLE`s for the SQLite migration path. Queries: `getById`, `getByRevisionId`, `getHistoryForPattern` (LIMIT/OFFSET-paginated, ORDER BY `created_at DESC`), `observeHistoryForPattern`, `countForPattern`, `insert`, `upsert` (INSERT OR IGNORE on `(pattern_id, revision_id)` for idempotent Realtime backfill), `deleteByPatternId`. No `update` query — revisions are immutable. **Domain**: `ChartRevision` data class (Serializable) with the same envelope shape as `StructuredChart` minus `updatedAt` (revisions are immutable so the timestamp is single-valued). `toStructuredChart()` extension reconstructs a tip-shaped record so the existing `ChartCanvas` renderers can render a historical revision unchanged at the diff/preview call sites. `ChartBranch` data class with `DEFAULT_BRANCH_NAME = "main"` companion. **Mappers**: `ChartRevisionMapper.kt` + `ChartBranchMapper.kt` route through the document JSON envelope identical to `StructuredChartMapper`'s shape (extents + layers + craft_type + reading_convention). `String.toStorageVariant()` and `String.toCoordinateSystem()` extension functions in `StructuredChartMapper.kt` were promoted from `private` to `internal` so the new mapper can reuse them — same package, same semantics, no behavior change. **Repository surface**: `ChartRevisionRepository` interface (`getRevision`, `getHistoryForPattern` paginated, `observeHistoryForPattern` Flow, `append` immutable INSERT — no `update` or `delete`; cleanup happens transitively via `pattern_id` `ON DELETE CASCADE` in migration 015). `ChartRevisionRepositoryImpl` follows the local-first / remote-fallback / sync-or-enqueue pattern from `StructuredChartRepositoryImpl`. **`StructuredChartRepository` extension**: `create()`, `update()`, and `forkFor()` all now call a private `appendRevisionFromTip(...)` that writes a fresh `ChartRevision` mirroring the chart's drawing payload + lineage. `update()` reads `previousChart` from the local DS BEFORE the local update and threads the previous tip's `revisionId` as the new revision's `parentRevisionId` — load-bearing for chained ancestry. `create()` and `forkFor()` additionally call `ensureDefaultBranch(...)` which idempotently INSERT-OR-IGNOREs a `"main"` row in `chart_branches` pointing at the initial revision — without this, forked patterns would have a populated revision history but an empty `chart_branches` table and the Phase 37.4 branch picker would surface no branches. The new `ChartRevisionRepository` + `LocalChartBranchDataSource` ctor params are nullable with `null` defaults so existing test call-sites that construct the repo directly without seeding a revision/branch layer (e.g. `FakeStructuredChartRepository` use-case tests) continue to compile unchanged — production wiring (RepositoryModule) always passes non-null. **Sync wiring (ADR-013 §8)**: `SyncEntityType.CHART_REVISION` + `CHART_BRANCH` added to the enum. `SyncExecutor` exhaustively routes both: `CHART_REVISION` INSERT → `remote.append(...)`; UPDATE/DELETE branches `error()` with an explicit message because RLS forbids them and SyncManager never enqueues those operations (a defensive `error` surfaces an accidentally-enqueued non-INSERT at execute time rather than silently dropping the pending row). `CHART_BRANCH` INSERT/UPDATE both map to `upsert(...)` (idempotent on `(pattern_id, branch_name)`); DELETE wired for Phase 37.4 branch deletion. **Realtime**: `RealtimeSyncManager` gains a 5th channel `chart-revisions-<ownerId>` alongside projects / progress / patterns / project-segments — owner-scoped filter mirrors the per-segment-progress pattern from ADR-010 §6 (NOT public-fan-out, ADR-013 §10 — bounds Realtime cost to self-authored work and avoids the "every public-pattern revision broadcasts to N forkers" multiplier; cross-fork awareness is Phase 38's "watch upstream" subscription concern, not Phase 37's). Insert events route through `LocalChartRevisionDataSource.upsert(...)` (INSERT OR IGNORE de-dups self-authored echoes). UPDATE/DELETE/SELECT branches no-op since revisions are append-only at the RLS layer. `localChartRevision` ctor param is nullable with `null` default + a guard in `subscribe` that only opens the channel when the dependency is wired — keeps existing `RealtimeSyncManagerTest` constructions valid. **Koin DI**: `RepositoryModule` registers `LocalChartRevisionDataSource`, `LocalChartBranchDataSource`, `RemoteChartRevisionDataSource`, `RemoteChartBranchDataSource` (last two only when Supabase is configured), `ChartRevisionRepositoryImpl` as `single<ChartRevisionRepository>`. `StructuredChartRepository` factory updated to thread the new deps. `SyncModule` registers `RemoteChartRevisionSyncOperations` + `RemoteChartBranchSyncOperations` aliases, threads them through `SyncExecutor`, and threads `localChartRevision` into `RealtimeSyncManager`. **Tests (+22 commonTest)**: `ChartRevisionRepositoryImplTest` (14 tests) covers append-with-INSERT-sync, commit-message round-trip incl. null auto-saves, lineage chaining, getRevision miss + case sensitivity, getHistoryForPattern ordering / pagination / empty-pattern / patternId scoping, observeHistoryForPattern current snapshot, parametric symbol round-trip through document JSON, and the forward + reverse failure recovery paths from ADR-013 Consequences→Negative §2 (re-append on the same revisionId is idempotent at INSERT OR IGNORE; PendingSync retry on a re-fired payload is a local no-op). `StructuredChartRepositoryImplTest` gains 8 new tests against a separate `setUpWithHistory()` factory: create appends initial revision row matching tip, create bootstraps `main` branch pointing at initial revision, create enqueues both CHART_REVISION + CHART_BRANCH INSERTs alongside the tip INSERT, update appends a new revision linking parent to previous tip, update enqueues a CHART_REVISION INSERT in addition to the STRUCTURED_CHART UPDATE, forkFor appends a revision and ensures a default branch on the fork, plus a sanity case that the existing forkFor data-spine path with no revision/branch deps still creates the fork tip (regression anchor for the optional ctor param defaults). **Test fakes**: `FakeRemoteChartRevisionDataSource` (append-only mirror of the production interface) + `FakeRemoteChartBranchDataSource` added next to the existing structured-chart / project-segment fakes. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (993 tests, +22 from 971 baseline — within ADR-013's +25–35 target range; the 3-test undershoot reflects the FakeStructuredChartRepository in domain/usecase still satisfying the unchanged interface so use-case-layer tests didn't need new cases this slice), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (275 keys, unchanged — 37.1 is data layer, no i18n surface). **Ktlint recurring gotcha**: my initial `setUpWithHistory()` helper return type used `Triple<...>:` colon-spacing that ktlint's auto-format split across lines — `:shared:ktlintFormat` auto-fixed via wrapping the return-type after the function name; same recurring class as the Phase 32.2 / 33.4 / 35.1c / 36.3 multiline-formatting gotcha. **Append-then-update non-atomicity** (ADR-013 Consequences→Negative §2 — both failure directions documented): forward failure (revision INSERT succeeds, tip UPDATE fails) leaves the local history list one revision ahead of `chart_documents.revision_id` until the next sync round retries the tip UPDATE; reverse failure (remote revision INSERT fails but remote tip UPDATE somehow lands first — rare but possible if the tip UPDATE's PendingSync entry races ahead of the revision INSERT entry under heavy retry pressure) creates a temporary inconsistency window where remote `chart_documents.revision_id` points at a revision that does not yet exist in remote `chart_revisions`. There is **no FK** between `chart_documents.revision_id` and `chart_revisions.revision_id` (soft mirror per ADR-013 §4) so the tip UPDATE is not blocked at the database layer if the revision INSERT hasn't landed — this is by design (the alternative is a Supabase RPC `append_chart_revision` which couples KMP repos to Postgres-side semantics no other write path uses; deferred per ADR-013 implementer voice unless telemetry shows divergence as a user-visible issue). PendingSync coalescing handles both directions and the inconsistency window is bounded to a single sync cycle. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-013 §11**: no UseCase wiring (`GetChartHistoryUseCase` is Phase 37.2), no UI (`ChartHistoryScreen` Phase 37.2; `ChartDiffScreen` Phase 37.3; branch picker Phase 37.4), no diff algorithm (Phase 37.3), no commit-message field on `update(chart)` signature (caller passes `null` today; commit-with-message UI in Phase 37.2's save flow). The `appendRevisionFromTip` private helper accepts a `commitMessage` parameter today — wired as null on every call site so the column round-trips correctly + Phase 37.2 can flip the message-bearing call sites in one diff without touching the persistence layer. **Forward-compat anchors for Phase 38** (PR/merge): `ChartRevision.authorId` is already provisioned and routes through INSERT-time RLS (`author_id = auth.uid()`); the `chart-revisions-<ownerId>` Realtime channel is owner-scoped by design so a Phase 38 PR that introduces multi-author commits will need an explicit "watch upstream" subscription mechanism (right shape, not implicit fan-out via channel design today). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 3 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass — all 7 fixed pre-commit. **HIGH-1** (`update()` TOCTOU on read-then-write — two concurrent saves on the same chart could both read the same prior tip and produce a branching parent chain): added `private val writeMutex = Mutex()` field on `StructuredChartRepositoryImpl`; `create()`, `update()`, and `forkFor()` now wrap their entire read/write triples in `writeMutex.withLock { … }`. SQLite is single-writer at the driver layer, but the read happens before the write inside the repository — an in-process race would still observe the pre-update tip on both callers without the mutex. **HIGH-2** + **LOW-2** (`ensureDefaultBranch` always enqueued a CHART_BRANCH INSERT even when the local INSERT-OR-IGNORE was a no-op, AND racing devices would both generate distinct UUIDs for the same `(pattern_id, "main")` row — the server-side `onConflict = "pattern_id,branch_name"` upsert would silently overwrite `id` on the losing device): refactored `ensureDefaultBranch` to call `localChartBranch.getByPatternIdAndName(patternId, "main")` first and short-circuit with no-op if a "main" row already exists. The local upsert + sync enqueue happen exactly once per pattern. **MEDIUM-1** (`executeChartRevision` `error("...")` on UPDATE/DELETE branches would mark the entry FAILED and trigger an indefinite retry storm on a row that can never succeed): changed both branches to `return true` silent no-op, matching `executeProgress`'s convention for unsupported operations. The doc comment now flags that the UPDATE/DELETE branches surface upstream bugs via PendingSync log inspection rather than throwing. **MEDIUM-2** (`createdAt = chart.updatedAt` could tie or out-of-order the `getHistoryForPattern` ORDER BY when a caller constructs a chart with a stale `updatedAt`): switched to `createdAt = Clock.System.now()` inside `appendRevisionFromTip` so the ordering key is always wall-clock time at append. The `chart.updatedAt` semantics is now exclusively the tip pointer's lastWrite-time, decoupled from history timestamping. **MEDIUM-3** (Realtime `chart-revisions-<ownerId>` channel handler silently dropped DELETE events, but `ON DELETE CASCADE` on `chart_revisions.pattern_id` will fire one DELETE per revision row when a pattern is deleted — local revision rows would never be cleaned up): added `FOREIGN KEY (pattern_id) REFERENCES PatternEntity(id) ON DELETE CASCADE` to both `ChartRevision.sq` + `ChartBranch.sq` + `5.sqm` so SQLite cascades locally when a pattern is deleted (matches the `Progress.sq` / `ProjectSegment.sq` precedent), AND added a `PostgresAction.Delete` branch to `handleChartRevisionAction` that calls `localChartRevision.deleteByPatternId(old.patternId)` for cross-device cleanup parity. Calling `deleteByPatternId` per-event is wasteful but idempotent — subsequent calls on the same patternId are no-ops. **LOW-1** (`RemoteChartRevisionDataSource.append` used `table.insert(...)` which would throw `RestException` 23505 on a re-enqueued duplicate, contradicting the doc comment's "successful no-op" claim): changed to `table.upsert(...) { onConflict = "revision_id"; ignoreDuplicates = true; select() }` returning `decodeSingleOrNull` and falling back to the input revision when the upsert was a no-op. Revisions are immutable once written so `ignoreDuplicates` is the semantically correct shape — never overwrite, only insert-once. Reviewer-acknowledged-out-of-scope: dependency injection for null-default optional ctor params (`appendRevisionFromTip` / `ensureDefaultBranch` no-op when their deps are null — production wiring always provides non-null; existing `SyncExecutor` uses the same `?: return true` null-guard pattern); `commitMessage: String?` always-null-today (Phase 37.2 will flip the message-bearing call sites in one diff); iOS Closeable/lifecycle (no `expect/actual` types, no `Closeable` patterns, no `CoroutineScope` leaked into iOS).

- **Phase 37.0**: ADR-013 cut for collaboration core — opens Phase 37 with the data-model + UX shape decided before any code lands. ADR sized at ~470 lines EN + JA summary (matches the ADR-012 EN+JA-summary precedent). **Key decisions resolved by the agent team**: (1) Append-only history lives in a new sibling `chart_revisions` table; `chart_documents` keeps `UNIQUE (pattern_id)` and stays as the tip pointer — every existing read path (`getByPatternId`, `observeByPatternId`, `existsByPatternId`, fork's `forkFor`, sync, Realtime channel `chart-documents-<ownerId>`) continues unchanged. The repurpose-`chart_documents`-as-append-only alternative (drop UNIQUE) was rejected because it forces every consumer to re-add a "tip" filter and emits Realtime events on every revision insert from the same user across devices. (2) Tip pointer = `chart_documents.revision_id` (no schema change to chart_documents). Write path becomes "INSERT chart_revisions row → UPDATE chart_documents tip". Append-then-update is non-atomic; PendingSync coalescing handles the network-drop window per the existing best-effort idiom. Server-side RPC for atomic append+update was rejected for MVP — couples KMP repos to Postgres-side semantics that no other write path uses; revisit only if telemetry shows tip-divergence as a user-visible issue. (3) Branch table `chart_branches(pattern_id, branch_name, tip_revision_id)` with `(pattern_id, branch_name)` UNIQUE — schema ships in 37.1 (same migration as `chart_revisions`); UI ships in 37.4. "main" auto-created on first revision. Single-tip simplification (only the checked-out branch's tip is materialized in `chart_documents`) is a deliberate scope cut — chart docs are <100KB so re-materializing on switch is sub-millisecond. (4) `commit_message TEXT NULL` column on `chart_revisions`, captured at save time. Auto-saves write null; explicit save-with-message writes the user-supplied string. Editing past commit messages is out of scope. (5) Diff algorithm is cell-level over `(layer.id, x, y)` triples; layer-property diffs (visibility, name, lock) tracked separately; layers added/removed enumerated as one `LayerAdded`/`LayerRemoved` rather than blowing up into N `CellAdded`/`CellRemoved` per cell. Position-keyed (not symbol-keyed) so a "moved" cell shows up as add+remove, not as a "moved" category — knitters reading a diff care about "what's in this position now vs before" more than "which symbols moved" (Phase 37+ can add move-detection as a post-process if telemetry shows noisy diffs after pattern reorganizations). Polar charts diff identically (`(x, y)` key is `(stitch, ring)` on polar). Parametric symbols diff via `ChartCell` data class equality — parameter edits surface as `CellModified`. Algorithm is O(N + M) over total cell counts; ~10K cells per side runs in well under a millisecond, no memoization needed. (6) UX surface = dedicated `ChartHistoryScreen` + `ChartDiffScreen` (separate screens, NOT a tab in ChartViewer). Tab-in-Viewer was rejected because it conflates "edit current state" with "browse past states" — two distinct mental models, and tab-switching loses scroll position + makes deep-linking harder. History screen reachable from ChartViewer overflow + ProjectDetail pattern-info section. Diff view uses synchronized side-by-side `ChartCanvas` rendering at half-width on tablets / stacked on phones, changed cells highlighted with traffic-light palette (green=added / yellow=modified / red=removed) — distinct from the per-segment overlay palette to avoid overloading visual language. Synchronized pan/zoom across the two diff panes is the harder UX engineering risk surface for 37.3. (7) `author_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES profiles(id) ON DELETE SET NULL` provisioned now even though Phase 37 always has `owner_id == author_id` — Phase 38 PR/merge introduces multi-author commits, and a Phase 38 migration to backfill `author_id` would be wasted work. ON DELETE SET NULL preserves history after the author account is deleted. (8) No UPDATE/DELETE policies on `chart_revisions` — revisions are immutable once written, mirroring Git's append-only history invariant. **Phase 37 sub-slice plan** (locked in as ADR §9): 37.0 (this ADR, no code) → 37.1 (`chart_revisions` + `chart_branches` schema, domain `ChartRevision`, repository, sync wiring, default-"main" auto-create on first save; +25–35 commonTest, migration 015) → 37.2 (`GetChartHistoryUseCase`, `ChartHistoryViewModel`, `ChartHistoryScreen` Compose+SwiftUI; +6–10 commonTest, 6–8 i18n keys) → 37.3 (`GetChartDiffUseCase`, `ChartDiffScreen` Compose+SwiftUI, cell-level + layer-property diff; +12–18 commonTest, 8–12 i18n keys) → 37.4 (branch picker UI, "New branch" / "Switch branch" / restore-revision flows; +10–15 commonTest, 6–8 i18n keys). Slice 37.4 is the only one that may slip out of MVP without breaking earlier slices — 37.1/37.2/37.3 form a coherent read-only history experience even if branch never ships. **Forward-compat anchors for Phase 38**: `chart_revisions.author_id` already provisioned (multi-author PR/merge); diff algorithm already cell-level (PR/merge can compute diff-of-diffs against the same shape); attribution UI already supports "Forked from <title> by <author>" deep link (Phase 36.5) which can deepen to "View source's history" using the public-pattern Realtime subscription on `chart_revisions` (RLS already in §1 of the ADR). **Explicitly NOT in MVP** (per ADR-007 "Minimal Git semantics; no CRDT in v1"): pull-request workflow (Phase 38), three-way merge (Phase 38), CRDT concurrent editing (post-v1 if ever), cherry-pick / rebase / squash / amend (out of scope indefinitely), editing past commit messages, branch protection rules, multi-author diff blame (Phase 38+), full fork-chain ancestry walk in attribution UI, server-side atomicity RPC, cached PNG revision thumbnails for the history list (reuse Phase 36.4 live-render `ChartThumbnail` at smaller scale), `commit_message` validation/max-length (UI enforces a soft 200-char limit, server accepts any TEXT). Realtime channel count grows from 4 to 5 per authenticated user (the new `chart-revisions-<ownerId>` channel is the 5th alongside projects/progress/patterns/project-segments) — bounded cost; if Phase 39 closed beta surfaces a connection-budget cap, channels coalesce then. Storage cost grows linearly with edit count (a power user with 200 edits → 200 revision rows × ~50KB each = ~10MB per pattern); retention policy not in MVP (Phase 37+ can add daily snapshots beyond N days if storage telemetry surfaces it). No test delta this slice (ADR is documentation only). Pre-push invariants unchanged (no code touched); 818 shared tests, 275 i18n keys.

- **Phase 36.5**: "Forked from" attribution UI on ProjectDetail (ADR-012 §6) — fifth and final slice of Phase 36, the closing piece of the fork-with-attribution loop that 36.1 (`parentPatternId` data spine) and 36.3 (fork orchestration write to `parentPatternId = sourcePattern.id`) provisioned. With this slice, a forker's project detail view surfaces the source pattern + author with a tap-to-view link to the source's chart viewer when the source is still public. **State extension**: `ProjectDetailState` gains `parentPattern: Pattern?` + `parentPatternAuthor: User?`. The signal that the current pattern was forked is `pattern?.parentPatternId != null` (the existing field). Three render states are derived: (a) `parentPatternId == null` → not forked, render nothing; (b) `parentPatternId != null && parentPattern == null` → source was deleted/private/lookup-failed, render plain `state_forked_from_deleted`; (c) `parentPattern != null` → render parametric `label_forked_from`, tappable when `parentPattern.visibility == PUBLIC`. **Resolution coroutine**: new `observeParentAttribution()` in `init { }` next to `loadChartImages()` / `loadProgressPhotoUrls()`. Subscribes to `patternFlow.map { it?.parentPatternId }.distinctUntilChanged()` (so a regular pattern edit that changes title/description but not `parentPatternId` does not retrigger the fetch) and `flatMapLatest { parentId -> flow { ... } }` so an in-flight resolution is cancelled when the parent id changes — load-bearing only for a hypothetical future re-link path that swaps `project.patternId` (write-once per ADR-012 §1 means the first-pass `collect` would not race today, but the structure is the correct one and matches the cancellation-safe pattern from Phase 36.3's `ForkPublicPatternUseCase`). Both `patternRepository.getById` and `userRepository.getById` failures degrade gracefully — caught with explicit `if (e is CancellationException) throw e` rethrow per the same Phase 36.3 KDoc rationale, then the catch returns null and the UI renders the deleted-source branch. **No new use case**: the existing `patternRepository.getById(parentId)` + `userRepository.getById(source.ownerId)` call pair is short enough that wrapping in a dedicated UseCase would be ceremony for one call site (matches the precedent in `SharedWithMeViewModel.kt` which calls `patternRepository.getById` + `userRepository.getByIds` directly). **`UiOverlay`** gains `parentPattern: Pattern?` + `parentPatternAuthor: User?` fields; the main `combine` block forwards them into `ProjectDetailState`. **Compose UI**: `PatternInfoSection` private composable extended with `parentPattern: Pattern?` + `parentPatternAuthor: User?` + `onParentPatternClick: (String) -> Unit` params. Renders the row right under the title row (above the structured-chart links). When `pattern.parentPatternId != null`, picks one of three branches: `state_forked_from_deleted` plain text (testTag `forkedFromDeletedLabel`), parametric `label_forked_from` plain text non-tappable when `visibility != PUBLIC` (testTag `forkedFromLabel`), or parametric `label_forked_from` clickable Text with `clickable(role = Role.Button)` for TalkBack a11y parity with the iOS `Button(action:)` mirror (testTag `forkedFromLink`). Author name resolves via `parentPatternAuthor?.displayName ?: stringResource(Res.string.label_someone)` per the Phase 33.1.7 ActivityFeed precedent. **NavGraph**: the `composable<ProjectDetail>` block plumbs `onParentPatternClick = { parentPatternId -> navController.navigate(ChartViewer(patternId = parentPatternId, projectId = null)) }` — `projectId = null` because the user is browsing someone else's pattern, so segment overlay (which is project-scoped per ADR-010 §4) does not apply. **iOS mirror**: SwiftUI `patternInfoSection` helper extended with the same params + a new `forkedFromRow(parentPattern:parentPatternAuthor:onTap:)` private helper. Three render branches mirror Compose: `Text(LocalizedStringKey("state_forked_from_deleted"))` for the deleted-source branch (auto-resolves through xcstrings per the 33.1.6 SwiftUI literal-promotion table), and for the resolved branch a `String(format: NSLocalizedString("label_forked_from", comment: ""), source.title, authorName)` parametric resolution wrapped in `Text(verbatim:)` to avoid LocalizedStringKey re-resolution of user-authored strings (same idiom as `label_activity_*_by` from Phase 33.1.7). Tappable variant is a `Button(action:)` with `.buttonStyle(.plain)`, non-tappable variant is a plain `Text`. **`Visibility.PUBLIC` Swift bridging gotcha**: the Kotlin enum case `PUBLIC` bridges to Swift as `.public_` (trailing underscore — `public` is a Swift reserved word; same trailing-underscore mapping as `PatternEditScreen.swift`'s `VisibilityOption.toVisibility() { .publicVisibility: return .public_ }`). Documented inline at `forkedFromRow`. Author-null fallback uses `parentPatternAuthor?.displayName ?? NSLocalizedString("label_someone", comment: "")`. **i18n**: 2 new keys added to all 5 sources (275 total, +2): `label_forked_from` parametric ("Forked from: %1$s by %2$s" / "%1$s（%2$s）からフォーク" — JA puts the parenthetical author after the title for natural reading; iOS xcstrings uses `%1$@` / `%2$@`) and `state_forked_from_deleted` non-parametric ("Forked from a deleted pattern" / "削除されたパターンからフォーク"). Reuses `label_someone` from Phase 33.1.7 for the null-author fallback. **Koin**: `userRepository = get()` added to `ViewModelModule`'s `ProjectDetailViewModel` factory; `UserRepository` was already a `single<UserRepository>` in `RepositoryModule` (consumed by `SharedWithMeViewModel` since Phase 5b). **Tests**: +3 commonTest in `ProjectDetailViewModelTest` (33 → 36): (a) `parent attribution resolves source pattern and author when forked` — both fields populated with full PUBLIC source + named author, (b) `parent attribution leaves parentPattern null when source was deleted` — `parentPatternId` set but no source row in repo, parentPattern stays null (deleted-source branch), (c) `parent attribution falls back gracefully when author lookup returns null` — source resolves but author missing from `userRepository`, `parentPatternAuthor` null (UI then routes through `label_someone` at the Compose layer). All 4 `createViewModel*` factory helpers updated with `userRepository = userRepository` plumbing; class-level `private val userRepository = FakeUserRepository()` field added next to the existing `patternRepository` / `authRepository` fields (kotlin.test instantiates a fresh test class instance per `@Test`, so this gives each test a clean repo just like the pre-existing pattern). Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass — HIGH (race in `observeParentAttribution`'s `collect` body — older fetch can clobber newer one because plain `collect` does not cancel in-flight body when a new emission arrives) and MEDIUM1 (`catch (_: Exception)` swallows `CancellationException` per the project's own Phase 36.3 KDoc anti-pattern) both fixed pre-commit by refactoring to `flatMapLatest { parentId -> flow { ... } }` with explicit `if (e is CancellationException) throw e` rethrows in both repo-call try/catches; MEDIUM2 (test isolation — class-level `FakePatternRepository` shared across `"source-pat"` ids in tests a + c) verified unfounded since kotlin.test instantiates a fresh test class per `@Test` (same as the existing `userRepository` / `authRepository` fields); LOW1 (Compose `clickable` Text missing `Role.Button` — TalkBack would announce as plain text not button) fixed pre-commit; LOW2 (no test for PRIVATE-source render branch) addressed via an explanatory comment block above the resolved-test noting the ViewModel surfaces parentPattern regardless of visibility — the gate lives at the Compose / SwiftUI layer. Second-pass review APPROVED with one new LOW (the tappable Text has no `onClickLabel` so TalkBack uses the generic "double-tap to activate" announcement instead of something like "view source pattern" — consistent with existing codebase patterns on similar tappable items, deferred). Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 818, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 275). **Phase 36 closure**: with this slice, the entire ADR-012 fork-with-attribution loop is end-to-end functional — Phase 36.1 added the data spine, 36.2 added chart cloning, 36.3 wired up orchestration + Snackbar feedback, 36.4 surfaced the work in Discovery via thumbnails + chartsOnly filter, and 36.5 closes the loop by making the attribution observable to the forker on their own project detail. **Scope cuts unchanged**: iOS Discovery thumbnail live-render (Phase 36.4.1 polish) + iOS toast for chart-clone failure (Phase 36.5+ polish) remain deferred per the Tech Debt Backlog; the cached PNG thumbnail column on `chart_documents` is permanently scoped to "if telemetry shows perf regression" per ADR-012 §8. Next slice opens Phase 37 (Collaboration Core — commit history, branch, diff view per ADR-007).

- **Phase 36.4**: Discovery `chartsOnly` filter + chart-preview thumbnail (ADR-012 §4 + §5) — fourth slice of Phase 36, the Discovery-surface upgrade that finally makes the 35.x editor investment visibly observable to non-author users in the public-pattern list. **Data layer**: new `data class PublicPatternsResult(patterns: List<Pattern>, patternsWithCharts: Set<String>)` envelope returned by `PublicPatternDataSource.getPublic(searchQuery, limit, chartsOnly)`. Per ADR-012 §5 the `Pattern` data class deliberately does NOT learn about chart presence — fetching chart data inline would balloon the Discovery list query JSON. Instead the data source exposes `patternsWithCharts` as a companion set populated by a single secondary `chart_documents` query against the returned id batch.
