The companion set is **always** populated (regardless of `chartsOnly`) so PatternCard can decide per-row whether to render the live thumbnail without re-querying. **Remote impl**: `RemotePatternDataSource.getPublic` adds an INNER JOIN via `Columns.raw("*, chart_documents!inner(pattern_id)")` when `chartsOnly = true` (server-side filter; index on `chart_documents.pattern_id` from migration 012 bounds the cost per ADR-012 §4 negative consequences); the nested `chart_documents` field on each pattern row is dropped silently by the existing `Json { ignoreUnknownKeys = true }` so the `Pattern` deserializer does not need to learn about it. Companion-set query: `chart_documents.select(Columns.raw("pattern_id")) { filter { isIn("pattern_id", patternIds) } }` decoded into a small private `@Serializable ChartDocPatternIdRow` carrier with `@SerialName("pattern_id")`. The companion-set path runs even when `chartsOnly = true` for symmetry — alternative was special-casing the call site, but the index makes the secondary query cheap regardless and the symmetry simplifies the contract (Discovery always reads `result.patternsWithCharts`). **PatternRepositoryImpl call-site**: `getByVisibility(PUBLIC)` updated to read `.patterns` from the new envelope; the companion set is unused at the repository layer (only Discovery needs it). **Use case**: `GetPublicPatternsUseCase` accepts `chartsOnly: Boolean = false` param and returns `UseCaseResult<PublicPatternsResult>` (the envelope, not the bare `List<Pattern>` per pre-36.4). **DiscoveryViewModel**: `DiscoveryState` gains `chartsOnlyFilter: Boolean` + `patternsWithCharts: Set<String>` (always populated, so the iOS Swift surface can read `state.patternsWithCharts.contains(pattern.id)` directly without bridging a Kotlin Set through ObjC). Private `FilterState` data class extended with `chartsOnlyFilter`; the `combine` block widens from 4 → 5 source flows (kotlinx.coroutines `combine` 5-arg overload). New `DiscoveryEvent.ToggleChartsOnly` `data object` event flips the flag and re-loads via the existing `load(searchQuery)` path which now reads `filterState.value.chartsOnlyFilter` and propagates to the use case. Difficulty + sort stay client-side (the `combine` block reapplies them automatically); only `searchQuery` and `chartsOnly` reach the data source. **Compose UI**: new `ChartThumbnail` composable in `shared/.../ui/chart/ChartThumbnail.kt` per ADR-012 §5 — wraps a 64dp `Canvas` with a `LaunchedEffect(patternId)` that fetches `StructuredChartRepository.getByPatternId(patternId)` (Koin-injected). Catches transient fetch exceptions and falls back to the placeholder background; the Discovery list-fetch already named which patterns have charts via `patternsWithCharts`, so a per-row fetch failure here is non-fatal. The render layer reuses the existing public top-level helpers (`drawSymbolPath` / `cellScreenRect` from `SymbolDrawing.kt`; `drawPolarGrid` / `drawPolarCells` / `polarLayoutFor` from `PolarDrawing.kt`) — keeps the diff bounded and avoids refactoring the gestural `ChartCanvas` in `ChartViewerScreen.kt`. A new private `drawRectThumbnail` helper draws the rect-grid path with no row-label gutter, no segment overlay, no parameter slot text — just grid lines + symbol glyphs (or unknown-symbol `unknownBg` rect placeholder). Polar reuses the public `drawPolarCells` directly (no thumbnail-specific stripped variant needed since polar is overlay-free in v1). `DiscoveryScreen.kt` adds the "Charts only" `FilterChip` as the leading item in the `LazyRow` between search field and difficulty chips so it stays visible without horizontal scrolling, with `chartsOnlyChip` testTag. `DiscoveryPatternCard` accepts new `hasChart: Boolean` + `onChartClick: () -> Unit` params and conditionally renders `ChartThumbnail(pattern.id, onChartClick)` as the leading column of an outer `Row` (replacing the previous single-column `Card` layout) — thumbnail tap routes through `onChartViewerClick(pattern.id)` to `ChartViewer(patternId = patternId, projectId = null)`. NavGraph's `composable<Discovery>` block plumbs the new `onChartViewerClick` callback to `navController.navigate(ChartViewer(patternId, projectId = null))`. **iOS surface**: `DiscoveryFilterSection` gains the leading `chartsOnlyChip` chip; `DiscoveryPatternRow` accepts `hasChart: Bool` + `onChartTap: () -> Void` and renders an `Image(systemName: "square.grid.3x3.fill")` button as a static "has chart" placeholder thumbnail with `chartThumbnail_<patternId>` accessibility identifier. **Live mini-render on iOS deferred to Phase 36.4.1** — mirroring it requires factoring `StructuredChartViewerScreen.ChartCanvasView` (private, gestural, ~200 LOC tightly bound with segments + transforms) out into a thumbnail-friendly variant, which is a meaningful refactor; same pattern as Phase 36.3 deferring the iOS chart-clone-failure toast to a later polish slice while keeping the data layer at platform parity. The companion-set data layer (`state.patternsWithCharts`) IS at parity, so the only iOS gap is rendering fidelity. iOS toolbar tap on a row's thumbnail navigates via `path.append(Route.chartViewer(patternId: pattern.id, projectId: nil))`. **i18n**: 2 new keys added to all 5 sources (273 total, +2): `label_filter_charts_only` ("Charts only" / "チャートのみ" — chip label) + `action_view_chart_thumbnail` ("View chart preview" / "チャートプレビューを表示" — thumbnail tap a11y label). Both `label_*` / `action_*` per the role-prefix convention. **Tests**: +2 commonTest in `GetPublicPatternsUseCaseTest` (5 → 7): `populates patternsWithCharts companion set when chartsOnly is false`, `chartsOnly true filters list to chartful patterns` — covers both the always-populated companion set and the server-side filter path. +3 commonTest in `DiscoveryViewModelTest` (10 → 13): `initial load populates patternsWithCharts companion set`, `ToggleChartsOnly flips filter and re-loads with server-side filter`, `ToggleChartsOnly twice returns to unfiltered list with companion set intact` — covers the ViewModel→state plumbing of both the toggle event and the companion-set forwarding. **`FakePublicPatternDataSource`** (test fake) gained a `markHasChart(patternId)` affordance + matching `chartsOnly` filter logic; `assertTrue` import added to test files where needed. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Kover exclusion**: added `ChartThumbnailKt*` to the Compose-UI exclusion list alongside the other screen-level Composables. Pre-push invariants all green: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest`, `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (273 keys). **Ktlint recurring gotcha** (matching the Phase 32.2 / 33.4 / 35.1c / 36.3 thread): the new test method bodies routed `result.value.patterns.first().id` / `.title` chains where ktlint's `chain-method-call` rule required forced wrapping after the multiline `assertEquals(...)` constructor reformat. `:shared:ktlintFormat` auto-fixed; the diff stayed equivalent (just split each `.` chain across multiple lines). **Scope cuts unchanged**: iOS live mini-render Phase 36.4.1 polish; "Forked from" attribution UI on ProjectDetail Phase 36.5; iOS toast for chart-clone failure Phase 36.5+ polish. Cached PNG thumbnail column on `chart_documents` is permanently scoped to "if telemetry shows perf regression" per ADR-012 §8.

- **Phase 36.3**: Fork-orchestration use-case wiring (ADR-012 §3, §7) — third slice of Phase 36, the use-case layer that ties together 36.1's `parentPatternId` data spine and 36.2's `StructuredChartRepository.forkFor` repo method. Closes the in-code anchor comment that 36.1 left in `ForkPublicPatternUseCase.kt`. **Use case**: `ForkPublicPatternUseCase` gains a `StructuredChartRepository` ctor param (5 params total — Koin `factory` line in `UseCaseModule.kt` updated to `factory { ForkPublicPatternUseCase(get(), get(), get(), get(), getOrNull()) }`). The `sourcePattern.copy(...)` block now writes `parentPatternId = sourcePattern.id` — the actual write that the 36.1 spine was provisioned for. Chart clone runs **after** `patternRepository.create(forkedPattern)` and **before** `projectRepository.create(forkedProject)` per ADR-012 §3 sequence. **Best-effort semantics (ADR-012 §7)**: chart-clone failure does NOT roll back the already-created pattern + the about-to-be-created project — surfaced via two new fields on `ForkedProject`. **Cancellation safety**: manual try/catch around the `forkFor` call (NOT `runCatching`) because stdlib `runCatching` swallows `CancellationException` — a job cancellation during chart clone must propagate so the rest of the use case stops writing into a cancelled scope; mirrors the outer try/catch's CancellationException-rethrow pattern. The inner catch only catches `Exception`, so the surfaced error is guaranteed to be `Exception`-typed and `(chartCloneResult.exceptionOrNull() as Exception?)?.toUseCaseError()` is safe (in-code comment explains the type-narrowing — initially had a defensive `if (it is Exception) ... else UseCaseError.Unknown(it)` branch but the `else` was dead since the inner `catch` only catches `Exception`; code review LOW1 simplified to the cast). **`ForkedProject` envelope**: the data class lives in `ForkSharedPatternUseCase.kt` (shared between the two fork use cases since Phase 26). Gains `chartCloned: Boolean = false` and `chartCloneError: UseCaseError? = null` with safe defaults so `ForkSharedPatternUseCase`'s call site at line 110 (no chart clone there per Phase 36 scope being Discovery-only — direct sharing from Phase 4b is out of scope per ADR-012 §8) compiles unchanged via the defaults. **`forkFor` returns null when the source has no chart** — that is NOT a failure. The Boolean-mapping `Result.success(cloned != null)` distinguishes three states: (a) `Result.success(true)` cloned, (b) `Result.success(false)` source had no chart, (c) `Result.failure(e)` clone threw. **DiscoveryViewModel channel pivot**: `Channel<String>` (carrying just projectId) → `Channel<DiscoveryForkResult>` carrying a tri-state payload `(projectId, chartCloned, chartCloneFailed)`. The third field `chartCloneFailed = result.value.chartCloneError != null` exists specifically so the Snackbar can distinguish "metadata-only public pattern → no chart to clone → success path" from "chartful pattern hit transient storage failure → degraded path". Branching the Snackbar on `chartCloned` alone (the initial implementation, caught by code review MEDIUM1) would surface the failure copy on every metadata-only fork, which is a UX regression: a public pattern may legitimately never have had a chart, and telling the user "chart copy failed — try re-forking" in that case is misleading. iOS `KoinHelper.kt` bridge renamed `wrapDiscoveryForkedProjectIdFlow` → `wrapDiscoveryForkedProjectFlow`. SwiftUI `DiscoveryScreen.swift` consumer reads `result.projectId` for navigation. **Snackbar — Compose only by design**: Compose Discovery surfaces the success/failure copy via `launch { snackbarHostState.showSnackbar(...) }` (NOT awaited) before navigation; the host-launched coroutine survives the parent Composable's unmount briefly enough to render at the next destination's edge. **iOS deliberately does NOT surface a transient toast** on `chartCloneFailed=true` — SwiftUI lacks a non-blocking toast helper in this codebase, and the existing `.alert` host is blocking which would contradict ADR-012 §7 ("surfaces error without blocking navigation"). The chart-clone failure recovery path on iOS is ProjectDetail's existing "Create structured chart" CTA (same recovery path as a metadata-only public pattern). Adding an iOS toast helper is a Phase 36.5+ polish item; the data layer (chartCloneFailed flag) is correct and unit-tested today and the iOS gap is documented inline at `DiscoveryScreen.swift:142–153` with the ADR §7 citation. **i18n**: 2 new keys added to all 5 sources (271 total, +2): `message_forked_successfully` ("Forked successfully!" / "フォークしました！") + `message_forked_chart_failed` parametric-free fallback ("Forked (chart copy failed — try re-forking from project detail)" / "フォークしました（チャートのコピーに失敗しました — プロジェクト詳細から再フォークしてください）"). Both `message_*` per the Phase 33.1.6 transient-action-completion-feedback convention. **Tests**: +5 commonTest in `ForkPublicPatternUseCaseTest` (5 → 10): (a) source has chart → `chartCloned=true` + null error, (b) source no chart → `chartCloned=false` + null error (success path, NOT failure), (c) chart clone throws → pattern + project still landed + `chartCloneError` non-null, (d) `forkedPattern.parentPatternId == sourcePattern.id` (closes the 36.1 anchor), (e) project row landed in repo (separate from in-memory envelope assertion). +1 commonTest in `DiscoveryViewModelTest` (9 → 10, code review LOW2 fix): chart-clone failure path emits `chartCloned=false, chartCloneFailed=true` so the Snackbar tri-state mapping doesn't regress at the ViewModel→channel layer (separate from the use-case-layer coverage). The existing happy-path ViewModel test gained `assertFalse(forkResult.chartCloneFailed)` to anchor the no-chart success path. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens/commas/apostrophes in backticks). **ADR-012 §3 worked-skeleton update** (code review MEDIUM2): the ADR's code block originally showed `runCatching { ... }` and `chartCloneResult.getOrNull() != null` — both subtly different from the implementation pattern (cancellation-unsafe, `Boolean` mapping logic divergent). Updated to match the actual `Result<Boolean>` + manual try/catch pattern + the new tri-state Snackbar table. JA ADR is a summary file with no code block, no JA edit needed (matches the Phase 36.1 / 36.2 ADR-edit precedent). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 0 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass — all 4 fixed pre-commit (MEDIUM1 tri-state `chartCloneFailed` field; MEDIUM2 ADR §3 worked-skeleton update; LOW1 dead `else` branch removed via `as Exception?` cast with explanatory comment; LOW2 net-new `DiscoveryViewModelTest` chart-clone failure regression anchor). Second-pass review APPROVED with one new LOW (inline FQNs in the new test body — promoted to top-level imports for consistency with `ChartViewerViewModelTest.kt` style). Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest`, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 271). Suite-level totals are 968 (963 baseline post-36.2 + 5 use-case + 1 ViewModel = 968 — ahead of the +5 task target because the LOW2 fix added a 6th test). **Ktlint recurring gotcha**: ktlint required two newline placements that the JVM toolchain accepted inline — `chartCloneResult` initial assignment needed line break before `.getOrDefault(...)` chain, and the `failNext = RuntimeException(...)` start in the new ViewModel test needed a multiline expression on a new line. Same class as the Phase 32.2 / 33.4 / 35.1c gotchas already documented in Tech Debt Backlog; `:shared:ktlintFormat` auto-fixes both. **Scope cuts unchanged**: Discovery `chartsOnly` filter + chart-preview thumbnail Phase 36.4; "Forked from" attribution UI on ProjectDetail Phase 36.5; iOS toast for chart-clone failure Phase 36.5+ polish.

- **Phase 36.2**: Chart-clone repository method (ADR-012 §2) — second slice of Phase 36, smallest atomic data layer that unblocks 36.3 (`ForkPublicPatternUseCase` orchestration). Pure repository surface; no schema change, no migration. **Interface**: `StructuredChartRepository.forkFor(sourcePatternId, newPatternId, newOwnerId): StructuredChart?` — KDoc spells out the envelope-id-rewrite contract (fresh `id`, `patternId`, `ownerId`, `revisionId`, `createdAt`, `updatedAt`; `parentRevisionId = source.revisionId` per ADR-012 §2 commit-rooted lineage; `contentHash` carried verbatim per ADR-008 §7 drawing-identity invariant; `schemaVersion`/`storageVariant`/`coordinateSystem`/`extents`/`layers`/`craftType`/`readingConvention` all preserved byte-for-byte). Returns null when source has no chart — caller (Phase 36.3 use case) treats this as the metadata-only fork branch per ADR-012 §3 best-effort semantics. **Impl**: leverages the existing `getByPatternId(sourcePatternId)` resolution path which already does local-then-remote fallback when online — a forker who has not yet cached the source pattern still hits a fresh copy. The clone uses `source.copy(...)` so any future fields added to `StructuredChart` are picked up automatically without touching `forkFor`. Local persistence routes through `local.insert()` (not `upsert` — the cloned `newPatternId` is brand-new from the use-case orchestration immediately above this call, so no UNIQUE collision on `pattern_id`). Sync wiring reuses `SyncEntityType.STRUCTURED_CHART + SyncOperation.INSERT`, which `SyncExecutor.executeStructuredChart` already maps to `remote.upsert(chart)` — idempotent retry, PendingSync coalescing handles offline/reconnect identically to a regular create. No new SyncEntityType. `Clock.System.now()` computed inside the impl per the ADR-012 §2 "fresh created_at / updated_at" contract (other write paths take time from the use-case layer; the ADR signature drove this divergence and matches the pattern that the time stamping is part of the fork's atomic write). **Audit per task brief — `parentRevisionId` silent-overwrite footgun**: `StructuredChart.parentRevisionId: String?` has **NO default value**, so kotlinx-serialization always emits the field on the wire regardless of `encodeDefaults`. This structurally protects against the same class of bug that Phase 36.1 fixed on `Pattern.parentPatternId` via `@EncodeDefault(NEVER)` — `Pattern` had `= null` as a backward-compat default for legacy clients (added in migration 014), `StructuredChart.parentRevisionId` has been a required field since Phase 29 so legacy clients always carried it. Audit comment added inline in `StructuredChart.kt` explicitly forbidding adding a default to keep this invariant visible. **Tests**: +8 commonTest in `StructuredChartRepositoryImplTest` (9 → 17 in this file): (a) source has no chart returns null + 0 sync calls, (b) cloned envelope mints fresh ids and rewrites `pattern_id`/`owner_id`, (c) `parentRevisionId == source.revisionId`, (d) `contentHash` preserved, (e) byte-equal document round-trip across rich layers (multi-cell, parametric `ch-space` symbol with parameters map, locked/invisible flags, multiple layers), (f) sync INSERT enqueued for cloned envelope, (g) cloned chart retrievable by `newPatternId` without disturbing source, (h) fork-of-fork chains `parentRevisionId` to immediate predecessor (ancestry walks the chain, not the original — Phase 37 collaboration concern). Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha: no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks. **Test fakes**: `FakeStructuredChartRepository` (use-case test fake) gains a `forkFor` override that mints deterministic ids (`"fork-${size}"`) so future use-case tests can assert against them — real envelope-id correctness lives in the impl test. Inline `object : StructuredChartRepository` in `ChartViewerViewModelTest.kt:138` got a `forkFor = null` stub. **Pre-push invariants all green** (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` — `StructuredChartRepositoryImplTest` 17 tests passing, +8 from 9 baseline; `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 269 keys unchanged — 36.2 is repository-layer, no i18n surface). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 3 LOW first pass — all addressed pre-commit. **HIGH** asymmetry note added to the StructuredChart.kt audit comment so the next reader understands `craftType` / `readingConvention` deliberately keep their defaults (schema-v1 backward-compat anchor, symmetric round-trip under `encodeDefaults = false`) and won't misapply `@EncodeDefault(NEVER)` to them. **MEDIUMs** addressed inline (round-trip equality assumption note on test (g); FakeStructuredChartRepository timestamp-divergence comment so Phase 36.3 use-case tests don't assert on fake timestamps). LOWs were style-only or no-action. **Scope cuts**: use-case-level orchestration of `parentPatternId` (36.1's data spine) + `forkFor` (36.2's data spine) is Phase 36.3; Discovery `chartsOnly` filter + thumbnail Phase 36.4; "Forked from" attribution UI Phase 36.5.

- **Phase 36.1**: Pattern fork attribution data spine (ADR-012 §1) — first slice of Phase 36, smallest atomic data layer that unblocks 36.2 (chart-clone repo method), 36.3 (`ForkPublicPatternUseCase` extension), 36.4 (Discovery `chartsOnly` filter), and 36.5 (attribution UI). **Schema**: Supabase migration 014 (`014_pattern_attribution.sql`) adds `parent_pattern_id UUID NULL REFERENCES public.patterns(id) ON DELETE SET NULL` to `public.patterns` plus a partial index `WHERE parent_pattern_id IS NOT NULL` (forks are a minority of rows, so the partial index keeps reverse-lookup cost bounded without bloating the row-count index). `IF NOT EXISTS` on both `ADD COLUMN` and `CREATE INDEX` for idempotent re-application; ADR-012 §1's DDL block updated in lock-step. SQLDelight: `4.sqm` (`ALTER TABLE PatternEntity ADD COLUMN parent_pattern_id TEXT;` no DEFAULT — column starts NULL on existing rows) and `Pattern.sq` `CREATE TABLE` extended with the column at the END so positional binding indices for the existing 12 columns stay stable. The `update:` SQLDelight query deliberately does NOT include `parent_pattern_id` — ADR-012 §1 invariant: set once at fork time (Phase 36.3) and never changed afterwards; the existing column value is preserved across regular `update` writes by virtue of being absent from the `SET …` list. **Domain**: `Pattern` data class gains `parentPatternId: String? = null` at the end of the `data class Pattern(...)` ctor (default keeps all existing call sites compiling unchanged — verified: every `Pattern(...)` and `pattern.copy(...)` site in `shared/src/commonMain` and `shared/src/commonTest` uses named arguments, so positional shift is impossible). Annotated `@SerialName("parent_pattern_id")` for kotlinx.serialization round-trip with Supabase JSON. **`@EncodeDefault(EncodeDefault.Mode.NEVER)` on the field** (with `@OptIn(ExperimentalSerializationApi::class)` at the data class level) is the load-bearing part of this slice — without it, a regular pattern edit synced from a device whose local cache predates migration 4.sqm would serialize `"parent_pattern_id": null` and the Supabase PATCH would silently overwrite the server-side attribution back to NULL, defeating the entire ADR-012 §1 invariant. The annotation suppresses field emission only when the value equals the default null; non-null fork values still serialize correctly. Currently defensively redundant with the `Json { ignoreUnknownKeys = true }` in `SyncModule.kt:34` (which inherits the kotlinx.serialization 1.11.0 default `encodeDefaults = false` — the exact runtime that already drops null defaults), but if anyone ever flips that to `encodeDefaults = true` for another field, the annotation immediately becomes the only protection against the silent-erasure footgun. The `@EncodeDefault` is encode-only and does not affect deserialization (verified in second-pass review: both supabase-kt's internal Json instance and `SyncExecutor.kt:55-56` `decodeFromString<Pattern>` correctly populate the field when `"parent_pattern_id": "<uuid>"` is present in the wire payload). **Mappers**: `PatternMapper.toDomain()` adds the `parentPatternId = parent_pattern_id` line; `LocalPatternDataSource` plumbs `parent_pattern_id = pattern.parentPatternId` through all 3 INSERT call sites (`insert`, `upsert` insert-branch, `upsertAll` insert-branch). `update`/`upsert`-update-branch/`upsertAll`-update-branch deliberately don't touch the column — the SQLDelight `update:` query omission is the invariant guard. **`ForkPublicPatternUseCase`**: an in-code anchor comment was added above the `sourcePattern.copy(...)` block flagging that Phase 36.3 will add `parentPatternId = sourcePattern.id` here once the chart-clone path lands. The current `.copy(...)` deliberately omits the override so 36.1 ships pure data-layer plumbing without changing fork semantics — Phase 36.3 owns the actual attribution write. ADR-012 §3. **Tests**: +7 commonTest (PatternMapperTest 17 → 19, +2 cases for null + non-null `parentPatternId` on `toDomain()`; LocalPatternDataSourceTest 9 → 14, +5 cases — default-null insert, non-null insert+getById round-trip, update preserves parentPatternId across a title rename, `upsert` insert-branch round-trip, `upsertAll` insert-branch round-trip). The upsert insert-branch tests are structurally correct because `@BeforeTest setUp()` creates a fresh in-memory SQLite via `createTestDriver()` for every test — no pre-existing row at `pat-fork`, so the upsert path takes the INSERT branch genuinely. **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass. **HIGH** (`@EncodeDefault(NEVER)` to prevent the sync-update silent-overwrite-to-null footgun) was the load-bearing fix described above; landed pre-commit. **MEDIUM1** (in-code anchor comment on `ForkPublicPatternUseCase` for Phase 36.3 readers) landed pre-commit. **MEDIUM2** (ADR-012 §1 DDL block out-of-sync with `IF NOT EXISTS` in the actual migration file) landed pre-commit on the EN ADR; the JA ADR is a summary file pointing back to EN with no DDL block, so no JA edit needed. **LOW1** (additional upsert and upsertAll insert-branch tests) landed pre-commit, bringing the test delta to +7 from the originally-planned +5. Second-pass review APPROVED with one wording-clarity LOW on the comment block in `ForkPublicPatternUseCase` ("inherited otherwise" was ambiguous about whether transitive grandparent attribution was intentional); fixed pre-commit by rewording to make the Phase 36.1 vs 36.3 scope split explicit. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest`, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 269 keys unchanged — 36.1 is data-layer, no i18n surface). **Scope cuts**: chart-side fork (`StructuredChartRepository.forkFor` per ADR-012 §2) is Phase 36.2; the use-case-level wiring of `parentPatternId = sourcePattern.id` and the chart-clone orchestration is Phase 36.3; Discovery `chartsOnly` filter + thumbnail are Phase 36.4; "Forked from" attribution UI on ProjectDetail is Phase 36.5. Net new commits: this is the first slice; no chart_documents or Discovery code touched. Migration 014 ships orphan-able rows by design (forks survive source deletion via SET NULL) per ADR-012 §1.

- **Phase 35.1d**: Polar tap-to-toggle for per-segment progress — closes the Phase 34 polar-deferral banner. Kotlin `ChartViewerScreen.kt` gesture handler drops `if (isPolar) return@pointerInput` + the unconditional `extents as? ChartExtents.Rect` cast, replacing both with a `when (extents) { is Rect -> resolveHit; is Polar -> resolvePolarHit }` sealed-exhaustive branch. New `resolvePolarHit(offset, sizePx, polar, visibleLayers)` helper delegates to `polarLayoutFor` (Phase 35.1b) + `GridHitTest.hitTestPolar` (Phase 35.1a) + existing `topmostLayerAt` — `cell.x = stitch`, `cell.y = ring` matches the storage convention already used by the Phase 35.1b/c overlay + glyph passes. `PolarDeferredNotice` composable removed, `isPolar` param dropped from `ChartCanvas` (dead after the banner + gesture guards + rect-overlay guard all fell). iOS `StructuredChartViewerScreen.swift` mirror: deferred-notice VStack branch dropped, `guard !isPolar` removed from both `handleTap` / `handleLongPress`, new `resolveAnyHit(location:size:)` dispatches to `resolveHit` (rect) or `resolvePolarHit` (polar). Swift `resolvePolarHit` inlines the Kotlin `hitTestPolar` algorithm because `PolarCellLayout` doesn't bridge cleanly through the Shared framework (same lock-step pattern as the 35.1b/c polar geometry): atan2 + π/2 shift, inner-hole return nil, outer-exclusive, fp-defensive `floor` + `min(max(…, 0), N-1)`. `isPolar: Bool` field dropped from `ChartCanvasView` entirely (also dropped the stale `!isPolar` guard on the rect `draw(into:)` overlay branch — dead but would have silently suppressed rect overlays if a future refactor routed polar through the rect path). Retired `message_segment_progress_polar_deferred` i18n key from all 5 sources (241 keys, down from 242) — feature shipped, banner key would be misleading bookkeeping. **Critical code-review catch**: first-pass review caught a HIGH where the `ChartViewerViewModel.tapCell` / `longPressCell` methods still contained `if (_state.value.isPolar) return` short-circuits — without removing those, the Screen-level wiring would dispatch events that got silently swallowed at the ViewModel boundary, so polar tap-to-toggle would have shipped end-to-end no-op'd despite the gesture handler looking correct. Fixed pre-commit; second-pass review APPROVED. Second-pass fix also dropped the iOS `isPolar` field entirely + added a regression comment explaining 35.1d's dispatch structure. +2 commonTest (`tapCell on polar chart toggles segment state via use case` + `longPressCell on polar chart marks segment done`) — the prior `isPolar flag … disables tap events` test inverted semantically so it was split into the pure state-check (`isPolar flag mirrors the chart coordinate system`) plus the two new regression anchors. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest`, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 241).

- **Phase 35.1c**: Polar symbol rendering (ADR-011 §2 final piece) — paints the glyph inside every visible polar cell. `shared/src/commonMain/.../ui/chart/PolarDrawing.kt` new `DrawScope.drawPolarCells(polar, chart, hiddenLayerIds, catalog, layout, textMeasurer, parsedPathCache, symbolColor, unknownBg, unknownFg)`. For each in-range cell: inscribed-square side `min(ringThickness, 2·r_center·sin(sweep/2))` clamped to ≥1f (the `sin(sweep/2)` factor is the half-chord at r_center = innerR + (ring + 0.5)·ringThickness), bounds = axis-aligned square centered on `PolarCellLayout.cellCenter(stitch, ring)`, then `DrawScope.rotate(degrees = cellRadialUpRotation·180/π, pivot = cell center)` wraps the `drawSymbolPath(def, bounds, rotation = cell.rotation, ...)` call so the glyph's local "up" points radially outward AND the author's discrete 0/90/180/270 composes on top inside the rotated bounds. Unknown symbols: filled `unknownBg` rect + `?` glyph via `TextMeasurer`, rendered upright-along-radial by virtue of being inside the same `rotate` scope. Stroke width `max(1f, side * 0.06f)` mirrors rect's `cellSize * 0.06f`. Out-of-range cells silently skipped, mirroring `drawPolarSegmentOverlay` defensive clipping. `ChartViewerScreen.kt` Polar branch calls `drawPolarCells` AFTER `drawPolarSegmentOverlay` — overlay-under-glyph ordering per ADR-011 §2 (matches rect AC-1.2). `iosApp/.../StructuredChartViewerScreen.swift` `drawPolar` mirror: per-cell `var subcontext = context` + `translateBy(px, py)` / `rotate(by: .radians(thetaCenter))` / `translateBy(-px, -py)` rotates around the cell center, then calls existing `drawSymbolPath` / `drawUnknown` with the rotated subcontext so the same shared `SymbolRenderTransform.mapCommand` applies `cell.rotation` within the bounds. **iOS formula lock-step**: inline `thetaCenter = stitch*sweep + sweep/2` recomputes what `PolarCellLayout.cellRadialUpRotation` returns on the Kotlin side (the function is not bridged to Swift since it's a Kotlin `object` member); added a warning comment pointing at the Kotlin authority so any future formula change (e.g. Phase 35.x widthUnits > 1 arc-spanning cells) is caught in lock-step. **Scope cuts** — parametric slot text inside polar wedges NOT implemented (deferred to Phase 35.2+ alongside polar editor; rect parametric `drawParameterSlots` unchanged); polar tap-to-toggle deferred (Phase 35.2); per-ring radial spokes still outermost-only (Phase 35.x polish). No test delta (visual/rendering code, no commonTest visual-diff infra set up — geometry spine at `PolarCellLayout` already has 32 tests covering `cellCenter`/`cellRadialUpRotation` from Phase 35.1a). Code review: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 2 LOW. HIGH1 fixed pre-commit (iOS lock-step comment). HIGH2 (`return@forEach` label-shadowing concern) not taken — `drawPolarSegmentOverlay` ships the identical pattern since Phase 34; changing only one sibling creates inconsistency, the current code is correct, and the reviewer's concern is latent-future not current-runtime. MEDIUMs both pre-existing patterns (iOS `max(1, ...)` type inference matches `cellSize * 0.06` line 311; `cell.x/y` type matches Phase 34 `drawPolarSegmentOverlay` usage). LOW1 fixed (KDoc note on shared `parsedPathCache` accumulator). LOW2 (`.sp` on canvas pixel value) skipped per consistency with rect renderer's Phase 31 unknown-symbol pattern. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck`, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 815, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 242). 815 shared tests (unchanged).

- **Phase 35.1b**: Polar viewer rendering (ADR-011 §2) — ring grid, segment overlay, and deferred-notice wiring for round charts. `shared/src/commonMain/.../ui/chart/PolarDrawing.kt` new file with `polarLayoutFor(width, height, polar): PolarCellLayout.Layout` (inner 15% reserved so inner rings stay readable when rings is small; outer 0.47 leaves canvas margin), `DrawScope.drawPolarGrid(polar, layout, color)` (concentric ring boundaries + outermost-ring radial spokes — per-ring spokes is a Phase 35.x polish item per ADR-011 §2), `polarWedgePath(wedge, layout)` (annular-wedge `Path` tracing outer arc CW then inner arc CCW to close the region, with `-90°` shift to reconcile `PolarCellLayout`'s 12-o'clock-CW convention with Compose `Path.arcTo`'s 3-o'clock-CW-on-y-down convention), `DrawScope.drawPolarSegmentOverlay(polar, chart, hiddenLayerIds, segments, layout, doneColor, wipColor, wipStrokeWidthPx)` (done/wip wedge paint mirroring the rect AC-1.1/AC-1.2 semantics; done = filled, wip = stroke). `ChartViewerScreen.kt` Polar branch in `ChartCanvas` wires layout + grid + segment overlay + the pre-existing `PolarDeferredNotice` `message_segment_progress_polar_deferred` banner (AC-1.4). Tap-to-toggle intentionally early-returns on `isPolar` — polar gesture handling is cross-cutting with editor authoring and stays deferred to Phase 35.2+. `isPolar` flag also plumbed through the `ChartCanvas` signature. iOS `StructuredChartViewerScreen.swift` mirror: `PolarLayout` struct inlined in Swift (avoids bridging the Kotlin `PolarCellLayout.Layout` / `Wedge` data classes through the Shared framework), `polarLayout(for:canvasSize:ringsCount:)`, `polarWedgePath(stitch:ring:stitchesInRing:layout:)` (SwiftUI `Path.addArc` with `clockwise:false` for outer / `clockwise:true` for inner — under y-down screen coords this renders visually CW matching the CW-positive convention), `drawPolar(...)` replaces the prior empty polar branch. `segmentsVersion` sentinel forces Canvas re-eval on segment map mutation. ADR-011 §1 second-to-last paragraph deferral ("symbol rendering inside polar wedges is deferred to a follow-up slice") shipped with the commit. No test delta (rendering code). 815 shared tests. Commit 1e58f7d.

- **Phase 35.1a**: Polar coord transform + hit-test helpers (ADR-011 §1) — pure-Kotlin geometry spine for round charts, landed as an atomic slice before any viewer/editor wiring. `shared/src/commonMain/.../domain/chart/PolarCellLayout.kt` new object with `Layout(cx, cy, innerRadius, ringThickness)`, `Wedge(innerRadius, outerRadius, startAngle, sweepAngle)`, `wedgeFor(stitch, ring, extents, layout)`, `cellCenter(stitch, ring, extents, layout): Pair<Double, Double>`, and `cellRadialUpRotation(stitch, ring, extents): Double`. `GridHitTest.hitTestPolar(screenX, screenY, extents, layout): Cell?` per the ADR 7-step algorithm — inner-hole tap returns null (matches flat outside-grid semantics), outer-ring boundary exclusive (`radius >= innerRadius + rings*ringThickness` → null), floor+coerceIn defensive against fp boundary rounding. Angle convention: 12 o'clock = 0, clockwise positive (shift via `atan2(dy, dx) + π/2`, mod 2π normalize); stitch 0 of each ring *starts* at 12 o'clock so its wedge spans `[0, 2π/N)` and its center sits at `π/N` — a half-stitch CW offset, not centered at 12 o'clock. `cellRadialUpRotation` returns the stitch center angle in radians (compatible with Compose `rotate(deg)` / SwiftUI `.rotationEffect(.radians(rot))` since positive theta = CW rotation on screen = geometrically correct outward pointing). `cellRadialUpRotation` intentionally does NOT take `Layout` — rotation is geometry-pure, not pixel-scaled; one test asserts this contract by reading only the extents. +32 commonTest (15 PolarCellLayoutTest + 17 hitTestPolar; 847 total — up from 815). Coverage: wedge geometry at ring boundaries, 4 cardinal-clock taps against ring 1 (8 stitches), atan2 fourth-quadrant, 9 o'clock wraparound on ring 2 (12 stitches), exact inner+outer radius boundaries (inner inclusive, outer exclusive), rings=0 + zero ringThickness degeneracy guards, non-origin layout center, near-12-o-clock-from-left wraparound verifying `(rawTheta % 2π + 2π) % 2π` normalization. Pre-push invariants all green (`ktlintCheck` with one post-autoformat fix on `GridHitTest.kt` line-82 multiline chain, `compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `testAndroidHostTest` 847, `koverVerify`, `verify-i18n-keys.sh` 242). **Scope cuts explicit** — viewer polar overlay paint (ADR-011 §2) deferred to Phase 35.1b; editor polar craft (§1 + §3 mirror ops, §4 batch row-done, §5 layer ops, §6 grid resize) deferred to Phase 35.2+; symbol rendering inside polar cells deferred with the viewer wiring. The Phase 34 `message_segment_progress_polar_deferred` notice stays intact — tap-to-toggle for polar is cross-cutting with editor authoring and does not land in 35.1a. Test-name hygiene: all new backticked names follow the Phase 32 CI gotcha — no parens, commas, or apostrophes (Kotlin/Native rejects these while JVM tolerates).

## Closed Tech Debt trails

These items were active Tech Debt during the beta-foundation phases (33.x onward) and have since been closed. They live here as a historical trail so future readers researching "how did we close i18n" or "how did we kill Maestro `text:` brittleness" have one place to look. The corresponding CLAUDE.md `## Tech Debt Backlog` entries reference this archive instead of carrying the full prose.

- **i18n sweep across remaining shared screens** (**CLOSED as of Phase 33.1.15** — left here as historical trail; zero shared Compose surfaces remain that hardcode English. Any new screen added to `shared/src/commonMain/.../ui/*` must migrate literals to `stringResource(Res.string.*)` on first commit and update all 5 i18n sources.): Phase 33.1 landed the `compose.components.resources` plumbing (+ chart editor reference), Phase 33.1.1 migrated `SymbolGalleryScreen` (+ fixed the AGP 9.x CMP-resource-packaging bug that Phase 33.1 shipped with latent — see CI Known Limitations), Phase 33.1.2 migrated `ChartViewerScreen`, Phase 33.1.3 migrated `ProjectListScreen` (+ introduced the `hint_` prefix and the "any shared-screen migration that changes a user-visible literal hit by a Maestro regex selector needs a testTag preflight" rule — see Phase 33.1.3 Completed entry for the commit `b0fb3d8` search-field follow-up fix), Phase 33.1.4 migrated `OnboardingScreen` (+ introduced the `body_*` role prefix for paragraph body copy paired with a `title_*` headline; also caught a latent HIGH in `iosAppUITests/OnboardingUITests.swift` where `app.staticTexts["English title"]` queries would break on Japanese-locale simulators — migrated to `app.otherElements["onboardingPage1..3"]` via `.accessibilityIdentifier`), Phase 33.1.5 migrated `LoginScreen` (+ established the `action_*` vs `label_*` precedent for interactive button labels per code-review MEDIUM1 — toggle-mode buttons are `action_toggle_to_*` not `label_toggle_to_*`; documented `title_error` for single-button error alerts in the convention; followed-up MEDIUM3 deferred — net-new `LoginUITests.swift` to write alongside Maestro Login flows when Supabase is exercised end-to-end), Phase 33.1.6 migrated `ProfileScreen` (+ introduced the `message_*` role prefix for transient action-completion feedback like Snackbar/Toast; added the SwiftUI literal-promotion table to the convention doc distinguishing auto-localizing APIs like `Text("key")` from overload-ambiguous ones like `.alert("key", ...)`; established that SwiftUI state-branch containers need a concrete layout node like `ZStack` — a bare `Group` is layout-transparent and propagates accessibility modifiers to each child branch independently, breaking the landmark query), Phase 33.1.7 migrated `ActivityFeedScreen` (+ parametric activity templates with `%1$s` / `%1$@` substitution preserving Japanese `{name}が{verb}` grammar, and unified the author-lookup fallback on `label_someone` across platforms — Android was incorrectly rendering "You"), Phase 33.1.8 migrated `SettingsScreen` (+ established platform-idiom divergence is acceptable for dialog confirm-button wording — Compose `AlertDialog` uses short "Delete" and iOS `.confirmationDialog` uses full "Delete Account"; also codified extending the `.confirmationDialog` "needs explicit `LocalizedStringKey` wrap" rule to its `message:` closure content, not just the outer title parameter), Phase 33.1.9 migrated `DiscoveryScreen` (+ codified the empty-state-body key-convention as `state_*_body` suffix to match the established `state_no_projects_body` / `state_no_matching_projects_body` siblings; established that `.navigationTitle` on non-conditional literals should still wrap explicitly with `LocalizedStringKey(...)` for consistency with all preceding 33.1.x migrations, even though the convention-doc literal-promotion table says a bare literal would work — consistency wins; introduced `label_difficulty_*` as a distinct domain prefix from `label_status_*` because they are different filter taxonomies; per-chip testTag landmarks `difficulty{All,Beginner,Intermediate,Advanced}Chip` established as the pattern for multi-chip filter bars that will otherwise have locale-dependent Maestro taps), and Phase 33.1.10 migrated `PatternLibraryScreen` (+ promoted `Difficulty.labelKey` from `DiscoveryScreen.kt` private to `ui/components/DifficultyLabels.kt` public shared extension — first shared i18n helper extension in the codebase; established the precedent that when a second screen needs the same enum→StringResource mapping, promote to `ui/components/` and add an exhaustive test rather than duplicate the `when` block; also harmonized iOS and Android delete-confirmation wording by switching iOS from a generic short body to a parametric `dialog_delete_pattern_body` via `String(format: NSLocalizedString(...), pendingDeleteName)`), and Phase 33.1.13 migrated `SharedContentScreen` (+ established that an iOS-only key still shipping in all 5 i18n sources for `verify-i18n-keys.sh` parity needs an explicit intent comment in the shared EN strings file so future readers don't assume symmetric Android usage — see `state_could_not_load`; also established that JA translations semantically diverging from bare-literal EN — `プロジェクト数` vs `Projects` — should carry a comment in the JA strings file when the divergence is intentional for contextual clarity rather than a translator judgement call; also established that `default` branches in Swift enum switches forced by Kotlin→ObjC bridging should return a locale-neutral non-empty fallback like `enum.name` rather than empty string so future Kotlin enum additions without matching Swift updates surface visibly rather than as blank UI cells), and Phase 33.1.14 migrated `SharedWithMeScreen` (+ established that platform-idiom divergence for a list-row render style — Android single pipe-separated line vs iOS bullet-separated HStack fragments — is acceptable only if **both platforms consume the same parametric keys**; a code reviewer caught iOS silently dropping the "From"/"Shared on" prefixes because `Text(verbatim: sharerName)` rendered the bare value and the parametric keys defined in xcstrings went unused — generalizable lesson is that "iOS renders fragments visually" does not permit skipping the parametric keys; route through `String(format: NSLocalizedString("key", comment: ""), arg)` so translators see the full sentence context and future platform re-renders stay consistent; also bundled two pre-existing Android bugs as i18n-adjacent fixes — the raw enum name render `share.permission.name` → "VIEW"/"FORK" uppercase and the sharer-null branch that omitted the "From" prefix entirely — both harmonized via `label_someone` fallback and `label_permission_{view,fork}`; `label_share_status_*` established as a distinct domain prefix from `label_status_*` since share status and project status are separate taxonomies). The following shared Compose screens still hardcode English and need the same `stringResource(Res.string.*)` treatment: `CommentSection` (1 explicitly enumerated after 33.1.14). Also deferred from 33.1.12 scope: `UserPickerDialog.kt` (Android-only, triggered from ProjectDetailScreen toolbar "Share with user" IconButton — contentDescription is migrated but the dialog body itself is not). Each migration adds its own domain keys to all 5 i18n sources and should be cut as its own PR. **Note for Maestro flows**: once a screen's title becomes i18n'd, any existing `assertVisible: "<English title>"` must be replaced with the screen's stable testTag (as done for `P1_symbol_gallery.yaml` and the `onboardingPage{1,2,3}` testTags in 33.1.4) — otherwise the flow fails the moment CMP resolves to the Japanese locale or the (now-asynchronous) resource takes a beat to load. Same rule applies to **iOS XCUITests**: any `app.staticTexts["literal"]` query against i18n'd copy must pivot to `app.otherElements["testTag"]` (33.1.4 caught this on Onboarding). Also: Maestro `tapOn: "text"` uses regex; literal `...` matches 3 chars but Unicode `\u2026` (`…`) is 1 char — any U+2026 ellipsis introduction (common for placeholders per the `state_loading` style) must either update the flow's regex or route through a testTag.

- **Maestro `text: "Back"` / `text: "Clear search"` brittleness** (**CLOSED as of Phase 33.4** — left here as historical trail; both halves are resolved. Non-dialog sites: Phase 33.2 pivoted all 12 shared screens to `backButton` / `clearSearchButton` / `editProjectButton` / `filter*Chip` testTags. Dialog-content sites: Phase 33.4 landed the `expect/actual` `Modifier.dialogTestTagsAsResourceId()` helper (path (b) — invasive Compose workaround from the 33.2 open-question list) that applies `.semantics { testTagsAsResourceId = true }` inside the AlertDialog window itself, bypassing the root Box's inability to propagate through the window boundary. All 9 Android Maestro flows now use `id:` selectors for dialog content (`newProjectDialog`, `editProjectDialog`, `projectNameInput`, `totalRowsInput`, `createProjectButton`, `saveButton`). Verified on both en-US (8/8 ✅) and ja-JP (8/8 ✅) Android emulator runs — the ja-JP pass is now locale-independent and no longer load-bearing on the dialogs staying English-hardcoded. Two holdout iOS nav-title text assertions (`assertVisible: "New Project"` / `"Edit Project"`) remain because SwiftUI `NavigationStack` title is not an `accessibilityIdentifier`-addressable element; documented with inline comments pointing at the pending iOS ProjectList i18n sweep.)

- **Android per-app locale non-functional** (**CLOSED in Phase 33.3** — left here as historical trail; `androidApp/build.gradle.kts` now opts into `generateLocaleConfig = true` with `localeFilters += listOf("en", "ja")` and `androidApp/src/main/res/resources.properties` declares `unqualifiedResLocale=en-US`. AGP generates `xml/_generated_res_locale_config.xml` and auto-injects `android:localeConfig` into the merged manifest. Android Settings > App Info > Language picker works end-to-end on Android 13+; ja-JP Maestro run 8/8 ✅.): historical context — Android 13+'s `LocaleManagerService` stored per-app locale values when set via `adb shell cmd locale set-app-locales <pkg> --locales ja-JP` but the runtime `Activity.Configuration.getLocales()` did not honor them, so CMP's `Res.string.*` and Android-native `R.string.*` both resolved to the system locale regardless of the user's selection. Discovered during Phase 33.2-verify; resolved in Phase 33.3. See the Phase 33.3 Completed entry for the `localeFilters` aapt2-vs-BCP-47 format gotcha captured as a Gradle inline comment.

- **ViewModel error-message localization** (**CLOSED as of Phase G.1 stage b/c** — left here as historical trail; the original concern was that ViewModels held raw `errorMessage: String?` populated from Kotlin exception messages, so JA users would see English text. Phase G.1 stage b/c migrated every affected ViewModel to a typed `errorMessage: ErrorMessage?` channel where `ErrorMessage` is a sealed type that maps 1:1 to localized `StringResource` values via `toErrorMessage()`. UseCaseError's legacy `NotFound(message: String)` / `Validation(message: String)` variants — which carried hardcoded English strings — were replaced with semantic typed variants like `ResourceNotFound`, `SignInRequired`, `RequiresConnectivity`, `BlankField`, etc. The mapping layer at `ErrorMessage.toErrorMessage(error: UseCaseError)` plus the screen-side `stringResource(error.titleKey)` / `stringResource(error.bodyKey)` extensions render the right copy per locale. See the `UseCaseResult.kt` file-level KDoc at `shared/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/github/b150005/skeinly/domain/usecase/UseCaseResult.kt` for the canonical reference. Any ViewModel added after this migration must hold `ErrorMessage?` (not `String?`) for displayed errors.)

- **Maestro E2E for chart editor** (**CLOSED as of Phase 32 (the Phase 32 Completed entry references this as `P1_chart_editor.yaml`)** — left here as historical trail; the original concern was that the "Edit structured chart" entry-point on `ProjectDetailScreen` is gated on `state.pattern != null` (Project ↔ Pattern linkage), so any Maestro flow exercising the editor needs a multi-step prelude: onboarding → pattern create → project create with pattern link → project detail → open chart editor. The flow at `e2e/flows/android/P1_chart_editor.yaml` (header note: "Closes the Tech Debt Backlog 'Maestro E2E for chart editor' entry") implements that prelude end-to-end via the helper composition `complete_onboarding_android.yaml` + `create_pattern_android.yaml`. Validates the full path: place a cell → save → confirm the chart was created. Self-contained — no Supabase requirement; pattern + project + chart all live in local-only mode. Tagged `p1` + `android`. The iOS side is gated on the open Maestro + iOS 26 SwiftUI-Button-tap reliability bug — the same `skip-ios26` tag exclusion applies until Maestro ships an iOS 26 fix.)

- **iOS Discovery thumbnail live-render** (**CLOSED as of Phase 36.4.1b** — left here as historical trail; the original concern was that iOS Discovery's `DiscoveryPatternRow` shipped with a static `Image(systemName: "square.grid.3x3.fill")` placeholder, while Compose's `ChartThumbnail` rendered a live mini-chart via the public `drawSymbolPath` / `drawPolarGrid` / `drawPolarCells` helpers. Phase 36.4.1a extracted the rendering primitives (grid + symbol-glyphs path drawing) from `StructuredChartViewerScreen.swift`'s private `ChartCanvasView` into a standalone `Components/ChartRenderingKit.swift` (~11 KB / 200 LOC) — the third consumer surfacing here was the trigger that closed the inline-helper duplication. Phase 36.4.1b then added `Components/ChartThumbnailView.swift` (~9 KB) which wraps the kit primitives in a tappable Button + `@StateObject PathCommandCache` for symbol path memoization + `@State chart: StructuredChart?` for async loading. `DiscoveryPatternRow` now renders `ChartThumbnailView(patternId: pattern.id, onTap: onChartTap)` instead of the placeholder. iOS now achieves rendering parity with Compose's `ChartThumbnail` for grid + symbols + polar — segment overlay, row/ring labels, and parameter slot text are deliberately omitted (thumbnail-friendly variant). The cached-PNG thumbnail column on `chart_documents` remains permanently scoped to "if telemetry shows perf regression" per ADR-012 §8 — live render is correct (always matches current chart state) and Discovery's `List` keeps the fetch demand-driven (off-screen rows do not fetch).)

- **Phase 41.5.1**: F1 ADR-016 §41.5 consumer-pattern deviation cleanup — closes the only known §41.5.1 deviation that existed at Phase 41.5 documentation time (`PackManagementViewModel` injecting `EntitlementResolver` directly to compute `PackStatus.Locked` inline, per the §41.5.3 reference table's ⚠ row). Lifts the gate-site rule from "honored except one place" to "honored fully" before the cleanup deviation could propagate as copy-paste precedent. **No user-facing change**: `PackManagementScreen` continues to render the lock badge / disable per-row download for Pro packs the user lacks entitlement to; only the layer that owns the gate decision moves. **New `domain/symbol/SymbolPackCatalog.kt`** — sibling interface to `SymbolCatalog`. `interface SymbolPackCatalog { suspend fun listInventory(): PackInventory }` with `data class PackInventory(rows, totalDownloadedBytes)`. The `PackRow` data class + `PackStatus` 4-state enum move from `ui.packmanagement` to `domain.symbol` so they're catalog-layer return shapes (Kotlin/Native ObjC bridge exports simple class names regardless of source package, so iOS Swift consumers continue to reference `PackRow` / `PackStatus.locked` etc unchanged). **New `domain/symbol/DefaultSymbolPackCatalog.kt`** — production impl injecting `LocalSymbolPackDataSource` + `EntitlementResolver`. Owns the entire status fold (Locked / NotDownloaded / UpdateAvailable / Downloaded), stable ordering (FREE first, then PRO; alpha-by-id within tier), and total-bytes math. Snapshots `isPro()` once per `listInventory()` call so every row in a single call sees a coherent gate view. **`PackManagementViewModel` refactor** — drops `LocalSymbolPackDataSource` + `EntitlementResolver` ctor params; replaced with a single `SymbolPackCatalog`. `load()` and `refresh()` become thin wrappers around `catalog.listInventory()`. The `isProEntitled` field on `PackManagementState` was found to be dead state (the screen never read it; verified by grep) and was deleted. The ViewModel is now Pro-policy-agnostic — it forwards user intent + renders resolved state, and a future Pro-policy refinement (per-pack entitlement, trial users get partial Pro, grace-period extension) lands in the catalog impl with zero ViewModel change. **Sibling-not-extension rationale**: `SymbolCatalog` is consumed on the Compose / SwiftUI render hot path (`get(id)` is microsecond-scale synchronous), inventory is per-screen-load suspending. Different cadences, different consumer sets — bloating `SymbolCatalog` would invite the render hot path to accidentally touch pack-level metadata. **DI updates**: `RepositoryModule` registers `single<SymbolPackCatalog> { DefaultSymbolPackCatalog(...) }` right after the existing `CompositeSymbolCatalog` registration; `ViewModelModule` `PackManagementViewModel` factory pivots from `localSymbolPackDataSource = get(), entitlementResolver = get()` to `symbolPackCatalog = get()`. **Test reorganization**: gate-fold tests moved from `PackManagementViewModelTest` to a new `DefaultSymbolPackCatalogTest` (16 cases against a real SQLDelight in-memory driver + the existing `EntitlementResolver` test fakes — empty mirror / 4 status branches × FREE pack / 4 status branches × PRO pack including the "Pro pack with payload on disk but lost entitlement reads as Locked not Downloaded" defense-in-depth case / ordering / total-bytes counts only downloaded / Locked excluded from totals / metadata round-trip / **per-call gate snapshot pinned via cachedActiveSubscription call counter (`gate snapshot is taken exactly once per listInventory call`) + gate-flip companion test for second-call snapshot re-evaluation** (review HIGH+MEDIUM-1 fixes; replaces the original weak gate-snapshot test that used a static resolver) / **Pro pack payload persisting on disk after entitlement lapse still contributes to `totalDownloadedBytes`** (review HIGH fix anchoring the documented "physical presence not accessibility" semantics)). `PackManagementViewModelTest` narrows to state-machine concerns (11 cases — load happy path / load error / load empty / refresh dispatches sync / refresh without dispatch / manifest fetch failure / manifest persist failure / in-flight guard / unexpected exception / sync-then-re-read-failure / clear-error) using a `FakeSymbolPackCatalog` that returns canned `PackInventory`. Net commonTest +13 (1435 → 1448). Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **ADR-016 updates**: §41.5.3 reference table flips `PackManagementViewModel` from ⚠ to ✅ (gate-delegated) and gains a new `DefaultSymbolPackCatalog` ✅ Compliant gate-site row; §41.5.5 third bullet rewritten from "one such site exists" to "one such site existed at Phase 41.5 documentation time and was retired in §41.5.6"; new §41.5.6 "Update: closing the `PackManagementViewModel` deviation" subsection records the cleanup as the worked example. JA summary mirror updated in parallel. **CLAUDE.md `## Tech Debt Backlog` "ADR-016 §41.5 deviations" subsection deleted** — the only entry under it is now closed. **Pre-push invariants**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest`, `:shared:koverVerify`, `verifyI18nKeys` (429 keys, unchanged — slice is data-layer + DI + test reorganization, no UI surface). iOS app builds via `xcodebuild ... build`. **Forward-compat**: when Phase 41.6+ lands the ADR-016 §5.2 "Free up storage" affordance or the per-pack download dispatch, those operations either extend `SymbolPackCatalog` or graduate to a new `PackDownloadCoordinator` per the §41.5.3 forward-looking entry. Either way, the gate decision stays in domain layer; the ViewModel forwards user intent + renders resolved state. The §41.5.4 checklist applies unchanged. With this slice the codebase has zero open §41.5.1 deviations.
- **Phase 41.5**: F1 `EntitlementResolver` consumer pattern documentation — fifth and final slice of Phase 41, **closes Phase 41 entirely**. Documentation-only: ADR-016 §41.5 amendment (EN ~80 lines + JA summary subsection ~30 lines) lifting the gate-site-vs-call-site convention out of "implicit precedent" and into "load-bearing rule for any future Pro feature". No code change. No test delta (1435 unchanged). No i18n delta (429 unchanged). **The rule** (§41.5.1): any feature gating behavior on Pro entitlement MUST inject `EntitlementResolver` at the **gate site** — the domain-layer surface (catalog / use case / repository / coordinator) where the Free vs. Pro decision is actually made — and the **call site** (UI / ViewModel) MUST NOT inject it or call `isPro()` directly. Three load-bearing reasons: (1) one `isPro()` call per feature (Pro-policy changes — grace period extension, trial users get partial Pro, a la carte unlocks bypassing `isPro()` for one symbol — happen in one file per feature, not scattered across N call sites); (2) UI layer becomes Pro-policy-agnostic (`ChartEditorScreen` doesn't know what "Pro" means; it just renders whatever `SymbolCatalog.get(id)` returned — null → "?", non-null → draw — making UI tests + screenshot tests + Maestro flows resilient to entitlement-policy changes); (3) test isolation (ViewModel + UI tests use a `FakeSymbolCatalog` returning either the bundled symbol or null without ever touching `EntitlementResolver` / `SubscriptionRepository` / `AuthRepository`). The flip side: call sites MAY know whether something is gated (a `null` return from `SymbolCatalog.get(id)` carries that signal, lock badge in palette reads `SymbolCatalog.listLockedPro(category)`) but MUST NOT know **why** (which subscription state, which `expiresAt`, which billing-retry stage — that stays inside the gate). **Pro-affording UX exception** (§41.5.2, **forward-looking — no current consumer**): a future call site whose primary job is **reflecting** Pro state to the user (Settings "Pro since $date" row, "Manage subscription" screen, paywall "you are already Pro" branch) MAY read `isPro()` directly without violating §41.5.1. Discriminator: "show or hide a feature" / "enable or disable an action" / "render lock badge or full symbol" is **gating** and goes through gate site; "tell user current Pro state" / "decide post-purchase routing" is **affording** and UI may read `isPro()` directly. As of Phase 41.5 NO consumer matches this exception — the carve-out exists so future affording surfaces have a documented place to land without watering down the gate-site rule. `PackManagementViewModel` does NOT qualify (its direct injection drives `PackStatus.Locked` which gates the per-row download action — that's gating, not affording). **Reference table of actual current consumers** (§41.5.3) — honestly catalogued after a code-review pass corrected initial claims: `CompositeSymbolCatalog` (Domain, gate site — injects resolver, `get/listByCategory/all` use `isPro()` to gate; `listLockedPro()` uses `isPro()` to early-return empty when user IS Pro and is an observability surface for the UI to render lock badges, NOT a gating call) ✅; `ChartEditorViewModel` (UI call site, gate-delegated — reads `symbolCatalog.listLockedPro(category)` for palette badges, does NOT inject resolver, does NOT call `isPro()` directly) ✅; `PackManagementViewModel` (UI call site — injects `EntitlementResolver` directly at line 106, calls `isPro()` in `readSnapshot()` at line 202 to derive `PackStatus.Locked`) ⚠ **non-compliant deviation** (logged under new Tech Debt Backlog subsection "ADR-016 §41.5 deviations"; recommended cleanup is to extend `SymbolCatalog` (or introduce sibling `SymbolPackCatalog`) with a gated `PackRow.{Available, NeedsUpdate, Downloaded, Locked}` sealed method and refactor `PackManagementViewModel` to delegate); `PaywallViewModel` (UI, NOT a consumer — does NOT inject `EntitlementResolver`, does NOT call `isPro()`, post-purchase routing reads `RestoreResult.Success.proActive` and `PurchaseResult.Success` from `RevenueCatService`). Future consumers: Phase 35.2 polar editing → `PolarEditorAvailability` tri-state `Free | Pro | LockedPro`; post-v1 PR approval → `PullRequestApprovalPolicy` consulted by `MergePullRequestUseCase`; Pack management free-up-storage / per-pack download (Phase 41.5+) → `PackDownloadCoordinator` exposing sealed `Available | Locked` state. **Checklist for new Pro features** (§41.5.4) — 7 steps: (1) identify gate site (push out of ViewModel/Composable into domain layer); (2) inject `EntitlementResolver` at gate site only via Koin constructor injection; (3) expose Pro-policy-agnostic interface (nullable / sealed `Available | Locked` / paywall-trigger Channel — MUST NOT leak `Boolean isPro` to consumers); (4) test gate-site branches at gate-site test (Pro / non-Pro / unauthenticated / feature-specific edge cases — `CompositeSymbolCatalogTest` Pro-gate cases as precedent); (5) test call-site reaction with Fake gate; (6) surface paywall trigger via Channel per Phase 41.3b `_paywallRequests: Channel<Unit>(BUFFERED)` precedent in `ChartEditorViewModel`, NOT via `isPro()` check at call site; (7) document new gate site in §41.5.3 follow-up amendment to ADR-016 OR in feature's own ADR. **Out of scope** (§41.5.5): deciding which existing features become Pro (product / monetization-strategist deliberation per-feature in own ADR or PRD); refining `EntitlementResolver` API (separate amendment if richer surface needed for Pro Lite / Pro Plus / partial-trial); migration discipline for "shipped Pro-gating in wrong layer" (one such site exists as of Phase 41.5 — `PackManagementViewModel` per §41.5.3 + Tech Debt Backlog "ADR-016 §41.5 deviations"; behavior is correct, only the layer is wrong; address via the §41.5.3 cleanup recommendation; future additional violations addressed inline, no general-purpose migration plan needed). **Closes Phase 41 wave**: Phase 41.0 (ADR-016) → 41.1.0–41.1.5 (data spine + migration 020/021/022 + Edge Function `request-pack-download`, shipped as commits `5ce2eb0` → `73a5e0d`) → 41.2a (subscription mirror + `EntitlementResolver`) → 41.2b (pack sync + `LocalSymbolPackDataSource` + `SymbolPackSyncManager`) → 41.2c (`CompositeSymbolCatalog` composing bundled + downloaded + Pro gate) → 41.3a (`RevenueCatService` infrastructure + `PaywallViewModel` infra, commit `4ad3e22`) → 41.3b (Compose + SwiftUI `PaywallScreen` + Settings entry + ChartEditor `_paywallRequests` channel seam, commits `27d9847`+`36bb093` refactor) → 41.4 (`SymbolCatalog.listLockedPro`, `PackManagementViewModel` + `PackManagementScreen`, ChartEditor lock badge cell renderer, "Manage Symbol Packs" Settings entry, +22 i18n keys, +19 commonTest, commit `1eb9fb8`) → 41.5 (this slice, doc-only). With this slice the entire ADR-016 F1 Pro subscription + dynamic symbols loop is end-to-end functional and the consumer pattern for future Pro features is locked in. **Pre-push invariants** (doc-only — no `make ci-local` invariants triggered, but verified for completeness): `:shared:ktlintCheck` ✅, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64` ✅, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1435 tests, unchanged from 41.4 baseline) ✅, `:shared:koverVerify` ✅, `verifyI18nKeys` (429 keys, unchanged) ✅. **Forward-compat anchors**: §41.5.3 reference table is the integration seam any future Pro-feature ADR amendment extends; the §41.5.4 checklist is the operational template for a new Pro feature landing PR. Phase 39 closed-beta launch readiness is the natural next slice now that the F1 loop is closed (HARD-GATE: TestFlight artifact upload, Play VERSION_CODE bump, tester invites — all user-side actions per Phase 39.0 prep entry). **Pre-Phase-40 polish item — CLAUDE.md slimming**: with Phase 41 closed, the "Completed" section will hold Phase 38.x + 39.x + 41.x as the active beta wave; promotion to [docs/en/phase/completed-archive.md](../docs/en/phase/completed-archive.md) per the `### Archive policy` cadence happens at Phase 40 GA's major-release commit, not now.

- **Phase 41.2c**: F1 `CompositeSymbolCatalog` — third and final code slice of Phase 41.2 wave (per ADR-016 §4.1), composes the bundled compile-time `DefaultSymbolCatalog` (offline fallback) with the downloaded packs from 41.2b's `LocalSymbolPackDataSource`, gated by 41.2a's `EntitlementResolver`. **Closes Phase 41.2.** **`domain/symbol/CompositeSymbolCatalog.kt`** implements the existing `SymbolCatalog` interface with the synchronous `get(id)` / `listByCategory(category)` / `all()` contract that Compose & SwiftUI render hot paths consume via `koinInject()`. **Lookup order**: downloaded packs first → if entry's parent pack is `tier='pro'` and `entitlementResolver.isPro()` returns false, return null (renderer paints "?"); else return downloaded → else fall through to bundled. **Memory snapshot pattern (decode-on-refresh + cache)**: the agent-team trilemma decision rejected (a) decode-on-every-`get` (ms-scale JSON parse vs µs-scale render — would dwarf draw cost on a 16×16 grid at 60Hz = ~256 calls/frame) in favor of (b) decode once per `refresh()` + cache the result in a `MutableStateFlow<DownloadedSnapshot>`. **`DownloadedSnapshot`** immutable data class: `byId: Map<String, DownloadedEntry>` for `get` hot path, `byCategory: Map<SymbolCategory, List<DownloadedEntry>>` for category filter, `allEntries: List<DownloadedEntry>` for `all`. `EMPTY` companion singleton for cold-launch / empty-cache fast path. `DownloadedSnapshot.from(entries)` static builder pre-sorts by id within category. **`DownloadedEntry`** carries `(SymbolDefinition, SymbolPackTier)` — pack-level tier from the metadata mirror is authoritative for v1; per-symbol tier in the wire format is forward-compat (ADR-016 §3.4) and explicitly NOT consulted on the gate. Test `pack-level tier overrides per-symbol tier from wire format` pins this — a FREE pack with payload entries mistakenly tagged PRO MUST still render for non-Pro users. **Lifecycle**: constructor schedules a single `applicationScope.launch { try { refresh() } catch (CancellationException) { throw } catch (Exception) { println(...) } }` warm-up on the existing `applicationScopeQualifier`-scoped CoroutineScope; until warm-up completes the snapshot is `EMPTY` and every read falls through to bundled — that's the "sync still in flight" UX from ADR-016 §8 #3. **`refresh()`** suspending + `Mutex.withLock`-serialized so a second concurrent caller waits rather than tramples (test `concurrent refresh callers leave a coherent snapshot` smoke-verifies). **Cross-pack id collision policy**: packs sorted with `compareBy({ it.updatedAt }, { it.id })` then iterated so newer-`updatedAt`-wins (last write to the LinkedHashMap wins) with deterministic tie-break on pack id when timestamps coincide (plausible if server batch-updates metadata in one transaction; without the secondary sort, the winner depended on SQLite scan order — non-deterministic across cold/warm cache). Test `cross-pack id collision with equal updatedAt tie-breaks deterministically on pack id` pins this. **Per-pack version**: within a single pack, consumes the newest cached version via 41.2b's `LocalSymbolPackDataSource.getLatestPayload(packId)` (already pack-internal latest-wins via `ORDER BY version DESC LIMIT 1`). Test `version-bump round trip surfaces newest version through the catalog` exercises a v1 → v2 bump via the catalog API. **Defense-in-depth payload validation**: `decodePayload()` checks (a) embedded `packId` matches the row's pack id, (b) embedded `version` matches the row's version column (Phase 41.2b SymbolPackSyncManager already surfaces a Failure.Parse on mismatch but the client is the last line of defense if that discipline ever lapses), (c) `decoded.schemaVersion <= SymbolPackPayload.CURRENT_SCHEMA_VERSION` — newer schema version rejected outright rather than letting `Json { ignoreUnknownKeys = true }` silently produce a partially-populated `SymbolDefinition` by ignoring removed/changed fields. ADR-016 §3.4 mandates the server splits to a new pack id on breaking schema changes, but this client-side guard catches the regression. Tests `payload with mismatched packId is rejected` / `payload with mismatched version is rejected` / `payload with higher schemaVersion than client supports is rejected`. **Broken payloads degrade gracefully**: JSON parse fail (`SerializationException`) / invariant violation (`SymbolPackPayload.init`'s `require(version > 0)` etc., raised as `IllegalArgumentException`) / unknown SymbolCategory wire value (mapper raises `IllegalStateException` via `error()`) all silently skip the offending entry or pack while keeping the rest of the catalog intact. Tests `broken payload skips that pack but keeps the rest` / `payload entry with unknown category is dropped but rest of pack survives`. The bundled catalog still renders for its symbols — partial decode failure must not blank the entire palette. **Behavioral divergence between `get()` and `listByCategory` / `all` for Pro-shadows-bundled-free**: when a Pro downloaded entry shadows a bundled FREE entry of the same id and the user is not Pro, `get()` returns null (render-time lookup must NOT silently substitute a different free symbol for the requested Pro one) while `listByCategory` / `all` keep the bundled free entry visible (the Pro override is dropped — the user sees what they CAN see). Test `listByCategory keeps bundled free entry when pro pack supplies same id and user is not pro` pins the divergence; the comment block at the call site names the rationale. **`isPro()` snapshot per call**: `get()` / `listByCategory` / `all` each read `entitlementResolver.isPro()` once at the top into `val isUserPro = ...` so the within-call view stays coherent under any mid-call subscription state change. **Koin DI dedup + swap**: previous codebase had two `single<SymbolCatalog>` registrations (`di/SymbolModule.kt:14` and `di/RepositoryModule.kt:273` — same key, Koin's last-wins behavior left the RepositoryModule registration as the effective one but the duplicate was a sleeping bug). This slice deletes the SymbolModule registration (file kept as empty `module { }` placeholder so future symbol-only DI additions have a natural home) and replaces the RepositoryModule registration with `single<SymbolCatalog> { CompositeSymbolCatalog(bundled = DefaultSymbolCatalog.INSTANCE, localSymbolPackDataSource = get(), entitlementResolver = get(), json = get(), applicationScope = get<CoroutineScope>(applicationScopeQualifier)) }`. The `SymbolCatalog` consumer surface (Compose `ChartEditorScreen` / `ChartDiffScreen` / `ChartViewerScreen` / `ChartThumbnail` / `PolarDrawing`, ViewModel `ChartEditorViewModel` / `SymbolGalleryViewModel`, iOS `KoinHelper.getSymbolCatalog()`) needs zero changes — the interface stays identical, the production binding swaps at the DI site. **No external sync trigger in 41.2c**: Phase 41.3 will wire the post-purchase RevenueCat callback + foreground-resume hook to call `CompositeSymbolCatalog.refresh()` after Phase 41.2b's `SymbolPackSyncManager.sync()` lands new payloads. Until then `refresh()` runs only at process boot via the init warm-up. The `snapshot: StateFlow<DownloadedSnapshot>` accessor is exposed (private mutable + asStateFlow public) so Phase 41.4's pack-management screen can `collect { repaint }` after the user toggles a pack, but Phase 41.2c has no observer. **Tests (+25 commonTest, 1370 → 1395)**: `CompositeSymbolCatalogTest` — empty store falls through to bundled, downloaded overrides bundled with same id, Pro symbol returns null on entitlement miss, Pro symbol resolves on entitlement, free pack returns regardless, Pro miss does NOT fall back to bundled even when bundled has same id (defense-in-depth), cross-pack id collision newer-updatedAt wins, equal-updatedAt tie-breaks deterministically on pack id, version-bump round trip via catalog API, listByCategory merges bundled+downloaded with stable id ordering, listByCategory drops Pro entries when not entitled, listByCategory keeps bundled free entry when Pro shadow + non-Pro user, listByCategory empty for empty category, `all` combines bundled+downloaded ordered by category-then-id, `all` drops Pro when not entitled, broken payload skips pack but keeps rest, payload mismatched packId rejected, payload mismatched version rejected, payload higher schemaVersion rejected, payload entry with unknown category dropped but rest survives, refresh reflects newly-seeded packs, pack-level tier overrides per-symbol tier (forward-compat invariant), `DownloadedSnapshot.from(emptyList())` returns EMPTY singleton, `DownloadedSnapshot.from` sorts byCategory by id, concurrent refresh callers leave coherent snapshot. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). Test fakes: `StaticBundledCatalog` (immutable bundled `SymbolCatalog` with id/category lookup), `StubSubscriptionRepository` (cachedFor/sub keyed surface satisfying the full `SubscriptionRepository` interface). `LocalSymbolPackDataSource` exercised via real SQLDelight in-memory driver (`createTestDriver`) — real schema migration validation of the 41.2b `7.sqm` is a side benefit. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1395 tests, +25 from 1370 baseline — comfortably within ADR-016 §6 41.2 catalog-portion budget of "+25"), `:shared:koverVerify`, `verifyI18nKeys` (391 keys, unchanged — slice is data + DI layer, no UI surface). iOS app builds via `xcodebuild -project iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅. **Code review iterations**: first pass surfaced 0 CRITICAL / 3 HIGH / 4 MEDIUM / 4 LOW — all 11 fixed pre-commit. **HIGH-1** (init warm-up swallowed exceptions silently — `applicationScope.launch { refresh() }` on a `SupervisorJob` scope drops uncaught exceptions to the platform's default handler with no observability path; a transient SQLDelight failure or unexpected parse exception would silently leave the snapshot empty and every chart cell would fall through to bundled forever) fixed by wrapping the launch body in try/catch with `CancellationException` rethrow + `println` log of the exception (TODO comment names Phase 41.4 promotion to a `refreshError: StateFlow` for the pack-management UI). **HIGH-2** (`decodePayload` catch-comment misleading + `IllegalArgumentException` catch lumped two distinct failure sources) fixed by splitting into separate `SerializationException` and `IllegalArgumentException` catches with explicit comments naming each source (kotlinx.serialization parse failure vs `SymbolPackPayload.init`'s `require()` failure). **HIGH-3** (no schemaVersion forward-compat guard — `decodePayload` validated `packId` and `version` but not `schemaVersion`; a server-side regression that ships a v2-schema payload with the v1-schema id would silently produce partially-populated `SymbolDefinition` entries via `Json { ignoreUnknownKeys = true }` ignoring removed fields) fixed by adding `if (decoded.schemaVersion > SymbolPackPayload.CURRENT_SCHEMA_VERSION) return null`. **MEDIUM-1** (cross-pack `updatedAt` tie-break non-deterministic — `sortedBy { it.updatedAt }` does NOT guarantee a stable winner when two packs share an `updatedAt` and the source `getAllPacks()` SQLite scan has no `ORDER BY` clause) fixed via `compareBy({ it.updatedAt }, { it.id })` + new test exercising the tie-break with two packs sharing exact-equal timestamps. **MEDIUM-2** (`listByCategory` / `get` divergence for Pro-shadows-bundled-free undocumented + untested) fixed by inline comment block + new test pinning the divergent behavior. **MEDIUM-3** (`DownloadedSnapshot.from` `associateBy` silently drops duplicate ids) fixed by KDoc note explicitly documenting the caller-pre-deduplicates contract; no `require()` guard added (defensive overreach for an internal-visibility helper with one production caller). **MEDIUM-4** (`get()` did not snapshot `isPro()` while `listByCategory` / `all` did — inconsistent shape across the 3 hot-path methods) fixed by adding `val isUserPro = entitlementResolver.isPro()` at the top of `get()` matching the other two. **LOW-1** (`val isPro` shadows the `EntitlementResolver.isPro()` method name) fixed by renaming the local to `isUserPro` in all three methods. **LOW-2** (KDoc "newer wins" prose ambiguous given ascending `sortedBy` + LinkedHashMap last-wins semantics) fixed by reflowing the class-level KDoc to spell out "iterated oldest-`updatedAt`-first so a newer pack's entry overwrites an older one in the accumulation map" + tie-break addendum. **LOW-3** (`DownloadedSnapshot.from(non-empty)` produces distinct instances for semantically-equal inputs) acknowledged as no-fix-required (`data class equals` works correctly). **LOW-4** (no concurrent `refresh()` test) fixed by `concurrent refresh callers leave a coherent snapshot` smoke test using `coroutineScope { async { } }`.
