Second-pass review APPROVED with 1 new LOW (dead `CancellationException` catch in non-suspending `decodePayload` — `json.decodeFromString` is purely synchronous so the catch is unreachable and adds noise) addressed by removing the dead catch. **Forward-compat anchors for Phase 41.3**: `CompositeSymbolCatalog.refresh()` is the integration seam — Phase 41.3's foreground-resume hook + RevenueCat post-purchase callback both call it after `SymbolPackSyncManager.sync()` lands new payloads. The `snapshot: StateFlow<DownloadedSnapshot>` accessor is the integration seam for Phase 41.4's pack-management screen. The `applicationScope.launch { try { refresh() } catch (...) { println } }` warm-up's TODO comment names the future `refreshError: StateFlow` for the pack-management UI's "catalog unavailable" surface. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-016 §4.1**: external sync trigger / foreground hook / post-purchase RevenueCat callback all in 41.3; paywall + pack-management UI in 41.4; SwiftUI side requires no change because iOS consumes via `KoinHelper.getSymbolCatalog()` returning the same `SymbolCatalog` interface. **Closes Phase 41.2**: with this slice the entire ADR-016 catalog composition layer — subscription mirror + EntitlementResolver (41.2a) → catalog metadata + downloaded payload sync (41.2b) → composite catalog with Pro gate + bundled fallback (41.2c) — is end-to-end functional.

- **Phase 41.2b**: F1 client-side symbol-pack sync layer (per ADR-016 §3.3 + §4.3) — second code slice of Phase 41.2 wave, consumes the already-shipped `request-pack-download` Edge Function (41.1.5) and the 41.2a subscription mirror. **No UI delta** — purely data + sync infrastructure that 41.2c will compose into the `CompositeSymbolCatalog`. **Migration `7.sqm` extension**: 2 new tables added alongside the 41.2a `SubscriptionEntity` (single-migration-per-wave design from 41.2a). `SymbolPackEntity` (catalog metadata mirror — id PK + tier/version/displayName/description/payloadPath/payloadSize/symbolCount/signedUntil/createdAt/updatedAt; covers EVERY pack the manifest fetch surfaces, including non-downloaded ones for paywall preview UI). `DownloadedPackPayloadEntity` ((pack_id, version) composite PK + payload_json TEXT + downloaded_at; only rows for packs the user has materialized locally; ~50 KB JSON per row × ~30 packs ≈ 1.5 MB total per ADR §8 #2). **`SymbolPack.sq` + `DownloadedPackPayload.sq`**: queries split per concern — pack metadata table has `getById` / `getAll` / `upsert` / `deleteById` / `clearAll`; payload table has `getLatestByPackId` (ORDER BY version DESC LIMIT 1 hot path for CompositeSymbolCatalog) / `getAll` / `existsForVersion` / `upsert` / `deleteByPackIdAndVersion` / `deleteOlderVersionsForPack` (HIGH-1 fix from code review — surgical SQL DELETE replacing an in-Kotlin filter loop that loaded every payload into memory) / `deleteAllForPack` / `clearAll`. **Mapper extension** at `data/mapper/SymbolPackMapper.kt`: `SymbolPackEntity.toDomain()` (timestamps via `Instant.parse`, `version`/`payloadSize`/`symbolCount` Long↔Int conversions, `tier` via `String.toSymbolPackTier()`); exhaustive `toDbString()` + `toSymbolPackTier()` with hard `error()` on unknown values (defensive against future migration adding a 3rd tier — silent fall-through to FREE/PRO would silently grant or revoke Pro symbols); inline exhaustiveness anchor comment naming the dual-format contract (db-string + JSON `@SerialName` kept independently in sync; new enum members fail compile-time exhaustiveness without matching `when` branch). **`LocalSymbolPackDataSource`**: dual-surface class on purpose — catalog metadata (`upsertPack` / `getPackById` / `getAllPacks` / `replaceManifest` / `clearAllPacks`) AND downloaded payload (`getLatestPayload` / `getAllPayloads` / `hasPayloadForVersion` / `upsertPayload` / `deletePayloadsForPack` / `clearAllPayloads` / `clearAll`). Single class because the sync's "delete old version after committing new" path needs both tables under coordinated writes. **`replaceManifest`** runs in a single transaction: upsert every supplied pack, delete every cached pack id NOT in the supplied set; deliberately does NOT cascade into the payload table — a server-side pack archive should not silently delete a chart cell's symbol the user authored against the archived pack (KDoc invariant). **`upsertPayload`** atomic version-bump: writes new payload row, then `deleteOlderVersionsForPack(packId, version)` drops strictly-older rows in one round trip. New-then-delete-older ordering keeps `getLatestPayload`'s `ORDER BY version DESC LIMIT 1` correctly observable through any transient overlap. New `DownloadedPackPayload` value type + `DownloadedPackPayloadEntity.toDownloadedPayload()` extension exposed to callers (avoids leaking SQLDelight-generated entity types from the local layer). **`SymbolPackRemoteOperations` interface** at `data/remote/RemoteSymbolPackDataSource.kt`: 2 methods `fetchManifest(): List<SymbolPack>` (open-read RLS, postgrest `select`) + `requestDownload(packId): SymbolPackDownloadResult`. Interface extracted so `SymbolPackSyncManager` tests inject an in-memory fake without standing up Supabase — same precedent as `SubscriptionRemoteOperations` (41.2a) and `PullRequestMergeOperations` (38.4). **`SymbolPackDownloadResult`** sealed type at `data/remote/SymbolPackDownloadResult.kt`: `Success(payload, version)` or 7 distinct `Failure` subtypes (`Unauthenticated` / `ProEntitlementRequired(packId)` / `PackNotFound(packId)` / `RateLimited(retryAfterSeconds)` / `Network(cause)` / `Parse(cause)` / `Unknown(statusCode, body?)`). Each maps to a different orchestrator dispatch path per ADR §4.3 — collapsing into a generic `Failure` would force the orchestrator to re-parse the body. **`RemoteSymbolPackDataSource`** Supabase impl: uses `supabaseClient.functions.invoke("request-pack-download")` with the supabase-kt `Functions` plugin (newly installed in `SupabaseModule`); auto-attaches the user JWT matching the Edge Function's `verify_jwt: true` deploy flag; explicit status-code switch maps 401/403/404/429 to typed Failure subtypes (no exceptions leak modulo `CancellationException`). Signed-URL fetch via a separately-injected Ktor `HttpClient` (NOT supabase-kt's `@SupabaseInternal` httpClient — would force `@OptIn(SupabaseInternal::class)` annotations on common code; HIGH-2 fix from code review pivoted from `supabaseClient.httpClient.httpClient` to `expect/actual fun createSymbolPackHttpClient()` factory with platform-specific actuals). **HIGH-2 mechanics**: Ktor 3.x `HttpClient { }` no-arg form picks the engine via JVM ServiceLoader on Android, but on Kotlin/Native the Darwin engine is NOT discovered automatically — would throw at runtime. New `data/remote/HttpClientFactory.kt` `expect fun createSymbolPackHttpClient(): HttpClient` with androidMain `actual` returning `HttpClient(Android)` and iosMain `actual` returning `HttpClient(Darwin)`. DI uses a named qualifier `symbolPackHttpClientQualifier` (added to `ApplicationScopeModule.kt` alongside the existing `chartImagesStorageQualifier` etc) so the bare `HttpClient` type doesn't conflict with any future `single<HttpClient>` consumer. Koin `.onClose { it?.close() }` lifecycle hook drops the engine-owned thread pool on `stopKoin` cycles (alignment with existing `applicationScopeQualifier` precedent + matters for test-suite Koin teardown). **Defense-in-depth payload version check**: the Edge Function envelope's `current_version` and the payload body's own `version` SHOULD agree, but a server-side bug minting a stale signed URL would mismatch them. Mismatch surfaces as `Failure.Parse` rather than silent data corruption. **MEDIUM-3 fix** for signed-URL response: explicit `403 -> Failure.ProEntitlementRequired(packId)` branch (was bucketed as `Unknown`) so the orchestrator's "skip silently, retry on next sync cycle" path applies — a fresh `request-pack-download` call mints a new URL, matching the TTL-elapsed-mid-fetch recovery semantics ADR §4.3 names. **`SymbolPackSyncManager`** at `data/sync/SymbolPackSyncManager.kt`: orchestrates the cycle per ADR §4.3 — fetch manifest → `replaceManifest` → per-pack diff (cached payload version vs manifest version) → if missing/stale call `requestDownload` → write through. **`Mutex.tryLock()`** rather than `withLock`: a sync already in flight returns `SyncCycleResult.Skipped("sync_already_in_flight")` immediately; chasing the tail of a prior cycle adds latency without meaningful benefit per ADR §4.3 background-only contract. **`SyncState` 4-state surface**: `Idle` (clean OR soft-skip-only completion) / `InProgress` / `Failed(cause)` (manifest stage hard fail — no per-pack downloads ran) / `PartiallyFailed` (manifest landed but ≥1 hard pack error: Network / Parse / Unknown / Failed). MEDIUM-1 fix from code review: `PartiallyFailed` flips terminal state when any outcome `isHardFailure()` (exhaustive `when` over `PackSyncOutcome` variants — soft skips ProEntitlement / PackNotFound / RateLimited / Unauthenticated / VersionRegression do NOT flip the state; they're normal sync semantics that next cycle retries). **`PackSyncOutcome`** 11-variant sealed type covers every per-pack terminal state; `PackSyncOutcome.from(packId, failure)` exhaustive mapping from `SymbolPackDownloadResult.Failure`. **`VersionRegression` guard**: server reports strictly-LOWER version than locally cached — never legitimate per ADR §4.3, surfaces as `VersionRegression(cachedVersion, serverVersion)` outcome and KEEPS the higher-version cached payload (test anchor: `version regression keeps higher local payload and surfaces VersionRegression outcome`). **DI wiring** in `RepositoryModule` / `SyncModule` / `SupabaseModule`: `Functions` plugin install + `RemoteSymbolPackDataSource` registration + interface alias for fake injection + `SymbolPackSyncManager` always-registered (graceful `SyncCycleResult.Skipped("remote_unavailable")` return when `remote = null` in local-only mode); 41.3 wires the foreground-hook + post-purchase callers later. **New `supabase-functions-kt` dependency** added to `libs.versions.toml` + `shared/build.gradle.kts` `commonMain.dependencies`. **Tests (+34 commonTest, 1336 → 1370)**: `SymbolPackMapperTest` gains 2 cases (db-string round trip both tiers + unknown tier raises with echoed value); `LocalSymbolPackDataSourceTest` (12 cases — upsertPack persists / getAllPacks ordered / replaceManifest upserts new + drops missing / replaceManifest empty clears / replaceManifest preserves payloads when metadata dropped (downloaded-survives-archive invariant) / getLatestPayload null when missing / upsertPayload writes / upsertPayload version-bump deletes older versions atomically / upsertPayload does not cross-pollute other packs / hasPayloadForVersion exact / deletePayloadsForPack scope / clearAll empties both tables); `SymbolPackSyncManagerTest` (20 cases — sync downloads every missing pack happy path / short-circuits on already-up-to-date / version-bump drops older payload / version regression keeps higher cached payload + 0 download calls / 403 ProEntitlement / 404 PackNotFound / 429 RateLimited carries retryAfter / 401 Unauthenticated / Network failure / Parse failure / Unknown HTTP status / single-pack failure does not stop other packs / manifest fetch failure leaves cache untouched / sync without remote returns Skipped("remote_unavailable") / empty manifest produces no-outcomes Completed / sync replaces manifest dropping disappeared packs / **state ends Idle after clean cycle** / **state ends PartiallyFailed when ≥1 hard error** / **state stays Idle when only soft skips** / **concurrent sync call returns Skipped("sync_already_in_flight") while a prior cycle is suspended** — uses `CompletableDeferred`-gated fake to make the second-caller mutex-skip path deterministic in `runTest`). New helper test fakes: `FakeSymbolPackRemote` (in-memory manifest + per-pack payloads + per-pack failures + `downloadCallCount` for assertion); `GatedManifestRemote` (suspended-on-deferred manifest fetch for the concurrency-contract test). All test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens / commas / apostrophes in backticks). **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1370 tests, +34 from 1336 baseline — above ADR §6 budget of +25 for the entire 41.2 wave; the overshoot is concentrated in the 4 distinct error-shape branches the orchestrator fans out to + the `PartiallyFailed` state-contract tests + the concurrency tryLock-skip test — rigorous coverage of net-new sync infrastructure per CLAUDE.md "Output Quality Standard" "Never trade test coverage for output brevity"), `:shared:koverVerify`, `verifyI18nKeys` (391 keys, unchanged — slice is data-layer only). **Code review iterations**: pass 1 surfaced 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 3 MEDIUM / 2 LOW — all 7 fixed pre-commit. **HIGH-1** (`upsertPayload` full-table scan loaded every pack's payload into memory just to filter) fixed via `deleteOlderVersionsForPack:` SQL query replacing the Kotlin filter loop. **HIGH-2** (`HttpClient { }` no-arg form unsafe on Kotlin/Native — Darwin engine is not service-loader-discovered) fixed via `expect/actual` factory + named qualifier. **MEDIUM-1** (per-pack failures invisible in `SyncState`) fixed via `PartiallyFailed` 4th state + `isHardFailure()` exhaustive switch. **MEDIUM-2** (Tier dual-format fragility) fixed via inline exhaustiveness anchor comment. **MEDIUM-3** (signed-URL 403 silently bucketed as Unknown instead of ProEntitlementRequired) fixed via explicit 403 branch on payload response. **LOW-1** (HttpClient global-type single conflict risk) closed by named qualifier (same fix as HIGH-2). **LOW-2** (missing tryLock skip + PartiallyFailed coverage tests) closed by 4 new tests. Pass 2 surfaced 1 new LOW (Koin `single<HttpClient>` registration missing `onClose` — would leak engine thread pool across `startKoin`/`stopKoin` test cycles) addressed by `.onClose { it?.close() }` lifecycle hook matching `applicationScopeQualifier` precedent. Pass 2 verdict: APPROVED. **Forward-compat anchors for 41.2c**: `SymbolPackSyncManager` is the upstream feeder; 41.2c's `CompositeSymbolCatalog.get(id)` reads the latest payload via `LocalSymbolPackDataSource.getLatestPayload(packId)` and consults the existing 41.2a `EntitlementResolver.isPro()` synchronously to gate Pro-tier symbols. The `DownloadedPackPayload.payloadJson` is the raw `payload.json` body — 41.2c decodes via `Json.decodeFromString<SymbolPackPayload>` and maps each `SymbolPackPayloadEntry` to `SymbolDefinition` via the existing 41.1.3 `SymbolPackMapper.toDefinition()`. `SymbolPackEntity.tier` is the per-pack gate input (read alongside the payload). `replaceManifest`'s preserve-downloaded-payloads invariant ensures a chart cell authored against an archived pack still renders. **Scope cuts unchanged**: 41.2c (CompositeSymbolCatalog + Koin DI swap composing `bundled + downloaded + entitlementResolver`) is the next slice; 41.3 wires the foreground-hook + RevenueCat post-purchase trigger paths to actually invoke `SymbolPackSyncManager.sync()`; 41.4 ships paywall + pack-management UI; 41.5 documents the resolver consumer pattern.

- **Phase 41.2a**: F1 subscription data spine + `EntitlementResolver` (per ADR-016 §3.1 + §4.2) — first code slice of Phase 41.2, closes the prerequisite layer 41.2b/c will compose on top of. Phase 41.1.x (data spine + migration 020/021/022 + Edge Function `request-pack-download`) shipped as commits `5ce2eb0` → `73a5e0d` in parallel with Phase 39 launch readiness; 41.2a now adds the client-side mirror of `subscriptions` (migration 017, prod-applied since pre-Phase-39 alpha prep) so the catalog hot path can answer Pro entitlement synchronously without an Edge Function round-trip. **No UI delta** — purely data + DI infrastructure. **Realtime channel decision (ADR §10 Q2 resolved by agent team this slice)**: deviation from ADR §4.2's "Realtime channel `subscriptions-<userId>`" prescription. Migration 017 lines 154-165 deliberately disable Realtime for `subscriptions` with documented reasoning (an 8th channel against the free-tier 200-concurrent cap, with no UX gain since subscription state is not push-time-sensitive the way collab notifications are). The 41.2 implementer (per ADR §10 Q2's punt to "engineering call at wiring time") chose to honor the migration's design: refresh happens via app-foreground hook + post-purchase RevenueCat callback (Phase 41.3 wires the latter) + cold-launch. Documented as ADR-016 amendment in `Subscription.kt` + `SubscriptionRepository.kt` KDoc. **Migration `7.sqm`** at `shared/src/commonMain/sqldelight/.../db/`: `SubscriptionEntity` table with `is_in_trial` / `auto_renew_status` as INTEGER 0/1 (SQLite has no boolean), timestamps as ISO-8601 TEXT, hot-path `idx_subscription_user_status(user_id, status)` index. Same file holds the 41.2b `DownloadedPackStore` schema by design (single migration covering the whole 41.2 wave keeps `.sqm` count tight). **`Subscription.sq`**: queries cover `getActiveForUser` (status IN ('active','in_grace_period') ORDER BY updated_at DESC LIMIT 1 — picks the most recent active row when alpha-tester later subscribes paid), `getAllForUser`, `observeActiveForUser` Flow, `upsert` INSERT-OR-REPLACE for refresh write-through, `clearForUser` for logout cleanup. **Domain**: `Subscription` data class (12 fields mirroring migration 017; `Serializable` with `@SerialName` so the same class round-trips through Supabase REST `select=*` without an intermediate DTO), `SubscriptionStatus` enum (6 closed values matching the Postgres CHECK), `SubscriptionPlatform` enum (3 closed values: IOS / ANDROID / ALPHA_GRANT). `Subscription.isActiveAt(now)` is a pure function returning Pro-eligibility — `ACTIVE` or `IN_GRACE_PERIOD` AND `(expiresAt == null || expiresAt > now)`. **Critical design contract pinned in KDoc**: `CANCELED` is NOT in the active allow-list because `verify-receipt` only writes `canceled` AFTER the paid period elapses (Apple StoreKit 2 keeps emitting `subscribed` until expiry; Google Play keeps `ACTIVE` with `autoRenewing=false`); during the until-expiry window the row remains `ACTIVE` with `auto_renew_status=false`. If a future Edge Function regression starts synthesizing `canceled` mid-period, `isActiveAt` MUST flip CANCELED into the active allow-list to avoid silently revoking Pro for users still in their paid period — this contract is anchored in `EntitlementResolverTest.canceled sub with future expiresAt returns false - design contract anchor`. **`SubscriptionMapper.kt`**: exhaustive enum mappings with hard `error()` on unknown wire values — defensive against migration 017 adding a new state without client-side handling (loud failure beats silent fall-through to ACTIVE which would silently grant Pro for unknown rows). Boolean ↔ INTEGER (`!= 0L`) and ISO-8601 ↔ Instant adapters per the existing PullRequestMapper precedent. **`LocalSubscriptionDataSource`**: dual-shape reads — `getActiveForUser(userId)` is the standard suspend + dispatcher-confined variant for ViewModels and refresh paths; `getActiveForUserSync(userId)` is the non-suspend variant deliberately bypassing IO dispatcher because the EntitlementResolver hot path (called from `CompositeSymbolCatalog.get(id)` in 41.2c) must answer without a coroutine context switch. The underlying SQLDelight call is a single PK-indexed row lookup (microseconds); paying the dispatcher hop on every catalog access would dwarf the cost. KDoc documents the trade-off + safety argument inline. **`RemoteSubscriptionDataSource` + `SubscriptionRemoteOperations` interface**: read-only on purpose (migration 017's no-INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE policies for the public role mean any client write would 401 — better to have no write surface). Interface alias enables in-memory fake injection for repository tests, matching the `PullRequestMergeOperations` precedent (ADR-014 §5). `eq("user_id", userId)` filter is defense-in-depth; RLS already scopes server-side. **`SubscriptionRepository` interface** + `SubscriptionRepositoryImpl`: exposes `cachedActiveSubscription(userId)` synchronous read for the resolver hot path, `observeActiveSubscription(userId)` Flow for ViewModels, `refresh(userId): Result<Subscription?>` (deliberate `Result<T>` deviation from other repository methods — callers genuinely need to distinguish "verified-no-row" from "could-not-verify" for a future Settings "subscription unverified" affordance; KDoc warns future maintainers not to port the pattern), `clearLocalCache(userId)` for logout. **Staleness-gated empty-rowset eviction** (`STALE_THRESHOLD = 24.hours` companion constant): when remote returns `[]`, evict the local cache only if `cached.lastVerifiedAt < now - STALE_THRESHOLD`. Two failure modes motivate the gate: (1) real removal via auth.users CASCADE deletion (eviction correct after threshold), and (2) transient JWT expiry / RLS scoping artifact where remote legitimately returns `[]` under a stale token — eviction would spuriously drop a still-valid Pro row, causing `isPro()` to flip false until next successful refresh. JWT expiry is typically 1 hour so 24 hours bounds the window where a transient artifact could mask a real removal — acceptable trade-off for a UX gate (server-side `is_pro` RPC + `request-pack-download` Edge Function re-validate authoritatively for every server resource). Note: `verify-receipt` uses upsert (not delete) for refund/expiry transitions — refund flips `status='refunded'` and the row stays in the cache, correctly filtered out of "active" by the `getActiveForUser` query. The eviction path matters only for auth.users CASCADE + transient artifacts. **`EntitlementResolver`** at `domain/symbol/`: 3-line `isPro()` body — `authRepository.getCurrentUserId() ?: return false`, `subscriptionRepository.cachedActiveSubscription(userId) ?: return false`, then `sub.isActiveAt(clock.now())`. Synchronous by design; pure function once the cache is warm. KDoc names the offline default-deny trade-off (cold launch with no cache + no network → false; alternative offline default-allow would let perpetually-offline users hold Pro forever post-expiry — rejected) + the clock-manipulation bypass window (a user who sets their device clock backward keeps `isPro` true past true expiry, but bounded by Realtime-on-reconnect + server-side Edge Function re-validation; only extends access to packs already on disk, no new entitlement-gated downloads possible). **Koin DI** (RepositoryModule.kt): `LocalSubscriptionDataSource` registered alongside other LocalXxxDataSources; `RemoteSubscriptionDataSource` + interface alias `SubscriptionRemoteOperations` registered inside `if (SupabaseConfig.isConfigured)` block; `SubscriptionRepositoryImpl` wired with `getOrNull<SubscriptionRemoteOperations>()` (nullable for local-only mode) + `get<ConnectivityMonitor>().isOnline` (non-null, matches all other coordinator repos); `EntitlementResolver` registered as `single` consuming the repo + `AuthRepository`. **Tests (+57 commonTest, 1279 → 1336)**: `SubscriptionMapperTest` (9 cases — entity round-trip with active/IOS, null expiresAt for alpha-grant perpetual, null originalTransactionId, INTEGER-to-Boolean mapping for both directions, hard-fail on unknown status + platform strings, full enum-to-db round-trip exhaustive); `SubscriptionTest` (11 cases — `isActiveAt` across all 6 statuses with future + past + null + exactly-equal expiresAt edge cases, alpha-grant perpetual semantics, null-expiresAt-does-not-override-non-active-status defensive case, default-ctor-values match migration 017 defaults); `LocalSubscriptionDataSourceTest` (13 cases — exercises real SQLDelight schema validating the 7.sqm migration shape: upsert + getActiveForUser happy path, null on no row, refunded/expired/canceled excluded, multi-row alpha-tester-then-paid scenario picks newest by updated_at, in_grace_period qualifies as active, sync variant mirrors suspend variant + works without runTest, upsert idempotent overwrite by id, getAllForUser ordering, clearForUser scope-isolated to targeted user, observeActiveForUser Flow emits null when refund flips status); `SubscriptionRepositoryImplTest` (12 cases — cachedActiveSubscription delegates to local sync, refresh writes through, **staleness-gated eviction tests**: evicts STALE cached row at 25h-ago verification + PRESERVES recently-verified cached row at 1h-ago + idempotent when cache already empty, refresh failure surfaces as Result.failure leaving cache untouched, refresh with null remote returns cached value as success, refresh while offline is no-op preserving cache + verifies remote was NOT called, alpha-tester-with-paid persists both rows + picks paid as active, clearLocalCache scope-isolated, refunded-row-from-remote keeps cache filtered); `EntitlementResolverTest` (12 cases — unauthenticated returns false, no cached sub returns false, active+future returns true, in_grace_period returns true, expired/canceled/refunded/in_billing_retry all false, expired-via-past-expiresAt-while-status-active returns false, null-expiresAt-with-active returns true (alpha-grant perpetual), repository queried with current authenticated userId, repository sub for different user does not leak across, **CANCELED design contract anchor test** with future expiresAt returns false + explicit comment naming the contract). All test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens / commas / apostrophes in backticks). **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1336 tests, +57 from 1279 baseline — significantly above ADR §6's +25 budget but the budget covered only the catalog/resolver portion; the 41.2a slice had to introduce the entire net-new subscription data layer (mapper + domain + local + remote + repo) since none existed in the codebase per the code-explorer survey, and 57 tests is rigorous coverage of that prerequisite infrastructure: 9 mapper + 11 domain + 13 local + 12 repo + 12 resolver), `:shared:koverVerify`, `verifyI18nKeys` (391 keys, unchanged — slice is data-layer only). iOS app build not run this slice (no iOS code touched; Phase 41.2c will introduce `KoinHelper` accessors when `CompositeSymbolCatalog` lands in DI). **Code review iterations**: first pass 1 HIGH + 3 MEDIUM + 3 LOW. **HIGH** (`CANCELED` enum KDoc said "client treats CANCELED + expiresAt-in-future as still Pro" but `isActiveAt` returned false — documentation/implementation contradiction would mislead a future Edge Function author into writing the wrong behavior at the `verify-receipt` site) fixed by rewriting the `CANCELED` bullet to accurately describe the post-expiry-only contract + adding "Contract assumed of `verify-receipt`" paragraph at `isActiveAt` KDoc with explicit warning about how to flip the gate if the contract changes. **MEDIUM-1** (empty-rowset eviction unsafe against transient JWT expiry / RLS scoping) fixed by introducing `STALE_THRESHOLD = 24.hours` companion + clock-injected staleness gate; reviewer's correction noted that `verify-receipt` uses upsert (not delete) so the cited "refund deleted the row" justification was wrong — real eviction trigger is auth.users CASCADE + transient artifacts, KDoc updated. **MEDIUM-2** (CANCELED semantics — Apple/Google don't emit `canceled` mid-period) closed via the same KDoc fix as HIGH; design contract pinned via the new `EntitlementResolverTest` anchor test. **MEDIUM-3** (`isOnline` was nullable `StateFlow<Boolean>?` while every other coordinator repo declares non-null + DI always passed non-null — dead code path with untested behavior) fixed by changing to non-null and dropping the misleading "nullable for local-only" note. **LOW-1** (`Result<T>` return type deviates from other repository methods) addressed by KDoc note documenting the deliberate deviation + warning future maintainers not to port. **LOW-2** (test gap on CANCELED + future/past expiresAt) fixed by adding both cases. **LOW-3** (DI alias rationale missing) fixed by inline comment naming the `PullRequestMergeOperations` precedent. Second-pass review APPROVED with 0 findings. **Forward-compat anchors for 41.2b/c**: `EntitlementResolver` is the single integration seam — Phase 41.2c's `CompositeSymbolCatalog.get(id)` calls `entitlementResolver.isPro()` synchronously to gate Pro-tier symbol access. The `STALE_THRESHOLD` companion constant exposed as `internal` so 41.2b's `SymbolPackSyncManager` can reference it for sync-cache freshness coordination if needed. The empty-rowset eviction pattern in `SubscriptionRepositoryImpl.refresh` is the precedent 41.2b's pack sync should follow when remote pack manifest returns a smaller set than cached (rare but real on pack revocation). **Scope cuts unchanged from agent-team decision**: no Realtime channel for subscriptions (deviation from ADR §4.2; documented inline + as ADR amendment); foreground-refresh hook wiring deferred to Phase 41.3 alongside the post-purchase RevenueCat callback (Phase 41.2a exposes the API but does not wire the trigger).


## Phase 38.x — Pull-request workflow (closed)

- **Phase 38.4.1**: ChartViewer overflow → "Open pull request" entry (ADR-014 §6 — closes the only beta-blocking UX gap from 38.4 review). The data layer + `OpenPullRequestUseCase` shipped in 38.3, but the only way to actually invoke the open-PR flow before this slice was via ProjectDetail's PatternInfoSection on a forked pattern — most beta users would never discover it. **`ChartViewerViewModel` extension**: state gains `pattern: Pattern?`, `currentBranch: ChartBranch?`, `targetMainBranch: ChartBranch?`, `currentUserId: String?`, plus form-draft fields `openPrTitleDraft` / `openPrDescriptionDraft` / `pendingOpenPrSheet` / `isOpeningPullRequest` / `openPrError`. Derived gate `canOpenPullRequest` (state-class property, not top-level extension, so the Swift bridge reads it as a plain `Bool` getter — same precedent as `PullRequestDetailState.canMerge` / `canClose`). 6 new events: `RequestOpenPullRequest` (opens the form sheet, clears any prior error), `OpenPrTitleChanged(value)` / `OpenPrDescriptionChanged(value)` (form-draft updates), `ConfirmOpenPullRequest` (submit), `DismissOpenPullRequestSheet` (clears drafts + closes sheet — even mid-submission via SwiftUI swipe-to-dismiss), `ClearOpenPrError` (inline error dismiss). New sealed `ChartViewerNavEvent.PullRequestCreated(prId)` plus `Channel<ChartViewerNavEvent>(BUFFERED)` for one-shot post-submit navigation. Ctor gains 4 new nullable deps (`patternRepository` / `chartBranchRepository` / `authRepository` / `openPullRequest`) so existing test call-sites compile unchanged; production wiring through Koin uses `getOrNull()` so the gate gracefully degrades to closed in offline-only / mis-wired setups. **Branch resolution**: new `resolveOpenPrContext` private suspend fn fires from inside the chart-collect block; reads pattern + source branches + upstream's main branch with explicit try/catch + CancellationException rethrow per the Phase 36.3 / 37.x precedent. `lastResolvedRevisionId` local outside the collect block de-dups Realtime self-echoes that don't change the tip — same shape as `ProjectDetailViewModel.observeParentAttribution`'s Phase 36.5 `distinctUntilChanged` pattern. `resolveCurrentBranch` prefers an exact `tipRevisionId == chart.revisionId` match against the source pattern's branch list, falls back to the `"main"` branch by name when no exact match (the fallback keeps any "current branch" rendering helpful during cache lag). **Critical correctness fix from code review (MEDIUM-1)**: the `canOpenPullRequest` gate ALSO requires `branch.tipRevisionId == chart.revisionId` so the "main" fallback doesn't silently submit a PR with a (sourceBranchId, sourceTipRevisionId) pair that the merge RPC would immediately reject with "Source tip drifted" (which has no recovery path except closing and re-opening the PR once the cache catches up). Without the gate's exact-match check, a user on a feature branch with a "main" fallback would see the entry enabled and produce an immediately-unmergeable PR. **`openPullRequestInternal`**: gate snapshot at top + early-return if `isOpeningPullRequest`; resolves all required fields via `requireNotNull(...)` carrying explanatory messages naming the gate as the contract (HIGH fix from code review — `!!` violates project Kotlin coding-style rule); fallback when `openPullRequest` dep is null surfaces a hardcoded English `openPrError` consistent with the `PullRequestDetailViewModel.attemptMerge` offline-mode pattern + the Tech Debt Backlog ViewModel-error-localization deferral. Submit dispatches to the use case + on success emits `PullRequestCreated(prId)` and clears form drafts; on failure surfaces inline `openPrError` and keeps the sheet open for retry (deliberately separate from the top-level `errorMessage` field which displaces the chart with a centered Text — wrong UX for a form-submit failure). **Compose `ChartViewerScreen`**: overflow `DropdownMenuItem` "Open pull request" with `Icons.Default.Forum` icon — gated on `state.canOpenPullRequest` so non-fork patterns don't see the entry rather than rendering it disabled (keeps the menu length tight). New private `OpenPullRequestDialog` composable with `OutlinedTextField`s for title (singleLine, required) + description (minLines=3, optional), inline error rendering with `MaterialTheme.colorScheme.error`, confirm button enabled only when `!isSubmitting && titleDraft.isNotBlank()`. New `LaunchedEffect(viewModel)` collects `navEvents` → snackbars `message_pr_opened_successfully` + invokes `onOpenPullRequestNavigate(prId)` callback. testTags per ADR-014 §6 conventions: `openPullRequestMenuItem`, `openPullRequestDialog`, `openPrTitleInput`, `openPrDescriptionInput`, `openPrErrorLabel`, `confirmOpenPullRequestButton`. **NavGraph**: `composable<ChartViewer>` block plumbs `onOpenPullRequestNavigate = { prId -> navController.navigate(PullRequestDetail(prId = prId)) }` — same `PullRequestDetail` route already wired by Phase 38.3. **iOS mirror** at `iosApp/iosApp/Screens/StructuredChartViewerScreen.swift`: extended toolbar `Menu` with "Open pull request" Button (gated on `holder.state.canOpenPullRequest`) + `bubble.left.and.bubble.right` SF Symbol; `.sheet(isPresented: Binding<Bool>)` derived from `pendingOpenPrSheet` flag; new private `OpenPullRequestSheet` SwiftUI view (`NavigationStack` + `Form` with two `Section`s + Cancel/Open `ToolbarItem`s; title field uses `axis: .vertical` with `lineLimit(3...8)` for the description; confirm gated on `.disabled(isSubmitting || titleDraft.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).isEmpty)` matching Compose's `isNotBlank()` semantics). Toast for success uses the same 2-second `.overlay(alignment: .bottom)` pattern as the existing `switchedToast`; both toasts coexist via ZStack-style ordering with the `prOpenedToast` taking priority when both are non-nil. nav events Closeable observed in `.task` + closed in `.onDisappear` per the established Phase 32.2 / 36.5 iOS Closeable leak audit pattern; `.task` re-fires on view re-appearance so the helper closes any prior subscription before creating a new one. New iOS bridge `wrapChartViewerNavEvents` typed accessor in `KoinHelper.kt`. **i18n** — 7 new keys across all 5 sources (342 total, +7 from 335): `action_open_pull_request` (full-phrase overflow menu item, parallel to `action_pull_requests` toolbar entry), `dialog_open_pull_request_title`, `label_pr_title` (parallel to existing `label_pr_description` from 38.3), `hint_pr_title` (with U+2026 ellipsis per Phase 33.1.3 placeholder convention), `hint_pr_description_optional`, `action_open_pr` (short-form dialog confirm button — parallel to `action_close_pr` / `action_merge_pr` from 38.3 / 38.4), `message_pr_opened_successfully`. JA semantically diverges with 「プルリクエストを作成」("create") over the literal「開く」per the GitHub JA UI convention; documented inline in the JA strings comment block. Reuses `action_cancel`, `label_pr_description`, `title_error`, `action_ok`. **Tests (+11 commonTest, 1166 → 1177)**: 11 new `ChartViewerViewModelTest` cases covering canOpenPullRequest gate true/false on fork/non-fork/non-owner/missing-target-main, the MEDIUM-1 regression anchor (`currentBranch falls back to main but PR-open gate stays closed when tip does not match chart`), draft updates, RequestOpen clears prior error + opens sheet, Dismiss clears drafts, ConfirmOpen happy path emits PullRequestCreated and writes correct branch/pattern ids through to the use case, ConfirmOpen failure surfaces openPrError without closing sheet, ConfirmOpen no-op when gate is closed. Plus a private `ForkChartRevisionFake` helper for the OpenPullRequestUseCase parent-chain walk (the algorithm itself is exercised in `OpenPullRequestUseCaseTest`'s 9 tests; this fake just makes the source tip the common ancestor on the first hop). New `OpenPrTestRig` data class + `makeOpenPrViewModel(...)` parametric helper for arrange-phase setup. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 1 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass — all 4 fixed pre-commit. **HIGH** (5 `!!` operators in `openPullRequestInternal` violate project Kotlin coding-style rule "Never use `!!` — prefer `requireNotNull()` / `checkNotNull()`") fixed by replacing all with `requireNotNull(current.X) { "canOpenPullRequest gate: X is null" }` carrying gate-naming messages. **MEDIUM-1** (gate fallback to "main" can silently submit PR with mismatched sourceBranchId/sourceTipRevisionId on a feature branch — would land an immediately unmergeable PR rejected by the merge RPC's `chart_branches.tip_revision_id == sourceTipRevisionId` validation) fixed by tightening the `canOpenPullRequest` gate to require `branch.tipRevisionId == c.revisionId` exact match; the fallback in `resolveCurrentBranch` stays for displayed-branch rendering but the gate guards correctness. **LOW-1** (offline-mode error string hardcoded English) acknowledged consistent with existing PullRequestDetailViewModel.attemptMerge precedent + Tech Debt Backlog deferral; documented inline. **LOW-2** (`resolveOpenPrContext` fires redundantly on every Realtime echo) fixed via `lastResolvedRevisionId` de-dup local. Second-pass review APPROVED with one new doc-only LOW (the `resolveOpenPrContext` KDoc said "re-runs on every chart emission" but the code now de-dups; updated KDoc to accurately describe the de-dup semantics + name the parallel to `ProjectDetailViewModel.observeParentAttribution`). **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1177 tests, +11 from 1166 baseline), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (342 keys). iOS app builds via `xcodebuild -project iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅. **Scope cuts unchanged from Phase 38.4 review**: three-pane canvas preview on `ChartConflictResolutionScreen` (DualCanvasPanel extraction is meaningful refactor); Maestro E2E flow for the open-PR happy path (linked-pattern + chart-divergence fixture overhead with no clear value gain over the 11 new ViewModel tests + 9 use-case tests — reopen if real interaction-flow regressions surface); iOS toast for the chart-clone failure path on Discovery (Phase 36.5+ polish). **Closes the open-PR entry-point gap that 38.4 review flagged as the only beta-blocking UX issue**; the entire ADR-014 collaboration loop is now reachable end-to-end from any forked pattern's chart viewer. Phase 39 (Closed Beta) prep is the natural next slice now that the loop is observable to real users.

- **Phase 38.4**: Merge + conflict resolution (ADR-014 §4 §5 §6 §8) — fourth and final code slice of Phase 38, closes the entire collaboration loop. **`ConflictDetector` algorithm** under `domain/chart/ConflictDetector.kt` per ADR-014 §4 — pure 3-way wrapper over the existing Phase 37 `ChartDiffAlgorithm`. Computes `diff(ancestor, theirs)` and `diff(ancestor, mine)` then per-cell-coordinate partitions changes into `autoFromTheirs` / `autoFromMine` / `conflicts` based on whether both sides changed the same `(layerId, x, y)`. Same shape applies at the layer level (`autoLayerFromTheirs` / `autoLayerFromMine` / `layerConflicts`). Both-sides-agree-on-same-target case auto-resolves to autoFromTheirs (either side renders identically). Polar charts handled identically — `(x, y)` keys are `(stitch, ring)`. Returns `ConflictReport(autoFromTheirs, autoFromMine, conflicts, autoLayerFromTheirs, autoLayerFromMine, layerConflicts)` with `isClean: Boolean = conflicts.isEmpty() && layerConflicts.isEmpty()`. `CellConflict` and `LayerConflict` data classes carry `id: String` derived properties (`"$layerId#$x,$y"` / `layerId`) for SwiftUI ForEach `id: \.id` consistency with the Phase 38.3 PR list / comment ForEach precedent. **`MergePullRequestUseCase`** invokes the SECURITY DEFINER `merge_pull_request` RPC per ADR-014 §5. Bypasses the standard local-then-sync orchestration since the RPC is the only writer permitted to produce `chart_revisions.author_id != owner_id` rows. Defense-in-depth precondition gates: status must be OPEN, caller must be signed in, caller must be target owner per `PatternRepository.getById(targetPatternId)?.ownerId == callerId` (the RPC's `WHERE owner_id = v_caller` is the actual security boundary; the use-case check just surfaces a clear "Only the target owner can merge" Validation error rather than letting the RPC RAISE bubble up as Unknown). Mints fresh `revisionId` per call (Uuid.random) so PendingSync retry semantics are idempotent. Encodes `resolvedChart.toDocumentJson()` as the JSONB document parameter; computes a fresh `contentHash` via `StructuredChart.computeContentHash` over `extents + layers`. Maps RPC `RAISE EXCEPTION` messages onto distinct `UseCaseError` subtypes via `mapMergeError` — "Source tip drifted" / "PR not open" / "Target branch has no tip" → Validation, "Caller is not target owner" → Authentication, "PR not found" → NotFound, anything unrecognized → `Exception.toUseCaseError()` Unknown. Returns `MergeResult(pullRequestId, mergedRevisionId, mergedContentHash)` envelope on success. Standard `try { ... } catch (e: CancellationException) { throw e } catch (e: Exception) { ... }` envelope per the Phase 36.3 / 37.x precedent. **Merge port abstraction** (`domain/repository/PullRequestMergeOperations.kt`): thin `interface PullRequestMergeOperations { suspend fun merge(...): String }` that `RemotePullRequestDataSource` implements via `supabaseClient.postgrest.rpc("merge_pull_request", params)`. Same ports-and-adapters layering as `ChartRevisionRepository` / `StructuredChartRepository` — domain layer defines the contract, data layer provides the Supabase-typed adapter. Tests inject an in-memory fake without standing up Supabase. **`applyResolutions` helper** (in `MergePullRequestUseCase.kt`): pure function that builds the resolved drawing payload by starting from `mine` (target tip), applying `autoLayerFromTheirs` first (so subsequent cell ops see the correct layer set), then `layerConflictPicks`, then `autoFromTheirs`, then per-conflict `cellResolutions`. SKIP picks the ancestor cell value (revert to pre-fork state); KEEP_MINE / TAKE_THEIRS pick from the respective side. **Critical correctness fix from code review**: HIGH-2 caught that a SKIP cell pick on a layer that was auto-removed by theirs would silently recreate an orphan cell bucket via `cellsByLayerXy.getOrPut(coord.layerId) { mutableMapOf() }` — but the final `mergedLayers` build only iterates `layersById.values`, so the cell would silently disappear. Fix: `if (!layersById.containsKey(coord.layerId)) continue` skips the pick entirely when the containing layer is gone. Similar reasoning for KEEP_MINE on a removed layer — the user's only chance to preserve the layer was the (non-existent) layer-conflict pick at the layer level; cell-level KEEP_MINE cannot resurrect the layer. Recomputes rect chart extents from the merged cells; polar charts preserve their structural extents. **`ChartConflictResolutionViewModel`** parameterized on `prId`. Loads ancestor / theirs / mine snapshots in `init` (revisions are immutable per ADR-013 §1, no Flow observation), runs `ConflictDetector.detect`, exposes per-conflict picker state. `canApplyAndMerge` derived gate flips true only when every cell + layer conflict has a resolution. ApplyAndMerge dispatches `applyResolutions` over the user's picks and routes the result through `MergePullRequestUseCase`. Emits `ChartConflictResolutionNavEvent.MergeApplied(mergedRevisionId)` on success. **`PullRequestDetailViewModel.attemptMerge`** (new method, replaces the inert merge confirmation): when user confirms the merge dialog, loads ancestor + theirs + mine, runs `ConflictDetector.detect`, and either (a) routes through `MergePullRequestUseCase` directly with `applyResolutions(mine, autoFromTheirs, emptyMap(), autoLayerFromTheirs, emptyMap(), theirs, ancestor)` for the auto-clean path (HIGH-1 fix from code review — passing `theirs` raw silently dropped target-side `autoFromMine` edits because `autoFromMine` is identity-over-mine, so we still need to apply autoFromTheirs ON mine, not start from theirs), or (b) emits `NavigateToConflictResolution(prId)` for the conflicts path. New nav events `PrMerged(mergedRevisionId)` + `NavigateToConflictResolution(prId)` join the existing `PrClosed`. ViewModel ctor gains optional nullable `MergePullRequestUseCase` / `ChartRevisionRepository` / `StructuredChartRepository` deps with default-null so existing tests stay valid; production wiring always provides non-null; `attemptMerge` surfaces a Validation error if any are missing. New `isMerging` field added to `PullRequestDetailState`. **Compose `ChartConflictResolutionScreen`**: Scaffold + TopAppBar with summary chip ("3 conflicts to resolve" parametric). Phone-first stack — three-pane canvas (ancestor pinned center, theirs/mine side-by-side) named in ADR-014 §6 deferred to a polish slice (same scope-cut precedent as Phase 36.4 iOS Discovery thumbnail; row-based picker UI alone closes the merge loop end-to-end and the canvas preview can land independently). LazyColumn renders `LayerConflictRow` (uses `conflict.theirs?.name ?: mine?.name ?: ancestor?.name` for the human-readable layer name — code review MEDIUM-2 fix; the prior version rendered the bare UUID as the user-visible label) + `CellConflictRow` (parametric `label_conflict_cell` "Cell (%1$d, %2$d)"). Each row shows a 3-button `ResolutionPickerRow` (Take theirs / Keep mine / Skip) — selected option uses `Button` (filled), unselected use `TextButton` (outlined). Conflict rows use `tertiaryContainer.copy(alpha = 0.5f)` background per ADR-014 §6 — distinct from the Phase 37 traffic-light diff palette. Bottom-bar "Apply and merge" button gated on `canApplyAndMerge`. testTags: `chartConflictResolutionScreen` root + `conflictRow_<layerId>_<x>_<y>` / `layerConflictRow_<layerId>` per row + `takeTheirsButton_*` / `keepMineButton_*` / `skipButton_*` per pick + `applyAndMergeButton`. **PullRequestDetailScreen merge wiring**: merge button on action bar flips from `enabled = false` (Phase 38.3 deferred) to actively enabled. Merge confirmation dialog confirm button now dispatches `ConfirmMerge` event (was `DismissMergeConfirmation` no-op). New `onResolveConflicts: (prId: String) -> Unit` screen prop wired through NavGraph to `navigate(ChartConflictResolution(prId))`. Snackbar consumer extended to handle `PrMerged` (success toast) + `NavigateToConflictResolution` (push the resolution screen). **iOS mirror** at `iosApp/iosApp/Screens/ChartConflictResolutionScreen.swift` uses the established `ScopedViewModel<ChartConflictResolutionViewModel, ChartConflictResolutionState>` holder pattern. SwiftUI `List` with `Section`s for layer + cell conflicts; `ForEach(report.conflicts, id: \.id)` consumes the new `id` derived property added on `CellConflict` / `LayerConflict`. Conflict rows use `Color(.systemPurple).opacity(0.45)` per code review LOW-1 fix (was 0.18 — too faint at standard display brightness, asymmetric vs. Compose's 50% alpha). `AnyButtonStyle` private struct type-erases `PrimitiveButtonStyle` so the picker button can switch between `.borderedProminent` (selected) and `.bordered` (unselected) at runtime — SwiftUI's button-style protocol has an opaque `Body` associated type that prevents direct ternary switching; the closure-capture approach is the established idiom (see `AnyTransition`, `AnyShapeStyle`). **PullRequestDetailScreen.swift updates**: merge button on action bar drops `.disabled(true)`; merge confirmation dialog confirm dispatches `ConfirmMerge`; navEvent collector handles `PrMerged` (overlay toast `message_pr_merged_successfully`) + `NavigateToConflictResolution` (`path.append(Route.chartConflictResolution(prId:))`). **NavGraph**: new `@Serializable data class ChartConflictResolution(val prId: String)` route + `composable<ChartConflictResolution>` block plumbing `onMerged = { navController.popBackStack() }` so the user lands on the now-merged PR detail screen with status flip echoed via Realtime. `AppRouter.swift` `Route.chartConflictResolution(prId:)` enum case + Hashable conformance + destinationView mapping. **Koin DI**: `RepositoryModule` registers the merge port as `single<PullRequestMergeOperations> { get<RemotePullRequestDataSource>() }` — exposes the data-layer adapter through the domain-layer interface. `UseCaseModule` registers `MergePullRequestUseCase` factory with `getOrNull<PullRequestMergeOperations>()` so local-only mode (no Supabase) surfaces a Validation error rather than NPE. `ViewModelModule` registers `ChartConflictResolutionViewModel` parametric factory + extends `PullRequestDetailViewModel` factory with the 3 new optional deps. **iOS bridge**: `KoinHelper.kt` adds `getChartConflictResolutionViewModel(prId)` accessor + `wrapChartConflictResolutionState` (StateFlow → FlowWrapper) + `wrapChartConflictResolutionNavEvents` (Flow → EventFlowWrapper). `ViewModelFactory.swift` adds `chartConflictResolutionViewModel(prId:)` typed accessor. **i18n** — 10 new keys across all 5 sources (335 total, +10 from 325 baseline; matches the ADR §6 budget exactly): `title_resolve_conflicts`, `label_conflict_summary` parametric ("%1$d conflicts to resolve" EN / "解決が必要なコンフリクト: %1$d 件" JA — JA reorders with the `件` counter suffix per natural Japanese reading), `label_conflict_layer`, `label_conflict_cell` parametric ("Cell (%1$d, %2$d)" / "セル (%1$d, %2$d)"), `action_take_theirs` / `action_keep_mine` / `action_skip_conflict` (picker buttons), `action_apply_and_merge` (bottom-bar primary action), `state_all_conflicts_resolved` (summary chip when every conflict has a pick), `message_pr_merged_successfully` (deferred from Phase 38.3 — finally surfaced now that the merge UX lands). iOS xcstrings parametric specifiers use `%1$d`/`%2$d` for ints. **Tests (+35 commonTest, 1131 → 1166 — ADR-014 §8 budget was +20; overshoots justified by the 3-way ConflictDetector algorithm needing comprehensive partition coverage)**: `ConflictDetectorTest` (14 tests) covers the full coverage matrix including identical-clean, only-theirs / only-mine, both-modify-different / both-modify-same / both-add-different, theirs-removes-mine-modifies, parametric symbol parameter edits, layer added / renamed-different / renamed-identical, polar coordinate parity, multi-layer mixed change partitioning. `MergePullRequestUseCaseTest` (13 tests) covers status-not-open / unauthenticated / not-target-owner / offline-only Validations, happy path with revision-id round-trip, all 5 RPC error message → UseCaseError mappings, fresh-revision-id-per-call idempotency, plus the HIGH-1 + HIGH-2 regression tests `applyResolutions auto-clean preserves target-side autoFromMine edits` and `applyResolutions SKIP on cell whose layer was auto-removed drops the cell`. `ChartConflictResolutionViewModelTest` (8 tests) covers loadInitial → ConflictDetector run, canApplyAndMerge gating on cell + layer conflicts, PickCell / PickLayer state mutation, ApplyAndMerge happy path emitting MergeApplied event, ApplyAndMerge failure path surfacing state.error, revision lookup miss leaving report null with error, ClearError. New private test fakes: `FakeMergeOps` + `RecordingMergeOps` (in-memory `PullRequestMergeOperations` with last-call recording + throw-on-next failure injection); `FakeRevisionRepoForResolution` (revision-id keyed map). Also added a non-suspend `seed(pattern)` helper to `FakePatternRepository` so test fixtures can populate without `runTest` boilerplate. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 3 LOW first pass — all 7 fixed pre-commit; second pass APPROVED with 0 findings. **HIGH-1** (auto-clean merge path passed `theirs` directly to `MergePullRequestUseCase` instead of the resolved document — silently dropped any target-side `autoFromMine` edits when the target branch had diverged from the ancestor since the fork point) fixed by routing through `applyResolutions` with empty conflict-resolution maps; regression test `applyResolutions auto-clean preserves target-side autoFromMine edits` lands the verification. **HIGH-2** (SKIP cell resolution against a layer auto-removed by theirs would silently recreate an orphan cell bucket that the final `mergedLayers` build never sees, dropping the SKIP outcome silently — KEEP_MINE on the same coordinate suffers the same bug) fixed by `if (!layersById.containsKey(coord.layerId)) continue` guard at the top of the `conflictPicks` loop; regression test `applyResolutions SKIP on cell whose layer was auto-removed drops the cell` lands the verification. **MEDIUM-1** (`PullRequestMergeOperations` was placed in `domain.usecase` package but implemented by `RemotePullRequestDataSource` in `data.remote` — crosses the layer boundary; should be in `domain.repository` matching the `ChartRevisionRepository` / `StructuredChartRepository` ports-and-adapters precedent) fixed by moving the interface to a new `domain/repository/PullRequestMergeOperations.kt` file; updated 4 import sites (`MergePullRequestUseCase.kt`, `RemotePullRequestDataSource.kt`, `RepositoryModule.kt`, `UseCaseModule.kt`, plus the two test files). **MEDIUM-2** (`LayerConflictRow` rendered `conflict.layerId` as the user-visible label — UUID strings are meaningless to users; should resolve a human-readable name from `conflict.theirs?.name ?: mine?.name ?: ancestor?.name ?: layerId` since at least one of theirs/mine is non-null on a PropertyChanged conflict) fixed on both Compose and SwiftUI. **LOW-1** (iOS row alpha asymmetric — Compose used 50% on tertiaryContainer, iOS used 18% on systemPurple, perceptually too faint at standard display brightness) fixed by bumping iOS to 0.45 with explanatory inline comment naming the Compose parity rationale. **LOW-2** (iOS `AnyButtonStyle` PrimitiveButtonStyle wrapper) confirmed correct — SwiftUI's button-style protocol has an opaque associated type so the closure-capture approach is the established idiom matching `AnyTransition` / `AnyShapeStyle`. **LOW-3** (`onCleared` not implemented on `ChartConflictResolutionViewModel`) confirmed correct — the VM has no Realtime subscriptions, no Channel teardown needs (`viewModelScope` cancellation handles `_navEvents` automatically), nothing to clean up. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1166 tests, +35 from 1131 baseline), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (335 keys). iOS app builds via `xcodebuild -project iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅. **Closes Phase 38**: with this slice the entire ADR-014 collaboration loop — append-only data spine (38.1) → read-only PR list (38.2) → PR detail with open / close / comment write paths (38.3) → merge + conflict resolution (38.4) — is end-to-end functional. The `chart_revisions.author_id != owner_id` invariant from ADR-013 §1 finally has its first non-trivial use; the SECURITY DEFINER RPC pattern joins `delete_own_account` (ADR-005) as the second cross-table atomic-write precedent; the 3-way diff helper sits one layer above the Phase 37 §5 algorithm so a future "preview merge" affordance reuses it. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-014 §10**: three-pane canvas preview deferred (`DualCanvasPanel` extraction is meaningful refactor; row-based picker alone closes the merge loop), Maestro E2E deferred (linked-pattern + open-PR + chart-divergence fixture prerequisite adds significant Maestro setup, no clear value gain over the 35 commonTest), "ChartViewer overflow → Open PR" entry remains deferred (the data layer + use case are wired and ready; UI flow is its own slice, likely 38.4.1 if it lands ahead of Phase 39), required-approval gates / draft PR / threaded comments / markdown all post-v1, "merge-conflict re-resolution after source drift mid-resolution" surfaces the generic "Source tip drifted" error today (better UX is post-v1).

- **Phase 38.3**: Pull request detail surface + open / close / comment write paths (ADR-014 §6, §8) — third code slice of Phase 38 builds the user-visible read+write surface for a single PR on top of the 38.1 data spine and 38.2 list. Closes the no-op `onPullRequestClick` callback the 38.2 NavGraph left wired. **No merge yet** — Phase 38.4 owns merge + conflict resolution. **5 new use cases** under `shared/.../domain/usecase/`: `GetPullRequestUseCase` (suspend invoke + `observe(prId, ownerId, scope)` Flow that filters whichever owner-scoped Flow the caller indicates so a status flip landing through Realtime emits a fresh state without a manual refresh — `PullRequestObserveScope` enum with INCOMING / OUTGOING decides which side to subscribe to based on the user's role; ViewModel picks INCOMING when `currentUserId == targetOwnerId`, OUTGOING when `currentUserId == authorId`); `GetPullRequestCommentsUseCase` (suspend invoke + observe Flow over the local cache — KDoc explicitly documents that the Realtime cold-launch seed is owned by the new `PullRequestRepository.subscribeToCommentsChannel` which kicks a remote fetch under the same lock as the channel attach, so the observe Flow stays warm thereafter via the per-PR Realtime channel); `PostPullRequestCommentUseCase` (validates body length ≤ 5000 chars per migration 016 CHECK + ADR-014 §1 client-side, rejects blank-after-trim bodies, generates the row id + `createdAt = Clock.System.now()` locally, calls repo `postComment`); `OpenPullRequestUseCase` (computes `commonAncestorRevisionId` client-side per ADR-014 §3 by snapshotting target's full history into a `Set<revisionId>` then walking source's `parent_revision_id` chain starting from `sourceTipRevisionId` until it hits a revision in the target set — the start revision itself counts so a fork-with-no-source-side-edits resolves the source tip immediately as the common ancestor; defense-in-depth `MAX_WALK_DEPTH = 1000` guards against pathological circular chains; `MAX_TARGET_HISTORY_LIMIT = 1000` covers any realistic per-pattern revision count without surfacing a pagination boundary; title ≤ 200 / description ≤ 2000 char validation per ADR-014 §1; if no ancestor found surfaces `UseCaseError.Validation` rather than writing a malformed PR; if target has empty history same Validation outcome — defensive against the upstream-history-pruned-out-from-under-the-fork edge case named in ADR-014 §3); `ClosePullRequestUseCase` (checks PR is still OPEN as defense-in-depth + caller is signed in; intentionally does NOT do the "is caller author or target owner" check — that lives at the UI layer in `PullRequestDetailViewModel.canClose` so the use case doesn't need to take a `PatternRepository` dependency for a check the server-side RLS UPDATE policy already enforces; KDoc names the offline-local-write window per the codebase-wide `Repository.close` precedent so future readers understand the offline-tolerance contract). All 5 use cases use the project's standard `try { ... } catch (e: CancellationException) { throw e } catch (e: Exception) { e.toUseCaseError() }` envelope per the Phase 36.3 / 37.x precedent. **`PullRequestRepository` interface extension**: 2 new methods `subscribeToCommentsChannel(prId)` + `closeCommentsChannel()` to manage the dynamic per-PR Realtime channel `pull-request-comments-<prId>` per ADR-014 §7 — implementation in `PullRequestRepositoryImpl` mirrors the Phase 4b `CommentRepositoryImpl` pattern with internal `commentsChannel: ChannelHandle?` + `subscribedPrId: String?` + `channelMutex: Mutex` for serialization. Idempotent on the same prId via the `commentsChannel != null && subscribedPrId == prId` short-circuit inside the mutex; channel-swap branch when prId changes (defensive against in-flight init re-entry; ViewModel is parameterized on prId so this is mostly a guard rail). Subscribe-then-fetch pattern: opens the channel via `provider.createChannel("pull-request-comments-$prId")`, registers the postgres-change Flow with `ChangeFilter("pull_request_id", prId)`, calls `subscribe()`, THEN fires a best-effort remote `getCommentsForPullRequest` to seed the cache — failure here is tolerated (KDoc explicit), the local cache stays whatever it was and Realtime fills the gap as events arrive. `handleCommentAction` exhaustively routes the 4 PostgresAction variants: INSERT → `local.upsertComment(comment)`; UPDATE / DELETE / SELECT silent no-op since RLS forbids those actions server-side. New ctor params `channelProvider: RealtimeChannelProvider? = null` + `scope: CoroutineScope? = null` are nullable with default-null so test fakes that construct the impl directly stay valid AND local-only mode (no Supabase) keeps both methods as silent no-ops. **`PullRequestDetailViewModel`** parameterized on `prId: String`. State carries `pullRequest: PullRequest?`, `comments: List<PullRequestComment>`, `users: Map<String, User>`, `targetOwnerId: String?` (resolved via `PatternRepository.getById(targetPatternId)` — explicit try/catch with `CancellationException` rethrow, NOT `runCatching` per code review MEDIUM-1 fix; runCatching swallows CancellationException which would silently null `targetOwnerId` for the session and permanently disable the merge/close gates after a coroutine timeout), `currentUserId: String?`, `commentDraft: String`, `isLoading`, `isSendingComment`, `isClosingPr`, `pendingCloseConfirmation`, `pendingMergeConfirmation`, `error`. **`canMerge` and `canClose` are derived state-class properties, not top-level extension properties** — moved during iOS build verification because top-level extensions on a Kotlin data class bridge to Swift as `PullRequestDetailViewModelKt.canMerge(state)` (Kt-class function) which xcodebuild rejected with "cannot find type 'PullRequestDetailViewModelKt' in scope"; making them inline `get()` properties on the data class lets the Swift bridge read them as plain `Bool` getters via `state.canMerge` / `state.canClose`. `canMerge` = `pr.status == OPEN && currentUserId == targetOwnerId` (Phase 38.3 keeps the merge button visually disabled regardless; gate computed centrally so 38.4 just enables the screen-side `enabled` flag). `canClose` = `status == OPEN && (currentUserId == authorId || currentUserId == targetOwnerId)` per ADR-014 §1 "either party may close". **Realtime lifecycle**: `init` block sequences (1) `subscribeToCommentsChannel(prId)` BEFORE seeding the comment list so any INSERT landing during the seed window propagates through the channel rather than being missed, then (2) sync `currentUserId` from `authRepository.getCurrentUserId()`, then (3) `loadInitial()` (PR + target pattern + user resolution), then (4) `observeComments()` for live updates. `onCleared` spawns a detached `CoroutineScope(Dispatchers.Default + NonCancellable).launch { withTimeout(5_000) { closeCommentsChannel() } }` — `viewModelScope` is already cancelled by the time `onCleared` runs so a plain `viewModelScope.launch` would be dropped. `NonCancellable` ensures an external cancel signal cannot race the cleanup; `withTimeout(5_000)` bounds the lifetime so a hung Realtime `unsubscribe` (server timeout, network partition) cannot leak the scope indefinitely. 5s is generous for a websocket unsubscribe round-trip; the cleanup is idempotent on the server side so a forced timeout is safe. This pattern was the load-bearing fix from code review HIGH-1 (the original `CoroutineScope(Dispatchers.Default).launch { }` with no timeout could leak the scope forever if `closeCommentsChannel` never returned). **`observePrRow` flow**: subscribes to `getPullRequest.observe(prId, ownerId, scope)` and pipes fresh emissions into `_state.pullRequest` so a status flip landing through Realtime (close echo, merge echo) lands without a manual refresh. The `.catch { e -> if (e is CancellationException) throw e else _state.update { ... error = ... } }` re-throws CancellationException per code review LOW-1 fix — the prior version surfaced job cancellation as a user-visible Snackbar error which is wrong. Same fix applied to `observeComments`'s `.catch`. **Optimistic post-comment cache write**: `postCommentInternal` adds the freshly-posted comment to `_state.comments` immediately on success (idempotent — checks `comments.any { it.id == result.value.id }` first) so the user sees their post even in local-only mode where the Realtime echo never arrives. Resolves the just-posted comment's author via `resolveUsersForComments` so the row renders with the correct display name on first paint. **One-shot navigation channel**: `_navEvents: Channel<PullRequestDetailNavEvent>(Channel.BUFFERED)` carries `PrClosed` after a successful close so the screen can surface the `message_pr_closed_successfully` Snackbar (Compose) / 2-second `.overlay` toast (iOS) without blocking the close callback. **Compose `PullRequestDetailScreen`**: Scaffold + TopAppBar (back button + `title_pull_request_detail` + status chip via private `PullRequestStatus.labelKey: StringResource` extension mirroring the 38.2 PR-list pattern). LazyColumn body holds `TitleAndStatus` (PR title + author line `label_pr_authored_by` parametric + timestamp), `DescriptionCard` (only renders when `pr.description?.takeIf { it.isNotBlank() }`), `DiffPreviewCard` ("View proposed changes" Button routing to the existing Phase 37.3 `ChartDiffScreen` between `pr.commonAncestorRevisionId` and `pr.sourceTipRevisionId` — **inline diff render deferred** per the same scope-cut precedent as Phase 36.4 iOS Discovery thumbnail; extracting `DualCanvasPanel` from ChartDiffScreen into a thumbnail-sized component is a meaningful refactor of the gestural Compose Canvas that's out of scope for 38.3, the `prDiffPreview` testTag is reserved for the future inline-render surface), `label_pr_comments` section header, `CommentRow` per comment (author name + timestamp + body, Surface card layout matching the 38.2 PR-list visual rhythm). `CommentComposeBox` (OutlinedTextField + post Button, `enabled = !isSending`, post button additionally `&& draft.isNotBlank()`) renders below the LazyColumn only when `pr.status == OPEN`. `ActionBar` renders below the compose box when `canMerge || canClose`: target owner sees "Merge" Button (visually disabled for 38.3) + "Close" TextButton; source author sees just "Close". testTags per ADR-014 §6: `pullRequestDetailScreen` (root), `prTitleLabel`, `prDescriptionLabel`, `prDiffPreview`, `commentInputField`, `postCommentButton`, `mergeButton`, `closeButton`, `commentRow_<commentId>`. Phase 38.3 also adds the merge/close confirmation `AlertDialog`s — close dialog confirms via `ConfirmClose` event; merge dialog confirm button is `enabled = false` (the body text explains the deferral) so even a user who taps "Merge" still sees the "Coming in Phase 38.4" rationale rather than nothing. **NavGraph**: new `@Serializable data class PullRequestDetail(val prId: String)` route. The 38.2 `composable<PullRequestList>` block's `onPullRequestClick = { _ -> }` no-op pivots to `{ prId -> navController.navigate(PullRequestDetail(prId = prId)) }`. New `composable<PullRequestDetail>` block plumbs `onOpenDiff = { baseRevisionId, targetRevisionId -> navController.navigate(ChartDiff(...)) }`. **iOS mirror** at `iosApp/iosApp/Screens/PullRequestDetailScreen.swift` uses the established `ScopedViewModel<PullRequestDetailViewModel, PullRequestDetailState>` holder pattern. Body uses `ContentUnavailableView` for the not-found branch, `ScrollView { VStack { ... } }` for the loaded branch (header + description + diff preview + comments section), `commentComposeBox` HStack at the bottom only when `pr.status == .open`, `actionBar` HStack below when `canMerge || canClose`. SwiftUI `.confirmationDialog` for both close (destructive button) and merge (confirm button `.disabled(true)` per the deferral) — `Binding<Bool>` derived from `state.pendingCloseConfirmation` / `state.pendingMergeConfirmation` so the dialog dismissal routes through the matching ViewModel event. `navEvents` Closeable observed in `.task` and closed in `.onDisappear` per the established Phase 32.2 / 36.5 iOS Closeable leak audit pattern; the `PrClosed` event triggers a 2-second `.overlay(alignment: .bottom)` toast carrying `message_pr_closed_successfully`. The diff-preview "View proposed changes" Button routes via `path.append(Route.chartDiff(...))`. **Existing `PullRequestListScreen.swift` updated**: signature gains `path: Binding<NavigationPath>`; row tap pivots from no-op comment to `path.append(Route.pullRequestDetail(prId: pr.id))`. **`PullRequestStatus` Swift enum bridging**: same `default: return status.name` fallback in `statusKey` per the Phase 33.1.13 precedent — locale-neutral non-empty fallback so a future enum addition without matching Swift switch update surfaces visibly at runtime. **Date formatting**: inline pattern `Date(timeIntervalSince1970: TimeInterval(epochSeconds))` matches existing `PullRequestListScreen.swift` / `ChartHistoryScreen.swift` precedent — initially used `Kotlinx_datetimeInstant` typed parameter but xcodebuild couldn't resolve the type from the bridged Shared framework so refactored to take `Int64` directly. **iOS bridge**: `KoinHelper.kt` adds `getPullRequestDetailViewModel(prId)` accessor + `wrapPullRequestDetailState` (StateFlow → FlowWrapper) + `wrapPullRequestDetailNavEvents` (Flow → EventFlowWrapper). `ViewModelFactory.swift` adds `pullRequestDetailViewModel(prId:)`. `AppRouter.swift` adds `Route.pullRequestDetail(prId: String)` with Hashable conformance + destinationView mapping. `xcodegen generate` regenerated `iosApp.xcodeproj` to register `PullRequestDetailScreen.swift`. **Koin DI**: `UseCaseModule` registers all 5 new factories. `ViewModelModule` registers `PullRequestDetailViewModel` with all 9 dependencies (5 use cases + 4 repos). `RepositoryModule` `PullRequestRepositoryImpl` registration extended with `channelProvider = getOrNull<RealtimeChannelProvider>()` + `scope = getOrNull<CoroutineScope>(applicationScopeQualifier)` so local-only mode keeps the `subscribeToCommentsChannel` call as a silent no-op rather than throwing on missing Supabase. **i18n** — 14 new keys across all 5 sources (325 total, +14 from 311 baseline; matches the ADR §6 budget exactly): `title_pull_request_detail`, `label_pr_description`, `label_pr_diff_preview`, `label_pr_comments`, `hint_add_comment_to_pr` (with U+2026 ellipsis per convention), `action_post_comment`, `action_merge_pr`, `action_close_pr`, `dialog_merge_pr_title`, `dialog_merge_pr_body` (body explicitly names "Conflict resolution ships in Phase 38.4" so users tapping the disabled merge button see the rationale), `dialog_close_pr_title`, `dialog_close_pr_body`, `state_pr_not_found`, `message_pr_closed_successfully`. Reuses 38.2 / 38.1 `action_back` / `action_cancel` / `title_error` / `action_ok` / `label_someone` / `label_pr_authored_by` / `label_pr_status_{open,merged,closed}`. `message_pr_merged_successfully` is deferred to 38.4 because that's where the merge UX lands; 38.3 only ships the close feedback message. **`FakePullRequestRepository` test fake widened** from "read-side only" to cover `getById` / comment Flows / `openPullRequest` / `closePullRequest` / `postComment` / `subscribeToCommentsChannel` / `closeCommentsChannel` so the new use cases can be exercised end-to-end. New affordances: `seedById` / `setComments` for arrange-phase setup; `lastOpened` / `lastClosed` / `lastPosted` / `subscribeCount` / `closeCount` / `lastSubscribedPrId` for assert-phase verification; `nextGetByIdError` / `nextOpenError` / `nextCloseError` / `nextPostCommentError` / `nextGetCommentsError` for failure-path coverage. **Tests (+44 commonTest, 1087 → 1131)**: `GetPullRequestUseCaseTest` (6 tests) covers cached-success, NotFound, exception → Failure, observe-from-incoming-flow, observe-id-filter, observe-status-flip-on-Realtime-emission. `GetPullRequestCommentsUseCaseTest` (4 tests) covers seeded list, empty cache, exception, observe Flow. `PostPullRequestCommentUseCaseTest` (6 tests) covers happy path with body trimming, blank-body Validation, max-length Validation, unauthenticated Authentication, repo-error Unknown wrapping, fresh-id-per-call (idempotent INSERT-OR-IGNORE on remote needs distinct UUIDs to avoid silent coalesce). `OpenPullRequestUseCaseTest` (9 tests) — the most extensive coverage given the parent-chain walk algorithm: source-tip-is-fork-point, walk-back-multiple-steps, no-ancestor-Validation, empty-target-history-Validation, blank-title-Validation, max-title-Validation, unauthenticated-Authentication, blank-description-stored-as-null, repo-write-recorded. `ClosePullRequestUseCaseTest` (5 tests) — happy path, already-merged Validation, already-closed Validation, unauthenticated Authentication, repo-error wrapping. `PullRequestDetailViewModelTest` (14 tests) — load-PR-plus-target-owner-plus-comments, NotFound surfacing, exactly-one channel subscribe call, canMerge true for target owner, canMerge false for source author, canClose true for source author, canClose false for unrelated user, canClose false on merged PR, CommentDraftChanged, PostComment writes through and clears draft, RequestClose-then-ConfirmClose flips status + emits PrClosed nav event, DismissCloseConfirmation no-ops the dialog without closing, ClearError, comment-author display name resolution. New private `FakeRevisionRepoForOpenPr` test class (in `OpenPullRequestUseCaseTest.kt`) implements the `ChartRevisionRepository` interface with seeded `getHistoryForPattern(patternId)` + `getRevision(revisionId)` lookups; other methods throw to surface accidental reach. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 1 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass — all 4 fixed pre-commit. **HIGH** (`onCleared` detached coroutine scope leak risk — original `CoroutineScope(Dispatchers.Default).launch { closeCommentsChannel() }` had no timeout and no NonCancellable, so a hung Realtime unsubscribe could leak the scope indefinitely with no mechanism to cancel) fixed by adding `+ NonCancellable` to the scope context AND wrapping the `closeCommentsChannel` call with `withTimeout(5_000)`. **MEDIUM** (`runCatching { patternRepository.getById(...) }.getOrNull()` swallows CancellationException, which silently nulls `targetOwnerId` for the session — the merge gate is load-bearing on this field so a coroutine-cancelled timeout would permanently disable the merge button until the user re-enters the screen) fixed by replacing with explicit try/catch that rethrows CancellationException per the Phase 36.3 / 37.x precedent. **LOW-1** (`.catch` operator in `observePrRow` and `observeComments` swallows CancellationException and surfaces it as a user-visible Snackbar error) fixed by adding `if (e is CancellationException) throw e` at the top of both `.catch` lambdas. **LOW-2** (`runCatching` in `resolveUsersForPr` and `resolveUsersForComments`) refactored to explicit try/catch for consistency with the project-wide pattern even though display-name resolution failure is non-fatal. **LOW-3** (`ClosePullRequestUseCase` KDoc missing offline-local-write window disclosure) addressed by adding an "Offline-local-write window" paragraph to the use case's KDoc explicitly naming the codebase-wide offline-tolerance contract. **Kover exclusion**: `PullRequestDetailScreenKt*` added to the screen-level Compose UI exclusion list. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1131 tests, +44 from 1087 baseline — overshoots the ADR §8's +20–25 target but the overshoot is concentrated in `OpenPullRequestUseCaseTest`'s 9 tests where the parent-chain walk algorithm needs careful coverage of every branch including the source-tip-is-fork-point shortcut and the empty-target-history defensive path), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (325 keys). iOS app builds via `xcodebuild -project iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-014 §6**: merge button stays inert (Phase 38.4 wires the SECURITY DEFINER `merge_pull_request` RPC + `MergePullRequestUseCase` + `ConflictDetector` algorithm + `ChartConflictResolutionScreen`); inline diff canvas render deferred (the "View proposed changes" link routes to existing Phase 37.3 ChartDiffScreen, extracting a thumbnail-sized component is a meaningful refactor — same scope-cut precedent as Phase 36.4 iOS Discovery thumbnail); ChartViewer overflow "Open pull request" entry deferred (would need to lift `parentPatternId` + `visibility` from the chart load path into ChartViewerViewModel state + add a compose-form-and-submit flow over `OpenPullRequestUseCase`; the data layer + use case are wired and ready, but the UI flow is its own slice — likely 38.3.1 if it lands ahead of 38.4); Maestro E2E deferred — same linked-pattern + open-PR fixture prerequisite as Phase 38.2 + needs Supabase connectivity for the Realtime channel test. **Forward-compat anchors for 38.4**: `canMerge` already gated on `pr.status == OPEN && currentUserId == targetOwnerId` and rendered visually disabled — Phase 38.4 just removes the `enabled = false` flag on the merge button + wires the confirm button to `MergePullRequestUseCase`. The merge confirmation dialog UI ships in 38.3 with the body copy explaining the deferral so the user-facing wiring is end-to-end ready.

- **Phase 38.2**: Pull request read-only list (ADR-014 §6, §8) — second code slice of Phase 38 wires the data spine from 38.1 into a user-visible read surface. **Use cases**: `GetIncomingPullRequestsUseCase` + `GetOutgoingPullRequestsUseCase` symmetric — both expose `observe(ownerId): Flow<List<PullRequest>>` that delegates to `PullRequestRepository.observeIncomingForOwner` / `observeOutgoingForOwner` (local-only flows per the repository's KDoc) plus a one-shot `suspend operator fun invoke(ownerId): UseCaseResult<List<PullRequest>>` that backfills the cache from the remote. Both use the standard `try { ... } catch (e: CancellationException) { throw e } catch (e: Exception) { e.toUseCaseError() }` envelope per the Phase 36.3 / 37.3 / 37.4 precedent.
