Repository ctor param is non-null because `PullRequestRepository` is unconditionally registered in `RepositoryModule` (it handles local-only mode internally via `remote = null`), matching `GetChartHistoryUseCase`'s precedent. **`PullRequestListViewModel`** parameterized on `defaultFilter: PullRequestFilter` (a new top-level `@Serializable enum class` with INCOMING / OUTGOING — `@Serializable` so the route can carry it). State carries `filter: PullRequestFilter`, `pullRequests: List<PullRequest>`, `users: Map<String, User>` (resolved post-list-load via `UserRepository.getByIds` — same pattern as `ActivityFeedViewModel.resolveUsers`), `isLoading`, `error`. Filter switching via `_filter: MutableStateFlow<PullRequestFilter>` + `flatMapLatest` — `SelectFilter` event flips `_filter.value` (and resets `users = emptyMap()` so a stale author entry from the old filter cannot bleed into the new one via `resolveUsers`'s dedup-by-key skip). **Cold-launch seeding contract embedded inside `flatMapLatest`** — the prior `viewModelScope.launch { ... }` for the seed escaped `flatMapLatest`'s cancellable scope and could surface the prior filter's error after the user had already switched (caught by code review HIGH-1; fixed by moving the seed inside a single `flow { val seed = ...; emitAll(observe(...)) }` block so seed and observe share lifetime). **`resolveUsers` race fix** (code review HIGH-2): the prior version captured `currentUsers = _state.value.users` BEFORE the `userRepository.getByIds` suspend, then merged via `currentUsers + resolved` AFTER, which silently dropped concurrent resolutions when two `onEach` emissions arrived back-to-back under network pressure. Fixed by reading inside `_state.update { current -> current.copy(users = current.users + resolved) }` so the merge always sees the latest accumulated map; `ActivityFeedViewModel.resolveUsers` carries the same race but is left unfixed in this slice (Tech Debt note inline). **Compose `PullRequestListScreen`** — Scaffold with TopAppBar (back button + title `title_pull_requests`), `FilterChipRow` between header and list (with `incomingFilterChip` / `outgoingFilterChip` testTags), main body groups PRs by `STATUS_DISPLAY_ORDER = listOf(OPEN, MERGED, CLOSED)` so OPEN PRs always render first regardless of created_at ordering. Each `PullRequestRow` shows: title + status chip on first line (parametric `prTitleLabel_<id>` / `prStatusChip_<id>` testTags), author line `label_pr_authored_by` parametric (`%1$s` resolves to `state.users[pr.authorId]?.displayName ?: stringResource(label_someone)`), and a timestamp via the existing `Instant.formatFull()` helper. Tap on a row routes through `onPullRequestClick` which is wired as no-op for 38.2 — Phase 38.3 will route to `PullRequestDetailScreen`. Status chip uses `AssistChip` with `enabled = false` + `disabledLabelColor = onSurface` for static rendering. Empty state surfaces `state_no_pull_requests` headline + `state_no_pull_requests_body` description. Root testTag `pullRequestListScreen`. **Status enum extension** `PullRequestStatus.labelKey: StringResource` with exhaustive `when` on the 3 cases — `OPEN → label_pr_status_open`, `MERGED → label_pr_status_merged`, `CLOSED → label_pr_status_closed` (private to the screen file; promote to `ui/components/` if a second consumer surfaces, same pattern as Phase 33.1.10's `Difficulty.labelKey` promotion). **NavGraph** new `@Serializable data class PullRequestList(val defaultFilter: PullRequestFilter)` route + `composable<PullRequestList>` block; the `PullRequestFilter` enum routes through kotlinx-serialization natively without any ordinal-int conversion. **iOS mirror** at `iosApp/iosApp/Screens/PullRequestListScreen.swift` uses the established `ScopedViewModel<PullRequestListViewModel, PullRequestListState>` holder pattern. SwiftUI body uses `ContentUnavailableView` for empty state, `List(ordered, id: \.id)` body, custom `FilterChipButton` private struct for selectable chip rendering (Capsule background + accent overlay; `accessibilityIdentifier` parameter for `incomingFilterChip` / `outgoingFilterChip` parity), `PullRequestStatusBadge` private struct for the status chip (renamed from initial `StatusBadge` per code review fix — collision with the project-status `StatusBadge` already defined in `ProjectListScreen.swift`). `statusKey` private property uses `default: return status.name` per the Phase 33.1.13 `SharedContentScreen.swift` `Difficulty` precedent — locale-neutral non-empty fallback so a future `PullRequestStatus` addition without a matching Swift switch update surfaces visibly at runtime rather than silently mislabeled as "Open". **Entry points**: (a) `ProjectListScreen` (Compose) gains an `onSuggestionsClick` callback wired through NavGraph to `navigate(PullRequestList(defaultFilter = INCOMING))`; toolbar IconButton uses `Icons.Default.Forum` with `action_pull_requests` contentDescription (NEW key, distinct from `title_pull_requests` per the role-prefix discipline established in Phase 33.1.3 — toolbar action vs screen title can diverge in JA, with the JA value `プルリクエストを開く` carrying the verb suffix for natural TalkBack announcement). testTag `pullRequestsButton`. (b) `ProjectListScreen.swift` mirror gains the same Menu item with `action_pull_requests` label + `pullRequestsButton` accessibilityIdentifier. (c) `ProjectDetailScreen` `PatternInfoSection` (both Compose + SwiftUI) gains a new "Pull Requests" link beneath the existing chart-related links — surfaces unconditionally; the default-filter selection happens at the outer screen layer via `pattern.parentPatternId != null ? OUTGOING : INCOMING` (forks default to Outgoing; upstream patterns default to Incoming) per ADR-014 §6. testTag `openPullRequestsLink`. **iOS bridge**: `KoinHelper.kt` adds `getPullRequestListViewModel(defaultFilter: PullRequestFilter)` accessor + `wrapPullRequestListState`. `ViewModelFactory.swift` adds `pullRequestListViewModel(defaultFilter:)`. `AppRouter.swift` adds `Route.pullRequestList(defaultFilter: PullRequestFilter)` with Hashable conformance and `destinationView` mapping. `xcodegen generate` regenerated `iosApp.xcodeproj` to register `PullRequestListScreen.swift`. **Author display name resolution**: 38.2 reuses `UserRepository.getByIds` which is already wired through `RepositoryModule` (consumed by `ActivityFeedViewModel`, `SharedWithMeViewModel`, `ProjectDetailViewModel` since Phase 36.5). Fallback to `label_someone` when the lookup misses (cold-launch with empty UserRepository cache, account deleted via ON DELETE SET NULL, or null `authorId` on the PR row itself). **i18n** — 10 new keys across all 5 sources (311 total, +10 from 301 baseline; ADR §6 budget called for 9, the +1 for `action_pull_requests` was added during code review per the role-prefix discipline): `title_pull_requests`, `action_pull_requests` (toolbar IconButton + iOS menu Label), `label_filter_incoming`, `label_filter_outgoing`, `state_no_pull_requests`, `state_no_pull_requests_body`, `label_pr_status_open`, `label_pr_status_merged`, `label_pr_status_closed`, `label_pr_authored_by` parametric (`%1$s` EN / `%1$s` JA / `%1$@` xcstrings — JA reads `<name>が作成` for natural grammar). Reuses `action_back` / `title_error` / `action_ok` / `label_someone`. **Tests (+22 commonTest, 1065 → 1087)**: `GetIncomingPullRequestsUseCaseTest` (5 tests) covers seeded list, empty cache, exception → Failure, observe Flow seeded, ownerId scoping. `GetOutgoingPullRequestsUseCaseTest` (5 tests) symmetric — same shape, distinct fake state to verify the outgoing path. `PullRequestListViewModelTest` (12 tests) covers default INCOMING + OUTGOING load, SelectFilter switches list and clears users, no-op SelectFilter on same filter, repo flow live emission, unauthenticated error path, user display name resolution, all-null-authorIds keeps users empty, ClearError, ownerId-scoping, seed-failure error surface (validates the HIGH-1 flatMapLatest fix), filter-switch users-clear (validates the MEDIUM-1 stale-users-bleed fix). New shared test fake `FakePullRequestRepository` implementing the full `PullRequestRepository` interface — read-side methods backed by per-ownerId `MutableStateFlow<List<PullRequest>>` so observe Flows stay live across `setIncoming` / `setOutgoing` calls; write-side methods (open / close / postComment / getCommentsFor / getById) `error("Not used by Phase 38.2 use cases")` to surface accidental cross-test reach. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 4 MEDIUM / 3 LOW first pass — HIGHs (escaped seed coroutine, stale `currentUsers` snapshot in `resolveUsers`) + MEDIUMs (stale users-map across filter switch, `title_pull_requests`-as-contentDescription role-prefix violation, iOS `default: return "label_pr_status_open"` silent mislabel, missing seed-failure regression test) + 1 LOW (outgoing scoping test parity) all addressed pre-commit. The remaining 2 LOWs were pre-existing inconsistencies (GetChartHistoryUseCase missing `CancellationException` rethrow; iOS alert dismiss button uses bare `String` literal that auto-promotes through SwiftUI overload resolution) — neither created by 38.2; flagged for separate sweep. **Kover exclusion**: `PullRequestListScreenKt*` added to the screen-level Compose UI exclusion list. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1087 tests, +22 from 1065 baseline — comfortably above the +10 ADR §8 budget; the bump is from the ViewModel surface needing more state-transition coverage than the ADR estimated, plus the LOW-3 outgoing scoping test parity), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (311 keys). iOS app builds via `xcodebuild -project iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-014 §6**: unread badge with last-seen-at tracking deferred to Phase 38.3 (the `countOpenIncomingForOwner` SQLDelight query is wired and ready, but the client-side last-seen-at storage + Badge composable land alongside the read-state mechanism); per-row tap routing to `PullRequestDetailScreen` is Phase 38.3; PR open / merge / comment flows are 38.3 / 38.4. Maestro E2E deferred — flow needs a pre-seeded PR fixture which adds significant Maestro setup with no clear value gain over the 22 ViewModel + use-case tests; reopen if Phase 38.3 surfaces a real interaction-flow regression. **Forward-compat anchors for 38.3**: the `onPullRequestClick: (String) -> Unit` callback is already plumbed through `PullRequestListScreen` + `PullRequestListScreen.swift` (currently no-op) so Phase 38.3 just changes the NavGraph wiring `{ _ -> }` → `{ navController.navigate(PullRequestDetail(prId = it)) }` without touching the screen layer.

- **Phase 38.1**: Pull request data spine (ADR-014 §1, §2, §3, §5, §7) — first code slice of Phase 38, lands the schema + domain + repository + sync + Realtime plumbing without any UI surface. Sets up `pull_requests` and `pull_request_comments` as new sibling tables alongside `chart_revisions`/`chart_branches` from Phase 37.1, plus the `merge_pull_request` SECURITY DEFINER RPC that's the only writer permitted to produce `chart_revisions.author_id != owner_id` rows. **Migration 016** (`016_pull_requests.sql`): `pull_requests` table with FKs to `patterns(id) ON DELETE CASCADE` on both source + target sides, FKs to `chart_branches(id) ON DELETE CASCADE` on both branch sides, and FKs to `chart_revisions(revision_id) ON DELETE RESTRICT` on `source_tip_revision_id` + `common_ancestor_revision_id` (matching the ADR-013 §1 standalone-UNIQUE FK target precedent — `revision_id` is the canonical commit identifier per ADR-008 §6). `merged_revision_id` FK uses `ON DELETE SET NULL` because chart_revisions are immutable (no DELETE policy in migration 015) and the merge result reference can dangle gracefully. `status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'open' CHECK (status IN ('open', 'merged', 'closed'))` is the closed enum (no DRAFT for v1). Partial unique index `WHERE status = 'open'` on `(source_branch_id, target_branch_id)` is INSERT-side only — prevents duplicate OPEN rows for the same branch pair, but allows close-and-reopen indefinitely (the closed rows accumulate; that's the correct audit-trail behavior). Three indexes for the list-screen hot paths: `(target_pattern_id, status, created_at DESC)`, `(source_pattern_id, status, created_at DESC)`, `(author_id, status)`. RLS: SELECT readable by author OR target owner; INSERT requires `author_id = auth.uid() AND source_pattern_id IN (...patterns I own)` plus the **load-bearing** `AND source_pattern_id IN (SELECT id FROM patterns WHERE parent_pattern_id = target_pattern_id)` clause that enforces the v1 fork-routing invariant — without it, an authenticated user could open a PR from any pattern they own against any target pattern UUID. UPDATE policy permits status flips by either party, with `WITH CHECK status IN ('open', 'closed')` so the merge transition (→ 'merged') is reachable only via the SECURITY DEFINER RPC. No DELETE policy — PRs are kept as audit trail, CASCADE on pattern deletion is the only cleanup path. `pull_request_comments` table similar shape: append-only, `length(body) <= 5000` CHECK, RLS gates on PR-participant set. **`merge_pull_request` SECURITY DEFINER RPC** (~70 lines plpgsql): validates PR exists, status='open', caller is target owner (`SELECT 1 FROM patterns WHERE id = v_pr.target_pattern_id AND owner_id = v_caller`); validates strategy in `('squash', 'fast_forward')`; validates source tip unchanged via `SELECT tip_revision_id FROM chart_branches WHERE id = v_pr.source_branch_id` against `v_pr.source_tip_revision_id` (drift = `RAISE EXCEPTION 'Source tip drifted; re-resolve required'`); captures `v_target_tip_pre_merge` from `chart_branches WHERE id = v_pr.target_branch_id` BEFORE the INSERT (HIGH-1 fix from ADR review — without this, the chart_documents UPDATE's subquery against the just-inserted row would silently zero out `parent_revision_id` if the row went missing for any reason); INSERTs the merged revision into `chart_revisions` with `author_id = v_pr.author_id` + `owner_id = v_caller`, threading `v_target_tip_pre_merge` as the new revision's `parent_revision_id` and using `RETURNING parent_revision_id INTO v_inserted_parent_revision_id` to verify the row actually landed (defensive; raises if `IS DISTINCT FROM v_target_tip_pre_merge`). Then UPDATEs `chart_branches.tip_revision_id` for target, UPDATEs `chart_documents` tip pointer for the target pattern, marks PR `status='merged' + merged_revision_id + merged_at = now()`. **Concurrency model**: `FOR UPDATE` on the PR row at the function start serializes concurrent merges — the second caller blocks until the first commits then sees `status='merged'` and bails on the "PR not open" check. The partial unique index prevents duplicate INSERT-side OPEN rows, NOT the merge race; these two mechanisms are complementary, not redundant. Same shape as `delete_own_account` from Phase 17 / ADR-005 — `REVOKE ALL ON FUNCTION ... FROM public; GRANT EXECUTE ... TO authenticated`. Both new tables added to `supabase_realtime` publication. **SQLDelight schemas**: `PullRequest.sq` mirrors the Postgres table with `TEXT` columns + INSERT-OR-REPLACE upsert (PR carries its own `(created_at, updated_at)` timestamps, sync layer treats INSERT and UPDATE both as upsert per ADR-014 §7) + 3 indexes mirroring the Postgres ones. Queries: `getById` / `getByTargetPattern` / `getBySourcePattern` / `getIncomingForOwner` (INNER JOIN on `PatternEntity` to scope by `owner_id` locally — RLS does the same server-side) / `getOutgoingForOwner` / paired observers + `countOpenIncomingForOwner` (Phase 38.2 unread badge) / `upsert` / `updateStatus` (close path) / `deleteById` / `deleteByPatternId` (CASCADE backfill — clears where source OR target matches; called with the same id passed twice to match `WHERE source_pattern_id = ? OR target_pattern_id = ?`). `PullRequestComment.sq`: append-only INSERT OR IGNORE upsert (rather than INSERT OR REPLACE — comments are immutable at RLS so a slightly-different copy arriving via Realtime echo should NOT silently overwrite). Both `.sq` files paired with `6.sqm` containing the SQLite migration. ON DELETE CASCADE on both pattern FKs at SQLite layer + on `pull_request_id` in comments. **Domain**: `PullRequest` data class (Serializable, `@SerialName` mappings) with `mergedRevisionId` / `mergedAt` / `closedAt` nullable + `authorId` nullable per ON DELETE SET NULL contract. `PullRequestStatus` enum (OPEN/MERGED/CLOSED) with `@SerialName("open")` / `("merged")` / `("closed")` matching the Postgres CHECK values verbatim. `PullRequest.canMerge(currentUserId, targetOwnerId)` extension method = `status == OPEN && currentUserId == targetOwnerId` — UI-affordance-only gate; the RPC's `WHERE owner_id = v_caller` clause is the actual security boundary (KDoc explicit about caller-supplies-correct-targetOwnerId contract). `PullRequestComment` data class (immutable, append-only). **Mappers**: `PullRequestMapper.kt` — `PullRequestEntity.toDomain()` + `PullRequestCommentEntity.toDomain()` + exhaustive `String.toPullRequestStatus()` (3-way `when` with hard `error()` for unknown wire values — defensive against future migrations adding a 4th status, hard fail beats silent fall-through to OPEN) + `PullRequestStatus.toDbString()` (3-way `when`, no else). **Repository**: `PullRequestRepository` interface ships 11 methods covering Phase 38.2/38.3 read-side + Phase 38.1 write-side. **Merge is NOT a repository method** per ADR-014 §5 — Phase 38.4 wires the RPC through a dedicated `MergePullRequestUseCase` that bypasses the local-then-sync orchestration (the RPC is the only writer permitted to produce author_id != owner_id rows; the caller cannot pre-write a stub locally and reconcile, so the standard local-first pattern doesn't apply). `PullRequestRepositoryImpl` follows the local-first / remote-fallback / sync-or-enqueue pattern from `ChartRevisionRepositoryImpl`. `closePullRequest` preserves a caller-supplied `closedAt` if present (idempotent re-close) and stamps a fresh `updatedAt = Clock.System.now()`. `observeIncomingForOwner`/`observeOutgoingForOwner` are local-only flows — KDoc explicitly documents the cold-launch seeding contract: callers should invoke `getIncomingForOwner` first to backfill the cache, then collect this Flow for live updates (Realtime keeps the cache warm thereafter). **Local data source**: `LocalPullRequestDataSource` with `withContext(ioDispatcher)` wrapping every query, separate `prQueries` + `commentQueries` accessors. **Remote data source**: `RemotePullRequestDataSource` implements both `RemotePullRequestSyncOperations` + `RemotePullRequestCommentSyncOperations` — single class, dual interface (matches the Phase 4b sharing precedent where RemoteShare combined ops). `getIncomingForOwner` does a two-step fetch: first the owner's pattern ids via `Columns.raw("id")` projection, then PRs targeting any of them via `isIn("target_pattern_id", patternIds)`. RLS already restricts visibility to participant set, but the explicit pattern-id filter is the semantically-correct "incoming" scope. Two-step is acceptable for 38.1 (no UI consumer yet); when 38.2 hot-path lands, consider promoting to a server-side view or RPC. `upsert` uses `onConflict = "id"` for PR-row idempotency; `appendComment` uses `ignoreDuplicates = true` because comments are immutable at RLS so a re-enqueued append should silently no-op (matches the `RemoteChartRevisionDataSource.append` precedent from Phase 37.1). **Sync wiring**: `SyncEntityType.PULL_REQUEST` + `PULL_REQUEST_COMMENT` enum values added. `SyncExecutor` exhaustively routes both: PR INSERT/UPDATE → `remote.upsert(pr)` (idempotent on id; status → MERGED transitions via the RPC and is NOT enqueued through PendingSync); PR DELETE silent no-op `return true` (PRs are audit trail; SyncManager never enqueues this — defensive fall-through matches `executeChartRevision`'s pattern). PR_COMMENT INSERT → `remote.appendComment(comment)`; UPDATE/DELETE silent no-op (RLS forbids; same precedent). New `RemotePullRequestSyncOperations` + `RemotePullRequestCommentSyncOperations` interfaces in `RemoteSyncOperations.kt` — split into two because the comment surface is append-only and shouldn't carry an `upsert` method, even though the production `RemotePullRequestDataSource` implements both. **Realtime**: `RealtimeSyncManager` gains 6th + 7th channels `pull-requests-incoming-<ownerId>` + `pull-requests-outgoing-<ownerId>` (per ADR-014 §7). Outgoing channel uses `ChangeFilter("author_id", ownerId)` for clean server-side scoping. Incoming channel uses **NO client-side filter** — single-eq `ChangeFilter` cannot express "target_pattern_id IN owned_patterns" (only equality is supported); RLS scopes the broadcast to PRs where the user is participant (author OR target owner) per migration 016. Both channels feed `handlePullRequestAction` which upserts via the local data source. INSERT OR REPLACE on `id` makes the dual-channel delivery idempotent — outgoing PRs get delivered through both the outgoing AND incoming channels (since they pass RLS as participant), causing 2x bandwidth on outgoing events; acceptable for v1 per ADR-014 Negative §2 channel-budget concerns, revisit consolidation if Phase 39 closed beta surfaces a connection cap. DELETE handler uses per-row `deleteById(old.id)` (NOT `deleteByPatternId` like the chart_revisions handler) because a PR sits at the join of two patterns (source + target) and Postgres emits one DELETE event per cascaded PR row — bulk-clear by pattern_id would over-delete; the asymmetry vs chart_revisions is deliberate and documented inline. The dynamic per-PR comments channel `pull-request-comments-<prId>` lands in Phase 38.3 alongside `PullRequestDetailScreen` and is NOT managed by `RealtimeSyncManager` (opened/closed on view lifecycle). `localPullRequest` ctor param is nullable with `null` default + a guard in `subscribe` — keeps existing test call-sites valid. **Koin DI**: `RepositoryModule` registers `LocalPullRequestDataSource` + `RemotePullRequestDataSource` (only when Supabase configured) + `PullRequestRepositoryImpl` as `single<PullRequestRepository>`. `SyncModule` registers both sync-ops aliases pointing at the same `RemotePullRequestDataSource` instance + threads `remotePullRequest` + `remotePullRequestComment` through `SyncExecutor` + threads `localPullRequest` through `RealtimeSyncManager`. **Tests (+32 commonTest, 1033 → 1065 — top of ADR §8's +25–35 target band)**: `PullRequestMapperTest` (6 tests) covers entity round-trip for all 3 statuses + lifecycle timestamps + unknown-status hard-fail + enum<->db exhaustive map + `canMerge` permutations. `PullRequestRepositoryImplTest` (15 tests) covers open/close/post paths, sync enqueue contracts, description + authorId round-trip, case-sensitive id lookup, incoming-vs-outgoing scoping (with seeded `LocalPatternDataSource` for the pattern-owner JOIN), local-only `observeIncomingForOwner` ordering, comment scoping + ascending order, comment INSERT-OR-IGNORE idempotency on Realtime echo, and the MERGED PR Realtime-echo round-trip preserving `mergedRevisionId` + `mergedAt`. `SyncExecutorTest` gains 7 PR-branch tests covering null-remote no-op, INSERT/UPDATE upsert dispatch, DELETE silent no-op, remote-failure propagation for retry, comment INSERT append, and forbidden-comment-UPDATE/DELETE silent-success. `RealtimeSyncManagerPullRequestTest` (4 tests, separate class — doesn't widen the existing test helper signature) covers the 7-channel subscribe count, outgoing `author_id` filter, incoming-no-filter RLS-driven path, and unsubscribe lifecycle. New test fakes: `FakeRemotePullRequestDataSource` implements both sync-ops interfaces with separate fail-flags. Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 3 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass. **HIGH** (Realtime DELETE handler comment claimed "bulk-clear PRs for the pattern" but the implementation calls `deleteById(old.id)` per-row, creating a documentation/intent mismatch that would mislead a future reader) fixed by rewriting the doc comment to accurately reflect the per-row delete semantics + name the chart_revisions vs PR asymmetry: PRs sit at a join of two patterns so per-row delete is the correct shape, while chart_revisions has a single parent so bulk-clear-by-pattern-id is fine. **MEDIUM-1** (`getIncomingForOwner` two-step remote fetch is N+1-adjacent — first the owner's patterns, then PRs filtered by those ids) acknowledged as acceptable for Phase 38.1 (no UI consumer yet); will become a hot path in Phase 38.2 and merits a server-side view or RPC then. **MEDIUM-2** (no server-side `updated_at` trigger on `pull_requests` — the client clock stamps `updated_at` on close) acknowledged as consistent with how other repositories behave in this codebase (e.g. `ProjectRepositoryImpl`); not a regression. **MEDIUM-3** (`observeIncomingForOwner` is local-only with no remote seed — cold launch with empty cache emits empty list before Realtime backfills) fixed by adding a KDoc note on the interface explicitly documenting the cold-launch seeding contract: callers should invoke `getIncomingForOwner` first. **LOW-1** (`canMerge` doesn't validate that `targetOwnerId` matches `targetPatternId`, trusts the caller — a ViewModel passing the wrong owner id silently flips the gate) fixed by adding a "Caller contract" KDoc paragraph naming the resolution path + the RPC's `WHERE owner_id = v_caller` clause as the actual security boundary. **LOW-2** (Realtime DELETE comment for incoming channel — same root cause as HIGH) addressed via the HIGH fix. **LOW-3** (`assertFalse(... .isNotEmpty())` double-negation in SyncExecutorTest reads awkwardly) fixed by switching to `assertTrue(... .isEmpty())`. **Append-then-update non-atomicity** (ADR-014 Consequences inherited from ADR-013): the merge RPC is atomic server-side via `FOR UPDATE` + transactional `INSERT` + 3 UPDATEs in one function body, so unlike `chart_revisions.append + chart_documents UPDATE` which is two PendingSync entries that can race, the merge transaction either lands fully or doesn't land at all. PR open/close still go through the standard local-then-sync path which has the usual best-effort-eventually-consistent semantics; that's acceptable because PR state is not load-bearing for diff correctness (the RPC re-validates `source_tip_revision_id` against the live tip at merge time and raises if drifted). **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-014 §8**: PR list / detail / merge UI all in 38.2 / 38.3 / 38.4; `MergePullRequestUseCase` (the RPC invocation) in 38.4; conflict detection algorithm + `ChartConflictResolutionScreen` in 38.4; per-PR comments Realtime channel in 38.3. No use cases ship in 38.1 — `PullRequestRepository`'s methods exist but no caller exercises them yet. No i18n keys (data layer; no user-visible surface). Pre-push invariants all green: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1065 tests, +32 from 1033 baseline), `:shared:koverVerify`, `bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` (301 keys, unchanged — 38.1 is data-layer, no i18n surface). **Forward-compat anchors for 38.2**: the local SQLDelight `getIncomingForOwner` query JOINs PatternEntity for owner scoping, so a future "unread badge count" derives from `countOpenIncomingForOwner(ownerId)` directly; the parametric Realtime channels can be filtered locally by status without server-side changes when the unread-mark mechanism lands. 38.3's per-PR comments channel will reuse the existing `ChannelHandle` abstraction with no new infrastructure.

- **Phase 38.0**: ADR-014 cut for pull-request workflow — opens Phase 38 with the data-model + UX shape decided before any code lands. ADR sized at ~1000 lines EN + ~125 line JA summary (matches the ADR-013 EN+JA-summary precedent; bigger than ADR-013's 801 because Phase 38 has more design surface — multi-author writes, RPC atomicity, conflict resolution UI, comment thread, merge strategy). **Key decisions resolved by the agent team**: (1) New `pull_requests` + `pull_request_comments` tables; PR is its own entity with FKs to `patterns` and `chart_branches` on both sides + a `common_ancestor_revision_id` snapshot captured at PR open time. The repurpose-`chart_revisions` alternative was rejected because it conflates commit history with PR routing. (2) Server-side `merge_pull_request` RPC running with `SECURITY DEFINER` is the **only** writer that can produce `author_id != owner_id` rows. ADR-013 deferred RPCs as "revisit if telemetry shows divergence"; Phase 38 is the trigger because Phase 38 needs atomicity that's user-observable, not just "best-effort eventually consistent" like Phase 37's tip pointer. The function takes `FOR UPDATE` on the PR row to serialize concurrent merge attempts; the partial unique index on `(source_branch_id, target_branch_id) WHERE status = 'open'` prevents INSERT-side duplicate OPEN PRs. These two mechanisms are complementary, not redundant. The function precedent is `delete_own_account` from Phase 17 / ADR-005. (3) **Squash is the default merge strategy**. Fast-forward auto-applies when applicable (resolved doc byte-equal to source tip's doc, no target-side divergence) but is detection-only — v1 still produces a 1-parent commit row so the testing surface stays bounded. Multi-parent merge-commit rejected because `chart_revisions.parent_revision_id` is single-valued; supporting it would force a schema redesign. Knitters do not benefit from multi-parent visualization. (4) **New `ChartConflictResolutionScreen`**, NOT a mode of `ChartDiffScreen`. ChartDiffScreen is read-only and 2-pane (base vs target); conflict resolution is interactive and 3-pane (ancestor pinned + theirs vs mine + per-cell picker). Reusing ChartDiffScreen would require adding interaction + a third-pane mode — bigger change than a new screen. The conflict-detection algorithm is a pure 3-way wrapper over the existing Phase 37 §5 cell-level diff (`ConflictDetector(ancestor, theirs, mine): ConflictReport`), shared between platforms. (5) **Approval shape collapses to merge / close**. v1 has no concept of "team" / "collaborator role"; the target owner is the implicit and sole approver, the merge button itself IS the approval action, the close button IS the rejection action. Comments are informational discussion, not gates. Required-approval is post-v1. (6) **One `PullRequestListScreen(filter: Incoming | Outgoing)`** parameterized — same data model, two perspectives. Avoid building two screens. (7) Realtime fan-out grows from 5 → 7 owner-scoped channels (`pull-requests-incoming-<ownerId>` + `pull-requests-outgoing-<ownerId>`) plus a dynamic `pull-request-comments-<prId>` opened only while PullRequestDetailScreen is on screen. (8) **Plain text only** for PR title / description / comments — Markdown rendering is render-target divergence between Compose `Text` and SwiftUI `Text` and there is no shared sanitizer in the codebase; soft 200 / 2000 / 5000 char limits enforced UI-side. **Phase 38 sub-slice plan** (locked in as ADR §8): 38.0 (this ADR, no code) → 38.1 (`pull_requests` + `pull_request_comments` schema, `merge_pull_request` RPC, domain `PullRequest` / `PullRequestStatus` / `PullRequestComment`, `PullRequestRepository` local + remote + impl, sync wiring, Realtime channels — no UI; +25–35 commonTest, migration 016) → 38.2 (`GetIncomingPullRequestsUseCase` / `GetOutgoingPullRequestsUseCase`, `PullRequestListViewModel`, `PullRequestListScreen` Compose+SwiftUI, entry points from ProjectList overflow + ProjectDetail; read-only — no PR open flow yet; +10 commonTest, 9 i18n keys) → 38.3 (`GetPullRequestUseCase`, `GetPullRequestCommentsUseCase`, `PostPullRequestCommentUseCase`, `OpenPullRequestUseCase`, `ClosePullRequestUseCase`, `PullRequestDetailViewModel`, `PullRequestDetailScreen`, "Open PR" entry from ChartViewer overflow on a forked pattern — no merge yet; +20–25 commonTest, 14 i18n keys) → 38.4 (`ConflictDetector` algorithm, `ConflictResolutionViewModel`, `ChartConflictResolutionScreen`, `MergePullRequestUseCase` invoking the RPC, merge wiring from PullRequestDetailScreen "Merge" button; +20 commonTest, 9 i18n keys). Slices 38.2 / 38.3 / 38.4 form a coherent flow: list → detail → merge. Slipping 38.4 out of MVP is acceptable (read-only review with merge gated behind "Coming soon"); slipping 38.3 leaves the list inert; slipping 38.2 leaves the data spine unobservable. **Forward-compat anchors for post-v1**: `author_id` becoming non-trivial sets up multi-author diff blame ("who last touched this cell"); the merge RPC pattern is reusable for any future cross-table atomic write; the conflict-detection helper sits one layer above the diff algorithm so a future "preview merge" affordance reuses it. **Explicitly NOT in Phase 38 MVP**: "Pull from upstream" affordance on a forked chart (Phase 38+; PR flow runs source → target only), required-approval gates / branch protection, cross-fork PR routing (PR target is always `source.parentPatternId` per ADR-012 §1), multi-author diff blame (Phase 38+ build atop populated `author_id`), CRDT concurrent editing (post-v1), cherry-pick / rebase / squash-with-fixup / amend, multi-parent merge-commit, editing past comments, draft PR state, PR templates / saved descriptions, comment reactions, @-mentions + push notifications, markdown / formatted comments, merge-conflict re-resolution after source drift mid-resolution (resolver re-enters with new source tip; v1 surfaces a generic error), in-detail diff at full pan/zoom (the embedded preview links out to the existing Phase 37.3 ChartDiffScreen). Realtime channel count growth from 5 → 7 (+1 dynamic per-PR while detail is open) is bounded; if Phase 39 closed beta surfaces a free-tier connection cap, channels coalesce then. **Code review**: 0 CRITICAL / 2 HIGH / 3 MEDIUM / 2 LOW first pass — all 7 fixed pre-commit. **HIGH-1** (silent NULL hazard in the merge RPC's `chart_documents` UPDATE — the original subquery `SELECT parent_revision_id FROM chart_revisions WHERE revision_id = v_new_revision_id` would silently return NULL and zero out `chart_documents.parent_revision_id` if the just-INSERTed row went missing for any reason) fixed by capturing the target's pre-merge tip into a local `v_target_tip_pre_merge` BEFORE the INSERT, threading it as the INSERT's `parent_revision_id` value, and using `INSERT ... RETURNING parent_revision_id INTO v_inserted_parent_revision_id` to verify the row landed; the chart_documents UPDATE then reads the local directly with no subquery dependency. **HIGH-2** (concurrency model documentation — the `FOR UPDATE` lock on the PR row is what prevents double-merge race, NOT the partial unique index which is INSERT-side only) fixed by adding an explicit "Concurrency model" paragraph in §5 of the ADR before the SECURITY DEFINER paragraph that distinguishes the two mechanisms as complementary. **MEDIUM-1** (`pull_requests` INSERT RLS did not actually enforce the "PR target must be source's upstream" invariant the ADR text claims — without this clause, an authenticated user could open a PR from any pattern they own against any target pattern they happened to know the UUID of) fixed by adding `AND source_pattern_id IN (SELECT id FROM public.patterns WHERE parent_pattern_id = target_pattern_id)` to the INSERT WITH CHECK clause; this also implicitly rejects internal cross-branch PRs within the same pattern, matching the ADR's "v1 routes PRs only fork → upstream" stance. **MEDIUM-2** (38.3 test budget at +15 was tight — five use cases + ViewModel needs 18–29 tests by precedent from Phase 36.3 / 37.2) fixed by bumping to +20–25, with a parallel update on the JA summary table. **MEDIUM-3** (JA summary omitted `common_ancestor_revision_id` from the column list, so an implementer reading only the JA for 38.1 would miss a required NOT NULL column + its client-side computation logic) fixed by reflowing the JA §1 schema bullet to include the column and the new fork-relationship RLS clause. **LOW-1** (fast-forward strategy description contradicted the implementation note — first paragraph defined FF as "tip-pointer move with no new revision row", second paragraph said v1 always produces a squash commit) fixed by rewording: v1 FF is "the resulting squash revision's document is byte-identical to source_tip's document — no conflicts, no target-side divergence", still produces a new revision row, with explicit note that true Git-style FF is reserved as a SQL enum value but no client path exercises it in 38.4. **LOW-2** (FK target `chart_revisions(revision_id)` not `chart_revisions(id)` deserved a comment so future readers don't "fix" it back to the PK) fixed by adding an inline comment documenting that the FK targets the standalone UNIQUE per ADR-013 §1 and matches the `chart_branches.tip_revision_id` precedent. Pre-push invariants green (`bash scripts/verify-i18n-keys.sh` — 301 keys, unchanged since this slice is doc-only). 1033 shared tests (unchanged — no code touched). **Scope cut**: PR open / close / merge / comment use cases land in 38.3 / 38.4; no migration ships in this slice. Migration 016 lands in 38.1 alongside the schema + RPC.


## Phase 39.x — Closed-beta tester rubric + F2 bug-reporting (closed)

- **Phase 39.5**: F2 bug-report submission flow + gesture triggers (per ADR-015 §3 + §6) — closes Phase 39.x. Surfaces the diagnostic data the 39.3 `EventRingBuffer` has been quietly accumulating: a tester who hits a bug shakes the iPhone (or 3-finger-long-presses on Android, or taps Settings → Beta → "Send Feedback" on either platform), reviews the auto-assembled GitHub Issue body, and submits to `https://github.com/b150005/skeinly/issues/new?template=beta-bug.yml&title=...&body=...`. **`BugSubmissionLauncher` `expect/actual`** at `shared/.../platform/`: Android actual builds the URL via `URLEncoder.encode(value, "UTF-8")` + `Intent(ACTION_VIEW, Uri.parse(url)).addFlags(FLAG_ACTIVITY_NEW_TASK)` (the FLAG is required because Koin injects the application Context); iOS actual builds via `NSURLComponents` + `NSURLQueryItem` + `UIApplication.sharedApplication.openURL` per ADR §3 — **NOT** `String.addingPercentEncoding(.urlQueryAllowed)` which silently fails to encode `&` / `=` / `?` (the `.urlQueryAllowed` character set is intended for pre-formed query strings, wrong tool for individual-component encoding; a freeform description containing `&` would silently truncate the body parameter at the GitHub-side parser; this gotcha is the exact reason `NSURLComponents` is the only correct shape, documented inline). **`DeviceContextProvider` `expect/actual`** at `shared/.../platform/`: read-only OS / device / locale / app-version surface. Android actual reads via `PackageManager.getPackageInfo` + `Build.MANUFACTURER`/`Build.MODEL`/`Build.VERSION.RELEASE`/`Locale.getDefault().toLanguageTag()`; iOS actual reads `Bundle.main.objectForInfoDictionaryKey("CFBundleShortVersionString")` + `UIDevice.currentDevice.systemVersion` + `NSLocale.currentLocale.localeIdentifier.replace("_", "-")` (NSLocale uses underscore separator; BCP 47 uses hyphen, so we normalize to match Android). **DeviceContext DTO seam**: `DeviceContext` data class + `DeviceContextProvider.snapshotContext()` extension under the same package. The ViewModel takes the DTO + a `(String, String) -> Unit` lambda rather than the `expect class` provider/launcher directly because expect/actual classes bridge to `final class` on each platform — commonTest cannot subclass them. The DI boundary owns the adaptation: `provider.snapshotContext()` + `launcher::launch`. **Pure formatter** `formatBugReportBody(description, events, posthogDistinctId, appVersion, osVersion, deviceModel, locale, platformName, timestamp)` at `shared/.../data/bug/BugReportBodyFormatter.kt`. Output shape matches ADR-015 §3 verbatim minus a per-event "Time" column (the EventRingBuffer was deliberately simplified after the ADR cut to drop per-emission `Clock.System.now()` calls; the surrounding "Timestamp:" field still anchors triage). **Privacy invariant (load-bearing)**: reads `event.name` + `event.properties` only, never `event.toString()` — `data class` toString leaks Kotlin FQN + hidden constructor params. Pipe + newline escaping in `escapeMarkdownPipe` is defense-in-depth (every current AnalyticsEvent variant's wireValue is a closed-enum identifier that structurally cannot contain `|` or newlines, but the helper protects future variants); promoted to `internal` so commonTest can reach it directly without subclassing the sealed AnalyticsEvent hierarchy from a different package (Kotlin/Native rejects sealed-extension across packages). PostHog distinct_id passed as `String?` and stubbed null in this slice — Phase 39.5 ships without PostHog SDK distinctId resolution plumbed through the shared layer; formatter renders `_Not available (PostHog SDK not initialized)._` so triagers know to skip the PostHog cross-reference attempt. **`BugReportPreviewViewModel`** at `shared/.../ui/bugreport/`: state holds user-edited description (capped at 4000 chars), pre-rendered Markdown body that re-renders on every keystroke so the user sees what'll be submitted, and `isSubmitting` flag. Submit dispatches title computation (first non-blank line of description, capped at 80 chars + "..." overflow indicator, "[Beta] " prefix; empty description yields default "[Beta] Bug report") + final body render + `submit(title, body)` lambda call. Re-snapshots the `EventRingBuffer` at submission time (vs. relying on the post-init snapshot) so any events captured between init and the user's tap are included. **`BugReportPreviewScreen`** Compose at `shared/.../ui/bugreport/`: Scaffold + TopAppBar with back nav + disclosure copy describing what'll be attached + `OutlinedTextField` for description (minLines=4, maxLines=12) + `SelectionContainer`-wrapped read-only preview of the body (lets a curious tester copy individual lines without forcing them through the GitHub hand-off; styling distinct from the editable description above so the boundary is visible) + filled-prominent "Submit on GitHub" button + bordered Cancel. testTags: `bugReportPreviewScreen` (root), `bugDescriptionField`, `bugReportPreviewBody`, `submitBugReportButton`, `cancelBugReportButton`. **iOS SwiftUI mirror** at `iosApp/iosApp/Screens/BugReportPreviewScreen.swift` uses the established `ScopedViewModel` holder pattern. SwiftUI `axis: .vertical` + `lineLimit(4...12)` mirrors the Compose minLines/maxLines. `Text(verbatim: state.previewBody)` + `.textSelection(.enabled)` mirrors the SelectionContainer. `.borderedProminent` Submit + `.bordered` Cancel + `role: .cancel` for the Cancel button so VoiceOver announces it correctly. **Android 3-finger long-press detector** in `MainActivity.dispatchTouchEvent` per ADR-015 §1: 500ms threshold matches Compose `combinedClickable` long-press default (Phase 39.0.2 Sprint B M6 swipe-context-menu precedent). Why root-level dispatch: nested Composables (LazyList, swipe containers) consume multi-touch sequences before the outer pointer-input modifier can observe them. `dispatchTouchEvent` runs **before** the view-tree hit test so the detector sees every pointer regardless of which descendant ultimately handles the gesture. Gated on `BuildFlags.isBeta && analyticsPrefs.analyticsOptIn.value` — both gates short-circuit on the fast path so the dispatch overhead on production is a single boolean read per touch event. Returns `true` (consume) only on the qualifying long-press emission so the still-down 3-finger contact does not resume scroll/zoom on the underlying surface. Reset state pre-navigation so a long-running navigate hand-off cannot re-fire the detector during the same gesture. **iOS shake bridge** at `iosApp/iosApp/Core/ShakeDetection.swift`: deliberate ADR-015 §1 deviation. The ADR's prescription was `ShakeDetectingController : UIHostingController` subclass installed in `SceneDelegate`. Skeinly's iOS app uses pure SwiftUI `App` lifecycle (no SceneDelegate, no UIHostingController exposed at the surface), so the prescribed shape does not directly fit. The idiomatic SwiftUI App equivalent is a `UIWindow.motionEnded` extension (`open class extension override`) that posts an `NSNotification` plus a `ViewModifier` that subscribes via `onReceive(NotificationCenter.default.publisher(...))`. This is the pattern Apple's SwiftUI WWDC samples use; UIWindow is the root responder for motion events in SwiftUI App lifecycle the same way SceneDelegate's hosting controller is when you opt into UIKit lifecycle. Documented as a deliberate ADR deviation in the file's header comment block. **Settings call sites** (Phase 39.4 left as no-op stubs): Compose NavGraph `composable<Settings>` block plumbs `onSendFeedback = { navController.navigate(BugReportPreview) }`; iOS `AppRouter.destinationView(for: .settings)` plumbs `SettingsScreen(onSendFeedback: { path.append(Route.bugReportPreview) })`. New `BugReportPreview` Serializable `data object` route + matching `composable<BugReportPreview>` block on Compose; new `Route.bugReportPreview` case + Hashable conformance + `destinationView` mapping on iOS. **iOS shake handler** at `AppRootView.body`: `.onShake { guard BuildFlags.isBeta && KoinHelperKt.analyticsOptInValue() else { return }; path.append(Route.bugReportPreview) }`. New synchronous `KoinHelperKt.analyticsOptInValue(): Boolean` accessor avoids the Kotlin/Native `Boolean` → `KotlinBoolean` (`.boolValue` access) bridging surface that observers see. No top-of-path dedup: NavigationPath does not expose a typed peek, and a duplicate preview stack is harmless — Cancel pops one, the prior view stays underneath. **i18n** (6 new keys, 391 total): `title_bug_report_preview` ("Send Feedback" / "フィードバックを送信" — same as the Settings entry per role-prefix discipline since the screen is itself the "Send Feedback" surface), `label_bug_description`, `hint_bug_description_placeholder` (with U+2026 ellipsis per Phase 33.x convention), `label_bug_report_preview_body` ("Diagnostic body to be attached" / "添付される診断情報"), `body_bug_report_includes_actions` (the disclosure copy that names everything getting attached + everything explicitly NOT — "no patterns, notes, photos, or PII"), `action_submit_bug_report` ("Submit on GitHub" / "GitHub で送信"). Reuses `action_back` / `action_cancel`. **Tests (+25 commonTest, 1241 → 1266)**: `BugReportBodyFormatterTest` (13 cases — section headers in order, description verbatim render, blank-description renders blank line under header so triagers see "section was empty" not "section missing", reproduction context lists every field, empty events renders explicit `_No actions captured_` disclosure + suppresses table chrome, populated events render proper table headers + rows, outcome event with no screen property renders em-dash columns, parametric outcome event does NOT leak `data class` toString into the table, posthog distinct_id null vs present branches, escapeMarkdownPipe pipe-escaping + newline-collapse + identity on safe strings, formatter is pure-deterministic). `BugReportPreviewViewModelTest` (12 cases — init renders empty preview with empty buffer, description-changed updates state + re-renders, description capped at 4000, submit invokes launcher with title + body, empty description uses default title, overlong first line truncated to title cap with "..." overflow, blank first line skipped, submit re-snapshots buffer so post-init events are included, refresh-preview re-runs against current snapshot, isSubmitting toggles back off after launch returns, preview body carries device context lines). All new test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **iOS test build green**: `xcodebuild build-for-testing` reports `** TEST BUILD SUCCEEDED **`. The iOS test target deliberately excludes `Core/Bridging/` (per the project.yml convention block) because that subdirectory holds Swift files importing the `Shared` framework which the `iosAppTests` target does not link. **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1266 tests, +25 from 1241 baseline — at upper end of ADR-015 §6's +10–15 estimate, overshoot reflects 13 formatter tests + 12 ViewModel tests; the formatter has more behavior surface than estimated due to escape/empty-state/null-distinct_id branches), `:shared:koverVerify`, `verifyI18nKeys` (391 keys, +6). iOS app + test BUILD SUCCEEDED. **Forward-compat anchors**: PostHog distinct_id stub (current null) is the only piece of the §3 body shape not yet plumbed through; a follow-up slice can extend `DeviceContext` (or add a sibling `TelemetrySessionId` accessor) without touching the formatter or ViewModel. The `BugSubmissionLauncher` URL pattern is the integration seam for any future "report by email" / "report via TestFlight feedback" alternate-submission path — pivot the lambda at the DI boundary, ViewModel + screen unchanged. **Closes Phase 39.x sub-slices**: 39.0 (rubric), 39.1 (ADR), 39.2 (build-flag), 39.3 (analytics + ring buffer), 39.4 (consent UI), 39.5 (gestures + submission). The Closed Beta launch gate (Phase 39.0 prep entry below) is now genuinely unblocked on the F2 dimension; remaining HARD-GATE items are the migration 016 prod verify, Android VERSION_CODE bump, TestFlight artifact validation, and tester invites.

- **Phase 39.4**: F2 onboarding consent UI + Settings → Beta section + `EventRingBuffer.clear()` (per ADR-015 §6) — third code-bearing slice of Phase 39.x. Closes the consent-UI gap before 39.5's bug-report submission flow lands; first user-visible Phase 39 surface (39.2 + 39.3 were pure infrastructure / data-layer). **`EventRingBuffer.clear()`** at `shared/.../data/analytics/EventRingBuffer.kt`: mutex-locked + idempotent on empty buffer. The clear path runs from `SettingsViewModel` when the user toggles diagnostic-data sharing OFF — drops any pre-revoke trail before a follow-up bug report can attach it. The mutex serializes against the in-flight `SharedFlow` collector in `start(scope)` so a concurrent emit cannot land into a buffer that was nominally cleared. **`OnboardingViewModel` extension**: optional `analyticsPreferences: AnalyticsPreferences? = null` + new `includeBetaConsent: Boolean = false` ctor flag wires a 4th carousel page on beta builds only. New `SetAnalyticsOptIn(value: Boolean)` event writes through to `analyticsPreferences.setAnalyticsOptIn(value)`; init-block observer mirrors the persisted value back into state via `prefs.analyticsOptIn.collect { value -> _state.update { it.copy(analyticsOptIn = value) } }` so a hypothetical external write (Settings toggle while onboarding is mounted — impossible today, defensive for the future) reflects in the UI. Defaults preserve existing test call-site compat (every prior `OnboardingViewModel(...)` constructor call stays valid). State seeded from `analyticsPreferences?.analyticsOptIn?.value ?: false` at init so the toggle paints in its correct position when an already-consented user re-enters onboarding (rare; only happens via a "Reset onboarding" debug path that doesn't ship publicly). **`OnboardingScreen.kt` + `OnboardingScreen.swift`**: render the `iconName == "diagnostic_data"` sentinel page with title (`title_diagnostic_consent`) + body (`body_diagnostic_consent`) + Toggle row + small explanation. **Sentinel-keyed (not index-keyed)** so a future 5th page does not silently break the consent surface — adding e.g. an `OnboardingPage(iconName = "video_intro")` between Library and Diagnostic Consent would shift indices but the renderer's `iconName == "diagnostic_data"` lookup remains stable. The sentinel design is documented inline at `OnboardingScreen.kt:65-69` and mirrored at `OnboardingScreen.swift:7-10`. **`SettingsScreen.kt`**: Privacy section gated behind `if (BuildFlags.isBeta)`, header renamed `label_privacy_section` → `label_beta_section` (the rename reflects "this section only exists on beta builds; what's gated here is beta-only feedback infrastructure, not general privacy"), new "Send Feedback" `ListItem` (callback `onSendFeedback: () -> Unit = {}` — no-op stub today; Phase 39.5 wires it to the `BugReportPreviewScreen` route + GitHub Issue prefill flow). `SettingsScreen.swift` mirrors the Beta Section + footer using the same `BuildFlags.isBeta` Swift accessor that Phase 39.2 wired. **`SettingsViewModel` extension**: optional `eventRingBuffer: EventRingBuffer? = null` ctor param. On `SetAnalyticsOptIn(false)` event, calls `viewModelScope.launch { eventRingBuffer?.clear() }` BEFORE the persisted preference flip — under the single-threaded Main dispatcher the suspension yields to the preference write, so the ordering visible to a concurrent bug-report snapshot is "events drained, opt-in OFF" (never "opt-in OFF + stale events still in buffer"). Toggle-on path does NOT clear the buffer (no privacy reason to drop existing events when the user re-grants consent). Phase 39.4 is the first slice that exercises the `eventRingBuffer.clear()` API; the buffer was added in 39.3 as `snapshot()`-only. **`ViewModelModule`**: explicit `viewModel { }` blocks introduced for both `OnboardingViewModel` + `SettingsViewModel` (replacing the auto-resolution `viewModelOf(::Class)` pattern) so the new optional deps are visible at the DI site, and `BuildFlags.isBeta` threads as `includeBetaConsent` for OnboardingViewModel. The auto-resolution form would have silently passed null for the optional params; the explicit form documents the wiring. **i18n** — 7 new keys + 3 stale renames across 3 sources (385 keys total, +12 from the 373 baseline that 39.3 left untouched; 39.3 added zero keys since it was data-layer-only): new keys `title_diagnostic_consent` / `body_diagnostic_consent` (4th onboarding page copy), `label_beta_section` (Settings header — replaces `label_privacy_section`), `label_diagnostic_data_sharing` / `body_diagnostic_data_explanation` (Settings + onboarding toggle row), `action_send_feedback` (Settings ListItem), `body_diagnostic_data_offer` (onboarding toggle subhead). Renamed-out: `label_privacy_section` / `label_allow_analytics` / `body_analytics_explanation` (the pre-39.4 framing was "usage analytics" but what we collect on beta is **diagnostic** data, not generalized usage tracking — the rename matches the privacy policy update that Phase 39.2 shipped). JA semantically diverges where natural: `body_diagnostic_data_explanation` reads ベータ版改善のため (for beta improvement) rather than the literal "to help us improve". **Tests (+9 commonTest, 1232 → 1241)**: `EventRingBufferTest` gains 2 cases (clear-empties-buffer / clear-on-empty-is-idempotent). `OnboardingViewModelTest` gains 5 cases (default `includeBetaConsent = false` produces 3 pages + `true` produces 4, persisted-init reads from `AnalyticsPreferences` value, `SetAnalyticsOptIn(true)` writes through to the prefs, state mirror updates from external flow emission, null-prefs constructor leaves toggle in default-OFF). `SettingsViewModelTest` gains 2 cases (toggle-OFF clears the EventRingBuffer before flipping the persisted preference; toggle-ON does NOT clear). Test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens / commas / apostrophes in backticks). **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1241 tests, +9 from 1232 baseline), `:shared:koverVerify`, `verifyI18nKeys` (385 keys). iOS `xcodebuild ... build` ✅. **Forward-compat anchor for 39.5**: `SettingsScreen`'s `onSendFeedback` callback is plumbed all the way through DI + NavGraph but currently no-op — Phase 39.5 just changes the NavGraph wiring `{ }` → `{ navController.navigate(BugReportPreview) }`. Same shape on iOS (`AppRouter.destinationView(for: .settings)` callback). The `EventRingBuffer.clear()` API now has a single caller (`SettingsViewModel.SetAnalyticsOptIn(false)`); 39.5 will optionally add a second caller path if a "discard pending bug report" affordance lands inside `BugReportPreviewScreen`. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-015 §6**: bug-report gesture detection (Android 3-finger long-press / iOS shake) + `BugReportPreviewScreen` Compose+SwiftUI + `BugSubmissionLauncher` `expect/actual` + `DeviceContextProvider` `expect/actual` + Markdown body formatter + 6 new i18n keys all in 39.5 — Phase 39.4 deliberately ships the consent UI without any way to *invoke* the bug report flow yet, so a tester who toggles the consent ON and immediately tries to file a report in this slice has nothing to tap. That's by design — the consent moment is the user-visible commitment, the gesture / submission UX lands as 39.5 alongside the routing.

- **Phase 39.3**: F2 PostHog wiring + screen/click instrumentation + bug-report event trail (per ADR-015 §6) — second code-bearing slice of Phase 39.x, finally observable to PostHog dashboards. **Sealed-interface extension** at `shared/.../data/analytics/AnalyticsEvent.kt`: two new variants `ScreenViewed(screen: Screen)` and `ClickAction(action: ClickActionId, screen: Screen)` join the existing F.3/F.4 outcome-typed variants (`ProjectCreated` / `RowIncremented` / `ChartEditorSave` / etc.). Critical engagement-vs-outcome distinction encoded in the type system per ADR-015 §6: outcome variants register **success** (a row landed in the DB), `ClickAction` registers **intent** (the user tapped — regardless of whether the underlying operation succeeded, no-oped, or surfaced an error). Concrete example documented inline at `ClickActionId.kt`: tapping "Mark Complete" on an already-completed project fires `ClickAction(MarkComplete, ProjectDetail)` but does not fire any outcome event because `ProjectDetailViewModel`'s status guard short-circuits the write path. The pair gives funnel visibility (engagement → success rate per action) that pure outcome events cannot. **Closed taxonomies** at `Screen.kt` (20 entries) and `ClickActionId.kt` (18 entries): each enum carries a `wireValue: String` matching the screen's existing testTag landmark from the Phase 33.x i18n sweep — keeping the mental model "the value PostHog sees is the same string Maestro / XCUITest queries against" so a single grep finds analytics + instrumented-test + route-name references at once. New entries land alongside the call site in the same commit per the cardinality discipline; no free-form `String` ever crosses the wire boundary. **`EventRingBuffer`** at `data/analytics/EventRingBuffer.kt`: bounded FIFO ring (`DEFAULT_CAPACITY = 10`, `Mutex` serialized) collecting from the same `tracker.events` SharedFlow that the Application layer already forwards into PostHog. Phase 39.5's bug-report submission flow will call `snapshot()` to attach the last 10 events to the GitHub Issue body. Privacy gating happens **upstream** at `AnalyticsTrackerImpl.track()` — when `analyticsOptIn` is OFF the tracker no-ops `tryEmit` before any subscriber sees the event, so the buffer naturally stays empty for users who never consent (no PII leak risk; bug reports of opted-out users would attach an empty trail). `start(scope)` is fire-once + idempotent on a second call. **Android NavController listener** in `MainActivity.kt`: `DisposableEffect(navController)` registers an `OnDestinationChangedListener` that bridges Compose Navigation type-safe routes onto the shared `Screen` enum via `routeStringToScreen()` — strips package prefix with `substringAfterLast('.')` and any `/{param}` suffix with `substringBefore('/')`, then exhaustive `when` over the 20 entries. Unmappable routes (e.g. `ForgotPassword`) silently no-op rather than firing a placeholder. `onDispose { removeOnDestinationChangedListener }` ensures the listener tears down when the activity is recreated mid-session. **iOS SwiftUI `.trackScreen()` ViewModifier** at `iosApp/iosApp/Core/ScreenTracking.swift`: `View` extension emits `AnalyticsEvent.ScreenViewed(screen)` on first `.task` activation. SwiftUI's `NavigationStack` does NOT expose a public destination-change event so each screen view is the natural anchor — the modifier is centralized at `AppRouter.destinationView(for:)` so adding a new `Route` case is one diff (Route case + destination view + `.trackScreen()` suffix), not three scattered edits. Pre-router screens (`OnboardingScreen` / `LoginScreen` / first `ProjectListScreen` push) declare their own `.trackScreen()` since they don't pass through the router. **Kotlin/Native ObjC bridging quirk documented inline** at `AppRouter.swift:153-167`: PascalCase Kotlin enum entries lowercase entirely (no camelCase split) on the Swift side — `Screen.ProjectDetail` (Kotlin) surfaces as `Screen.projectdetail` (Swift), `ClickActionId.SelectPaletteSymbol` → `.selectpalettesymbol`. Single-word entries stay tidy (`.discovery`); multi-word ones look unusual but are mechanical from the bridge. `@ObjCName` annotations would let us override but balloons the Kotlin enum declaration; deferred. **Application-layer init paths**: Android `SkeinlyApplication.onCreate` calls `eventRingBuffer.start(applicationScope)` unconditionally (the buffer is harmless on production — only ever fills with opt-in-gated events), then gates the PostHog SDK init on `BuildFlags.isBeta && posthogApiKey.isNotEmpty()` so production binaries skip PostHog entirely even with a stale opt-in payload. iOS `iOSApp.init` mirrors via new `KoinHelperKt.startEventRingBuffer()` accessor + `BuildFlags.isBeta` gate around `observeAnalyticsOptIn` / `observeAnalyticsEvents`. **`KoinHelper.kt`** gains 2 new exports: `getEventRingBuffer()` accessor and `startEventRingBuffer()` (resolves the buffer + the `applicationScopeQualifier`-tagged `CoroutineScope` and calls `buffer.start(scope)` — Swift never juggles the scope directly). **DI registration** in `PreferencesModule.kt`: `single { EventRingBuffer(tracker = get()) }`. **15 click instrumentations** plumbed into 9 ViewModels via the existing `analyticsTracker?.track(...)` null-safe pattern: `ProjectListViewModel.CreateProject`, `ProjectDetailViewModel.IncrementRow` / `DecrementRow` / `MarkComplete` / `Reopen`, `ChartEditorViewModel.Save` / `Undo` / `Redo` / `SelectPaletteSymbol`, `ChartViewerViewModel.OpenPullRequest` (existing fork of the typed-event `RequestOpenPullRequest`) / `SwitchBranch` (existing branch-switch toast), `DiscoveryViewModel.ForkPattern`, `OnboardingViewModel.Skip` / `Complete` (both fire `SubmitOnboarding` since the ViewModel does not distinguish at the analytics layer), `PatternEditViewModel.Save`, `PullRequestDetailViewModel.ConfirmMerge` / `ConfirmClose`. **Test affordance** `RecordingAnalyticsTracker.outcomeEvents`: filters captures to non-`ClickAction` non-`ScreenViewed` events so pre-39.3 tests asserting on `listOf(OutcomeEvent)` did not need to be rewritten to enumerate the surrounding ClickAction noise. 8 ViewModel test files updated to use the new accessor at the assertion sites; semantics unchanged. **Tests (+20 commonTest, 1212 → 1232)**: `ScreenAndClickActionEventTest.kt` (8 cases — covers `ScreenViewed.name == "screen_viewed"`, `properties` map shape with `screen` key, all 20 `Screen.wireValue` strings unique, `ClickAction.name == "click_action"`, properties carries both `action` + `screen`, all 18 `ClickActionId.wireValue` strings unique, `data class` equality round-trip). `EventRingBufferTest.kt` (12 cases — `DEFAULT_CAPACITY == 10`, capacity > 0 invariant, empty initial snapshot, FIFO arrival order, eviction at capacity, snapshot is immutable across subsequent emissions, idempotent `start()`, `start()` collects after subscription via `UnconfinedTestDispatcher` per `AnalyticsTrackerTest` precedent, `snapshot()` consistency under concurrent emission, etc.). All new test names follow the Phase 32 Kotlin/Native CI gotcha (no parens, commas, or apostrophes in backticks). **Pre-push invariants all green**: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1232 tests, +20 from 1212 baseline — well within ADR-015 §6's +12-18 estimate, the +2 overshoot reflects defensive test surface around the FIFO eviction + concurrent-emission paths), `:shared:koverVerify`, `verifyI18nKeys`. iOS `xcodebuild ... build` ✅ (verified during implementation; the bridging-quirk lowercase enum entries surface as `.projectdetail` etc. — documented inline at `AppRouter.swift` so future readers don't try to "fix" them back to camelCase). **No i18n keys touched** (Phase 39.3 is data-layer + entry-point wiring only — Phase 39.4 introduces the user-visible consent moment and is the first slice that adds keys). **Forward-compat anchors for 39.4 / 39.5**: the `BuildFlags.isBeta` gate is already in place at every PostHog initialization site, so flipping the consent UI on/off is a pure ViewModel-state change with no further plumbing. The `EventRingBuffer.snapshot()` API is the integration seam Phase 39.5's bug-reporter consumes; the buffer ships with no PII leakage risk because the upstream tracker already gates on opt-in. **Scope cuts unchanged from ADR-015 §6**: 4th onboarding consent page + Settings "Beta" section + i18n keys all in 39.4; bug-report gesture detection (Android 3-finger long-press / iOS shake) + `BugReportPreviewScreen` + `BugSubmissionLauncher` `expect/actual` all in 39.5.

- **Phase 39.2**: F2 build-flag plumbing + privacy policy update (per ADR-015 §5 + §4) — first code-bearing slice of Phase 39.x. **No behavioral change** (no UI surfaces touched, no SDK init wired); pure infrastructure for 39.3+ to consume. New `BuildFlags` `expect/actual` at `shared/.../config/BuildFlags.kt`: Android actual generated at build time by `generateBuildFlagsAndroid` Gradle task (mirrors the existing `generateSupabaseConfig` pattern — necessary because the AGP 9.x `com.android.kotlin.multiplatform.library` plugin does not expose `buildFeatures { buildConfig = true }` to shared android source sets); reads `version.properties` `VERSION_NAME` major component (`major == 0` ⇒ `isBeta = true`; the rule was pivoted from `-beta` suffix detection to major-zero on 2026-05-05 to align with the `0.X.Y` semver convention adopted in the same commit) and emits a `BuildFlags.android.kt` constant. iOS actual at `BuildFlags.ios.kt` reads the `IsBetaBuild` Info.plist key as `String` and compares `== "YES"` (xcconfig macro substitution always produces strings, not booleans — `as? Boolean` would always return null; mirrors `SupabaseConfig.ios.kt`'s String-based pattern). New Swift mirror at `iosApp/iosApp/Core/BuildFlags.swift` reads the same Info.plist key directly via `Bundle.main.object(forInfoDictionaryKey:)` per ADR §5 — Swift call sites avoid the KMP/Swift interop surface for a flag whose source is the Info.plist both sides already agree on. **iOS xcconfig wiring**: `iosApp/project.yml` adds `IS_BETA: "YES"` to `settings.base` + `IsBetaBuild: "$(IS_BETA)"` to `info.properties`. xcodegen regen wires `<key>IsBetaBuild</key><string>$(IS_BETA)</string>` into `iosApp/iosApp/Info.plist`. **Privacy policy update**: `docs/public/privacy-policy/index.html` (EN) + `docs/public/ja/privacy-policy/index.html` (JA) gain a "Diagnostic Data (Beta builds only)" subsection enumerating PostHog data fields collected on opt-in (app version, OS version, device model, locale, anonymous PostHog SDK distinct_id, screen names, categorical action names) + the never-collected list (pattern names / project titles / note text / search queries / comment bodies / photos / email / display names) + the disclosure that bug-report GitHub Issues include the anonymous distinct_id for cross-referencing PostHog dashboards (per ADR-015 §4 LOW-1 disclosure requirement) + revocation-takes-effect-immediately + opt-in default-off statement (GDPR + 改正個人情報保護法 named explicitly). The existing "Automatically Collected Information" section gains a corrected statement: "Production releases of the App do not activate any analytics, crash reporting, or tracking functionality. ... Some third-party SDKs (e.g. PostHog, Sentry) are linked into the binary, but they are never initialized in production builds — no network connections are opened and no data is collected." (factually accurate vs the earlier "do not include" framing — both Sentry + PostHog SwiftPM packages are unconditionally declared in `iosApp/project.yml`'s `packages:` block). +1 androidHostTest (`BuildFlagsTest.isBeta_matches_versionProperties_majorZero`); 1212 shared tests (-1 vacuous-test deletion + 1 new = +1 net from 1211 baseline; ADR-015 §6 estimated +3-5, the under-estimate is because BuildFlags semantically only has one value to assert against). Pre-push invariants all green: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest`, `:shared:koverVerify`, `verifyI18nKeys`. iOS `xcodebuild -project iosApp/iosApp.xcodeproj -scheme iosApp -destination 'generic/platform=iOS Simulator' -configuration Debug build` ✅. **iOS Phase 40 GA coupled-edit risk** (logged in Tech Debt Backlog under new "Phase 40 GA release prep" subsection): unlike Android's automated codegen path, iOS `IS_BETA: "YES"` is a hardcoded literal in `iosApp/project.yml` `settings.base` — a Phase 40 commit that bumps `version.properties` without flipping IS_BETA would ship a production binary that behaves as a beta build. Mitigated for Phase 39 by (a) inline COUPLED EDIT comment block at the top of `version.properties` naming the iOS line as a coupled edit, and (b) `BuildFlagsTest.isBeta_matches_versionProperties_majorZero` failing in CI when the major bumps from 0 to 1+ without the iOS edit (rule pivoted from `-beta` suffix detection to major-zero on 2026-05-05). Long-term mitigation deferred to Phase 40 prep: `scripts/verify-ios-beta-flag.sh` consistency check wired into ci.yml shared-checks. **Code review iterations**: first pass 2 MEDIUM (privacy "do not include" inaccurate vs unconditional SwiftPM linkage; iOS IS_BETA manual-flip risk at Phase 40) + 2 LOW (vacuous `isBeta_is_a_constant` test, Phase 40 process-dependency on test-assertion flip); second pass 1 MEDIUM (privacy "may be linked" hedging — PostHog and Sentry are unconditionally linked in every build, "may be" misrepresents the binary state); third pass APPROVED. All findings addressed pre-commit per CLAUDE.md "fix all reported issues" rule.

- **Phase 39.1**: ADR-015 cut for F2 beta-tester per-screen bug reporting — opens the F2 feature work (Phase 39.x) with the data-model + UX shape decided before any code lands. ADR sized at 1098 lines EN + 178 line JA summary. **Key decisions resolved by the agent team**: (1) Gesture-primary trigger — iOS shake (TestFlight conditioning, knitter-acceptable per the iOS preview-screen-with-Cancel safety net), Android 3-finger-long-press (Bugsnag/Sentry standard, more deliberate than shake which fires accidentally during knit-and-phone). Settings → Beta → "Send Feedback" entry as fallback + 4th onboarding card for discoverability. NO floating CTA (would contradict Phase 39.0.2 Sprint A's FAB+overflow consolidation). (2) PostHog free tier + custom typed events. **Critical reuse**: existing `AnalyticsPreferences` (`analytics_opt_in` boolean key, default false) + `AnalyticsTracker` (SharedFlow → Application-layer-collected → PostHog SDK forward) types from earlier Phase F.2/F.3 work-in-progress are kept verbatim — F2 only adds two new `AnalyticsEvent` sealed-interface variants (`ScreenViewed`, `ClickAction`) with companion `Screen` / `ClickActionId` enums for cardinality discipline (no free-form Strings at the wire boundary), plus a sibling `EventRingBuffer` (FIFO N=10, Mutex) that collects from the same SharedFlow for bug-report attachment. NO new `TelemetryGate` interface, NO new `TelemetryConsentRepository`, NO new keys, NO migration. (3) URL prefill via `https://github.com/b150005/skeinly/issues/new?template=beta-bug.yml&title=...&body=...` — Android `Intent(ACTION_VIEW)`, iOS `URLComponents.queryItems` + `UIApplication.shared.open` (the latter chosen over `addingPercentEncoding(.urlQueryAllowed)` because that character set does NOT encode `&` and would silently truncate body params containing it — found by code review MEDIUM-1). Reuses Phase 39.0 `.github/ISSUE_TEMPLATE/beta-bug.yml`. NO PAT in binary, NO Edge Function. (4) Privacy gate via existing default-false `analyticsOptIn` — consent capture happens via a 4th onboarding page on beta builds (NOT a separate post-onboarding modal), where the existing `hasSeenOnboarding` slot answers the "has consent been asked?" question structurally. Settings toggle for revoke/re-grant. Privacy policy update at `docs/public/privacy-policy/index.html` (EN at `https://b150005.github.io/skeinly/privacy-policy/`) + `docs/public/ja/privacy-policy/index.html` (JA at `https://b150005.github.io/skeinly/ja/privacy-policy/`) enumerating PostHog data fields + the never-collected list + PostHog `distinct_id`-in-issue-body disclosure for GDPR/PIPL. (5) Beta-only via `BuildFlags.isBeta` `expect/actual` (Android `BuildConfig.IS_BETA` derived from `version.properties` `*-beta*` suffix; iOS `IsBetaBuild` Info.plist key driven by xcconfig `IS_BETA = YES` on the beta scheme). Swift code reads `Bundle.main.object(forInfoDictionaryKey: "IsBetaBuild") as? Bool == true` directly — no Kotlin object bridge. iOS shake bridge subclasses `UIHostingController` at `SceneDelegate` (not `UIViewControllerRepresentable` nested in SwiftUI — motion events propagate to root responder only, the representable approach silently fails). **Sub-slice plan locked in as ADR §6**: 39.1 (this ADR, no code) → 39.2 (BuildFlags + privacy policy update + reuse-existing-types acknowledgment, +3-5 commonTest) → 39.3 (`posthog-android` ≥3.x + `PostHogIos` SwiftPM ≥3.x deps, `AnalyticsEvent.ScreenViewed` + `ClickAction` variants + `Screen` / `ClickActionId` enums, `EventRingBuffer` consuming `AnalyticsTracker.events`, NavController listener Android + `.trackScreen` ViewModifier iOS, ~15 click instrumentations, Application-layer PostHog init with `BuildFlags.isBeta && analyticsOptIn.value` gate, new `KoinHelper.analyticsTracker()` + `KoinHelper.analyticsPreferences()` accessors, +12-18 commonTest) → 39.4 (4th onboarding consent page Compose + SwiftUI writing through existing `AnalyticsPreferences.setAnalyticsOptIn`, Settings "Beta" section gated on `BuildFlags.isBeta`, i18n 8-10 keys, +6-10 commonTest) → 39.5 (Android 3-finger-long-press at `MainActivity.dispatchTouchEvent`, iOS `ShakeDetectingController : UIHostingController` subclass in `SceneDelegate`, `BugReportPreviewScreen` Compose + SwiftUI, `BugSubmissionLauncher` `expect/actual`, Markdown body formatting helper, +10-15 commonTest, 6-8 i18n keys). Each sub-slice independently shippable; slipping 39.5 leaves bug reporting unreachable (testers report manually as today, no regression). **Forward-compat anchors**: KMP shared `EventRingBuffer` + existing `AnalyticsTracker` SharedFlow contract reusable for v1.0 production (Phase 40+) with a different downstream collector (Sentry / Crashlytics / etc.) without rewriting any `tracker.track(AnalyticsEvent.X)` call site. **Explicitly NOT in F2 MVP**: in-app screenshot capture, crash auto-capture (Sentry / Firebase Crashlytics is Phase 40+), network log capture (request bodies are PII), state snapshot at bug time (PII), in-app feedback for v1.0 production, audio/video bug recording, in-app GitHub OAuth, server-side issue aggregation, reporter rate-limiting (≤10 testers, abuse risk zero), Markdown rendering preview (Compose vs SwiftUI render-target divergence with no shared sanitizer). **Code review iterations**: first pass 2 CRITICAL + 2 HIGH + 3 MEDIUM + 3 LOW (CRITICAL-1 broken privacy URL `/privacy.html` would 404; CRITICAL-2 parallel `TelemetryGate` / `TelemetryConsentRepository` design conflicting with already-existing `AnalyticsPreferences` + `AnalyticsTracker` would have caused undefined behavior at runtime through duplicate Koin bindings on overlapping keys); second pass after restructure surfaced 1 MEDIUM (`AnalyticsEvent` snippet missing `override val name` + `override val properties: Map<String, Any>?`) + 4 LOW (LIFO/FIFO terminology error, `KoinHelper.analyticsTracker()` accessor unscoped, `KoinComponent` requirement for `by inject()` undisclosed, PostHog SDK version unanchored); third pass APPROVED with 2 LOW deferred to 39.3 (`get()` form on overrides, `KoinHelper.analyticsPreferences()` accessor mention) — both surfaced as inline 39.3 scope additions before commit per CLAUDE.md "fix all reported issues" rule. No test delta this slice (ADR is documentation only); 1211 shared tests unchanged; pre-push invariants don't apply (no Kotlin / iOS code touched).

- **Phase 39.0.2 Sprint B**: Pre-beta MEDIUM polish (2026-04-30, continuation from Sprint A in same session) — closes 5 of the 6 MEDIUM findings from the same parallel ui-ux-designer + a11y-architect audit; M5 (ChartEditor zoom) deferred to post-beta with documented Tech Debt entry. Opens with a regression fix: **commit `0bbbce0`** `fix(e2e): pivot create_pattern_android helper through overflow menu` — Sprint A PR1 collapsed the AppBar to overflow but missed `e2e/helpers/create_pattern_android.yaml` in the 5-flow pivot sweep; the `P1 - Chart Editor (Phase 32)` Maestro flow that consumed the helper failed in CI for `29a23b7` with `Element not found: Id matching regex: patternLibraryButton`. Closed by adding the same `tapOn: id: "moreMenu"` preamble before `tapOn: id: "patternLibraryButton"`. Subsequent Sprint A commits' E2E got cancelled by concurrency-group `cancel-in-progress: true` on each push, masking the latent regression until the b7acf70 in_progress run started. **M1 commit `b98e186`** `feat(ui/symbol): hide internal symbol IDs from gallery cards` — removed the `Text(definition.id, fontSize = 10.sp)` debug-noise line from both Compose `SymbolCard` and SwiftUI `SymbolCardView`, plus the now-unused `import androidx.compose.ui.unit.sp` on Compose. The `testTag("symbolCard-${definition.id}")` / `.accessibilityIdentifier(...)` machinery stays intact for E2E + dev inspection (`adb shell uiautomator dump` still surfaces them). User-facing JA + EN labels + descriptions remain. Phase 30.1 originally shipped IDs always-visible "until Phase 33 i18n" — i18n closed at 33.1.15 so the IDs now serve no end-user purpose. Maestro flow `P1_chart_editor.yaml`'s `paletteSymbol_jis.knit.bobble` reference is editor-palette testTag, not gallery card text — unaffected. **M2 commit `087aeab`** `feat(ui/discovery): relocate sort to TopAppBar IconButton (clipping fix)` — Discovery filter LazyRow previously had a trailing `FilterChip`-styled sort dropdown competing for horizontal space with the difficulty chips, clipping the trailing 上級 / "Advanced" chip on JA-locale narrow screens. Pivoted Compose's `DiscoverySortDropdown` (FilterChip with sort-name label) → new `DiscoverySortMenu` (IconButton with `Sort` icon, identical `DropdownMenu` underneath). Wired into `TopAppBar.actions = { ... }` matching the iOS `ToolbarItem(.primaryAction) Menu` shape since Phase 36.4. Filter LazyRow now spans `fillMaxWidth()` with the wrapping `Row` collapsed; renamed `DiscoveryFilterSortRow` → `DiscoveryFilterRow`, dropped `sortOrder` + `onSortOrderChange` params. `label_sort_alphabetical` (short-form) import dropped from DiscoveryScreen — i18n source key stays in 5-source parity for ProjectList + PatternLibrary consumers. testTags `sortMenuButton` / `sortRecentItem` / `sortAlphabeticalItem` added.
