Code review surfaced MEDIUM (loss of always-visible current-sort label); fixed pre-commit by adding leading `Check` icon on the active `DropdownMenuItem` mirroring iOS's `systemImage: holder.state.sortOrder == .recent ? "checkmark" : ""` pattern — current sort discoverable inside the menu on both platforms with identical UX. iOS no change (already correct shape since Phase 36.4). **M3 commit `6fe07b2`** `feat(ios/ui): promote Mark Complete to prominent filled CTA` — Compose's `StatusToggleButton` (Material 3 `Button` for Mark Complete + `FilledTonalButton` for Reopen with CheckCircle / Refresh icons) was already correct; iOS used bare `Button(LocalizedStringKey(...))` inside `Form > Section` which renders as plain accent-text styling (visually a link, structurally low-emphasis). Closed iOS gap: Mark Complete = `Label("action_mark_complete", systemImage: "checkmark.circle.fill").frame(maxWidth: .infinity, alignment: .center)` + `.buttonStyle(.borderedProminent)` (full-width filled prominent, AccentColor #7B61FF tinted via Sprint A PR3); Reopen = same Label/frame shape with `systemImage: "arrow.counterclockwise"` + `.buttonStyle(.bordered)` matching Compose's `FilledTonalButton` lower-emphasis tonal. Reset Progress destructive button left as natural-width left-aligned text-link per iOS HIG (Settings → "Sign Out" / "Delete Account" precedent — primary CTA stands out, destructive corrective stays subtle is intentional hierarchy, not asymmetry to fix). accessibilityIdentifiers `markCompleteButton` / `reopenProjectButton` preserved. Code review 2 MEDIUM (1 addressed pre-commit via explicit `alignment: .center`; 1 left intentionally per iOS HIG) + 1 LOW (Liquid Glass rendering, reviewer confirmed correct). **M4 commit `96315cd`** `feat(ui): drop empty-state CTA on Android list screens (FAB dedup)` — Android-only finding: ProjectList + PatternLibrary EmptyStateView CTA (FilledTonalButton) visually competed with the always-visible Material 3 FAB bottom-right when the list was empty. Hiding the FAB would have broken ~6 Maestro Android flows (`createProjectFab` is tapped from clean state to begin sequences); chose instead to drop the empty-state CTA action — `EmptyStateView` already supported nullable `actionLabel` + `onAction` defaults, so the call sites just omit them. EmptyStateView still renders icon + title + body for context; FAB carries the action. iOS unchanged (toolbar `+` Button is structurally small, not visually competing — audit didn't flag iOS). `action_create_project` / `action_create_pattern` i18n keys stay in 5-source parity (iOS `ContentUnavailableView(actions: { Button(LocalizedStringKey(...)) })` consumers + xcstrings are now load-bearing references). Removed unused `import action_create_*` from Compose ProjectList + PatternLibrary. **M5 commit `d5b113e`** (docs-only) `docs(claude.md): defer Sprint B M5 (ChartEditor zoom) to post-beta` — investigation showed ChartEditor has NO zoom feature at all (only ChartViewer + ChartDiff carry `rememberTransformableState`); audit's "confirm zoom-to-fit IconButton with explicit accessibilityLabel" was prescriptive, not verification. Adding programmatic zoom + IconButton requires `transformableState` + scale/offset state + `Modifier.graphicsLayer` + inverse hit-test transform from screen coords back to grid coords through active scale/offset + 1-2 toolbar IconButtons + iOS MagnificationGesture mirror — meaningful feature work (~150 LOC Compose + ~100 LOC SwiftUI), not polish. Real Phase 39 risk surface bounded: default 8x8 grid renders ~40dp cells on phones (well above 24x24 SC 2.5.8); polar editing deferred to Phase 35.2+; users authoring 16x16+ rect grids would hit it (mitigation: landscape mode). Documented in new "Accessibility deferrals" Tech Debt Backlog subsection so the WCAG citation + scope estimate are not lost. Reopen post-beta if real usability complaints surface. **M6 commit `ae73670`** `feat(a11y): non-drag delete via long-press → context menu (WCAG 2.5.7)` — three Compose surfaces previously delivered delete only via SwipeToDismissBox (drag-only fails SC 2.5.7 for motor-impaired + screen reader users). Each `SwipeToDismiss*Card` / `SwipeToDismissNoteItem` now wraps the swipe surface in an outer `Box` with a sibling `DropdownMenu`. Inner cards (`ProjectCard`, `PatternCard`, `NoteItem`) gained `onLongClick: () -> Unit = {}` + replaced `Modifier.clickable(onClick)` with `Modifier.combinedClickable(role = Role.Button, onClick, onLongClick, onLongClickLabel = stringResource(action_delete*))` (`@OptIn(ExperimentalFoundationApi::class)`). Long-press routes through the same `onDeleteRequest` / `onDelete` callback as swipe, so both paths share the existing AlertDialog confirmation — single `*toDelete: String?` state slot prevents double-fire under concurrent gestures. testTags `projectContextDeleteItem` / `patternContextDeleteItem` / `noteContextDeleteItem` for E2E. NoteItem trade-off: ListItem had no primary onClick previously (notes are display-only); empty `onClick = {}` produces ripple feedback on tap (mildly misleading) — inline comment documents it; `customActions`-based alternative deferred (would need `Modifier.semantics` + `indication = null` + custom action label infrastructure that doesn't exist elsewhere in codebase). iOS no change: SwiftUI `.swipeActions(edge: .trailing, allowsFullSwipe: false) { Button(role: .destructive) }` is natively exposed to VoiceOver via the Actions rotor in iOS 15+. Code review surfaced MEDIUM (`onLongClickLabel` missing) — addressed pre-commit on all 3 surfaces with `stringResource(action_delete*)` so TalkBack announces "double-tap and hold to delete" verbatim instead of generic "double-tap and hold". `clickable` import auto-removed from ProjectList + PatternLibrary by ktlintFormat (cards were sole consumers); `combinedClickable` + `ExperimentalFoundationApi` + `Role` + `DropdownMenu`/`DropdownMenuItem` imports added per file as needed. **Sprint B test/build delta**: 1211 shared tests unchanged (UI a11y is runtime contract, not exercised by unit tests); ktlintCheck + compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64 + testAndroidHostTest + koverVerify + verifyI18nKeys (380 keys, unchanged — M2/M4 dropped imports only) all green on every PR; iOS BUILD + TEST BUILD SUCCEEDED. Code review APPROVED on each (M1 0 findings; M2 1 MEDIUM addressed pre-commit; M3 2 MEDIUM 1 addressed 1 acknowledged + 1 LOW; M4 0 findings; M6 1 MEDIUM addressed pre-commit + 1 LOW acknowledged). With M5 documented in Tech Debt Backlog, the 6-MEDIUM audit set is closed; Phase 39 launch prep (HARD-GATE items: migration 016 prod verify, Android VERSION_CODE bump, TestFlight artifact validation, tester invites, issue template index check) opens next session.

- **Phase 39.0.2**: Pre-beta UI/UX + a11y Sprint A (2026-04-30) — closes the 6 HIGH findings from a parallel ui-ux-designer + a11y-architect audit run against 30 captured screenshots (iOS ja: 19, Android ja: 10, Android en: 1; covering onboarding, project list empty + with-data, create-project sheet, project detail empty + with-progress, edit-project sheet, add-note dialog, overflow menu, symbol gallery, pattern library, settings, discovery, pattern edit). Audit ran in this session's transcript only (not persisted to docs/) — synthesis lives in commit messages of the 6 PRs below. **PR1 commit `29a23b7`** Compose `ProjectListScreen` AppBar overflow + brand title removal: 8 inline IconButtons → single overflow `MoreVert` `DropdownMenu`, `title = { }` empty (user directive 2026-04-30 "AppBarにブランドテキストは出す必要がない — 利用者にとっては必要のない情報"). Closes WCAG 1.4.10 / 1.4.4 / 2.5.8 — title was wrapping one letter per line down the left edge in both en and ja because the icon row consumed all horizontal space. `Modifier.dialogTestTagsAsResourceId()` (Phase 33.4 helper) applied on the DropdownMenu — empirically verified via `adb shell uiautomator dump` that all 8 testTags propagate as `resource-id` through the popup window, unblocking the 5 Maestro flow pivots (`P0_app_launch.yaml` / `P0_onboarding.yaml` / `P1_discovery_browse.yaml` / `P1_symbol_gallery.yaml` / `P2_navigation.yaml`) + 4 androidTest `NavigationFlowTest.kt` cases. **PR2 commit `1c1686a`** iOS `ProjectListScreen` parity: `.navigationTitle(LocalizedStringKey("app_name"))` removed, replaced with `.accessibilityElement(children: .contain)` + `.accessibilityIdentifier("projectListScreen")` per the Phase 33.1.6 ProfileScreen footgun precedent (a bare `.accessibilityIdentifier` without the `accessibilityElement` wrap gets absorbed into a child element and `app.otherElements["projectListScreen"]` queries time out). 8 iOS Maestro flows + 5 XCUITest queries pivoted from `assertVisible: "Skeinly"` / `app.navigationBars["Skeinly"]` to the new landmark; `tapOn: "Skeinly"` (back-nav via parent-title back-chevron) → `tapOn: "Back"` (iOS 17+ default chevron accessibilityLabel when parent has no `.navigationTitle`). **PR3 commit `e1fc6fb`** iOS brand color: new `Assets.xcassets/AccentColor.colorset/` with `#7B61FF` (light) + `#9B82FF` (dark, lifted for readability) + `ASSETCATALOG_COMPILER_GLOBAL_ACCENT_COLOR_NAME = AccentColor` build setting in `iosApp/project.yml`. SwiftUI auto-tints toolbar buttons / swipe accents / links / focus rings / empty-state CTA across the app; replaced one explicit `.tint(.blue)` on Discovery's swipe-Fork. The two semantic `.blue` references (`ActivityFeedScreen.swift:81` `case .started` + `DiscoveryScreen.swift:397` `case .intermediate`) intentionally stay distinct — they encode categories, not primary actions. `DesignTokens.brandAccent = .accentColor` added for explicit reference. **PR4 commit `e2c3de0`** iOS form-sheet a11y: explicit `.accessibilityLabel(LocalizedStringKey(...))` mirroring the `titleKey` on 5 TextFields in `createProjectSheet` / `editSheet` / `addNoteSheet` so VoiceOver continues announcing the field name after the user starts typing. Defensive even where SwiftUI's auto-derived label might already work — locks the contract against iOS 17→18 minor-version drift the audit observed. PatternEdit's section-header pattern + Profile / Login / PullRequest were out of scope (audit ranked MEDIUM, lower regression risk). **PR5 commit `5013934`** FilterChip non-color signal: new `ui/components/SelectedCheckmarkIcon.kt` Compose helper (`selectedCheckmarkIcon(selected): (@Composable () -> Unit)?`) applied to ProjectList status row (4 chips), Discovery filter row (5 chips inc. charts-only), PatternLibrary difficulty row (4 chips). iOS counterparts (`StatusFilterChip`, `DiscoveryFilterChip`, `DifficultyFilterChip` private structs) extended with `HStack { Image("checkmark") + Text }` conditional on `isSelected`. Closes WCAG 1.4.1 — pale-lavender fill alone was perceptually indistinguishable from disabled. Sort-dropdown chips deliberately untouched (different control shape — sort icon already serves as non-color cue). **PR6 commit `7edbf7d`** Snackbar / Toast a11y announcements: new `ui/components/LiveSnackbarHost.kt` Compose wrapper (`SnackbarHost` + `Modifier.semantics { liveRegion = LiveRegionMode.Polite }`) applied to 18 screens replacing every `SnackbarHost(snackbarHostState)` call. iOS `Core/AccessibilityAnnouncements.swift` provides `announceToVoiceOver(messageKey:)` + `(message:)` helpers; called from 5 toast trigger sites (PullRequestDetail PR-closed/merged, StructuredChartViewer switched-to-branch / opened-PR, ChartConflictResolution merge-applied, Discovery fork result, Settings password-changed / email-change-pending). Closes WCAG 4.1.3 — bare M3 SnackbarHost ships no liveRegion, SwiftUI `.overlay` toasts ship no `UIAccessibility.post`. **Sprint A test/build delta**: 1211 shared tests unchanged (UI a11y is a runtime contract, not exercised by unit tests); ktlintCheck + compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64 + testAndroidHostTest + koverVerify + verifyI18nKeys (380 keys) all green on every PR; iOS BUILD + TEST BUILD SUCCEEDED. Code review APPROVED on each (PR1 1 MEDIUM empirically resolved + 1 LOW fixed pre-commit; PR2 1 HIGH fixed pre-commit — `accessibilityElement(children: .contain)` precedent footgun; others 0 CRITICAL/HIGH). **Sprint B (next session)** continues with the audit's 6 MEDIUM findings: (1) Symbol Gallery hides internal `jis.knit.bind-off` IDs from cards, (2) Discovery filter row clipping (上級 chip cut off at right edge — split sort to dedicated trailing IconButton), (3) Empty-state CTA + FAB duplication on Android ProjectList / PatternLibrary (hide one), (4) ProjectDetail "完了にする" reads as link not primary action (filled accent button + checkmark icon), (5) ChartEditor 12dp cell SC 2.5.8 risk (confirm zoom-to-fit IconButton with explicit accessibilityLabel), (6) SwipeToDismissBox SC 2.5.7 non-drag alternative (long-press → context menu Compose; verify iOS `.swipeActions` exposure to VoiceOver). Sprint B scoped as 4-6 atomic PRs with same shape as Sprint A.

- **Phase 39.0.1**: Pre-launch infrastructure (2026-04-27 single-session sweep) — Supabase prod backfill + branch protection + self-hosted CI + security hardening, all completed before tester invites go out. (1) **Supabase prod schema migration** ([commit 80f00fb](https://github.com/b150005/skeinly/commit/80f00fb)): prod was 7 migrations behind (009 pattern_metadata / 010 progress_photos / 011 visibility_index / 013 project_segments / 014 pattern_attribution / 015 chart_revisions / 016 pull_requests). Resolved local-vs-remote 012_structured_chart version mismatch via `supabase migration repair --status reverted 20260417114618` + `--status applied 012`, then `supabase db push --include-all`. Migration 010 hit `operator does not exist: uuid = text` on the shared-progress-photos RLS policy (the JOIN compared `shares.pattern_id` UUID with `projects.pattern_id` TEXT — Phase 1 legacy schema mismatch). Patched the local file with `s.pattern_id::text` cast and applied the missing statements (bucket + 5 policies + ALTER TABLE activities CHECK) directly via `mcp__supabase__execute_sql`. All 16 migrations now match across local + prod. Closes Phase 39 Gate 1. (2) **Branch protection ruleset** ([commit 9054ea2](https://github.com/b150005/skeinly/commit/9054ea2), ruleset id `15581036`): `main-strict` ruleset with 6 rules (`update`, `non_fast_forward`, `deletion`, `required_linear_history`, `pull_request` requiring 1 approval + dismiss-stale + require-last-push-approval + require-thread-resolution, `required_status_checks` for 6 contexts). Bypass actor: Repository Admin role only — on a personal-account repo, this means Owner-only by default. `docs/en/repo-policy.md` + JA mirror documents the design + rationale; CLAUDE.md `## Development Workflow` section references it. Verified by attempting direct push: server returns "Bypassed rule violations" + "6 of 6 required status checks are expected" message confirming the rules are active. (3) **Self-hosted GHA runner pivot** ([commits 92fa802 → 1a119e1](https://github.com/b150005/skeinly/compare/92fa802...1a119e1)): originally provisioned a Lume macOS 26.4.1 VM (CPU 4 / RAM 8GB / disk 100GB) via `lume create --unattended tahoe`, manually completed Setup Assistant via VNC after the preset-driven setup hit `Text 'Set Up Later' not found`, installed Homebrew + xcodes + gh + JDK 17 + xcodegen + Maestro, manually installed Xcode 26.4.1 via `xcodes install` (Apple Developer 2FA prompts that env-var-passed app-specific password could not bypass), downloaded iOS 26.4 Simulator runtime, registered GHA runner as `lume-vm-1` with LaunchAgent. **Then pivoted to host-direct runner** because the threat model audit (see point 4 below) found the VM isolation provided minimal security delta given strict-ruleset restricts main pushes to Owner only and `pull_request` workflow trigger is blocked by GitHub's "Require approval for all outside collaborators" setting — meanwhile the VM added 70GB disk + Setup Assistant friction + duplicate Xcode/SDK + slower builds. Deregistered VM runner, deleted VM, installed runner binary at `/Users/b150005/Development/Tools/actions-runner-skeinly/` registered as `b150005mac-host` with labels `[self-hosted, macos, apple-silicon, host]`. All workflows migrated to single sequential self-hosted runner: `ci.yml` (3 jobs) + `e2e.yml` (2 jobs) + `security.yml` (matrix 2) + `pages.yml`. Per-job optimizations: dropped `actions/setup-java@v5` (use host JDK 17 via `JAVA_HOME` env), reused host Xcode + Simulator + Android SDK + Maestro + xcodegen (zero per-runner DL after first run). Per-job cleanup step deletes workspace `build/` folders + `~/Library/Developer/Xcode/DerivedData/iosApp-*` + Maestro test results (preserves `~/.gradle/caches/`, Android SDK, Xcode, user's other simulators). Android E2E `arch: x86_64 → arm64-v8a` for native HVF speed; `enable-kvm` Linux-only step removed. Deleted unused `ios-self-hosted.yml` (consolidated into ci.yml ios job) + `ci-base.yml` (ECC base template leftover). `release.yml` kept on GitHub-hosted (TestFlight signing complexity, tag-only trigger). First post-pivot CI run on host: `ci.yml ios` job completed in 6m18s (vs ~25min on macos-latest, 4× faster). Single-runner sequential trade-off: total cycle ~80min vs ~25min parallel — accepted for solo-dev simplicity per user choice. **Android E2E runtime gotcha**: host AVD persists across CI runs and across local-dev sessions, so a prior dev install of `io.github.b150005.skeinly.android` signed with user's local debug keystore conflicts with CI's default debug keystore — `INSTALL_FAILED_UPDATE_INCOMPATIBLE`. Fixed in [commit 7a9101b](https://github.com/b150005/skeinly/commit/7a9101b) by adding `adb uninstall io.github.b150005.skeinly.android || true` before the `adb install -r` step. (4) **Security hardening per audit** ([commit 8d6c6ae](https://github.com/b150005/skeinly/commit/8d6c6ae)): security-reviewer agent audit found 2 CRITICAL + 4 HIGH + 2 MEDIUM + 2 LOW. **CRITICAL C1** (public repo + self-hosted + `pull_request` trigger = arbitrary code execution by any GitHub user) closed by setting Repository Settings → Actions → "Fork pull request workflows from outside collaborators" → "Require approval for all outside collaborators" (was previously "Require approval for first-time contributors who are new to GitHub" which still allowed code execution from established GitHub users). **CRITICAL C2** (third-party action supply chain via mutable tag re-pointing) closed by SHA-pinning `reactivecircus/android-emulator-runner@v2` → `@e89f39f`, `gradle/actions/setup-gradle@v6` → `@50e97c2`, `softprops/action-gh-release@v3` → `@b430933`. Dependabot tracks the SHAs via existing `.github/dependabot.yml` `github-actions` ecosystem. **HIGH H3** (`ci.yml` lacked top-level `permissions:` block — silent inheritance of repo default) closed by explicit `permissions: contents: read` matching `e2e.yml` posture. **HIGH H4** (overzealous "全部 self-hosted" included `pages.yml` whose `id-token: write` permission should not exist in host process space) closed by reverting `pages.yml` to `runs-on: ubuntu-latest` (the static-file Pages deploy has no Apple Silicon dependency anyway). **MEDIUM M1** (`${{ steps.sim.outputs.dest }}` interpolated directly into shell — structurally vulnerable even though current value is system-controlled) closed by env-var-then-shell-var pattern: `env: XCODE_DEST: ${{ steps.sim.outputs.dest }}` then `xcodebuild ... -destination "$XCODE_DEST"`. **LOW L1** (`pages.yml` `actions/checkout@v4` while everywhere else is `@v6`) closed by version bump. Verified Repository Settings → "Secret scanning" + "Push protection" both ENABLED. Outstanding (post-beta, intentionally deferred): **HIGH H1** persistent workspace cross-run poisoning + **HIGH H2** runner runs as admin-group user with full Keychain access + **MEDIUM M2** shared `~/.gradle/caches/` between CI and local dev (all three would require runner isolation via Lume VM revival or similar — significant work, threat model accepts the residual risk for solo-maintainer with strict-ruleset main + fork PR approval gate); **LOW L2** unrestricted runner network egress (would require 3rd-party macOS firewall like Little Snitch); **user-side action item** Dependabot security updates not yet enabled (Settings → Code security & analysis); **user-side action item** `~/.ssh/id_ed25519` + `~/.ssh/b150005-GitHub` lack passphrase (advised `ssh-keygen -p` post-beta when convenient — silent exfiltration risk if runner ever compromised). All findings + mitigations + deferred items documented in `docs/en/repo-policy.md`'s Security section ([commit included]). **CodeQL Kotlin status update** (CLAUDE.md "CI Known Limitations" updated in same commit): the Kotlin 2.3.20-not-supported entry was outdated as of 2026-04-15 when CodeQL CLI 2.25.2 added Kotlin 2.3.20 support. The Security workflow's java-kotlin matrix entry continues to fail but with a different error: `CodeQL detected code written in Java/Kotlin but this run didn't build any of it` — root cause now is the CodeQL Kotlin extractor failing to capture the Gradle in-process compilation despite the documented `--no-daemon` + `kotlin.daemon.enabled=false` + `kotlin.compiler.execution.strategy=in-process` flags. Reproduces identically on host runner so not runner-specific. `continue-on-error: true` keeps the job from blocking CI; `required_status_checks` excludes this matrix entry. Investigation deferred. No code/test delta in this slice (infrastructure + docs only). (5) **Reverted self-hosted runner back to GitHub-hosted** (commit, single batch reverting `ci.yml` + `e2e.yml` + `security.yml` `runs-on:` from `[self-hosted, macos, apple-silicon, host]` to `ubuntu-latest` / `macos-latest`). Reasoning: even after closing CRITICAL C1 + C2 from the security audit, the host-runner setup carried two material problems: (a) **inherent residual security risk on a public repo** — H1 (persistent workspace cross-run poisoning) + H2 (admin-user keychain access) cannot be closed without runner isolation (Lume VM revival or equivalent), and the deferred items list was uncomfortable to ship with closed-beta tester invites going out; and (b) **host-PC operational overhead** — observed real failures during shakedown: CI `:shared:build` step hit `Gradle build daemon stopped: JVM GC thrashing` despite `GRADLE_OPTS=-Xmx6g` (commit `24194b9`), iOS E2E `xcrun simctl install` hung for 42 minutes before the 45-min timeout killed the job (host's iPhone 17 Pro Simulator carried a dev install of skeinly), Android E2E earlier hit `INSTALL_FAILED_UPDATE_INCOMPATIBLE` for the same reason on the host's persistent AVD (commit `7a9101b` adb uninstall fix). Each fix accreted complexity, and the host runner kept surfacing new state-persistence problems that GitHub-hosted ephemeral runners structurally do not have. Net cost-benefit: 4× iOS speedup (6m18s vs 25min on macos-latest) and ~$0/month CI cost vs. ongoing host maintenance burden + security exposure on a public repo + recurring user-side AVD/Simulator hygiene. Reverted to GitHub-hosted, **kept all security hardening that's still applicable**: SHA-pin third-party actions (still valid, supply chain risk applies regardless of runner), `permissions: contents: read` on ci.yml (defense in depth), env-var pattern for `${{ steps.sim.outputs.dest }}` (M1 fix is structurally correct), `pages.yml` on ubuntu-latest (was the right call from H4), `actions/checkout@v6` unification, `security.yml` concurrency block (queue management, applies to GitHub-hosted too), GHA "Fork pull request workflows from outside collaborators" set to "Require approval for all outside collaborators" (defense for any future self-hosted experiment + general OSS hygiene), Dependabot security updates enabled. Stopped LaunchAgent + uninstalled service + deregistered runner via `gh api -X DELETE /repos/b150005/skeinly/actions/runners/22` + deleted `/Users/b150005/Development/Tools/actions-runner-skeinly/` directory. `docs/en/repo-policy.md` "Security posture (self-hosted CI runner)" section deleted (no longer accurate; the branch protection ruleset section remains). Lume CLI itself stays installed on host for any future ad-hoc VM use, but no longer integrated with GHA. Net effect on Phase 39 launch: CI returns to the parallel-on-3-runners GitHub-hosted model (~25min total per push), all 6 required status checks (`Shared Module`, `Android (Build + Test)`, `iOS (Build + Test)`, `Android E2E (Maestro)`, `iOS E2E (Maestro)`, `CodeQL Analysis (swift, macos-latest, manual)`) targeting the canonical hosted runner labels they were originally written for. Lesson learned recorded for future readers: self-hosted on a public repo demands isolation (VM/container) — the apparent speedup from running on real hardware is offset by the security and maintenance burden, and ephemeral GitHub-hosted runners' fresh-state guarantee is more valuable than it looks.


---

## Phase 24.x — Push notifications (closed)

Phase 24 wave shipped 2026-05-09 → 2026-05-13 across 7 sub-slices (24.0 ADR + 24.1 data spine + 24.2 permission UX + 24.2e token acquisition + 24.3 send paths + 24.4 event matrix + 24.5 deep links + 24.6 privacy policy). All slices use the established lambda-seam DI + `expect/actual` patterns from earlier waves; no new architectural surface. Operator-side actions all completed (Apple `.p8` + Google SA + Firebase project + Database Webhook config). HARD-GATE for alpha tester invites satisfied at 24.6 close.

Detailed inline entries promoted from CLAUDE.md `### Completed` (Phase 24.0 / 24.1 / 24.2):

- **Phase 24.2**: KMP `expect/actual` push permission UX + Settings → Notifications row + entry-point dispatches (per ADR-017 §3.6) — closes the in-app pre-permission explainer surface end-to-end across both platforms; **token acquisition + `device_tokens` upsert deferred to Phase 24.2e** because user-side Firebase project setup (`google-services.json` decode + `firebase-messaging` Gradle dep) and Apple Developer Push capability (`.p8` + AppDelegate `didRegisterForRemoteNotificationsWithDeviceToken:` Channel pipe + `aps-environment` entitlement) are prerequisite manual ops not autonomously executable. Ships as 6 sub-commits 24.2a / 24.2b / 24.2c-1 / 24.2c-2 / 24.2c-3 / 24.2d under the same wave entry. **24.2a `41871d3` `NotificationPermissionPrompter` scaffolding**: new `interface NotificationPermissionPrompter` + `NotificationPermissionPrompterImpl(settings: Settings)` at `shared/.../notifications/NotificationPermissionPrompter.kt` — gates the in-app explainer via `multiplatform-settings` `Settings`-backed boolean (`notification_permission_prompted`). Single global "have we asked?" bit (NOT per-trigger map) per ADR §3.6 deliberate-choice — "Not now" reads as global decision; surfacing the same explainer at three different entry points would be nag-style anti-pattern. New `enum class NotificationPromptTrigger { PR_LIST_INCOMING_WITH_PRS, PR_DETAIL_OPENED, PR_COMMENT_POSTED }` carries call-site intent. Forward-compat margin: per-trigger personalization is achievable without churning callers (the trigger arg already exists at every call site even though state today is global). +14 commonTest (`NotificationPermissionPrompterImplTest` 11 cases — initial state, single global record-then-shouldPrompt-false across all 3 trigger inputs, idempotent re-record, dismiss-then-permission-asked round trip; `NotificationPermissionStatusTest` 3 cases — closed-enum invariants). New shared test fakes `InMemorySettings` (in-memory `multiplatform-settings.Settings` impl) + `FakeNotificationPermissionPrompter`. **24.2b `4c49107` `PushTokenRegistrar` `expect/actual` scaffolding**: new `expect class PushTokenRegistrar` at `shared/.../notifications/PushTokenRegistrar.kt` with 3 suspend methods (`queryPermissionStatus()` + `requestPermission()` + `registerForPushNotifications(locale: String): String?`) — `expect class` over `interface` because Android's actual carries non-trivial `Context` constructor dep that doesn't generalize to iOS (mirroring the established `BugSubmissionLauncher` precedent from Phase 39.5). New closed `enum class NotificationPermissionStatus { NOT_DETERMINED, GRANTED, DENIED }` mapping to iOS `UNAuthorizationStatus` (provisional + ephemeral collapse to GRANTED) + Android `NotificationManagerCompat.areNotificationsEnabled()` × API 33+ `POST_NOTIFICATIONS`. 24.2b ships no-op stubs on both actuals — the entire UI scaffolding (ViewModel + screens) compiles + runs without crashes; the Settings → Notifications row simply shows "Disabled" and registerForPushNotifications returns null until 24.2d swaps in real OS-level reads + 24.2e wires actual FCM/APNs token acquisition. **24.2c-1 `133ec29` permission ViewModel + OsSettingsLauncher + i18n**: `NotificationPermissionViewModel` at `shared/.../ui/notifications/` parameterized on lambdas (NOT the `expect class` directly — `expect class`-bridged `final class` cannot be subclassed in commonTest, so `queryPermissionStatus: suspend () -> NotificationPermissionStatus` + `requestPermission: suspend () -> NotificationPermissionStatus` + `registerForPushNotifications: suspend (locale) -> String?` + `openOsSettings: () -> Unit` lambdas form the test seam at the DI boundary; this is the established lambda-seam DI pattern from `BugReportPreviewViewModel` in Phase 39.5). State carries `osStatus: NotificationPermissionStatus`, `isExplainerVisible: Boolean`, `isRequestingPermission: Boolean`. 5 events: `TriggerEncountered(trigger)` (decides whether to surface explainer based on OS state + prompter), `UserAcceptedExplainer` (records prompter `permission_asked` + fires `requestPermission()` + on GRANTED routes through `registerForPushNotifications(locale)`), `UserDismissedExplainer` (records `recordInAppDismiss(PR_LIST_INCOMING_WITH_PRS)` as the audit-trail anchor — global state per ADR §3.6, the trigger arg is informational), `OpenOsSettingsRequested`, `RefreshStatus`. Init re-reads OS status; non-fatal failure paths swallow exception and keep current state. New `expect class OsSettingsLauncher` + Android/iOS stubs at `shared/.../notifications/OsSettingsLauncher.kt` — Android constructor takes `Context` (via Koin `androidContext()`); iOS parameterless. **i18n** (+11 keys, 419 → 430): `title_notifications_explainer`, `body_notifications_explainer` (the disclosure copy that names what notifications would be sent for + how to revoke later), `action_enable_notifications` / `action_not_now_notifications` (explainer CTAs), `state_notifications_enabled` / `state_notifications_disabled` (Settings row trailing label), `label_notifications_section` (Settings header), `body_notifications_explanation` (Settings row helper text), `action_open_os_settings` (deep-link CTA), plus 2 more for the explainer subhead + dismissed-state placeholder. Reuses `action_back` / `title_error` / `action_ok`. JA semantic divergence on "Not now" → 「あとで」 (more natural Japanese than literal「今は不要」). +15 commonTest (`NotificationPermissionViewModelTest` 15 cases — init refreshes status, TriggerEncountered surfaces explainer only when `osStatus == NOT_DETERMINED && shouldPrompt == true`, UserAcceptedExplainer records + fires permission request + on GRANTED registers token, UserDismissedExplainer records + closes dialog without firing OS prompt, OpenOsSettingsRequested invokes lambda, RefreshStatus updates osStatus, query-failure swallows exception silently, register-failure swallows silently after permission grant). **24.2c-2 `9c3028e` explainer Compose + SwiftUI Settings row + iOS bridge**: `NotificationPermissionExplainerDialog(isVisible, isRequestingPermission, onAccept, onDismiss)` at `shared/.../ui/notifications/` — Compose `AlertDialog` with title + body + Enable/Not now `TextButton`s, both disabled while `isRequestingPermission` plus a `CircularProgressIndicator` on the Enable button while the OS prompt round-trip is in flight. testTags: `notificationPermissionExplainerDialog` (root), `enableNotificationsButton`, `notNowNotificationsButton`. Mounted from `SettingsScreen` (Phase 41.x consumer; Compose). iOS mirror at `iosApp/iosApp/Screens/SettingsScreen.swift` adds `notificationHolder: ScopedViewModel<NotificationPermissionViewModel, NotificationPermissionState>` + `notificationExplainerBinding` (defensive — alert button closures fire synchronously before isPresented flips, so the dismissal-without-button path is only reachable on iOS swipe-to-dismiss-style interactions) + `notificationStatusLabelKey` 3-state mapping with `default:` arm preventing future enum addition silent-mislabel + `.alert(title_notifications_explainer, isPresented: notificationExplainerBinding)`. Beta section in Settings (Compose + iOS) gains the new "Notifications" `ListItem` with the trailing `state_notifications_*` label + tap routing to `OpenOsSettingsRequested`. New iOS bridge accessors `KoinHelperKt.getNotificationPermissionViewModel()` + `KoinHelperKt.wrapNotificationPermissionState(flow)`. **24.2c-3 `96a2ac6` (this session) entry-point dispatches + explainer mounts**: closes the loop where the explainer was nominally mounted (24.2c-2) but never surfaced because no surface dispatched `TriggerEncountered`. `PullRequestDetailNavEvent` gains `data object CommentPosted` — emitted on the success path of `postCommentInternal` so the screen layer can route the engagement signal to `NotificationPermissionViewModel` without coupling the notification subsystem into the PR detail ViewModel itself. Compose `PullRequestListScreen` takes optional koin-resolved `notificationViewModel`, fires `TriggerEncountered(PR_LIST_INCOMING_WITH_PRS)` via `LaunchedEffect` keyed on `(filter, pullRequests.isNotEmpty())`, mounts `NotificationPermissionExplainerDialog` as a Scaffold sibling. Compose `PullRequestDetailScreen` takes the same VM, fires `TriggerEncountered(PR_DETAIL_OPENED)` keyed on `state.pullRequest != null` (post-loadInitial, NOT during loading-spinner phase), routes the new `CommentPosted` nav event to `TriggerEncountered(PR_COMMENT_POSTED)`, mounts the explainer at the dialog level. iOS SwiftUI mirrors — both screens scope a `NotificationPermissionViewModel` via `ScopedViewModel`, derive `shouldDispatchIncomingTrigger` for the list dispatch (Bool diff at the SwiftUI layer, not full-state diff), observe `pullRequest != nil` for the detail dispatch via `.onChange`, add a `case is PullRequestDetailNavEventCommentPosted` arm to the nav collector, mount the `.alert(notificationExplainerBinding)` per the Settings → Notifications binding shape. Kotlin enum bridging confirmed: `NotificationPromptTrigger.PR_LIST_INCOMING_WITH_PRS` surfaces as `.prListIncomingWithPrs` on Swift (SCREAMING_SNAKE → camelCase per the `SettingsScreen.swift` `NOT_DETERMINED → .notDetermined` precedent). +1 commonTest (`PostComment success emits CommentPosted nav event for notification trigger` — locks the new ViewModel contract). The prompter's global "asked" bit makes a hypothetical refire (back-to-Incoming round trip / re-enter detail) idempotent. **24.2d `<this commit>` native registrar + manifest + OsSettingsLauncher**: real OS-level implementations replace 24.2b/c-1 no-op stubs. iOS `PushTokenRegistrar.ios.kt` bridges `UNUserNotificationCenter.getNotificationSettings(...)` + `requestAuthorization(options:completionHandler:)` onto coroutines via `suspendCancellableCoroutine`. Authorization options request `UNAuthorizationOptionAlert | Badge | Sound` (no critical / time-sensitive — those need separate Apple entitlement applications); `.provisional` and `.ephemeral` collapse to GRANTED at the domain layer per ADR §3.6 (provisional permits APNs token acquisition; ephemeral is App Clip lifetime). Android `PushTokenRegistrar.android.kt` reads `NotificationManager.areNotificationsEnabled()` (API 24+, our `minSdk = 26` floor is well above) plus API 33+ `Context.checkSelfPermission(POST_NOTIFICATIONS)` directly via platform APIs (NOT via `androidx.core` to avoid growing the shared module's Android dependency surface). Combined gate: GRANTED requires both legs; partial-grant cases collapse to DENIED so the UI surfaces the OS Settings deep-link. **API 33+ caveat**: `checkSelfPermission` cannot distinguish "never asked" from "denied" without an Activity (only `shouldShowRequestPermissionRationale` can); 24.2d's defensive choice is to treat any not-fully-granted state on API 33+ as DENIED — 24.2e refines this with the activity-scoped `ActivityResultLauncher`. Android `requestPermission` delegates to `queryPermissionStatus` for 24.2d (no Activity context at construction time; the real launcher is 24.2e). Real `OsSettingsLauncher.android.kt` builds `Intent(Settings.ACTION_APP_NOTIFICATION_SETTINGS).putExtra(EXTRA_APP_PACKAGE, packageName).addFlags(FLAG_ACTIVITY_NEW_TASK)` — the FLAG is load-bearing because the Application Context Koin injects has no Activity stack (same wiring as `BugSubmissionLauncher.android`). Real `OsSettingsLauncher.ios.kt` opens `NSURL(string: UIApplicationOpenSettingsURLString)` via `UIApplication.sharedApplication.openURL(...)` — `UIApplicationOpenSettingsURLString` always resolves on real devices + simulators (no `canOpenURL` gate needed). **`AndroidManifest.xml`** gains `<uses-permission android:name="android.permission.POST_NOTIFICATIONS" />` — required regardless of `minSdk` because the runtime request only fires once the manifest declares the permission (below API 33 the install-time grant stays implicit). `registerForPushNotifications` stays no-op on both platforms with a clear "Phase 24.2e wires FCM / APNs token + device_tokens upsert" header — token acquisition needs (a) Firebase project setup (`google-services.json` decode + Gradle plugin + `firebase-messaging` dep) and (b) Apple Developer Push capability (`.p8` registered + AppDelegate Channel pipe + `aps-environment` entitlement), both of which are user-side manual ops + not autonomously executable. **Tests (+1 commonTest, 1456 → 1486 across the entire 24.2 wave; +30 net)**: 24.2a +14, 24.2c-1 +15, 24.2c-3 +1; 24.2b / c-2 / d are platform-actual surfaces not testable in commonTest. **Pre-push invariants all green** at 24.2d: `:shared:ktlintCheck`, `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64`, `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` (1486 tests), `:shared:koverVerify`, `verifyI18nKeys` (430 keys, +11 from the 419 baseline). iOS `xcodebuild ... build` ✅. Android `:androidApp:assembleDebug` ✅. **Forward-compat anchors for Phase 24.2e**: lambda-seam DI pattern means the production wiring just changes the `registerForPushNotifications` lambda from `{ null }` to `{ locale -> registrar.registerForPushNotifications(locale) }` once 24.2e wires real FCM token acquisition + `DeviceTokenRepository` upsert. The Android Activity-scoped permission launcher path is the only meaningful behavioral change between 24.2d's "delegate to query" `requestPermission` and 24.2e's real prompt — the host `MainActivity.registerForActivityResult(RequestPermission()) { granted -> registrar.onPermissionResult(granted) }` block + a new `onPermissionResult(Boolean)` method on the registrar.

- **Phase 24.1**: Data spine (per ADR-017 §6) — `device_tokens` table + Edge Function `notify-on-write` shell + Database Webhook config doc + new EF-6 secret. **No client wiring this slice; no actual APNs/FCM sends** (Phase 24.3). **Migration 025 `device_tokens`** applied to prod via `mcp__supabase__apply_migration`: composite UNIQUE `(user_id, platform, token)` for idempotent client upserts; `locale TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'en-US' CHECK IN ('en-US', 'ja-JP')` closed enum; `ON DELETE CASCADE` on `user_id` so ADR-005 `delete_own_account` RPC cascades device tokens out atomically; `idx_device_tokens_user_platform` hot-path index for the Edge Function fan-out lookup; `BEFORE UPDATE` trigger touching `updated_at`; full RLS with own-row SELECT/INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE policies (service-role bypass for the Edge Function reads at fan-out time). **search_path lock** on `touch_device_tokens_updated_at()` per Supabase database-linter 0011 (`function_search_path_mutable`) — pinned to `public, pg_temp` to prevent attacker-controlled schema hijacking; applied as a follow-up migration to prod (Migration UI shows it as `phase_24_1_lock_touch_device_tokens_search_path`); the local migration 025 file's CREATE FUNCTION carries the `SET search_path = public, pg_temp` clause inline so re-application is idempotent. **Edge Function `notify-on-write`** at `supabase/functions/notify-on-write/`: shell receives Database Webhook deliveries from 3 source tables (`pull_requests` INSERT/UPDATE, `pull_request_comments` INSERT), verifies `Authorization: Bearer <SKEINLY_DATABASE_WEBHOOK_SECRET>` HTTP header via constant-time string compare (mirrors `revenuecat-webhook` Bearer pattern; **2026-05-09 correction**: ADR + Edge Function originally specified HMAC-SHA256 body signature against `x-supabase-webhook-signature` header, but per the [Supabase Database Webhooks doc](https://supabase.com/docs/guides/database/webhooks) and verified against the actual Dashboard UI, Database Webhooks do NOT auto-sign payloads — Dashboard exposes only Method / URL / Timeout / HTTP Headers / HTTP Parameters with no signing-secret field; pivoted to custom Authorization Bearer header via Dashboard's HTTP Headers section), parses payload, routes to pure helpers in `mapping.ts` for recipient computation, resolves display names + pattern title via service-role JOINs, then **logs each computed dispatch as `notify_on_write_skipped_send` structured log line** (Phase 24.1 SHELL — Phase 24.3 wires the actual APNs/FCM HTTP send + 410/404 token cleanup). Always returns 200 to Supabase's webhook retry logic — push delivery failures (Phase 24.3+) MUST NOT trigger Database Webhook retries (which would re-fan-out to all recipients, not just the failed one). **`mapping.ts`** pure helpers: `WebhookPayload` / `PullRequestRow` / `PullRequestCommentRow` typed projections; `TemplateKey` closed enum (5 templates: `pr_opened` / `pr_commented` / `pr_merged_to_author` / `pr_closed_to_author` / `pr_closed_to_owner`); `EN_TEMPLATES` + `JA_TEMPLATES` registries with parametric template functions + null-safe fallbacks (`Someone` / `誰か`, `a pattern` / `パターン`, `a pull request` / `プルリクエスト`); `renderBody(locale, key, params)` reads `device_tokens.locale` (Phase 24.3+) and selects the matching string with locale fallback to `en-US` for unknown locales; `computePrOpenedDispatches` (target owner notified, self-PR excluded), `computePrCommentedDispatches` (PR participant set MINUS comment author, deduplicated via Set), `computePrStatusChangeDispatches` (open → merged | closed branches with actor-vs-participant routing per ADR-014 §1 + §5; defense-in-depth no-ops for unexpected actor / null author_id / status flip from non-open). **Heuristic actor inference for `pull_requests` UPDATE** in absence of explicit `actor_id` column: merge → target owner (per ADR-014 §5 RPC `WHERE owner_id = v_caller`); close → defaults to target owner (Phase 24.4 may revisit if heuristic mis-attributes any real close). **Tests (+29 Deno tests, 34 → 63)**: `mapping.test.ts` covers template parity (EN/JA share key set, every key produces non-empty body in both locales), `renderBody` exhaustive locale + null fallback matrix (12 cases), `computePrOpenedDispatches` (3 cases including self-PR exclusion), `computePrCommentedDispatches` (5 cases including author exclusion variants + null author), `computePrStatusChangeDispatches` (8 cases including all status flip permutations + defense-in-depth no-ops). All tests pass via `deno test supabase/functions/notify-on-write/`. **`supabase/webhooks.md`** new doc — source of truth for the 3 Database Webhook configurations (NOT versioned in `supabase/migrations/` since Database Webhooks live in Dashboard UI; this doc is the reproduction recipe). Steps for create / verify / remove + the no-signing-secret-in-UI caveat per the 2026-05-09 correction. **EF-6 `SKEINLY_DATABASE_WEBHOOK_SECRET`** added to `release-secrets.md` (en + ja): `openssl rand -hex 32` generation, `supabase secrets set` registration, Dashboard `Authorization: Bearer <value>` HTTP header co-registration on each of the 3 webhooks, rotation procedure, dependency chain note. Bulk verification expected count updated from 5 → 6 Edge Function secrets. Rotation table extended. **Naming**: `SKEINLY_` prefix is load-bearing — Supabase reserves `SUPABASE_*` for platform-injected env vars per the [Edge Function limits doc](https://supabase.com/docs/guides/functions/limits#secrets), and `supabase secrets set` rejects names starting with that prefix. Phase 24.1 originally drafted `SUPABASE_DATABASE_WEBHOOK_SECRET` and was renamed pre-deployment after the prefix-reservation rule was surfaced (2026-05-09 user check). **`notify-on-write/README.md`** documents the architecture diagram, deployment, smoke test commands (curl with `Authorization: Bearer <secret>` header per the 2026-05-09 auth correction), Phase 24.1 SHELL contract (what's wired vs deferred), privacy notes. **User-side actions** (not autonomously executable): (1) `openssl rand -hex 32` to generate `SKEINLY_DATABASE_WEBHOOK_SECRET`, (2) `supabase secrets set SKEINLY_DATABASE_WEBHOOK_SECRET=<value>`, (3) `git checkout main && git pull origin main` (CRITICAL — see stale-source pitfall below), then `supabase functions deploy notify-on-write` (picks up `verify_jwt = false` from `supabase/config.toml` automatically), (4) Dashboard → Database → Webhooks → create 3 hooks per `supabase/webhooks.md` table — **each webhook uses Type = `Supabase Edge Functions` (NOT `HTTP Request`) with the function dropdown picking `notify-on-write`, and the auto-populated `Authorization: Bearer <anon key>` HTTP Headers row MUST be overwritten with `Bearer <SKEINLY_DATABASE_WEBHOOK_SECRET value>`** because the anon key is public-embedded in the mobile app (anyone with the app could otherwise POST hand-crafted payloads directly to the Edge Function URL and trigger fake push notifications). (5) trigger smoke test via curl per README. **End-to-end verified 2026-05-09** via curl × 3 (valid Bearer → HTTP 200 `{"ok":true,"dispatch_count":0}`; wrong Bearer → HTTP 401; missing Authorization → HTTP 401). **2026-05-09 retrospective (3 corrections during single-day deploy)**: (a) HMAC misconception — original ADR-017 cut assumed Supabase auto-signs payloads via HMAC-SHA256 against `x-supabase-webhook-signature`, which the official Database Webhooks doc (https://supabase.com/docs/guides/database/webhooks) and Dashboard UI both contradict; corrected to custom `Authorization: Bearer` HTTP header (commit `f490b57`). (b) Webhook type choice — interim instructions (`f490b57`) used `HTTP Request` type with manual URL entry, which is functionally equivalent but harder to maintain (URL typo risk, no rename resilience, opaque Dashboard listing); replaced with `Supabase Edge Functions` type after surfacing both options against the `supabase_functions.http_request()` trigger function definition (verified on prod via `pg_get_functiondef`) — the trigger passes HTTP Headers through unchanged regardless of UI type, so the Edge Function code path is identical between the two types (commit `1a4d8c3`). (c) Stale-source deploy — `supabase functions deploy notify-on-write` was first run while local repo was checked out to a pre-`f490b57` commit, deploying the old HMAC-checking source; the deployed function then 401-rejected every Bearer-bearing webhook delivery from the (correctly-configured) Database Webhooks. Diagnosed via `mcp__supabase__get_edge_function` (read raw deployed source) and resolved by redeploying the latest worktree files via `mcp__supabase__deploy_edge_function` MCP tool. Both notify-on-write and revenuecat-webhook READMEs now carry an explicit `git pull` step + `ezbr_sha256` verification recipe to prevent recurrence at next rotation / redeploy. Pre-push invariants: ktlintCheck UP-TO-DATE (no Kotlin touched), compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64 UP-TO-DATE (no Kotlin touched), testAndroidHostTest UP-TO-DATE (no test changes; 1456 commonTest unchanged), koverVerify UP-TO-DATE, verifyI18nKeys UP-TO-DATE (no i18n changes — push body strings live in Edge Function string table, not in shared resources, per ADR §3.7), Deno tests 63 pass (34 from revenuecat-webhook + 29 from notify-on-write). **Forward-compat anchor for Phase 24.2**: `device_tokens` table is the integration seam — Phase 24.2's `PushTokenRegistrar` `expect/actual` calls `INSERT ... ON CONFLICT (user_id, platform, token) DO UPDATE` from iOS (`UNUserNotificationCenter` `didRegisterForRemoteNotificationsWithDeviceToken` callback) + Android (`FirebaseMessaging.getInstance().token`). For Phase 24.3: `mapping.ts` `renderBody` is the integration seam for the actual APNs / FCM payload `body` field; `NotificationDispatch[]` from `routePayload` is the input to the per-(recipient, platform, token) fan-out loop.

- **Phase 24.0**: ADR-017 cut for push notifications (commit `1ed59e2`) — opens Phase 24 wave with the data shape, transport choice, trigger mechanism, event scope, permission UX, localization model, deep link routing, and 6-sub-slice plan locked in before any code lands. **User policy shift 2026-05-09**: Phase 24 reprioritized from `Post-v1.0` to active roadmap; new HARD-GATE for Phase 39 closed-beta tester invites is "Phase 24 collaboration push delivery exists end-to-end". **Key decisions resolved by agent team**: (1) **Two-stack push transport** — iOS = APNs direct (`.p8` + ES256 JWT signing in Edge Function via `djwt` JSR), Android = FCM HTTP v1 (Firebase Admin SDK SA → OAuth 2.0 access token → FCM v1 endpoint). NO Firebase iOS Push SDK — Apple stack is native and adding Firebase iOS dep for a feature Apple has natively isn't justified. Two code paths instead of one but each is ~50 lines of platform-specific code, sharing the same `notify-on-write` envelope (recipient lookup, locale resolution, body templating). FCM v1 chosen over deprecated server key API (Google sunset early 2026). (2) **Trigger source = Supabase Database Webhooks** (NOT Postgres triggers + `pg_net`) — Supabase-managed feature configured via Dashboard, no `pg_net` extension surface, UI-visible wiring. (Original ADR cut also claimed "auto-signed with HMAC-SHA256"; this was factually incorrect per the [Supabase Database Webhooks doc](https://supabase.com/docs/guides/database/webhooks) — corrected at Phase 24.1 deploy time on 2026-05-09 to a custom `Authorization: Bearer <secret>` HTTP header configured per-webhook in the Dashboard's HTTP Headers section. Decision A/B/C still resolves to B; only the auth-mechanism details changed.) Trade-off: webhook config is NOT versioned in `supabase/migrations/`; mitigation = `supabase/webhooks.md` doc (refreshed at every Phase 24.x slice that adds/removes webhooks). (3) **Phase 24 MVP event scope (3 events)** — (a) PR opened on owned pattern (target owner notified), (b) PR comment added (PR participant set MINUS comment author notified), (c) PR merged or closed by other party (other side notified). Other event types in `activities` table (chart edits, project updates, fork events, chart_revisions, subscriptions changes, share events) deliberately excluded — push noise erodes engagement; collaboration moments are the high-signal subset. (4) **`device_tokens` table** with `(user_id, platform, token)` UNIQUE composite key, RLS-gated own-row SELECT/INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE, ON DELETE CASCADE on user_id (Phase 17 / ADR-005 account deletion path). `locale` column carries BCP-47 tag for server-side localized notification rendering. Token rotation = client upsert; invalid token cleanup = APNs/FCM error code (410 BadDeviceToken / 404 UNREGISTERED) → Edge Function DELETE. (5) **Permission UX = deferred-prompt pattern** — NOT requested at app launch or onboarding (industry data shows 50–80% denial rate when decontextualized). Pre-permission in-app explainer dialog at first PR-related action (`PullRequestListScreen` Incoming with PRs / `PullRequestDetailScreen` open / first PR comment posted). Primary CTA "Enable" → triggers OS prompt; secondary "Not now" → records in-app dismiss without polluting OS denial state. New `NotificationPermissionPrompter` KMP service tracks "have we asked at trigger X?" via `Preferences`. Settings "Notifications" row deep-links to OS settings via `UIApplication.openSettingsURLString` / Android `Settings.ACTION_APP_NOTIFICATION_SETTINGS`. (6) **Localization = server-side based on `device_tokens.locale`** — Edge Function reads BCP-47 tag and selects EN/JA from in-function string table (~6 templates × 2 locales = 12 entries hardcoded). NOT client-renders because push lands in OS notification center even when app is killed; client cannot render then. Trade-off: notification body strings live in 2 places (Compose/SwiftUI for in-app + Edge Function for push). Mitigation: Deno test asserts `Object.keys(EN) == Object.keys(JA)` parity. (7) **Deep link routing** via `data.route` payload (`pull-request/<prId>` etc.). iOS = `UNUserNotificationCenterDelegate` parses + posts `Notification.Name("openPushRoute")` → `AppRootView` `.onReceive(...)` → `path.append(Route.pullRequestDetail(prId:))` (same NotificationCenter publisher pattern Phase 39.5 used for shake-to-bug-report). Android = `FirebaseMessagingService.onMessageReceived` builds `PendingIntent` with route extra → MainActivity `onNewIntent` → `navController.navigate`. Cold-start path: launch options (iOS) + intent extras (Android) feed same `openPushRoute` mechanism with one-shot `LaunchedEffect` after NavGraph mounts. (8) **NO Phase 24 in-app notification feed** — existing `activities` table + Phase 36.5 `ActivityFeedScreen` covers in-app surface; push is cross-medium amplifier, not duplicate UI. **Sub-slice plan (locked in as ADR §6)**: 24.0 (this ADR + CLAUDE.md promotion, no code) → 24.1 (`device_tokens` migration NNN + Edge Function `notify-on-write` shell + Database Webhook config doc + new `SKEINLY_DATABASE_WEBHOOK_SECRET` EF-6 secret registration; ~15 Deno tests + 0 commonTest + 0 i18n) → 24.2 (KMP `expect/actual` `PushTokenRegistrar` for iOS APNs registration + Android FCM token retrieval, `NotificationPermissionPrompter` service, pre-permission Composable + SwiftUI sheet, Settings "Notifications" row + OS deep-link, +25 commonTest + 12 i18n keys) → 24.3 (PR comment notification end-to-end with real APNs + FCM HTTP calls via `djwt`, recipient resolution via `pull_requests` JOIN, 410/404 token cleanup, +20 Deno tests) → 24.4 (PR-opened + merged + closed events, +10 Deno tests) → 24.5 (deep link routing iOS/Android native + cold-start path) → 24.6 (privacy policy update + closed-beta validation). Each independently shippable. **Forward-compat anchors**: `device_tokens.locale` field unlocks future personalization (timezone-aware send time, tester segmentation) without client-side path. `notify-on-write` Edge Function pattern reusable for future "table change → server-side action" flows beyond push. `data.route` payload shape extends to additional route types (`pattern/<patternId>` etc.) as new event sources land. **Explicitly NOT in Phase 24 MVP**: topic-based subscriptions (over-engineering at ≤100 testers; Phase 24+ if scale demands), rich notification content (Notification Service Extension scope), notification grouping/threading (Phase 24+ if testers complain about per-comment spam), scheduled/cron notifications (no current use case), push for non-collaboration events, email digest channel, Web Push (Skeinly is mobile-only). **Vendor pillars already prepared**: APNs `.p8` (vendor-setup A0a-2) + EF-1/2 secrets registered, `FIREBASE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_JSON` (EF-3) registered, iOS Bundle ID Push capability enabled in App ID + provisioning profile, Android FCM SDK SHA-1s registered. **Code review iterations**: ADR-only slice; no compile/test impact (1456 commonTest unchanged + verifyI18nKeys 391 keys unchanged + Deno tests 34 pass). Pre-push invariants `:shared:ktlintCheck` + `:shared:compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64` + `:shared:testAndroidHostTest` + `:shared:koverVerify` + `verifyI18nKeys` all green (doc-only changes). ADR sized 510 lines EN + ~190 line JA summary, matching ADR-015/016 precedent. Ships as Phase 24.0 = ADR + CLAUDE.md `### Planned — Phase 24` promotion + `### Completed` entry (this bullet) in one commit; Phase 24.1 (data spine) in next slice.

Wave-level status summary (from `### Planned — Phase 24 Push Notifications` section):

### Planned — Phase 24 Push Notifications (promoted 2026-05-09 to pre-Phase-40 GA scope)
- **Phase 24.0** ✅ — ADR-017 cut. See [docs/en/adr/017-phase-24-push-notifications.md](../docs/en/adr/017-phase-24-push-notifications.md) for full design.
- **Phase 24.1** ✅ — Data spine (`device_tokens` migration 025 + Edge Function `notify-on-write` shell + Database Webhook config doc).
- **Phase 24.2** ✅ — In-app pre-permission explainer + Settings → Notifications row + entry-point dispatches end-to-end on Compose + SwiftUI; native OS-level permission status read; OS Settings deep-link. Token acquisition + `device_tokens` upsert deferred to 24.2e.
- **Phase 24.2e** ✅ — FCM + APNs token acquisition + `device_tokens` upsert end-to-end on both platforms. New `DeviceTokenRepository` (commonMain) + `DeviceTokenRemoteOperations` Supabase port mirroring the `SubscriptionRemoteOperations` precedent (ADR-016 §4.2); Android `PushTokenRegistrar` calls `FirebaseMessaging.getInstance().token.await()` + `DeviceTokenRepository.upsertToken`; Activity-scoped `ActivityResultLauncher<RequestPermission>` wired via `attachLauncher` / `onPermissionResult` / `detachLauncher` lifecycle hooks on `MainActivity`. iOS `PushTokenRegistrar` routes `UIApplication.registerForRemoteNotifications()` through `NSObject.performSelector(NSSelectorFromString("registerForRemoteNotifications"))` (K/N's UIKit cinterop omits the symbol despite being public Obj-C since iOS 8); CONFLATED Channel<String?> + AtomicInt CAS guard for concurrent-call serialization; AppDelegate at `iosApp/iosApp/Core/Bridging/AppDelegate.swift` hex-encodes the 32-byte APNs token and forwards via `KoinHelperKt.handleApnsTokenReceived`; `@UIApplicationDelegateAdaptor(AppDelegate.self)` on `iOSApp` installs the bridge. `iosApp/iosApp/iosApp.entitlements` ships with `aps-environment = production` (TestFlight uses prod APNs; on-device debug push test is unsupported by design — Phase 24.4+ may revisit if a local-debug push iteration path becomes necessary). google-services Gradle plugin applies conditionally (only when `androidApp/src/{debug,release}/google-services.json` exists), so local dev + CI without the secret degrades gracefully (FCM init fails → `registerForPushNotifications` returns null silently). CI workflows (`ci.yml`, `e2e.yml`, `release.yml`) decode `FIREBASE_GOOGLE_SERVICES_JSON_BASE64` from `development` env (debug variant — Skeinly-Dev project) or `production` env (release variant — Skeinly Blaze project). +20 commonTest cases (1486 → 1506) covering `DeviceTokenRepositoryImpl` offline / sign-in / success / network failure / Unknown / locale variants / platform wire values / cancellation propagation + `RemoteDeviceTokenDataSource.ON_CONFLICT_COLUMNS` migration-025 anchor. Lambda-seam DI in `NotificationPermissionViewModel` (Phase 24.2c-1 precedent) makes the wire-up transparent — VM unchanged. **User-side prerequisites all satisfied at session start**: `androidApp/src/{release,debug}/google-services.json` placed locally (Skeinly Blaze + Skeinly-Dev Spark); Apple Developer Push capability + `.p8` (EF-1/EF-2) + Distribution Provisioning Profile with Push capability all registered. Pre-push invariants all green (1506 commonTest, ktlintCheck shared+androidApp, koverVerify, verifyI18nKeys 440 keys unchanged, assembleDebug, iOS xcodebuild build SUCCEEDED). Code review iterations: 0 CRITICAL / 1 HIGH / 2 MEDIUM / 3 LOW first pass; HIGH (Android `pendingResult` overwrite under concurrent `requestPermission`) fixed via early-return guard; MEDIUM-1 (iOS race on CONFLATED channel + tryReceive drain) fixed via AtomicInt CAS gate + try/finally; MEDIUM-2 (entitlements aps-environment hardcode) acknowledged as deliberate per session policy + documented inline; LOW-1 (`ON_CONFLICT_COLUMNS` test anchor) added; LOW-2 (`@Suppress`/val ignored idiom) replaced with comment-only branches preserving exhaustiveness; LOW-3 (Koin lookup caching in handleApnsTokenReceived) acknowledged informational, no action.
- **Phase 24.3** ✅ — APNs HTTP/2 + FCM HTTP v1 send paths wired (per [ADR-018](../docs/en/adr/018-phase-24-3-push-send-paths.md)). New `notify-on-write/apns.ts`: ES256 JWT signing via `jsr:@zaubrik/djwt@^3` (audited library — single source for both APNs ES256 and FCM RS256, `crypto.subtle.importKey("pkcs8", ...)` for the `.p8`, in-instance JWT cache 50-min TTL with 5-min refresh margin), production-only `https://api.push.apple.com` host (ADR-018 §3.5 — closed beta uses TestFlight builds with `aps-environment = production`; `device_tokens.environment` column deferred to Phase 24.4+), `apns-topic` header hardcoded to `io.github.b150005.skeinly`, body `{ aps: { alert: { title: "Skeinly", body: <renderBody locale> }, sound: "default" } }`. New `notify-on-write/fcm.ts`: SA RS256 JWT → OAuth 2.0 access token exchange → Bearer to FCM v1 `messages:send` endpoint, in-instance access token cache with 5-min margin (ADR-018 §3.2 — parallel to APNs JWT cache), 401 UNAUTHENTICATED triggers a single retry after forced cache reset (defensive against clock skew). New `notify-on-write/_fakes.ts`: `globalThis.fetch` monkey-patch with per-token APNs/FCM/OAuth response arranging, `generateTestApnsCredentials` + `generateTestServiceAccount` use WebCrypto `crypto.subtle.generateKey` + `exportKey("pkcs8")` to produce real ECDSA-P-256 / RSA-2048 PEMs at test runtime (no production key committed; importKey + signing path runs against valid cryptographic material). `index.ts` `dispatchAll(supabase, dispatches, apnsCreds, fcmSa): SendStats`: per-recipient `Promise.allSettled` over device_tokens (ADR-018 §3.3 — within recipient parallel, across recipients sequential), `processOutcome` runs `DELETE FROM device_tokens WHERE token = $1` on `delete_token` outcomes (ADR-018 §3.4 mapping: APNs `410 Unregistered` / `400 BadDeviceToken` / `400 DeviceTokenNotForTopic`, FCM `404 UNREGISTERED` / `403 SENDER_ID_MISMATCH`; everything else log + continue with structured `console.log` events `device_token_deleted` / `notify_on_write_transient_error` / `notify_on_write_config_error`), unknown reasons fall through to `transient_error` (fail-safe — never delete on unknown signal). Graceful degradation when secrets missing: APNs creds null → iOS dispatches log `apns_credentials_missing` + skip, same for FCM SA → Android skips; `send_stats.skipped_no_creds` counter surfaces the omission. **Tests (+33 Deno tests, 68 → 101)**: `apns.test.ts` 15 (3 JWT signing/caching incl. iat-advances-after-reset for ECDSA-P-256 deterministic-signature compatibility, 9 classifier matrix incl. unknown-4xx/5xx fall-through to transient, 3 e2e sendApns); `fcm.test.ts` 13 (3 OAuth caching, 7 classifier incl. UNAUTHENTICATED retry sentinel + 403-without-SENDER_ID_MISMATCH config_error, 3 sendFcm e2e incl. 401-retry-cache-reset via oauthCallCount); `dispatch.test.ts` 5 integration (single-success, mixed success/delete on same recipient verifies DELETE only the bad one, two-recipient fan-out verifies OAuth fetched once across pushes via cache, missing-creds → skipped_no_creds + zero fetch traffic, ghost-recipient zero-tokens skip silently). Type fixes: `crypto.subtle.importKey("pkcs8", buffer, ...)` requires `ArrayBuffer` not `Uint8Array<ArrayBufferLike>` so `base64DecodeToBuffer` returns `.buffer` directly. `jsr:@zaubrik/djwt@^3` is the actual JSR import (NOT `@djwt/djwt` — that namespace doesn't exist on JSR; verified via `https://jsr.io/api/scopes/zaubrik/packages` returning `djwt` v3.0.2). Pre-push invariants: 101 Deno tests pass (62 in `notify-on-write/` directory + 39 in `revenuecat-webhook/`) + `deno lint` clean. No KMP / Swift code touched, so commonTest / iOS xcodebuild / verifyI18nKeys all UP-TO-DATE. **User-side actions** (not autonomously executable): (1) `git checkout main && git pull origin main` then `supabase functions deploy notify-on-write` (existing 4 secrets `APPLE_APNS_KEY_P8` / `APPLE_APNS_KEY_ID` / `APPLE_TEAM_ID` / `FIREBASE_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_JSON` cover the whole 24.3 wiring — no new secrets); (2) Trigger smoke test via README curl recipe with a real PR-comment INSERT payload, verify a push lands on a TestFlight device whose `device_tokens` row exists. **Forward-compat anchors for Phase 24.4**: `mapping.ts`'s `computePrOpenedDispatches` / `computePrStatusChangeDispatches` already produce correct `NotificationDispatch[]` for PR-opened / PR-merged / PR-closed events — Phase 24.4 just needs a deploy + smoke test on real prod webhook deliveries for those event types. The `dispatchAll` shape generalizes without code change.
- **Phase 24.4** ✅ — PR-opened / merged / closed end-to-end dispatch was already covered by Phase 24.1 (mapping.ts `computePrOpenedDispatches` + `computePrStatusChangeDispatches` exhaustive recipient matrix + 3 Database Webhooks routing INSERT and UPDATE on `pull_requests`) + Phase 24.3 (`dispatchAll` runs the same Promise.allSettled loop for every dispatch regardless of templateKey). No additional Edge Function code change. The remaining work is user-side end-to-end validation: trigger each event type via real PR open / close / merge on a TestFlight build with a registered `device_tokens` row, verify push lands. CLAUDE.md `Tech Debt Backlog` does NOT need a follow-up entry because the code surface is identical to Phase 24.3's PR-comment path; the only delta is the Database Webhook fan-out tables (`pull_requests` INSERT for opened + UPDATE for status flip), which were already configured in Phase 24.1's webhooks.md.
- **Phase 24.5** ✅ — Deep link routing wired end-to-end across iOS + Android (per ADR-017 §3.8). **Edge Function**: `mapping.ts` `NotificationDispatch` gains `route: string` field; new `pullRequestRoute(prId)` helper produces `pull-request/<prId>` (uniform for all Phase 24 events — `computePrOpenedDispatches` keys off `row.id`, `computePrCommentedDispatches` off `comment.pull_request_id`, `computePrStatusChangeDispatches` off `row.id`). `apns.ts` payload now includes top-level `data: { route }` (alongside `aps`); `fcm.ts` message body includes `data: { route }` (delivered as `RemoteMessage.data` foreground + intent extras background). `index.ts` `sendOne` threads `dispatch.route` through both platform paths. **iOS**: `AppDelegate.swift` becomes `UNUserNotificationCenterDelegate`. `application(_:didFinishLaunchingWithOptions:)` registers self with `UNUserNotificationCenter.current()` + cold-start path checks `launchOptions[.remoteNotification]` and re-posts via `NotificationCenter` after `DispatchQueue.main.async` (so AppRootView's `.onReceive` is wired by the time the post lands; without the async dispatch the post would race scene-graph init). `userNotificationCenter(_:willPresent:withCompletionHandler:)` requests `[.banner, .list, .sound]` so foreground notifications get full UX parity with background. `userNotificationCenter(_:didReceive:withCompletionHandler:)` parses `userInfo["data"]["route"]` defensively. New `Notification.Name.openPushRoute` + `openPushRouteUserInfoKey` constants. `AppRootView` gains `.onReceive(NotificationCenter.default.publisher(for: .openPushRoute))` + private `parsePushRoute(_ raw: String) -> Route?` helper that maps `pull-request/<prId>` → `Route.pullRequestDetail(prId:)`; unknown / malformed routes return nil and the consumer silently drops. **Android**: new `androidApp/.../notifications/SkeinlyMessagingService.kt` extends `FirebaseMessagingService`. `onMessageReceived` (foreground only — background+killed are auto-displayed by FCM with `data` map flowing into MainActivity intent extras at tap) builds a `NotificationCompat`-styled banner with `PendingIntent` carrying `EXTRA_PUSH_ROUTE` to MainActivity. `onNewToken` no-op (Phase 24.2c-3 trigger paths re-acquire on next user-visible collaboration moment). New `collaboration` `NotificationChannel` (importance default) with EN + JA labels in `values/strings.xml` + `values-ja/strings.xml`. `AndroidManifest.xml` registers the service with `com.google.firebase.MESSAGING_EVENT` action filter, `android:exported="false"`. `MainActivity` gains `pushRoute by mutableStateOf<String?>(null)` + `EXTRA_PUSH_ROUTE: String = "route"` companion + `extractPushRoute(intent)` reading from intent extras in `onCreate` + `onNewIntent` (singleTop launchMode delivers the same Activity instance). `SkeinlyNavHost` gains `pushRoute` + `onPushRouteConsumed` parameters; `LaunchedEffect(pushRoute)` calls shared `parsePushRoute(raw): Any?` (commonMain helper, `internal` visibility for unit-testability) that returns the typed `PullRequestDetail(prId)` route, navigates, then resets host state. New deps: `firebase-messaging` direct (shared's `implementation` doesn't propagate to androidApp call sites) + `androidx.core:core-ktx` 1.13.1 (NotificationCompat / NotificationManagerCompat / ContextCompat). **Tests (+9 total)**: `mapping.test.ts` +3 (pullRequestRoute helper, comment route uses pull_request_id NOT comment.id, status-change route uses row.id); `ParsePushRouteTest.kt` +6 commonTest (pull-request → PullRequestDetail with prId, uuid prId verbatim, empty prId returns null, unknown prefix returns null, empty string returns null, prId containing slash preserved). **Deno**: 65 tests (62 + 3); **commonTest**: 1512 (1506 + 6). Pre-push invariants all green: ktlintCheck (auto-formatted), compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64, testAndroidHostTest, koverVerify, verifyI18nKeys (no string changes), assembleDebug, iOS xcodebuild build SUCCEEDED. **User-side actions** (not autonomously executable): (1) `git pull origin main && supabase functions deploy notify-on-write` — same secret set as 24.3 (no new secrets). (2) Trigger smoke test on a TestFlight iOS device + Play Internal Android device with a registered `device_tokens` row, verify tap on the delivered push lands on the PR detail screen. **Forward-compat anchor for Phase 24+ event sources**: `parsePushRoute` (Kotlin commonMain + Swift mirror) prefix table extends to `pattern/<patternId>` / `share/<token>` / etc. without restructuring the dispatch shape — `mapping.ts` `pullRequestRoute(prId)` already pattern-establishes the per-event-type helper.
- **Phase 24.6** ✅ — Privacy policy update for push notifications (per ADR-017 §3.11). New "Push Notifications" `<h3>` subsection added to both `docs/public/privacy-policy/index.html` (EN) and `docs/public/ja/privacy-policy/index.html` (JA mirror), placed inside the existing "Information We Collect" / 「収集する情報」 section adjacent to the Phase 39.2 "Diagnostic Data" subsection. Discloses: (a) the 4 collaboration event types that trigger push (PR opened on owned pattern, PR comment, PR merged or closed); (b) the 4 fields stored in `device_tokens` (anonymous APNs/FCM device token, BCP-47 locale, platform, user_id); (c) notification body content includes other Skeinly users' display names visible on the recipient's lock screen — symmetric data flow (other users see your name in their pushes); (d) revocation path is OS-level (Settings → Notifications → Skeinly), takes effect immediately; (e) account deletion (ADR-005) cascades device_tokens via FK; (f) Apple Push Notification service + Firebase Cloud Messaging are the routing infrastructure (links to Apple + Google privacy policies — JP versions on the JA page). JA copy uses natural Japanese phrasing throughout (「プッシュ通知」「許可付与が同意となります」「他の Skeinly ユーザーに関するデータ」「カスケード削除」), not literal EN translation. **Closed-beta validation** is the user-side action item that closes Phase 24.x: invite 1–2 testers via TestFlight Internal + Play Internal Testing, verify each of the 3 event types delivers push, verify cold-start tap routes correctly to PullRequestDetail, verify token cleanup on uninstall (the 410/404 path Phase 24.3 wired). HARD-GATE for Phase 39 closed-beta tester invites is satisfied at the close of this slice. **No code / test delta** — privacy policy doc is HTML-only, no shared resources or i18n keys touched. **User-side actions remaining**: deploy + smoke test for 24.3 / 24.5 (described in those entries), then closed-beta tester invites.

---

## Phase 26.x — Auth infrastructure: OAuth + MFA + biometric + post-OAuth profile gate (closed)

Phase 26 wave shipped 2026-05-14 → 2026-05-15 across 11 sub-slices (26.0 ADR + 26.1 Apple iOS + 26.2 Android Google Credential Manager + 26.x Apple-on-Android web-OAuth + 26.3 iOS Google GIDSignIn + 26.4 linkIdentity merge + 26.5 TOTP MFA + 26.6 biometric + 26.7 post-OAuth profile gate + 26.8 privacy policy + Tech Debt). Strategic motivation: future user-to-user pattern marketplace (operator note 2026-05-14) requires retrofittable-resistant auth foundation from start, so wave landed pre-alpha despite low current asset value. Per-platform OAuth uses native IDToken bridges (Apple iOS = `SignInWithAppleButton`, Apple Android = Supabase web-OAuth + Custom Tabs, Google iOS = `GIDSignIn` direct bridge, Google Android = `androidx.credentials` Credential Manager) — no Firebase iOS Push SDK added; two stacks instead of one but each ~50 LOC per platform.

Cross-cutting design decisions: lambda-seam DI throughout (mirrors AuthViewModel / BugReportPreviewViewModel / NotificationPermissionViewModel precedents) so commonTest doesn't pull supabase-kt; `AuthState.MfaChallengeRequired` sealed variant gates AAL2 at the navigation layer; recovery code stored bcrypt-hashed server-side via SECURITY DEFINER RPC; biometric template never leaves OS-managed secure enclave; sensitive-action gates live at ViewModel layer (not inside UseCase) to preserve Cancelled-vs-Failed UX distinction; `OAuthProfileSetup` route inserted between Authenticated transition and ProjectList one-time per install gated by `prefs.isCompleted`.

Inline entries promoted from CLAUDE.md `### Planned — Phase 26 Auth Infrastructure`:

### Planned — Phase 26 Auth Infrastructure (OAuth + MFA + Biometric) — **alpha-launch HARD-GATE**, 2026-05-14
Operator flagged 2026-05-14 while filling A0d-6 Data Safety (account creation methods sub-question). Apple Sign-In capability was set up at the App ID + Provisioning Profile level (A0a-1, A0a-4) but the actual app implementation was never wired — `iosApp.entitlements` carries only `aps-environment` + `com.apple.developer.associated-domains`, NOT `com.apple.developer.applesignin`; the codebase has zero references to SignInWithApple / GoogleSignIn / OAuth / SSO / MFA / biometric. Operator confirms intent: **ship the full auth surface (OAuth + MFA + biometric) before alpha launch**, motivated by a planned future user-to-user pattern marketplace (operator note 2026-05-14) — even though current asset value does not warrant MFA, building the auth foundation now avoids a difficult retrofit when marketplace ships (where seller / creator / buyer accounts hold real monetary value). Promotes to HARD-GATE (stricter than Phase 25 friend-only's "parallel" framing).

- **Phase 26.0** ✅ — ADR-022 cut. See [docs/en/adr/022-phase-26-auth-infrastructure.md](../docs/en/adr/022-phase-26-auth-infrastructure.md) (553 lines EN + 284 lines JA mirror). 8 decisions resolved with full agent-team deliberation: (a) **cross-platform symmetric OAuth** — Apple + Google on both iOS and Android, alongside email/password as fallback; (b) Supabase `signInWithIdToken` + native `auth.mfa.*` confirmed; biometric is session-gate ONLY, not primary identity; (c) **explicit `linkIdentity` flow** for account merge (silent auto-merge vetoed on OWASP grounds); (d) OAuth display_name from `user_metadata.name` first-sign-in, Apple relay email surfaced as-is, Google avatar imported on opt-in only; (e) HIG/Material primary OAuth button per platform with secondary OAuth + collapsed email/password fallback; (f) MFA opt-in for alpha + GA, mandatory at marketplace seller/creator role transition (Phase 50+); (g) TOTP recovery code 16-char base32, one-time display, bcrypt-hashed server-side; lost-device via magic-link recovery; lost-both = irrecoverable by design (no admin break-glass); (h) biometric scope = 5-min foreground re-auth gate + sensitive-action gates (account-deletion, MFA-disable); primary biometric login deferred (Supabase Auth doesn't bind biometric to identity natively). **Scope cuts**: passkey (Supabase no native support), SMS-MFA (SIM-swap risk), hardware keys (mobile-only over-engineering), WebView custom UI (HIG violation), phone-OTP primary, magic-link primary, email-only-alpha (A0d-6 lock-in pain), auto-merge, first-claim-wins. **New release-secrets**: 6 (3 Apple Sign-In: P8/KeyID/ServicesID; 3 Google OAuth: Web/iOS/Android client IDs) — all Dashboard-only, no GitHub Secret slots, no client bundles. **Total commonTest delta across 26.1-26.7**: ~106 (1536 → ~1642). **Operator-side actions**: Apple Developer Portal (Services ID + Sign In with Apple Key creation), Google Cloud Console (3 OAuth 2.0 client IDs), Supabase Dashboard (enable Apple + Google providers + paste credentials), A0d-6 Data Safety re-submission at Phase 26.7 close.
- **Phase 26.1** — iOS Apple Sign-In wiring. Add `com.apple.developer.applesignin` to `iosApp.entitlements`. Implement `AuthenticationServices` flow in SwiftUI LoginScreen (`SignInWithAppleButton` SwiftUI component or `ASAuthorizationAppleIDProvider` if more control needed). On success, send the resulting `identityToken` to Supabase via `signInWithIdToken(provider = "apple")`. Wire through `AuthViewModel` + `AuthRepository`. Configure Supabase Auth Apple provider in Dashboard (Services ID + Key ID + Team ID + `.p8` private key — see release-secrets.md for new secret slot).
- **Phase 26.2** — Android Google Sign-In wiring. Use `androidx.credentials` Credential Manager (Android 14+ recommended) or `com.google.android.gms:play-services-auth` (older API support). Implement Google ID token retrieval in Compose `LoginScreen` Android-specific path. Post ID token to Supabase via `signInWithIdToken(provider = "google")`. Configure Supabase Auth Google provider in Dashboard (OAuth 2.0 Web client ID + Android client ID + iOS client ID — see release-secrets.md for new secret slot).
- **Phase 26.x** ✅ — Apple-on-Android via Supabase web-OAuth + Custom Tabs (ADR-022 §6.1 symmetric coverage). Closes the cross-platform OAuth matrix: Apple-iOS (26.1) + Google-Android (26.2) + Google-iOS (26.3) + **Apple-Android (this slice)**. Architecture: supabase-kt's `signInWith(Apple)` (NON-IDToken) variant launches a Chrome Custom Tab to Supabase's hosted auth endpoint, which proxies through Apple's OAuth flow and redirects back to `skeinly://auth-callback`. `MainActivity.onCreate` + `onNewIntent` both call `supabaseClient.auth.handleDeeplinks(intent)` so the callback URL is parsed for cold-start AND warm-start paths. **Shared**: `AuthRepository.signInWithAppleViaWebOAuth()` is `suspend (): Unit` (no `OAuthSignInOutcome` envelope — supabase-kt browser-OAuth does NOT return a structured outcome; session emerges async on `observeAuthState()`). `AuthEvent.SignInWithAppleViaWebOAuth` object event + `handleAppleViaWebOAuth` private ViewModel handler with re-entrant guard. **Compose `LoginScreen.kt`** Apple button (previously disabled placeholder) now wires to the event — `testTag("signInWithAppleButton")` enabled when `!state.isSubmitting`. **SupabaseModule** `install(Auth)` block extended with `scheme = "skeinly"; host = "auth-callback"`. **AndroidManifest** new intent-filter for `skeinly://auth-callback` (DEFAULT + BROWSABLE categories, no `autoVerify` because custom schemes don't go through Play domain verification).
