MainActivity wires `getKoin().getOrNull<SupabaseClient>()` lazy lookup so local-only mode (no SupabaseConfig.isConfigured) silently no-ops the handleDeeplinks call. **Tests (+3 commonTest, 1512 → 1515)**: `apple via web oauth kicks off custom tabs and clears submit`, `apple via web oauth launch failure surfaces generic error`, `apple via web oauth submit guards reentry`. New `FakeAuthRepository.signInWithAppleViaWebOAuth()` call-counter stub. **i18n**: zero new keys — `action_continue_with_apple` already exists from Phase 26.2 placeholder. **Operator-side actions** (Dashboard-only, no GitHub Secrets / no client bundle changes): (1) Supabase Dashboard → Authentication → URL Configuration → Additional Redirect URLs → add `skeinly://auth-callback`. (2) Apple Developer Portal: **no new work** — the existing Phase 26.1 Apple Sign-In Key + Services ID handle Apple's OAuth endpoint server-side; Apple never sees the mobile app's custom URL scheme (only Supabase's HTTPS callback). Wiring activates immediately after Step 1; no client app rebuild needed if the user already has a Phase 26.x+ build. iOS path NOT exercised — iOS Apple sign-in goes through native SignInWithAppleButton + IDToken (Phase 26.1); the `scheme/host` config is symmetric but iOS Compose LoginScreen does not render (iOS uses SwiftUI LoginScreen.swift).
- **Phase 26.3** ✅ — iOS Google Sign-In via `GIDSignIn` SDK direct bridge (ADR-022 §6.2). Architecture decision: iOS Google takes the same direct-bridge pattern as iOS Apple Sign-In (Phase 26.1) — Swift owns presentation (GIDSignIn requires `UIWindow.rootViewController`), Kotlin owns repository forward. Bypasses the `OAuthClient.acquireGoogleIdToken` seam entirely. New iOS files: `GoogleSignInBridge.swift` (`Core/Bridging/`, mirrors `AppleSignInBridge` precedent + `@MainActor` + `signIn(forward:)` + `handle(url:)` for OAuth callback). New shared infra: `AuthEvent.SignInWithGoogleIdToken(idToken, nonce?)` variant + `AuthViewModel.handleGoogleIdToken` private helper routing to existing `forwardGoogleIdToken` + `KoinHelperKt.signInWithGoogleIdToken(idToken, nonce)` top-level bridge fn (parity with `signInWithAppleIdToken` shape, nullable nonce because GIDSignIn 8.x stamps no nonce by default — Supabase accepts nonceless Google ID tokens; parity with Android Phase 26.2 Credential Manager path). `OAuthClient.ios.actual` updated KDoc to document the direct-bridge pattern + still returns `OAuthIdTokenResult.Failure` (a structurally clean error path for any caller that hypothetically routes through the seam; `google id token bypasses acquisition seam` test locks the contract). `AppRouter.handleDeepLink` gives `GoogleSignInBridge.shared.handle(url:)` first crack at incoming URLs before falling through to `parseExternalRoute` — Google's OAuth callback URL scheme is consumed before the Universal Link parser runs against it. **SwiftPM dep**: `GoogleSignIn` from `https://github.com/google/GoogleSignIn-iOS` from "8.0.0" — adds both `GoogleSignIn` + `GoogleSignInSwift` products to `iosApp` target. **URL scheme**: `project.yml` `CFBundleURLTypes` gains a second entry referencing `$(GOOGLE_REVERSE_CLIENT_ID)` xcconfig variable. Production CI (`release.yml` `build-ios` job) decodes `IOS_GOOGLE_SERVICES_PLIST_BASE64` (production env) to `iosApp/iosApp/GoogleService-Info.plist` then runs `PlistBuddy -c "Print :REVERSED_CLIENT_ID"` to derive the URL scheme value, written into `iosApp/local.xcconfig` alongside `DEVELOPMENT_TEAM`. `build-ios` job gains `environment: production` (was previously env-unscoped) to access the plist secret. `ci.yml` + `e2e.yml` write the xcconfig variable empty — those workflows do not exercise the Google Sign-In flow. Half-configured release (plist secret missing) degrades gracefully — Apple Sign-In + email/password remain functional, Google Sign-In silently fails at runtime. **SwiftUI**: LoginScreen.swift gains a "Continue with Google" `Button` below the SignInWithAppleButton + divider, styled as `.bordered` + `.controlSize(.large)` Material-ish look with an SF Symbol `g.circle.fill` colored at Google's brand red `#EA4335` (avoids licensed PNG asset). Accessibility id `continueWithGoogleButton`. Apple HIG prominence preserved (Apple button stays first + native styling; Google is the secondary OAuth + a custom-styled button per Google's branding allowance for the iOS surface). **Tests (+6 commonTest, 1506 → 1512)**: `google id token success transitions to authenticated`, `google id token with explicit nonce forwards nonce to repo`, `google id token link required surfaces challenge`, `google id token repo failure surfaces generic error`, `google id token submit guards reentry`, `google id token bypasses acquisition seam`. **i18n**: zero new keys — `action_continue_with_google` already exists from Phase 26.2 (en + ja + xcstrings). **Docs**: `release-secrets.md` (en + ja) `IOS_GOOGLE_SERVICES_PLIST_BASE64` status flips from "Phase 26.2 forward-compat slot" to "Phase 26.3 WIRED" with the PlistBuddy + xcconfig flow documented; bulk verification production env table extended from 3 → 4 entries. **Operator-side actions** (satisfied at session start): (1) production iOS `GoogleService-Info.plist` placed locally + `IOS_GOOGLE_SERVICES_PLIST_BASE64` GitHub Secret in `production` env ✅; (2) Cloud Console OAuth iOS Client created ✅ (Phase 26.2 prerequisite); (3) Supabase Auth Google provider configured ✅ (Phase 26.2). Wiring activates on the next tag-push triggered `release.yml` run.
- **Phase 26.4** ✅ — linkIdentity merge flow for OAuth ↔ email/password account collision (ADR-022 §6.3). When `signInWithIdToken` returns Supabase's `user_already_exists`, the app now surfaces an inline link-identity prompt: user types their existing password → `signInWithEmail(challenge.email, password)` → on success calls `client.auth.linkIdentityWithIdToken(provider, pendingIdToken) { nonce = ... }` to bind the OAuth identity to the existing account. Three-step state machine in `AuthViewModel.handleSubmitLinkIdentity` with re-entrant guard. **Domain models extended**: `LinkIdentityChallenge` + `OAuthSignInOutcome.LinkIdentityRequired` gain `pendingIdToken: String` + `nonce: String?` so the resolution step can re-submit the same token Supabase already rejected (carried in-memory only, no persistence — short-lived JWT). **Surface added**: `AuthRepository.linkPendingIdentity(provider, pendingIdToken, nonce)` + `AuthRepositoryImpl` impl calling `auth.linkIdentityWithIdToken` (supabase-kt 3.6 API verified via JAR introspection; takes `IDTokenProvider` + idToken + config block with `nonce` field — server-side verifies nonce match + token-email vs session-email match, preventing the OWASP A07 silent-merge takeover vector). **Event**: new `AuthEvent.SubmitLinkIdentity(password)` + existing `DismissLinkIdentityPrompt` repurposed as Cancel binding. **Compose `LoginScreen.kt`**: previously had NO link-identity rendering (placeholder text only in JA spec — iOS had a simple `.alert`); now adds `AlertDialog` with body + password `OutlinedTextField` + Submit/Cancel buttons + `isSubmitting` disabled binding. `rememberSaveable` keyed on `challenge.pendingIdToken` (not email) so same-email re-challenges get a fresh password buffer. Submit button carries `state_linking_identity` `contentDescription` while in-flight so TalkBack announces the pending state. **SwiftUI `LoginScreen.swift`**: replaced Phase 26.1's `.alert` with `.sheet` hosting a new `LinkIdentityForm` view (SecureField + buttons + ProgressView). `capturedLinkEmail @State` captures the challenge email at presentation time to prevent flicker-to-empty during the ~300ms sheet dismiss animation when Kotlin clears the state. iOS submit button carries `.accessibilityLabel` switching between action / state strings per VoiceOver guidance. **Identity-link-failure path**: when `linkPendingIdentity` throws AFTER `signInWithEmail` succeeded, the prompt clears + session stays Authenticated + `println` structured-log surfaces `(provider, errorClass, message)` for observability — pendingIdToken intentionally NOT logged to avoid credential leak. Tech Debt: Phase 26.7 will surface a Settings → Linked Accounts retry path (alpha tester signal will reveal whether the silent fallback is acceptable). **i18n (+5 keys)**: `title_link_identity` / `body_email_already_used_link_prompt` / `action_link_identity` / `action_dismiss_link_identity` / `state_linking_identity` × en + ja CMP + iOS xcstrings (471 → 476). **Tests (+11 commonTest)**: 1 `AuthRepositoryImplTest` null-client; 10 `AuthViewModelTest` cases — full-state-machine apple, full-state-machine google nonce-null, password-fails-stays-on-challenge, identity-link-fails-keeps-session-intact, uses-challenge-email-ignores-form-email, submit-guards-reentry (via `AuthRepository by authRepo` delegation + CompletableDeferred gate), submit-no-op-when-no-challenge, dismiss-drops-pending-token-zero-retention, apple-challenge-populates-pendingIdToken-nonce, google-challenge-populates-pendingIdToken-null-nonce. Plus call-counter additions to FakeAuthRepository (`lastLinkedProvider`, `lastLinkedIdToken`, `lastLinkedNonce`, `linkPendingIdentityCallCount`, `linkPendingIdentityError`, `lastSignInEmail`). **Pre-push invariants all green**: ktlintCheck, compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64, testAndroidHostTest, koverVerify, verifyI18nKeys (476), verifyIosBetaFlag, assembleDebug, `xcodebuild build` iOS Simulator. **Code review iterations**: 0 CRITICAL / 0 HIGH / 3 MEDIUM (rememberSaveable key + dead i18n key + silent link-failure) / 2 LOW (SwiftUI email flicker + missing a11y label) — ALL 5 findings landed in fix-up commit before push. **Tech Debt for Phase 26.7**: surface a Settings → Linked Accounts retry path when `handleSubmitLinkIdentity`'s identity-link branch fails after a successful password sign-in — alpha currently silent-fallback per ADR-022 acceptance.
- **Phase 26.5** ✅ — MFA via TOTP end-to-end on Compose + SwiftUI (ADR-022 §6.4, indexed in ADR as "Phase 26.4" but CLAUDE.md sub-slice 26.5 per the handoff numbering). **Migration 034** `mfa_recovery_codes` applied to prod (`mcp__supabase__apply_migration` 2026-05-14): table with own-row SELECT RLS only, bcrypt code_hash + consumed_at audit trail, UNIQUE partial index on `(user_id) WHERE consumed_at IS NULL` for single-active-row invariant, ON DELETE CASCADE on auth.users for ADR-005 + ADR-023 parity. **3 SECURITY DEFINER RPCs** (all `search_path = ''` locked + `REVOKE EXECUTE FROM anon, PUBLIC` + `GRANT EXECUTE TO authenticated`): `register_mfa_recovery_code(p_code_hash text)` wipes any prior active code + inserts fresh hash atomically; `consume_mfa_recovery_code(p_code text) RETURNS boolean` bcrypt-verifies via `extensions.crypt(plain, stored) <> stored` idiom + `FOR UPDATE` lock prevents concurrent double-consume; `hash_recovery_code(p_plain text) RETURNS text` server-side bcrypt helper (cost 10 ~100ms) — KMP-portable bcrypt impl not needed client-side. **AuthState extended**: new `AuthState.MfaChallengeRequired(userId, email)` sealed variant. `observeAuthState()` now combines `sessionStatus + refreshCauseFlow + mfa.statusFlow` (the latter is the load-bearing addition); when `MfaStatus.enabled && !active` emit MfaChallengeRequired instead of Authenticated. Verify path elevates AAL2 → statusFlow re-emits with `active = true` → observe flow yields plain Authenticated → root navigator pops the gate screen. **Agent-team deliberation** (architect / product-manager / security-reviewer / implementer) on "where does the gate live" resolved to AuthState variant over form-state field: AAL2 enforcement at navigation layer beats per-screen form because root navigator already routes on AuthState, and form-level only works for screens still hosting the user (LoginScreen) — post-sign-in AAL1 sessions emerge Authenticated everywhere otherwise. **`AuthRepository` extended (+7 methods)**: `observeMfaStatus(): Flow<MfaEnrollmentStatus>` (sealed: NotEnrolled / EnrolledUnverified(factorId) / Enrolled(factorId)) + `enrollMfaTotp(): MfaEnrollment` + `verifyMfaEnrollment(factorId, code)` + `submitMfaChallenge(code)` + `consumeRecoveryCode(plain): Boolean` + `disableMfa(factorId)` + `regenerateRecoveryCode(): String`. **`AuthRepositoryImpl`** wires supabase-kt 3.6 `auth.mfa.{enroll, retrieveFactorsForCurrentUser, createChallenge, verifyChallenge, unenroll}` (API surface verified via auth-kt-api.jar introspection — `FactorType.TOTP` parametric base, `TOTP.Response { secret, qrCode (SVG), uri }`, `MfaApi.statusFlow`, `MfaLevel { current, next: AAL1/AAL2 }`, `UserMfaFactor.isVerified` computed property) + `postgrest.rpc("hash_recovery_code"|"register_mfa_recovery_code"|"consume_mfa_recovery_code")` for the recovery-code layer. Client-side recovery code generation: `Uuid.random()`-seeded 16-char base32 (RFC 4648 alphabet minus `0`/`1`/`8` visual-confusion chars) yielding ~80 bits entropy, never persisted client-side. **`MfaEnrollmentViewModel`** + **`MfaChallengeViewModel`** with lambda-seam DI (mirrors AuthViewModel Phase 26.1 precedent — keeps VMs testable without supabase-kt). Enrollment 3-phase state machine: PairingQr (QR seed + manual entry surface; QR rendering deferred to follow-up Tech Debt for alpha) → ConfirmCode (6-digit TOTP + verify) → RecoveryCodeDisplay (one-time copy-on-tap). Challenge 2-phase: EnterCode (6-digit TOTP) ⇄ EnterRecoveryCode (base32 plaintext). 3-failed-attempt UX lockout in `MfaChallengeViewModel` per ADR §6.4 (server-side rate-limiting still active independently). **Compose screens**: `MfaEnrollmentScreen.kt` + `MfaChallengeScreen.kt` (testTag-driven for E2E + a11y-aware via labels + isError bindings). `NavGraph.kt` adds `MfaEnrollment` + `MfaChallenge` routes; AuthState observer adds the MfaChallengeRequired branch that `navigate(MfaChallenge) { popUpTo(Login) inclusive }` so back-tap from the gate falls through to Unauthenticated cleanly. **SwiftUI mirrors**: `MfaEnrollmentScreen.swift` + `MfaChallengeScreen.swift` via `ScopedViewModel<MfaXxxViewModel, MfaXxxUiState>` (Kotlin → Swift bridge through `KoinHelperKt.getMfaXxxViewModel()` + `wrapMfaXxxState(flow:)`). `AppRouter.swift` adds `Route.mfaEnrollment` + `Route.mfaChallenge` cases + hash entries + body branch for `AuthStateMfaChallengeRequired` (full-screen gate, NOT pushed onto path). **Settings → Security section** (Compose + SwiftUI): new "Two-factor authentication" row with trailing "Enabled"/"Disabled" label sourced from `observeMfaStatus()`. Tap routes to enrollment when NotEnrolled, or surfaces a destructive-confirmation dialog (`title_mfa_disable_confirm` + `body_mfa_disable_warning`) → `SettingsEvent.DisableMfaConfirmed` → `disableMfa(factorId)` when Enrolled. SettingsScreen.swift exposes new `onEnableMfaClick` init param. **Tests (+34 commonTest, 1661 → 1695)**: 7 `AuthRepositoryImplTest` null-client throws-when-unconfigured cases (observeMfa emits NotEnrolled / all 6 suspend methods throw IllegalStateException); 13 `MfaEnrollmentViewModelTest` cases (Start success + failure + idempotent, UpdateCode filter + cap, AdvanceToConfirm, SubmitCode short / happy / failure, DismissRecoveryCode, ClearError, re-entry guard via CompletableDeferred, MfaEnrollment data-class copy/equals, MfaEnrollmentStatus sealed-distinction); 14 `MfaChallengeViewModelTest` cases (UpdateCode digits-only / uppercase-alphanumeric, SubmitCode happy / short-rejection / failure-increments / 3-attempt lockout / post-lockout-no-call, SwitchToRecoveryCode resets, recovery happy + false + blank + throw, SwitchToTotp, ClearError); 3 `SettingsViewModelTest` MFA-disable cases (no-op when not enrolled + targets active factor ID + failure surfaces Generic error). +1 `RevenueCatAuthBridgeTest` `ControlledAuthRepository` shim (no-op throws for all 7 new methods + 1 setMfaStatus state-helper). **`FakeAuthRepository`** gains call-counter + outcome-override fields for every new method + `setMfaStatus(status)` test seam + `setAuthState` updated to capture MfaChallengeRequired's userId. **Cross-class compile fixes**: `RevenueCatAuthBridge` + `RealtimeSyncManager` both add `is MfaChallengeRequired -> Transient/wait` branches — AAL1 sessions don't identify with RevenueCat or subscribe to realtime channels (gate-equivalent to Loading). **Kover excludes** extended for the new Compose screens (`*ScreenKt*` pattern continues) + `AuthRepositoryImpl$Companion` (private base32 generator + RNG helper unreachable from commonTest without supabase-kt integration harness) + `AuthRepositoryImpl$observeAuthState$*` / `$observeMfaStatus$*` synthetic flow inner classes. Coverage gate passes at 80%+. **i18n (+28 keys, 475 → 503)**: `label_security_section` / `label_two_factor_auth` / `state_mfa_{enabled,disabled}` / `action_{enable,disable}_mfa` / `title_mfa_{enroll,confirm_code,recovery_code,challenge,disable_confirm}` / `body_mfa_{enroll_scan_qr,confirm_code,recovery_code_warning,challenge_prompt,disable_warning}` / `label_mfa_{manual_secret,recovery_code_input}` / `action_mfa_{advance_to_confirm,verify,recovery_code_saved,use_recovery_code,back_to_totp}` / `error_mfa_{invalid_code,invalid_recovery_code,locked,enroll_failed}` × en + ja CMP + iOS xcstrings. JA copy uses natural Japanese throughout (「2要素認証」「認証アプリでスキャン」「復旧コードを保管してください」「あとで」-style). **Pre-push invariants all green**: ktlintCheck (shared + androidApp) + compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64 + testAndroidHostTest (1695 tests) + koverVerify + verifyI18nKeys (503 keys) + verifyIosBetaFlag + assembleDebug + iOS `xcodebuild build`. **Operator-side actions**: none — Supabase Auth MFA is enabled by default at project creation; only verify Authentication → Settings → "Enable MFA" toggle is on (no `supabase secrets` / Dashboard URL Configuration / OAuth provider config changes needed). **Forward-compat anchors for Phase 26.6 (biometric)**: `AuthState.MfaChallengeRequired` gate at navigation layer composes with biometric re-auth gate as additional auth-flow state; lambda-seam DI in `MfaEnrollmentViewModel` + `MfaChallengeViewModel` extends to biometric callbacks without churning consumers. Tech Debt: KMP QR-code rendering (Compose + SwiftUI multiplatform library) deferred to follow-up — current implementation surfaces the otpauth URI + base32 secret as monospace text for manual entry into the authenticator app.
- **Phase 26.6** ✅ — Biometric re-auth + sensitive-action gates end-to-end on Compose + SwiftUI (ADR-022 §6.5). **Deps added**: `androidx.biometric:biometric:1.2.0-alpha05` + `androidx.lifecycle:lifecycle-process:2.9.5` to the `shared/` androidMain block (NOT androidApp's — the actuals import the symbols directly so they need to be on the shared classpath). **New commonMain types**: `expect class BiometricAuthenticator { fun canAuthenticate(): BiometricAvailability; suspend fun authenticate(title, reason): BiometricResult }` + closed enums `BiometricAvailability { Available, NoHardware, NotEnrolled, Lockout }` + `sealed interface BiometricResult { Success / Cancelled / Failed / Unavailable }` + `enum SensitiveAction { AccountDeletion, MfaDisable }` + `expect class AppLifecycleObserver { val events: Flow<AppLifecycleEvent> }` + `sealed interface AppLifecycleEvent { Backgrounded / Foregrounded }`. **`BiometricGuardian`** (commonMain): single Mutex-serialized orchestrator with `onBackgrounded()` + `suspend requireForResume(): BiometricResult` + `suspend requireForAction(SensitiveAction): BiometricResult`. Lambda-seam DI on `queryAvailability` + `performAuthentication` + `resolveString` + injectable `Clock` so commonTest can drive the state machine without standing up the BiometricPrompt / LAContext actuals OR the CMP resources runtime. Threshold read on every `requireForResume`; on threshold-not-exceeded / opt-out / cold-start (no prior background timestamp) the gate short-circuits to `Success`. On availability-not-Available the Guardian returns `Failed` from `requireForResume` (per ADR §3.8 — opted-in user on a degraded device signs out so they re-enable via OS Settings) and bypasses to `Success` from `requireForAction` (in-app destructive-confirm dialog at the call site remains the sole gate on no-hardware/no-PIN devices). Mutex+`@Volatile` combo prevents two simultaneous OS prompts when concurrent resume + action gates race. **`BiometricPreferences`** (commonMain, multiplatform-settings-backed): `biometricEnabled: StateFlow<Boolean>` + `reauthThresholdSeconds: StateFlow<Long>` + setters; `ThresholdChoice` closed enum `{ OneMinute=60, FiveMinutes=300, FifteenMinutes=900, OneHour=3600 }` with `fromSeconds(value)` defensive coercion to FiveMinutes (the default). Backed by the non-encrypted `skeinly_prefs` Settings instance (NOT the `named("auth")` encrypted store — threshold + opt-in are UX state, not credentials). **`BiometricLifecycleBridge`** (commonMain, top-level): `startBiometricLifecycleBridge(scope, guardian, lifecycleObserver, onResumeAuthInvalidated)` collects from `AppLifecycleObserver.events` and feeds `onBackgrounded()` / `requireForResume()`. Invokes the `onResumeAuthInvalidated` callback on `Failed`/`Cancelled`/`Unavailable` outcomes — the platform binding wires this to `SignOutUseCase()`. Code-reviewer caught the initial cut returning a `SharedFlow<BiometricResult>` that both platforms accidentally discarded, leaving the security loop open; folding the sign-out callback into the bridge fn closes it by construction. **Android actual `BiometricAuthenticator.android.kt`**: uses `BiometricManager.canAuthenticate(BIOMETRIC_STRONG or DEVICE_CREDENTIAL)` for availability + `BiometricPrompt(FragmentActivity, mainExecutor, AuthenticationCallback)` for prompting. `setAllowedAuthenticators(STRONG | DEVICE_CREDENTIAL)` enables device PIN/passcode fallback (mutually exclusive with `setNegativeButtonText`, so the OS provides its own localized "Use PIN" / "Cancel"). `@Volatile`-marked nullable strong reference to the host FragmentActivity attached at onCreate / detached at onDestroy (mirrors PushTokenRegistrar's launcher attachment pattern). `suspendCancellableCoroutine` with `invokeOnCancellation { prompt.cancelAuthentication() }` for clean teardown across config changes. Error-code → `BiometricResult` mapping covers `ERROR_USER_CANCELED` / `ERROR_NEGATIVE_BUTTON` / `ERROR_CANCELED` → `Cancelled`; `ERROR_NO_BIOMETRICS` / `ERROR_NO_DEVICE_CREDENTIAL` / `ERROR_HW_NOT_PRESENT` / `ERROR_HW_UNAVAILABLE` → `Unavailable`; everything else → `Failed`. **iOS actual `BiometricAuthenticator.ios.kt`**: `LAContext.canEvaluatePolicy(.deviceOwnerAuthentication, &error)` for availability with the err code → `BiometricAvailability` mapping; `LAContext.evaluatePolicy(.deviceOwnerAuthentication, localizedReason)` for prompting with hop back to `Dispatchers.Main` before resuming the Continuation. Fresh `LAContext` per evaluation per Apple's docs (single context should only be reused for the same logical authentication). `invokeOnCancellation { context.invalidate() }` cancels pending evaluation. `BetaInteropApi` opt-in for the `ObjCObjectVar<NSError?>` pattern handling the `&error` out-parameter (production-stable; Beta tag is wrapper-API-level only). **Android actual `AppLifecycleObserver.android.kt`**: `ProcessLifecycleOwner.get().lifecycle.addObserver(...)` lazily on first subscription via Flow's `onStart` (main-thread requirement satisfied via `withContext(Dispatchers.Main)`). `MutableSharedFlow` with `replay=0` + `BufferOverflow.DROP_OLDEST` (drop-old semantics; Guardian handles the no-signal-yet path structurally). **iOS actual `AppLifecycleObserver.ios.kt`**: `callbackFlow` registering `NSNotificationCenter.addObserverForName` for `UIApplicationWillEnterForegroundNotification` + `UIApplicationDidEnterBackgroundNotification`, removing via `awaitClose`. Wrapped in `shareIn(GlobalScope, SharingStarted.Eagerly, replay=0)` so the upstream observer-registration happens exactly once for the process lifetime regardless of collector count — closes the per-subscription `NSNotificationCenter` observer-leak that the original `MutableSharedFlow + onStart` shape would surface if multiple collectors subscribed (code-reviewer §HIGH-3). **`MainActivity`** pivoted `ComponentActivity` → `FragmentActivity` (the AndroidX hierarchy is `FragmentActivity` extends `ComponentActivity`, NOT the other way around as the original ADR §6.5 cut claimed — ADR amendment landed in this slice); all existing surfaces (`setContent`, `enableEdgeToEdge`, `registerForActivityResult`, `rememberNavController`, `dispatchTouchEvent` 3-finger gesture detector) keep working unchanged because FragmentActivity extends ComponentActivity. New `attachActivity(this)` / `detachActivity()` calls on the BiometricAuthenticator in `onCreate` / `onDestroy`. **`SkeinlyApplication`** + **`iOSApp.swift`**: both invoke `startBiometricLifecycleBridge(...)` after the RevenueCat bridge with `onResumeAuthInvalidated = { signOutUseCase() }`. **`BiometricSettingsViewModel`** (commonMain): observes preferences via combined `biometricEnabled` + `reauthThresholdSeconds` flow; events `ToggleEnabled(Boolean)` (re-queries availability at the toggle moment so a user who walks through OS Settings to enroll biometric mid-session can complete the toggle without re-mounting) + `SelectThreshold(ThresholdChoice)`. `canToggle` computed from `availability == Available`. **Compose `BiometricSettingsScreen`** + **SwiftUI `BiometricSettingsScreen.swift`**: toggle on/off + threshold radio picker (1m / 5m / 15m / 1h) + unavailable-status copy when OS reports NoHardware / NotEnrolled / Lockout. iOS uses `Form` + `Toggle` + `Section` for native HIG appearance; Compose uses `ListItem` + `Switch` + `RadioButton`-with-clickable-Row for Material 3 a11y semantics. **Settings → Security row** "Biometric authentication" with trailing "Enabled"/"Disabled" label sourced from the same singleton VM that drives the settings screen (so toggling on the pushed screen reactively updates the row's label). **Sensitive-action gate wiring** (CRITICAL design pivot from initial cut): gates live at the **ViewModel layer**, NOT inside the UseCase. `SettingsViewModel.performDisableMfa` + `SettingsViewModel.performDeleteAccount` both call `requireBiometricForX()` BEFORE flipping the spinner state — Cancelled returns silently (user intent → no error toast), Failed/Unavailable surface `ErrorMessage.Generic`. Initial cut pushed the gate down into `DeleteAccountUseCase` which forced a `UseCaseError.PermissionDenied` return on cancel, rendering "Permission denied" toast to a user who just tapped Cancel on the biometric dialog (code-reviewer §HIGH-2). Moving the gate up preserves the Cancelled-vs-Failed UX distinction. Both methods carry an `isXing = true` re-entry guard at the entry point so a quick back+re-tap during the biometric prompt window cannot queue two RPC calls (code-reviewer §MEDIUM-1). **i18n (+14 keys, 503 → 517)**: `title_biometric_settings` / `state_biometric_{enabled,disabled}` / `label_biometric_threshold_picker` / `value_biometric_threshold_{1m,5m,15m,1h}` / `body_biometric_{reauth,account_deletion,mfa_disable}_reason` / `state_biometric_unavailable_{no_hw,not_enrolled}` / `body_biometric_settings_explanation` × en + ja CMP + iOS xcstrings. JA uses natural Japanese (「生体認証」「再認証までの時間」「Skeinly に戻るには本人確認が必要です」). **Tests (+27 commonTest, 1695 → 1722)**: 10 `BiometricGuardianTest` (threshold short-circuits {disabled / cold-start / under-threshold}, fires prompt + clears timestamp on success, returns Failed on unavailable, propagates Cancelled, action-bypass on unavailable, action surfaces Cancelled with correct reason copy, AccountDeletion routes correct reason, edge-case at exact threshold boundary); 8 `BiometricSettingsViewModelTest` (init + toggle ON Available + toggle ON NotEnrolled blocked + toggle OFF always passes + SelectThreshold persists + reactive prefs flow + canToggle reflects unavailability + toggle ON re-queries availability); 3 new `SettingsViewModelTest` MFA-disable biometric cases (Cancelled silent / Failed error / Success falls through); 3 new SettingsViewModelTest AccountDelete biometric cases (Cancelled / Failed / Success); 2 `ThresholdChoiceTest` (canonical-values + out-of-range coercion); plus `FakeBiometricPreferences` test fake. **Kover excludes** extended: `BiometricSettingsScreenKt*` + `BiometricAuthenticator*` (platform actuals) + `AppLifecycleObserver*` (platform actuals) + `BiometricLifecycleBridgeKt*` (single launched collector — exercised by Guardian tests). **Pre-push invariants all green twice** (initial cut + after code-reviewer fix-up): ktlintCheck (shared + androidApp) + compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64 + testAndroidHostTest (1722 tests) + koverVerify (80%+ after excludes) + verifyI18nKeys (517 keys) + verifyIosBetaFlag + assembleDebug + iOS `xcodebuild build` SUCCEEDED. **Code review iterations**: 1 CRITICAL (sign-out loop not wired) + 3 HIGH (delete-account "Permission denied" toast / NSNotificationCenter observer leak / WeakReference KDoc) + 2 MEDIUM (re-entry guard on disable/delete) + 2 LOW (dead Spacer + iOS switch defensive default) — ALL 8 findings landed in fix-up before push. **Operator-side actions**: none — biometric is a client-only concern; no Dashboard config / secrets / migrations needed. **Tech Debt for Phase 26.7**: BiometricSettingsViewModel does not re-query availability on screen `onResume` (only at toggle-ON moment) — alpha tester signal will reveal whether the stale-read window is user-visible.
- **Phase 26.7** ✅ — Post-OAuth profile setup gate + Settings identity discriminator end-to-end on Compose + SwiftUI (ADR-022 §6.6). Closes the "first-time OAuth user lands on ProjectList with display_name = ''" gap by surfacing a one-time `OAuthProfileSetupScreen` between the first Authenticated transition and ProjectList. **New domain models**: `OAuthOnboardingMetadata` (displayName + pictureUrl + primaryProvider — extracted from supabase-kt `auth.currentUserOrNull()?.userMetadata`, reads `full_name` (Apple) → `name` (Google) → null for email/password); `LinkedIdentity` with computed `isAppleRelay` property (true when provider == Apple + email host ends with `@privaterelay.appleid.com`); `enum AuthProviderKind { Email, Apple, Google }`. **AuthRepository (+2 methods)**: `getOAuthOnboardingMetadata()` + `getLinkedIdentities()`; defensive `jsonStringValue` helper for non-primitive / non-string JsonElement handling; picture URL validated HTTPS scheme. **`OAuthProfileSetupPreferences`** (multiplatform-settings, non-encrypted, per-install scope). **`ImportOAuthAvatarUseCase`**: Ktor `body<ByteArray>()` download via `symbolPackHttpClientQualifier`, HTTPS + host allowlist (`*.googleusercontent.com` / `gstatic.com` / `lh3.google.com`), 1MB cap parity, JPEG magic-bytes validation, hands off to existing `storage.upload` + `publicUrl` chain. **`OAuthProfileSetupViewModel`** (lambda-seam DI mirroring MfaEnrollmentViewModel precedent): seeds from metadata, `UpdateDisplayName` / `UseOAuthAvatar` (calls import) / `ChooseDifferentAvatar` (resets flag) / `Submit` (validates non-blank → saves → marks completed → emits Completed nav event) / `Skip` (marks completed without saving) / re-entry guard. **Compose `OAuthProfileSetupScreen`** + **SwiftUI `OAuthProfileSetupScreen.swift`**: title + body + name field + (conditional) avatar tile (Google only) + Save/Skip buttons. **Navigation wiring**: NavGraph adds `OAuthProfileSetup` route; `LaunchedEffect(authState)` short-circuits through gate before ProjectList when `!prefs.isCompleted && metadata.displayName != null`; defers deep-link replay until gate completes. iOS `AppRouter.swift` adds `pendingOAuthSetupMetadata` state + `.onChange(of: authState is AuthStateAuthenticated)` Bool-discriminator collector (Kotlin sealed AuthState doesn't bridge as Equatable on Swift side) + `authenticatedContent` `@ViewBuilder` computed property keeps SwiftUI Group single-typed. **Settings → Account row**: "Signed in via" with primary provider label + Apple relay disclosure; multiple identities (Phase 26.4 linkIdentity success) surface as a "Linked accounts" section. Closed-set `providerLabelKey` helpers + defensive `default` SwiftUI switch arm. **i18n (+16 keys, 517 → 533)**: `title_oauth_profile_setup` / `body_oauth_profile_setup` / `label_oauth_profile_display_name` / `title_oauth_profile_avatar` / `action_{use_oauth_avatar,choose_different_avatar,skip_profile_setup,save_profile_setup}` / `state_oauth_avatar_{imported,importing}` / `label_signed_in_via` / `state_signed_in_via_{apple_relay,apple,google,email}` / `label_linked_identities` × en + ja CMP + iOS xcstrings. **Tests (+29 commonTest, 1722 → 1751)**: 12 `OAuthProfileSetupViewModelTest` (initial-state seeding / UpdateDisplayName + error clear / UseOAuthAvatar success + failure / ChooseDifferentAvatar reset / empty-name FieldRequired / Submit success Completed nav + markGateCompleted / Submit forwards imported avatar / Submit failure surfaces error skips mark / Skip without save / Submit re-entry guard / ClearError); 11 `ImportOAuthAvatarUseCaseTest` (happy / non-https / non-allowlisted host / 404 / non-JPEG / unauthenticated / malformed URL / empty body / oversized body / null storage); 6 `SettingsViewModelTest` Phase 26.7 cases (populates linkedIdentities / clears on Unauthenticated / throw-swallowed / Apple-relay invariant / multiple identities preserve order / initial empty state). **Kover excludes** extended: `OAuthProfileSetupScreenKt*` + `OAuthProfileSetupPreferencesImpl`. **Pre-push invariants all green**: ktlintCheck (auto-formatted KoinHelper) + compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64 + testAndroidHostTest (1751 tests) + koverVerify 80%+ + verifyI18nKeys (533 keys) + verifyIosBetaFlag + assembleDebug + iOS `xcodebuild build` SUCCEEDED. **Operator-side actions**: none — client-only feature, no Dashboard/secrets/migrations. **Tech Debt for Phase 26.8**: in-screen photo picker integration for the "Choose different" affordance (currently routes user to Settings → Profile for arbitrary uploads); BiometricSettingsViewModel does not re-query availability on screen `onResume` (only at toggle-ON moment — Phase 26.6 carryover).

- **Phase 26.8** ✅ — Privacy policy update + smoke test runbook + Tech Debt resolutions (ADR-022 §6.7, closes Phase 26 wave). **Tech Debt 1 (Phase 26.6 carryover) — BiometricSettingsViewModel onResume re-query**: new `BiometricSettingsEvent.RefreshAvailability` event re-queries OS biometric availability whenever the screen mounts (Compose `LaunchedEffect(Unit)` / iOS SwiftUI `.onAppear`). Closes the stale-read window when the user walks through OS Settings to enroll biometric / PIN and returns — toggle becomes enabled without requiring a process restart. **Tech Debt 2 (Phase 26.7 carryover) — OAuth setup "Choose different" hint**: new `OAuthProfileSetupState.chooseDifferentHintVisible` flag flips true on `ChooseDifferentAvatar` event + resets to false when user re-imports via `UseOAuthAvatar`. New i18n key `body_change_avatar_in_profile_hint` ("You can change your picture anytime in Settings → Profile." / 「画像はあとで 設定 → プロフィール からいつでも変更できます。」) surfaces below the avatar tile in both Compose + SwiftUI. Full in-screen photo picker integration deliberately deferred — existing `ProfileViewModel.UploadAvatar` covers arbitrary uploads at the canonical surface (Settings → Profile), avoiding a new `expect/actual` photo picker bridge for marginal UX gain. **Privacy policy update**: `docs/public/privacy-policy/index.html` + `docs/public/ja/privacy-policy/index.html` extended with 3 new `<h3>` subsections: "Sign-In with Apple or Google (OAuth)" (Apple `full_name` first-sign-in-only behavior + private email relay + Google `name` / `picture` claims + opt-in avatar download via host-allowlisted Google CDN); "Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA)" (TOTP server-side at Supabase + bcrypt-hashed recovery code + AAL1 → AAL2 elevation contract); "Biometric Authentication" (Face ID / Touch ID / fingerprint, biometric template stays in Secure Enclave / TEE, sensitive-action gates separate from foreground re-auth gate). Natural Japanese throughout. **Smoke test runbook**: new `docs/en/ops/auth-smoke-test.md` + `docs/ja/ops/auth-smoke-test.md` with 9 sections covering email/password baseline / Apple iOS / Apple Android web-OAuth / Google both platforms / linkIdentity merge / TOTP enrollment + challenge + recovery / biometric foreground + sensitive-action / Phase 26.7 Tech Debt availability refresh / account-deletion cascade verification via Supabase Dashboard. Each section carries a PASS/FAIL template + the operator's expected outcome per platform. Also includes the A0d-6 Data Safety re-submission recipe (Play Console + Apple App Store Connect privacy nutrition facts updates: photos / name / email / OAuth / MFA). **i18n (+1 key, 533 → 534)**: `body_change_avatar_in_profile_hint` × en + ja CMP + iOS xcstrings. **Tests (+3 commonTest, 1751 → 1754)**: 2 `BiometricSettingsViewModelTest` cases (RefreshAvailability picks up newly-enrolled / idempotent on unchanged state); 1 `OAuthProfileSetupViewModelTest` case (re-import hides hint) + extended existing `ChooseDifferentAvatar resets avatarImported flag` to also assert hint surfaces. **Pre-push invariants all green**: ktlintCheck + compileTestKotlinIosSimulatorArm64 + testAndroidHostTest (1754 tests) + koverVerify 80%+ + verifyI18nKeys (534) + verifyIosBetaFlag + assembleDebug + iOS `xcodebuild build` SUCCEEDED. **Operator-side actions remaining**: (1) run `docs/en/ops/auth-smoke-test.md` §1-§9 on real iOS + Android devices before sending first closed-beta tester invite; (2) on PASS, re-submit Play Data Safety + Apple App Privacy per the recipe in the runbook. **Phase 26 wave closes here**; Phase 24 + Phase 26 entries promoted to `docs/en/phase/completed-archive.md` in the next commit per the `### Archive policy` cadence.

**HARD-GATE positioning vs Phase 39 alpha launch**: Phase 26 lands BEFORE TestFlight tester invite + Play Internal Testing tester invite go out. A0d-6 Data Safety「アカウント作成方法」selections updated post-implementation to add **OAuth** + (with MFA shipped) **ユーザー名、パスワード、その他の認証**. A0a-1 Sign In with Apple capability already enabled in App ID + Provisioning Profile so no Apple Developer Portal work needed for OAuth; the new entitlement key + Supabase provider configs + new release-secrets entries (Apple Services ID / Key ID / Team ID / `.p8`; Google Web client ID + iOS / Android client IDs) are the user-side actions added by this wave. MFA + biometric add no new platform credentials but DO add new Settings UI surfaces + commonTest coverage (estimated +30-40 cases across the wave).

**Why MFA + biometric pre-alpha given current asset value is low**: operator's strategic direction (2026-05-14) targets a future user-to-user pattern marketplace where buyer / seller / creator accounts hold real monetary value (purchase history, payout balance, listing revenue). Retrofitting auth-security into an established user base post-marketplace launch is significantly harder than building it from the start — existing users may resist mandatory MFA enrollment, and account-takeover incidents during the retrofit window damage trust during the most-fragile market formation phase. Cost-of-now vs cost-of-later strongly favors now.
